

 
॥ kauṭilīya arthaśāstraṃ ॥

01.1.02 tasyāyaṃ prakaraṇādhikaraṇasamuddeśaḥ
01.1.03a vidyāsamuddeśaḥ, vṛddhasamuddeśaḥ, indriyajayaḥ, amātya utpattiḥ, mantripurohita utpattiḥ, upadhābhiḥ śaucāśaucajñānaṃ amātyānāṃ, -
01.1.03b gūḍhapuruṣapraṇidhiḥ, svaviṣaye kṛtyākṛtyapakṣarakṣaṇaṃ, paraviṣaye kṛtyākṛtyapakṣa upagrahaḥ,
01.1.03ch mantrādhikāraḥ, dūtapraṇidhiḥ, rājaputrarakṣaṇaṃ, aparuddhavṛttaṃ, aparuddhe vṛttiḥ, rājapraṇidhiḥ, niśāntapraṇidhiḥ, ātmarakṣitakaṃ, , iti vinayādhikārikaṃ prathamaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.04a janapadaniveśaḥ, bhūmicchidrāpidhānaṃ, durgavidhānaṃ, durganiveśaḥ, samnidhātṛnicayakarma, samāhartṛsamudayaprasthāpanaṃ, akṣapaṭale gāṇanikyādhikāraḥ,
01.1.04b samudayasya yuktāpahṛtasya pratyānayanaṃ, upayuktaparīkṣā, śāsanādhikāraḥ, kośapraveśyaratnaparīkṣā, ākarakarmāntapravartanaṃ, akṣaśālāyāṃ suvarṇādhyakṣaḥ
01.1.04ch viśikhāyāṃ sauvarṇikapracāraḥ, koṣṭhāgārādhyakṣaḥ, paṇyādhyakṣaḥ, kupyādhyakṣaḥ, āyudhādhyakṣaḥ, tulāmānapautavaṃ,
01.1.04d deśakālamānaṃ, śulkādhyakṣaḥ, sūtrādhyakṣaḥ, sītādhyakṣaḥ, surā'dhyakṣaḥ, sūnādhyakṣaḥ, gaṇikā'dhyakṣaḥ,
01.1.04e nāv'dhyakṣaḥ, go'dhyakṣaḥ, aśvādhyakṣaḥ, hasty'dhyakṣaḥ, rathādhyakṣaḥ, patty'dhyakṣaḥ, senāpatipracāraḥ, mudrā'dhyakṣaḥ, vivītādhyakṣaḥ, samāhartṛpracāraḥ,
01.1.04f gṛhapatikavaidehakatāpasavyañjanāḥ praṇidhayaḥ, nāgarikapraṇidhiḥ  ityadhyakṣapracāro dvitīyaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.05a vyavahārasthāpanā, vivādapadanibandhaḥ, vivāhasamyuktaṃ, dāyavibhāgaḥ, vāstukaṃ, samayasya anapākarma, ṛṇādānaṃ, aupanidhikaṃ, dāsakarmakarakalpaḥ,
01.1.05b sambhūya samutthānaṃ, vikrītakrītānuśayaḥ, dattasya anapākarma, asvāmivikrayaḥ, svasvāmisambandhaḥ, sāhasaṃ, vākpāruṣyaṃ, daṇḍapāruṣyaṃ, dyūtasamāhvayaṃ, prakīrṇakaṃ - iti, dharmasthīyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.06a kārukarakṣaṇaṃ, vaidehakarakṣaṇaṃ, upanipātapratīkāraḥ, gūḍhājīvināṃ rakṣā, siddhavyañjanairmāṇavaprakāśanaṃ, śaṅkārūpakarmābhigrahaḥ,
01.1.06b āśumṛtakaparīkṣā, vākyakarmānuyogaḥ, sarvādhikaraṇarakṣaṇaṃ
01.1.06ch ekāṅgavadhaniṣkrayaḥ, śuddhaścitraśca daṇḍa kalpaḥ, kanyāprakarma, aticāradaṇḍāḥ - iti kaṇṭakaśodhanaṃ caturthaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.07 dāṇḍakarmikaṃ, kośābhisaṃharaṇaṃ, bhṛtyabharaṇīyaṃ, anujīvivṛttaṃ, samayācārikaṃ, rājyapratisandhānaṃ, ekāiśvaryaṃ - iti yogavṛttaṃ pañcamaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.08 prakṛtisampadaḥ, śamavyāyāmikaṃ - iti maṇḍalayoniḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.09a ṣāḍguṇyasamuddeśaḥ, kṣayasthānavṛddhiniścayaḥ, saṃśrayavṛttiḥ, samahīnajyāyasāṃ guṇābhiniveśaḥ, hīnasandhayaḥ, vigṛhya āsanaṃ, sandhāya āsanaṃ, vigṛhya yānaṃ, sandhāya yānaṃ,
01.1.09b sambhūya prayāṇaṃ, yātavyāmitrayorabhigrahacintā, kṣayalobhavirāgahetavaḥ prakṛtīnāṃ, sāmavāyikaviparimarśaḥ,
01.1.09ch saṃhita prayāṇikaṃ, paripaṇitāparipaṇitāpasṛtāḥ sandhayaḥ, dvaidhībhāvikāḥ sandhivikramāḥ, yātavyavṛttiḥ, anugrāhyamitraviśeṣāḥ,
01.1.09d mitrahiraṇyabhūmikarmasandhayaḥ, pārṣṇigrāhacintā, hīnaśaktipūraṇaṃ, balavatā vigṛhya uparodhahetavaḥ, daṇḍa upanatavṛttaṃ,
01.1.09e daṇḍa upanāyivṛttaṃ, sandhikarma, samādhimokṣaḥ, madhyamacaritaṃ, udāsīnacaritaṃ, maṇḍalacaritaṃ - iti ṣāḍguṇyaṃ saptamaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.10 prakṛtivyasanavargaḥ, rājarājyayorvyasanacintā, puruṣavyasanavargaḥ, pīḍanavargaḥ, stambhavargaḥ, kośasaṅgavargaḥ, mitravyasanavargaḥ - iti vyasanādhikārikaṃ aṣṭamaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.11a śaktideśakālabalābalajñānaṃ, yātrākālāḥ, bala upādānakālāḥ, samnāhaguṇāḥ, pratibalakarma, paścāt kopacintā, bāhyābhyantaraprakṛtikopapratīkārāḥ
01.1.11b kṣayavyayalābhaviparimarśaḥ, bāhyābhyantarāścāpadaḥ, duṣyaśatrusamyuktāḥ, arthānarthasaṃśayayuktāḥ, tāsāṃ upāyavikalpajāḥ siddhayaḥ - ityabhiyāsyat karma navamaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.12 skandhāvāraniveśaḥ, skandhāvāraprayāṇaṃ, balavyasanāvaskandakālarakṣaṇaṃ, kūṭayuddhavikalpāḥ, svasainya utsāhanaṃ, svabalānyabalavyāyogaḥ, yuddhabhūmayaḥ, patty'śvarathahastikarmāṇi, pakṣakakṣa urasyānāṃ balāgrato vyūhavibhāgaḥ, sāraphalgubalavibhāgaḥ, patty'śvarathahastiyuddhāni, daṇḍabhogamaṇḍalāsaṃhatavyūhavyūhanaṃ, tasya prativyūhasthāpanaṃ - iti sāṅgrāmikaṃ daśamaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.13 bheda upādānāni, upāṃśudaṇḍāḥ - iti saṅghavṛttaṃ ekādaśaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.14 dūtakarma, mantrayuddhaṃ, senāmukhyavadhaḥ, maṇḍalaprotsāhanaṃ, śastrāgnirasapraṇidhayaḥ, vīvadhāsāraprasāravadhaḥ, yogātisandhānaṃ, daṇḍātisandhānaṃ, ekavijayaḥ - ityābalīyasaṃ dvādaśaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.15 upajāpaḥ, yogavāmanaṃ, apasarpapraṇidhiḥ, paryupāsanakarma, avamardaḥ, labdhapraśamanaṃ - iti durgalambha upāyaḥ trayodaśaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.16 parabalaghātaprayogaḥ, pralambhanaṃ, svabala upaghātapratīkāraḥ - ityaupaniṣadikaṃ caturdaśaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.17 tantrayuktayaḥ - iti tantrayuktiḥ pañcadaśaṃ adhikaraṇam
01.1.18 śāstrasamuddeśaḥ pañcadaśādhikaraṇāni sa-aśītiprakaraṇaśataṃ sa-pañcāśad'dhyāyaśataṃ ṣaṭślokasahasrāṇi iti
01.1.19ab sukhagrahaṇavijñeyaṃ tattvārthapadaniścitam ।
01.1.19chd kauṭilyena kṛtaṃ śāstraṃ vimuktagranthavistaram  (iti)
   Chapt .   Section.1: Enumeration of the sciences
  i) Establishing (the necessity of) philosophy
01.2.01 ānvīkṣikī trayī vārttā daṇḍanītiśca iti vidyāḥ
01.2.02 trayī vārttā daṇḍa nītiśca iti mānavāḥ
01.2.03 trayī viśeṣo hyānvīkṣikī iti
01.2.04 vārttā daṇḍanītiśca iti bārhaspatyāḥ
01.2.05 saṃvaraṇamātraṃ hi trayī lokayātrāvida iti
01.2.06 daṇḍanītirekā vidyā ityauśanasāḥ
01.2.07 tasyāṃ hi sarvavidyā''rambhāḥ pratibaddhā iti
01.2.08 catasra eva vidyā iti kauṭilyaḥ
01.2.09 tābhirdharmārthau yad vidyāt tad vidyānāṃ vidyātvam
01.2.10 sāṅkhyaṃ yogo lokāyataṃ ca ityānvīkṣikī
01.2.11 dharmādharmau trayyāṃ arthānarthau vārttāyāṃ nayānayau daṇḍanītyāṃ balābale ca etāsāṃ hetubhiranvīkṣamāṇā lokasya upakaroti vyasane'bhyudaye ca buddhiṃ avasthāpayati prajñāvākyakriyāvaiśāradyaṃ ca karoti
01.2.12ab pradīpaḥ sarvavidyānāṃ upāyaḥ sarvakarmaṇām ।
01.2.12chd āśrayaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ śaśvad ānvīkṣikī matā  (iti)
   Chapt .   Section.1, (I) Establishing (the necessity of) the Vedic Lore
01.3.01 sāma।ṛgyajurvedāḥ trayaḥ trayī
01.3.02 atharvaveda itihāsavedau ca vedāḥ
01.3.03 śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chandovicitirjyotiṣaṃ iti cāṅgāni
01.3.04 eṣa trayīdharmaścaturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ āśramāṇāṃ ca svadharmasthāpanād aupakārikaḥ
01.3.05 svadharmo brāhmaṇasya adhyayanaṃ adhyāpanaṃ yajanaṃ yājanaṃ dānaṃ pratigrahaśca
01.3.06 kṣatriyasyādhyayanaṃ yajanaṃ dānaṃ śastrājīvo bhūtarakṣaṇaṃ ca
01.3.07 vaiśyasyādhyayanaṃ yajanaṃ dānaṃ kṛṣipāśupālye vaṇijyā ca
01.3.08 śūdrasya dvijātiśuśrūṣā vārttā kārukuśīlavakarma ca
01.3.09 gṛhasthasya svadharmājīvaḥ tulyairasamāna।ṛṣibhirvaivāhyaṃ ṛtugāmitvaṃ devapitr'tithipūjā bhṛtyeṣu tyāgaḥ śeṣabhojanaṃ ca
01.3.10 brahmacāriṇaḥ svādhyāyo agnikāryābhiṣekau bhaikṣavratitvaṃ ācārye prāṇāntikī vṛttiḥ tad'bhāve guruputre sa-brahmacāriṇi vā
01.3.11 vānaprasthasya brahmacaryaṃ bhūmau śayyā jaṭā'jinadhāraṇaṃ agnihotrābhiṣekau devatāpitr'tithipūjā vanyaścāhāraḥ
01.3.12 parivrājakasya jita indriyatvaṃ anārambho niṣkiñcanatvaṃ saṅgatyāgo bhaikṣavrataṃ anekatrāraṇye ca vāso bāhyābhyantaraṃ ca śaucam
01.3.13 sarveṣāṃ ahiṃsā satyaṃ śaucaṃ anasūya ānṛśaṃsyaṃ kṣamā ca
01.3.14 svadharmaḥ svargāyānantyāya ca
01.3.15 tasyātikrame lokaḥ saṅkarād ucchidyeta
01.3.16ab tasmāt svadharmaṃ bhūtānāṃ rājā na vyabhicārayet ।
01.3.16chd svadharmaṃ sandadhāno hi pretya ca iha ca nandati
01.3.17ab vyavasthitāryamaryādaḥ kṛtavarṇāśramasthitiḥ ।
01.3.17chd trayyā'bhirakṣito lokaḥ prasīdati na sīdati  (iti)
   Chapt .   Ii) Establishing (the necessity of) Economics, and (iv) the Science of Politics
01.4.01 kṛṣipāśupālye vaṇijyā ca vārtā, dhānyapaśuhiraṇyakupyaviṣṭipradānād aupakārikī
01.4.02 tayā svapakṣaṃ parapakṣaṃ ca vaśīkaroti kośadaṇḍābhyām
01.4.03 ānvīkṣikī trayī vārttānāṃ yogakṣemasādhano daṇḍaḥ, tasya nītirdaṇḍa nītiḥ, alabdhalābhārthā labdhaparirakṣaṇī rakṣitavivardhanī vṛddhasya tīrthe pratipādanī ca
01.4.04 tasyāṃ āyattā lokayātrā
01.4.05 tasmāllokayātrā'rthī nityaṃ udyatadaṇḍaḥ syāt
01.4.06 na hyevaṃvidhaṃ vaśa upanayanaṃ asti bhūtānāṃ yathā daṇḍaḥ । ityācāryāḥ
01.4.07 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
01.4.08 tīkṣṇadaṇḍo hi bhūtānāṃ udvejanīyo bhavati
01.4.09 mṛdudaṇḍaḥ paribhūyate
01.4.10 yathā'rhadaṇḍaḥ pūjyate
01.4.11 suvijñātapraṇīto hi daṇḍaḥ prajā dharmārthakāmairyojayati
01.4.12 duṣpraṇītaḥ kāmakrodhābhyāṃ avajñānād vā vānaprasthaparivrājakān api kopayati, kiṃ'ṅga punargṛhasthān
01.4.13 apraṇītaḥ tu mātsyanyāyaṃ udbhāvayati
01.4.14 balīyān abalaṃ hi grasate daṇḍadharābhāve
01.4.15 sa tena guptaḥ prabhavati iti
01.4.16ab caturvarṇāśramo loko rājñā daṇḍena pālitaḥ ।
01.4.16chd svadharmakarmābhirato vartate sveṣu vartmasu  (iti)
   Chapt .   Section.2: Association with elders
01.5.01 tasmād daṇḍamūlāḥ tisro vidyāḥ
01.5.02 vinayamūlo daṇḍaḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ yogakṣemāvahaḥ
01.5.03 kṛtakaḥ svābhāvikaśca vinayaḥ
01.5.04 kriyā hi dravyaṃ vinayati nādravyam
01.5.05 śuśrūṣā śravaṇagrahaṇadhāraṇavijñāna ūhāpohatattvābhiniviṣṭabuddhiṃ vidyā vinayati na itaram
01.5.06 vidyānāṃ tu yathāsvaṃ ācāryaprāmāṇyād vinayo niyamaśca
01.5.07 vṛttacaulakarmā lipiṃ saṅkhyānaṃ ca upayuñjīta
01.5.08 vṛtta upanayanaḥ trayīṃ ānvīkṣikīṃ ca śiṣṭebhyo vārttāṃ adhyakṣebhyo daṇḍanītiṃ vaktṛprayoktṛbhyaḥ
01.5.09 brahmacaryaṃ ca ṣoḍaśād varṣāt
01.5.10 ato godānaṃ dārakarma cāsya
01.5.11 nityaśca vidyāvṛddhasamyogo vinayavṛddhy'rthaṃ, tanmūlatvād vinayasya
01.5.12 pūrvaṃ aharbhāgaṃ hasty'śvarathapraharaṇavidyāsu vinayaṃ gacchet ।
01.5.13 paścimaṃ itihāsaśravaṇe
01.5.14 purāṇaṃ itivṛttaṃ ākhyāyika udāharaṇaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ arthaśāstraṃ ca iti itihāsaḥ
01.5.15 śeṣaṃ ahorātrabhāgaṃ apūrvagrahaṇaṃ gṛhītaparicayaṃ ca kuryāt, agṛhītānāṃ ābhīkṣṇyaśravaṇaṃ ca
01.5.16 śrutādd hi prajñā upajāyate prajñāyā yogo yogād ātmavattā iti vidyānāṃ sāmarthyam
01.5.17ab vidyāvinīto rājā hi prajānāṃ vinaye rataḥ ।
01.5.17chd ananyāṃ pṛthivīṃ bhuṅkte sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Section.3: Control over the senses, (i) Casting out the group of six enemies
01.6.01 vidyā vinayaheturindriyajayaḥ kāmakrodhalobhamānamadaharṣatyāgāt kāryaḥ
01.6.02 karṇatvag'kṣijihvāghrāṇa indriyāṇāṃ śabdasparśarūparasagandheṣvavipratipattirindriyajayaḥ, śāstrānuṣṭhānaṃ vā
01.6.03 kṛtsnaṃ hi śāstraṃ idaṃ indriyajayaḥ
01.6.04 tad viruddhavṛttiravaśya indriyaścāturanto api rājā sadyo vinaśyati
01.6.05 yathā dāṇḍakyo nāma bhojaḥ kāmād brāhmaṇakanyāṃ abhimanyamānaḥ sa-bandhurāṣṭro vinanāśa, karālaśca vaidehaḥ
01.6.06 kopāj janamejayo brāhmaṇeṣu vikrāntaḥ, tālajaṅghaśca bhṛguṣu
01.6.07 lobhād ailaścāturvarṇyaṃ atyāhārayamāṇaḥ, sauvīraścājabinduḥ ।
01.6.08 mānād rāvaṇaḥ paradārān aprayacchan, duryodhano rājyād aṃśaṃ ca
01.6.09 madād dambhodbhavo bhūtāvamānī, haihayaścārjunaḥ
01.6.10 harṣād vātāpiragastyaṃ atyāsādayan, vṛṣṇisaṅghaśca dvaipāyanaṃ iti
01.6.11ab ete cānye ca bahavaḥ śatruṣaḍvargaṃ āśritāḥ ।
01.6.11chd sa-bandhurāṣṭrā rājāno vineśurajita indriyāḥ
01.6.12ab śatruṣaḍvargaṃ utsṛjya jāmadagnyo jita indriyaḥ ।
01.6.12chd ambarīṣaśca nābhāgo bubhujāte ciraṃ mahīm  (iti)
   Chapt .   I) The life of a sage-like king
01.7.01 tasmād ariṣaḍvargatyāgena indriyajayaṃ kurvīta, vṛddhasamyogena prajñāṃ, cāreṇa cakṣuḥ, utthānena yogakṣemasādhanaṃ, kāryānuśāsanena svadharmasthāpanaṃ, vinayaṃ vidyā upadeśena, lokapriyatvaṃ arthasamyogena vṛttim
01.7.02 evaṃ vaśya indriyaḥ parastrīdravyahiṃsāśca varjayet, svapnaṃ laulyaṃ anṛtaṃ uddhataveṣatvaṃ anarthyasamyogaṃ adharmasamyuktaṃ anarthasamyuktaṃ ca vyavahāram
01.7.03 dharmārthāvirodhena kāmaṃ seveta, na nihsukhaḥ syāt
01.7.04 samaṃ vā trivargaṃ anyonyānubaddham
01.7.05 eko hyatyāsevito dharmārthakāmānāṃ ātmānaṃ itarau ca pīḍayati
01.7.06 artha eva pradhāna iti kauṭilyaḥ
01.7.07 arthamūlau hi dharmakāmāviti
01.7.08 maryādāṃ sthāpayed ācāryān amātyān vā, ya enaṃ apāya sthānebhyo vārayeyuḥ, chāyānālikāpratodena vā rahasi pramādyantaṃ abhitudeyuḥ
01.7.09ab sahāyasādhyaṃ rājatvaṃ cakraṃ ekaṃ na vartate ।
01.7.09chd kurvīta sacivāṃḥ tasmāt teṣāṃ ca śṛṇuyān matam  (iti)
   Chapt .   Appointment of ministers
01.8.01 sahādhyāyino amātyān kurvīta, dṛṣṭaśaucasāmarthyatvāt iti bhāradvājaḥ
01.8.02 te hyasya viśvāsyā bhavanti iti
01.8.03 na iti viśālākṣaḥ
01.8.04 sahakrīḍitatvāt paribhavantyenam
01.8.05 ye hyasya guhyasadharmāṇaḥ tān amātyān kurvīta, samānaśīlavyasanatvāt
01.8.06 te hyasya marmajñabhayānnāparādhyanti iti
01.8.07 sādhāraṇa eṣa doṣaḥ iti pārāśarāḥ
01.8.08 teṣāṃ api marmajñabhayāt kṛtākṛtānyanuvarteta
01.8.09ab yāvadbhyo guhyaṃ ācaṣṭe janebhyaḥ puruṣādhipaḥ ।
01.8.09chd avaśaḥ karmaṇā tena vaśyo bhavati tāvatām
01.8.10 ya enaṃ āpatsu prāṇābādhayuktāsvanugṛhṇīyuḥ tān amātyān kurvīta, dṛṣṭānurāgatvāt iti
01.8.11 na iti piśunaḥ
01.8.12 bhaktireṣā na buddhiguṇaḥ
01.8.13 saṅkhyātārtheṣu karmasu niyuktā ye yathā''diṣṭaṃ arthaṃ saviśeṣaṃ vā kuryuḥ tān amātyān kurvīta, dṛṣṭaguṇatvāt iti
01.8.14 na iti kauṇapadantaḥ
01.8.15 anyairamātyaguṇairayuktā hyete
01.8.16 pitṛpaitāmahān amātyān kurvīta, dṛṣṭāvadānatvāt
01.8.17 te hyenaṃ apacarantaṃ api na tyajanti, sagandhatvāt
01.8.18 amānuṣeṣvapi ca etad dṛśyate
01.8.19 gāvo hyasagandhaṃ gogaṇaṃ atikramya sagandheṣvevāvatiṣṭhante iti
01.8.20 na iti vātavyādhiḥ
01.8.21 te hyasya sarvaṃ avagṛhya svāmivat pracaranti
01.8.22 tasmānnītivido navān amātyān kurvīta
01.8.23 navāḥ tu yamasthāne daṇḍadharaṃ manyamānā nāparādhyanti iti
01.8.24 na iti bāhudantī putraḥ
01.8.25 śāstravid adṛṣṭakarmā karmasu viṣādaṃ gacchet
01.8.26 tasmād abhijanaprajñāśaucaśauryānurāgayuktān amātyān kurvīta, guṇaprādhānyāt iti
01.8.27 sarvaṃ upapannaṃ iti kauṭilyaḥ
01.8.28 kāryasāmarthyādd hi puruṣasāmarthyaṃ kalpyate
01.8.29ab sāmarthyaśca  vibhajyāmātyavibhavaṃ deśakālau ca karma ca ।
01.8.29chd amātyāḥ sarva eva ete kāryāḥ syurna tu mantriṇaḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Appointment of counsellors and chaplain
01.9.01 jānapado abhijātaḥ svavagrahaḥ kṛtaśilpaścakṣuṣmān prājño dhārayiṣṇurdakṣo vāgmī pragalbhaḥ pratipattimān utsāhaprabhāvayuktaḥ kleśasahaḥ śucirmaitro dṛḍhabhaktiḥ śīlabalārogyasattvayuktaḥ stambhacāpalahīnaḥ sampriyo vairāṇāṃ akartā ityamātyasampat
01.9.02 ataḥ pādārghaguṇahīnau madhyamāvarau
01.9.03 teṣāṃ janapad'bhijanaṃ avagrahaṃ cāptataḥ parīkṣeta, samānavidyebhyaḥ śilpaṃ śāstracakṣuṣmattāṃ ca, karmārambheṣu prajñāṃ dhārayiṣṇutāṃ dākṣyaṃ ca, kathāyogeṣu vāgmitvaṃ prāgalbhyaṃ pratibhānavattvaṃ ca, saṃvāsibhyaḥ śīlabalārogyasattvayogaṃ astambhaṃ acāpalaṃ ca, pratyakṣataḥ sampriyatvaṃ avairatvaṃ ca
01.9.04 pratyakṣaparokṣānumeyā hi rājavṛttiḥ
01.9.05 svayaṃ drṣṭaṃ pratyakṣam
01.9.06 para upadiṣṭaṃ parokṣam
01.9.07 karmasu kṛtenākṛtāvekṣaṇaṃ anumeyam
01.9.08 yaugapadyāt tu karmaṇāṃ anekatvād anekasthatvācca deśakālātyayo mā bhūd iti parokṣaṃ amātyaiḥ kārayet ityamātyakarma ।
01.9.09 purohitaṃ udita uditakulaśīlaṃ sa-aṅge vede daive nimitte daṇḍanītyāṃ cābhivinītaṃ āpadāṃ daivamānuṣīṇāṃ atharvabhirupāyaiśca pratikartāraṃ kurvīta
01.9.10 taṃ ācāryaṃ śiṣyaḥ pitaraṃ putro bhṛtyaḥ svāminaṃ iva cānuvarteta
01.9.11ab brāhmaṇena edhitaṃ kṣatraṃ mantrimantrābhimantritam ।

01.10.01 mantripurohitasakhaḥ sāmānyeṣvadhikaraṇeṣu sthāpayitvā'mātyān upadhābhiḥ śodhayet
01.10.02 purohitaṃ ayājyayājanādhyāpane niyuktaṃ amṛṣyamāṇaṃ rājā'vakṣipet
01.10.03 sa sattribhiḥ śapathapūrvaṃ ekaikaṃ amātyaṃ upajāpayet - adhārmiko ayaṃ rājā, sādhu dhārmikaṃ anyaṃ asya tatkulīnaṃ aparuddhaṃ kulyaṃ ekapragrahaṃ sāmantaṃ āṭavikaṃ aupapādikaṃ vā pratipādayāmaḥ, sarveṣāṃ etad rocate, kathaṃ vā tava iti
01.10.04 pratyākhyāne śuciḥ । iti dharma upadhā
01.10.05 senāpatirasatpragraheṇāvakṣiptaḥ sattribhirekaikaṃ amātyaṃ upajāpayet lobhanīyenārthena rājavināśāya, sarveṣāṃ etad rocate, kathaṃ vā tava iti
01.10.06 pratyākhyāne śuciḥ । ityartha upadhā
01.10.07 parivrājikā labdhaviśvāsā'ntaḥpure kṛtasatkārā mahāmātraṃ ekaikaṃ upajapet - rājamahiṣī tvāṃ kāmayate kṛtasamāgama upāyā, mahān arthaśca te bhaviṣyati iti
01.10.08 pratyākhyāne śuciḥ । iti kāma upadhā
01.10.09 prahavaṇanimittaṃ eko amātyaḥ sarvān amātyān āvāhayet
01.10.10 tena udvegena rājā tān avarundhyāt
01.10.11 kāpaṭikaścātra pūrvāvaruddhaḥ teṣāṃ arthamānāvakṣiptaṃ ekaikaṃ amātyaṃ upajapet - asat pravṛtto ayaṃ rājā, sādhvenaṃ hatvā'nyaṃ pratipādayāmaḥ, sarveṣāṃ etad rocate, kathaṃ vā tava iti
01.10.12 pratyākhyāne śuciḥ । iti bhaya upadhā
01.10.13 tatra dharma upadhāśuddhān dharmasthīyakaṇṭakaśodhaneṣu karmasu sthāpayet, artha upadhāśuddhān samāhartṛsamnidhātṛnicayakarmasu, kāma upadhā śuddhān bāhyābhyantaravihārarakṣāsu, bhaya upadhāśuddhān āsannakāryeṣu rājñaḥ
01.10.14 sarva upadhāśuddhān mantriṇaḥ kuryāt
01.10.15 sarvatrāśucīn khanidravyahastivanakarmānteṣu upayojayet
01.10.16ab trivargabhayasaṃśuddhān amātyān sveṣu karmasu ।
01.10.16chd adhikuryād yathā śaucaṃ ityācāryā vyavasthitāḥ
01.10.17ab na tveva kuryād ātmānaṃ devīṃ vā lakṣyaṃ īśvaraḥ ।
01.10.17chd śaucahetoramātyānāṃ etat kauṭilyadarśanam
01.10.18ab na dūṣaṇaṃ aduṣṭasya viṣeṇa ivāmbhasaścaret ।
01.10.18chd kadācidd hi praduṣṭasya nādhigamyeta bheṣajam
01.10.19ab kṛtā ca kaluṣābuddhirupadhābhiścaturvidhā ।
01.10.19chd nāgatvā'ntaṃ nivarteta sthitā sattvavatāṃ dhṛtau

   Chapt .   Appointment of persons in secret service
01.11.01 upadhābhiḥ śuddhāmātyavargo gūḍhapuruṣān utpādayet kāpaṭika udāsthitagṛhapatikavaidehakatāpasavyañjanān sattritīṣkṇarasadabhikṣukīśca
01.11.02 paramarmajñaḥ pragalbhaśchātraḥ kāpaṭikaḥ
01.11.03 taṃ arthamānābhyāṃ protsāhya mantrī brūyāt - rājānaṃ māṃ ca pramāṇaṃ kṛtvā yasya yad akuśalaṃ paśyasi tat tadānīṃ eva pratyādiśa iti
01.11.04 pravrajyā pratyavasitaḥ prajñāśaucayukta udāsthitaḥ
01.11.05 sa vārttākarmapradiṣṭāyāṃ bhūmau prabhūtahiraṇyāntevāsī karma kārayet
01.11.06 karmaphalācca sarvapravrajitānāṃ grāsācchādanāvasathān pratividadhyāt
01.11.07 vṛttikāmāṃśca upajapet - etena eva veṣeṇa rājārthaścaritavyo bhaktavetanakāle ca upasthātavyam iti
01.11.08 sarvapravrajitāśca svaṃ svaṃ vargaṃ evaṃ upajapeyuḥ
01.11.09 karṣako vṛttikṣīṇaḥ prajñāśaucayukto gṛhapatikavyañjanaḥ
01.11.10 sa kṛṣikarmapradiṣṭāyāṃ bhūmau - iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
01.11.11 vāṇijako vṛttikṣīṇaḥ prajñāśaucayukto vaidehakavyañjanaḥ
01.11.12 sa vaṇikkarmapradiṣṭāyāṃ bhūmau - iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
01.11.13 muṇḍo jaṭilo vā vṛttikāmaḥ tāpasavyañjanaḥ
01.11.14 sa nagarābhyāśe prabhūtamuṇḍajaṭilāntevāsī śākaṃ yavamuṣṭiṃ vā māsadvimāsāntaraṃ prakāśaṃ aśnīyāt, gūḍhaṃ iṣṭaṃ āhāram
01.11.15 vaidehakāntevāsinaśca enaṃ samiddhayogairarcayeyuḥ
01.11.16 śiṣyāścāsyāvedayeyuḥ - asau siddhaḥ sāmedhikaḥ iti
01.11.17 samedhāśāstibhiścābhigatānāṃ aṅgavidyayā śiṣyasaṃjñābhiśca karmāṇyabhijane avasitānyādiśet - alpalābhaṃ agnidāhaṃ corabhayaṃ dūṣyavadhaṃ tuṣṭidānaṃ videśapravṛttijñānaṃ, idaṃ adya śvo vā bhaviṣyati, idaṃ vā rājā kariṣyati iti
01.11.18 tad asya gūḍhāḥ sattriṇaśca sampādayeyuḥ
01.11.19 sattvaprajñāvākyaśaktisampannānāṃ rājabhāgyaṃ anuvyāharet, mantrisamyogaṃ ca brūyāt
01.11.20 mantrī ca eṣāṃ vṛttikarmabhyāṃ viyateta
01.11.21 ye ca kāraṇād abhikruddhāḥ tān arthamānābhyāṃ śamayet, akāraṇakruddhāṃḥ tūṣṇīṃ daṇḍena, rājadviṣṭakāriṇaśca
01.11.22ab pūjitāścārthamānābhyāṃ rājñā rāja upajīvinām ।
01.11.22chd jānīyuḥ śaucaṃ ityetāḥ pañcasaṃsthāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Appointment of roving spies Rules for secret servants
01.12.01 ye cāpyasmabandhino avaśyabhartavyāḥ te lakṣaṇaṃ aṅgavidyāṃ jambhakavidyāṃ māyāgataṃ āśramadharmaṃ nimittaṃ antaracakraṃ ityadhīyānāḥ sattriṇaḥ, saṃsargavidyāṃ ca
01.12.02 ye janapade śūrāḥ tyaktātmāno hastinaṃ vyālaṃ vā dravyahetoḥ pratiyodhayeyuḥ te tīkṣṇāḥ

01.12.04 parivrājikā vṛttikāmā daridrā vidhavā pragalbhā brāhmaṇyantaḥpure kṛtasatkārā mahāmātrakulānyabhigacchet

sāmarthyayogāccāpasarpayet
01.12.07 teṣāṃ bāhyaṃ cāraṃ chatrabhṛṅgāravyajanapādukāsanayānavāhana upagrāhiṇaḥ tīkṣṇā vidyuḥ
01.12.08 taṃ sattriṇaḥ saṃsthāsvarpayeyuḥ
01.12.09 sūdārālikasnāpakasaṃvāhakāstarakakalpakaprasādhaka udakaparicārakā rasadāḥ
kubjavāmanakirātamūkabadhirajaḍāndhacchadmāno naṭanartakagāyanavādakavāgjīvanakuśīlavāḥ

01.12.12 na cānyonyaṃ saṃsthāḥ te vā vidyuḥ

01.12.17 kaṇṭakaśodhana uktāścāpasarpāḥ pareṣu kṛtavetanā vaseyurasampātinaścārārtham

01.12.20ab evaṃ śatrau ca mitre ca madhyame cāvapeccarān ।

01.13.01 kṛtamahāmātrāpasarpaḥ paurajānapadān apasarpayet
01.13.02 sattriṇo dvandvinaḥ tīrthasabhāpūgajanasamavāyeṣu vivādaṃ kuryuḥ
01.13.03 sarvaguṇasampannaścāyaṃ rājā śrūyate, na cāsya kaścid guṇo dṛśyate yaḥ paurajānapadān daṇḍakarābhyāṃ pīḍayati iti
01.13.04 tatra ye'nupraśaṃseyuḥ tān itaraḥ taṃ ca pratiṣedhayet
01.13.05 mātsyanyāyābhibhūtāḥ prajā manuṃ vaivasvataṃ rājānaṃ cakrire
01.13.06 dhānyaṣaḍbhāgaṃ paṇyadaśabhāgaṃ hiraṇyaṃ cāsya bhāgadheyaṃ prakalpayām-āsuḥ
01.13.07 tena bhṛtā rājānaḥ prajānāṃ yogakṣemāvahāḥ

01.13.09 tasmād uñchaṣaḍbhāgaṃ āraṇyakā'pi nirvapanti - tasya etad bhāgadheyaṃ yo'smān gopāyati iti
01.13.10 indrayamasthānaṃ etad rājānaḥ pratyakṣaheḍaprasādāḥ
01.13.11 tān avamanyamānān daivo'pi daṇḍaḥ spṛśati

01.13.15 ye cāsya dhānyapaśuhiraṇyānyājīvanti, tairupakurvanti vyasane'bhyudaye vā, kupitaṃ bandhuṃ rāṣṭraṃ vā vyāvartayanti, amitraṃ āṭavikaṃ vā pratiṣedhayanti, teṣāṃ muṇḍajaṭilavyañjanāḥ tuṣṭātuṣṭatvaṃ vidyuḥ
01.13.16 tuṣṭān bhūyo'rthamānābhyāṃ pūjayet

01.13.18 parasparād vā bhedayed enān, sāmantāṭavikatatkulīnāparuddhebhyaśca

01.13.22 kruddhalubdhabhītamāninaḥ tu pareṣāṃ kṛtyāḥ
01.13.23 teṣāṃ kārtāntikanaimittikamauhūrtikavyañjanāḥ parasparābhisambandhaṃ amitrāṭavikasambandhaṃ vā vidyuḥ

01.14.01 kṛtyākṛtyapakṣa upagrahaḥ svaviṣaye vyākhyātaḥ, paraviṣaye vācyaḥ
01.14.02 saṃśrutyārthān vipralabdhaḥ, tulyakāriṇoḥ śilpe vā upakāre vā vimānitaḥ, vallabhāvaruddhaḥ,
samāhūya parājitaḥ, pravāsa upataptaḥ, kṛtvā vyayaṃ alabdhakāryaḥ, svadharmād dāyādyād vā uparuddhaḥ,
mānādhikārābhyāṃ bhraṣṭaḥ, kulyairantarhitaḥ, prasabhābhimṛṣṭastrīkaḥ, kārābhinyastaḥ,
para uktadaṇḍitaḥ, mithyā''cāravāritaḥ, sarvasvaṃ āhāritaḥ, bandhanaparikliṣṭaḥ, pravāsitabandhuḥ
iti kruddhavargaḥ
01.14.03 svayaṃ upahataḥ, viprakṛtaḥ, pāpakarmābhikhyātaḥ, tulyadoṣadaṇḍena udvignaḥ, paryāttabhūmiḥ, daṇḍena upanataḥ, sarvādhikaraṇasthaḥ, sahasā upacitārthaḥ, tatkulīna upāśaṃsuḥ, pradviṣṭo rājñā, rājadveṣī ca - iti bhītavargaḥ
01.14.04 parikṣīṇaḥ, anyāttasvaḥ, kadaryaḥ, vyasanī, atyāhitavyavahāraśca - iti lubdhavargaḥ
01.14.05 ātmasambhāvitaḥ, mānakāmaḥ, śatrupūjā'marṣitaḥ, nīcairupahitaḥ, tīkṣṇaḥ, sāhasikaḥ, bhogenāsantuṣṭaḥ - iti mānivargaḥ
01.14.06 teṣāṃ muṇḍajaṭilavyañjanairyo yadbhaktiḥ kṛtyapakṣīyaḥ taṃ tena upajāpayet
01.14.07 yathā madāndho hastī mattenādhiṣṭhito yad yad āsādayati tat sarvaṃ pramṛdnāti, evaṃ ayaṃ aśāstracakṣurandho rājā paurajānapadavadhāyābhyutthitaḥ, śakyaṃ asya pratihastiprotsāhanenāpakartuṃ, amarṣaḥ kriyatām iti kruddhavargaṃ upajāpayet
01.14.08 yathā līnaḥ sarpo yasmād bhayaṃ paśyati tatra viṣaṃ utsṛjati, evaṃ ayaṃ rājā jātadoṣāśaṅkaḥ tvayi purā krodhaviṣaṃ utsṛjati, anyatra gamyatām iti bhītavargaṃ।upajāpayet
01.14.09 yathā śvagaṇināṃ dhenuḥ śvabhyo duhyate na brāhmaṇebhyaḥ, evaṃ ayaṃ rājā sattvaprajñāvākyaśaktihīnebhyo duhyate nātmaguṇasampannebhyaḥ, asau rājā puruṣaviśeṣajñaḥ, tatra gamyatām iti lubdhavargaṃ।upajāpayet
01.14.10 yathā caṇḍāla udapānaścaṇḍālānāṃ eva upabhogyo nānyeṣāṃ, evaṃ ayaṃ rājā nīco nīcānāṃ eva upabhogyo na tvadvidhānāṃ āryāṇāṃ, asau rājā puruṣaviśeṣajñaḥ, tatra gamyatām iti mānivargaṃ upajāpayet
01.14.11ab tathā iti pratipannāṃḥ tān saṃhitān paṇakarmaṇā ।
01.14.11chd yojayeta yathāśakti sa-apasarpān svakarmasu

   Chapt .   The topic of counsel
01.15.01 kṛtasvapakṣaparapakṣa upagrahaḥ kāryārambhāṃścintayet
01.15.02 mantrapūrvāḥ sarvārambhāḥ
01.15.03 tad।uddeśaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ kathānāṃ anihśrāvī pakṣibhirapyanālokyaḥ syāt ।
01.15.04 śrūyate hi śukasārikābhirmantro bhinnaḥ, śvabhirapyanyaiśca tiryagyonibhiriti
01.15.05 tasmān mantra uddeśaṃ anāyukto na upagacchet
01.15.06 ucchidyeta mantrabhedī
01.15.07 mantrabhedo hi dūtāmātyasvāmināṃ iṅgitākārābhyām
01.15.08 iṅgitaṃ anyathāvṛttiḥ
01.15.09 ākṛtigrahaṇaṃ ākāraḥ

01.15.16 sā eṣā mantriparamparā mantraṃ bhinatti

01.15.19 pratyakṣaparokṣānumeyā hi rājavṛttiḥ
01.15.20 anupalabdhasya jñānaṃ upalabdhasya niścitabalādhānaṃ arthadvaidhasya saṃśayacchedanaṃ ekadeśadṛṣṭasya śeṣa upalabdhiriti mantrisādhyaṃ etat
01.15.21 tasmād buddhivṛddhaiḥ sārdhaṃ adhyāsīta mantram
01.15.22ab na kañcid avamanyeta sarvasya śṛṇuyān matam ।
01.15.22chd bālasyāpyarthavadvākyaṃ upayuñjīta paṇḍitaḥ ।
01.15.23 etan mantrajñānaṃ, na etan mantrarakṣaṇam iti pārāśarāḥ
01.15.24 yad asya kāryaṃ abhipretaṃ tatpratirūpakaṃ mantriṇaḥ pṛcchet - kāryaṃ idaṃ evaṃ āsīt, evaṃ vā yadi bhavet, tat kathaṃ kartavyam iti
01.15.25 te yathā brūyuḥ tat kuryāt
01.15.26 evaṃ mantra upalabdhiḥ saṃvṛtiśca bhavati iti
01.15.27 na iti piśunaḥ
01.15.28 mantriṇo hi vyavahitaṃ arthaṃ vṛttaṃ avṛttaṃ vā pṛṣṭā anādareṇa bruvanti prakāśayanti vā
01.15.29 sa doṣaḥ

01.15.32 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
01.15.33 anavasthā hyeṣā

01.15.36 ekaśca mantrī yathā iṣṭaṃ anavagrahaścarati

01.15.39 mahādoṣaṃ upapannaṃ tu bhavati
01.15.40 tataḥ pareṣu kṛcchreṇārthaniścayo gamyate, mantro vā rakṣyate
01.15.41 deśakālakāryavaśena tvekena saha dvābhyāṃ eko vā yathāsāmarthyaṃ mantrayeta alterNative views approved
01.15.42 karmaṇāṃ ārambha upāyaḥ puruṣadravyasampad deśakālavibhāgo vinipātapratīkāraḥ kāryasiddhiriti pañcāṅgo mantraḥ
01.15.43 tān ekaikaśaḥ pṛcchet samastāṃśca
01.15.44 hetubhiśca eṣāṃ matipravivekān vidyāt
01.15.45 avāptārthaḥ kālaṃ nātikrāmayet
01.15.46 na dīrghakālaṃ mantrayeta, na teṣāṃ pakṣīyairyeṣāṃ apakuryāt

01.15.48 ṣoḍaśa iti bārhaspatyāḥ

01.16.06 śāsanaṃ evaṃ vācyaḥ paraḥ, sa vakṣyatyevaṃ, tasya idaṃ prativākyaṃ, evaṃ atisandhātavyaṃ, ityadhīyāno gacchet

01.16.12 parasya vāci vaktre dṛṣṭyāṃ ca prasādaṃ vākyapūjanaṃ iṣṭaparipraśnaṃ guṇakathāsaṅgaṃ āsannaṃ āsanaṃ satkāraṃ iṣṭeṣu smaraṇaṃ viśvāsagamanaṃ ca lakṣayet tuṣṭasya, viparītaṃ atuṣṭasya
01.16.13 taṃ brūyāt - dūtamukhā hi rājānaḥ, tvaṃ cānye ca

01.16.17 eṣa dūtadharmaḥ iti
01.16.18 vased avisṛṣṭaḥ pūjayā na utsiktaḥ
01.16.19 pareṣu balitvaṃ na manyeta
01.16.20 vākyaṃ aniṣṭaṃ saheta
01.16.21 striyaḥ pānaṃ ca varjayet
01.16.22 ekaḥ śayīta
01.16.23 suptamattayorhi bhāvajñānaṃ dṛṣṭam
01.16.24 kṛtyapakṣa upajāpaṃ akṛtyapakṣe gūḍhapraṇidhānaṃ rāgāparāgau bhartari randhraṃ ca prakṛtīnāṃ tāpasavaidehakavyañjanābhyāṃ upalabheta, tayorantevāsibhiścikitsakapāṣaṇḍavyañjana ubhayavetanairvā
01.16.25 teṣāṃ asambhāṣāyāṃ yācakamatta unmattasuptapralāpaiḥ puṇyasthānadevagṛhacitralekhyasaṃjñābhirvā cāraṃ upalabheta
01.16.26 upalabdhasya upajāpaṃ upeyāt
01.16.27 pareṇa ca uktaḥ svāsāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ pramāṇaṃ nācakṣīta
01.16.28 sarvaṃ veda bhavān iti brūyāt, kāryasiddhikaraṃ vā
01.16.29 kāryasyāsiddhāvuparudhyamānaḥ tarkayet - kiṃ bharturme vyasanaṃ āsannaṃ paśyan, svaṃ vā vyasanaṃ pratikartukāmaḥ, pārṣṇigrāhaṃ āsāraṃ antaḥkopaṃ āṭavikaṃ vā samutthāpayitukāmaḥ, mitraṃ ākrandaṃ vā vyāghātayitukāmaḥ, svaṃ vā parato vigrahaṃ antaḥkopaṃ āṭavikaṃ vā pratikartukāmaḥ, saṃsiddhaṃ vā me bharturyātrākālaṃ abhihantukāmaḥ, sasyapaṇyakupyasaṅgrahaṃ durgakarma balasamuddānaṃ vā kartukāmaḥ, svasainyānāṃ vā vyāyāmasya deśakālāvākāṅkṣamāṇaḥ, paribhavapramādābhyāṃ vā, saṃsargānubandhārthī vā, māṃ uparuṇaddhi iti
01.16.30 jñātvā vased apasared vā
01.16.31 prayojanaṃ iṣṭaṃ avekṣeta vā
01.16.32 śāsanaṃ aniṣṭaṃ uktvā bandhavadhabhayād avisṛṣṭo'pyapagacchet, anyathā niyamyeta

01.16.33chd upajāpaḥ suhṛdbhedo gūḍhadaṇḍātisāraṇam

01.17.29 taṃ anyaḥ sattrī pratiṣedhayet ityāmbhīyāḥ

01.18.12 kāruśilpikuśīlavacikitsakavāgjīvanapāṣaṇḍacchadmabhir
vā naṣṭarūpaḥ tadvyañjanasakhaśchidreṣu praviśya rājñaḥ śastrarasābhyāṃ
prahṛtya brūyāt - ahaṃ asau kumāraḥ, sahabhogyaṃ idaṃ rājyaṃ, eko
nārhati bhoktuṃ, ye kāmayante māṃ bhartuṃ tān ahaṃ dviguṇena
bhaktavetanena upasthāsyāmi iti  ityaparuddhavṛttam ।

01.19.01 rājānaṃ utthitaṃ anūttiṣṭhante bhṛtyāḥ
01.19.02 pramādyantaṃ anupramādyanti

01.19.07 tripauruṣī pauruṣī catur'ṅgulā naṣṭacchāyo madhyāhna iti catvāraḥ pūrve divasasyāṣṭabhāgāḥ

02.3.01 caturdiśaṃ janapadānte sāmparāyikaṃ daivakṛtaṃ durgaṃ kārayet, antardvīpaṃ sthalaṃ vā nimnāvaruddhaṃ audakaṃ, prāstaraṃ guhāṃ vā pārvataṃ, nirudakastambaṃ iriṇaṃ vā dhānvanaṃ, khañjana udakaṃ stambagahanaṃ vā vanadurgam
02.3.02 teṣāṃ nadīparvatadurgaṃ janapadārakṣasthānaṃ, dhānvanavanadurgaṃ aṭavīsthānaṃ āpadyapasāro vā
02.3.03 janapadamadhye samudayasthānaṃ sthānīyaṃ niveśayet, vāstukapraśaste deśe nadīsaṅgame hradasyāviśoṣasyāṅke sarasaḥ taṭākasya vā, vṛttaṃ dīrghaṃ catur'śraṃ vā vāstuvaśena vā pradakṣiṇa udakaṃ paṇyapuṭabhedanaṃ aṃsapathavāripathābhyāṃ upetam
02.3.04 tasya parikhāḥ tisro daṇḍāntarāḥ kārayet caturdaśa dvādaśa daśa iti daṇḍān vistīrṇāḥ, vistārād avagāḍhāḥ pāda ūnaṃ ardhaṃ vā, tribhāgamūlāḥ, mūlacatur'śrā vā, pāṣāṇa upahitāḥ pāṣāṇa iṣṭakābaddhapārśvā vā, toyāntikīrāgantutoyapūrṇā vā saparivāhāḥ padmagrāhavatīśca
02.3.05 caturdaṇḍāpakṛṣṭaṃ parikhāyāḥ ṣaḍdaṇḍa ucchritaṃ avaruddhaṃ taddviguṇaviṣkambhaṃ khātād vapraṃ kārayed ūrdhvacayaṃ mañcapṛṣṭhaṃ kumbhakukṣikaṃ vā hastibhirgobhiśca kṣuṇṇaṃ kaṇṭakigulmaviṣavallīpratānavantam
02.3.06 pāṃsuśeṣeṇa vāstucchidraṃ rājabhavanaṃ vā pūrayet
02.3.07a vaprasya upari prākāraṃ viṣkambhadviguṇa utsedhaṃ aiṣṭakaṃ dvādaśahastād ūrdhvaṃ ojaṃ yugmaṃ vā ā caturviṃśatihastād iti kārayet
02.3.07b rathacaryāsañcāraṃ tālamūlaṃ murajakaiḥ kapiśīrṣakaiścācitāgram
02.3.08 pṛthuśilāsaṃhataṃ vā śailaṃ kārayet, na tveva kāṣṭamayam
02.3.09 agniravahito hi tasmin vasati
02.3.10 viṣkambhacatur'śraṃ aṭṭālakaṃ utsedhasamāvakṣepasopānaṃ kārayet triṃśaddaṇḍāntaraṃ ca
02.3.11 dvayoraṭṭālakayormadhye saharmyadvitalāṃ adhyardhāyāyāmāṃ pratolīṃ kārayet
02.3.12 aṭṭālakapratolīmadhye tridhānuṣkādhiṣṭhānaṃ sa-apidhānacchidraphalakasaṃhataṃ indrakośaṃ kārayet
02.3.13 antareṣu dvihastaviṣkambhaṃ pārśve caturguṇāyāmaṃ devapathaṃ kārayet
02.3.14 daṇḍāntarā dvidaṇḍāntarā vā caryāḥ kārayet, agrāhye deśe pradhāvanikāṃ niṣkiradvāraṃ ca
02.3.15 bahirjānubhañjanīśūlaprakarakūpakūṭāvapātakaṇṭakapratisarāhipṛṣṭhatālapattraśṛṅgāṭakaśvadaṃṣṭrārgala upaskandanapādukāmbarīṣa udapānakaiḥ praticchannaṃ channapathaṃ kārayet
02.3.16 prākāraṃ ubhayato meṇḍhakaṃ adhyardhadaṇḍaṃ kṛtvā pratolīṣaṭtulā'ntaraṃ dvāraṃ niveśayet pañcadaṇḍād eka uttaraṃ ā'ṣṭadaṇḍād iti catur'śraṃ ṣaḍbhāgaṃ āyāmād'dhikaṃ aṣṭabhāgaṃ vā
02.3.17 pañcadaśahastād eka uttaraṃ ā'ṣṭādaśahastād iti tala utsedhaḥ
02.3.18 stambhasya parikṣepaḥ ṣaḍ।āyāmo, dviguṇo nikhātaḥ, cūlikāyāścaturbhāgaḥ
02.3.19 āditalasya pañcabhāgāḥ śālā vāpī sīmāgṛhaṃ ca
02.3.20 daśabhāgikau dvau pratimañcau, antaraṃ āṇīharmyaṃ ca
02.3.21 samucchrayād ardhatale sthūṇābandhaśca
02.3.22 ardhavāstukaṃ uttamāgāraṃ, tribhāgāntaraṃ vā, iṣṭakā'vabaddhapārśvaṃ, vāmataḥ pradakṣiṇasopānaṃ gūḍhabhittisopānaṃ itarataḥ
02.3.23 dvihastaṃ toraṇaśiraḥ
02.3.24 tripañcabhāgikau dvau kapāṭayogau
02.3.25 dvau parighau
02.3.26 aratnirindrakīlaḥ
02.3.27 pañcahastaṃ āṇidvāram
02.3.28 catvāro hastiparighāḥ
02.3.29 niveśārdhaṃ hastinakham
02.3.30 mukhasamaḥ saṅkramaḥ saṃhāryo bhūmimayo vā nirudake
02.3.31 prākārasamaṃ mukhaṃ avasthāpya tribhāgagodhāmukhaṃ gopuraṃ kārayet
02.3.32 prākāramadhye vāpīṃ kṛtvā puṣkariṇīdvāraṃ, catuḥśālaṃ adhyardhāntaraṃ sāṇikaṃ kumārīpuraṃ, muṇḍaharmyadvitalaṃ muṇḍakadvāraṃ, bhūmidravyavaśena vā niveśayet
02.3.33 tribhāgādhikāyāmā bhāṇḍavāhinīḥ kulyāḥ kārayet
02.3.34ab tāsu pāṣāṇakuddālāḥ kuṭhārīkāṇḍakalpanāḥ ।
02.3.34chd muṣuṇḍhīmudgarā daṇḍāścakrayantraśataghnayaḥ
02.3.35ab kāryāḥ kārmārikāḥ śūlā vedhanāgrāśca veṇavaḥ ।
02.3.35chd uṣṭragrīvyo'gnisamyogāḥ kupyakalpe ca yo vidhiḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Lay-out of the fortified city
02.4.01 trayaḥ prācīnā rājamārgāḥ traya udīcīnā iti vāstuvibhāgaḥ
02.4.02 sa dvādaśadvāro yukta udakabhramacchannapathaḥ
02.4.03 caturdaṇḍāntarā rathyāḥ
02.4.04 rājamārgadroṇamukhasthānīyarāṣṭravivītapathāḥ samyānīyavyūhaśmaśānagrāmapathāścāṣṭadaṇḍāḥ
02.4.05 caturdaṇḍaḥ setuvanapathaḥ, dvidaṇḍo hastikṣetrapathaḥ, pañcāratnayo rathapathaḥ, catvāraḥ paśupathaḥ, dvau kṣudrapaśumanuṣyapathaḥ
02.4.06 pravīre vāstuni rājaniveśaścāturvarṇyasamājīve
02.4.07 vāstuhṛdayād uttare navabhāge yathā uktavidhānaṃ antaḥpuraṃ prānmukhaṃ udanmukhaṃ vā kārayet
02.4.08 tasya pūrva uttaraṃ bhāgaṃ ācāryapurohita ijyātoyasthānaṃ mantriṇaścāvaseyuḥ, pūrvadakṣiṇaṃ bhāgṃ mahānasaṃ hastiśālā koṣṭhāgāraṃ ca
02.4.09 tataḥ paraṃ gandhamālyarasapaṇyāḥ prasādhanakāravaḥ kṣatriyāśca pūrvāṃ diśaṃ adhivaseyuḥ
02.4.10 dakṣiṇapūrvaṃ bhāgaṃ bhāṇḍāgāraṃ akṣapaṭalaṃ karmaniṣadyāśca, dakṣiṇapaścimaṃ bhāgaṃ kupyagṛhaṃ āyudhāgāraṃ ca
02.4.11 tataḥ paraṃ nagaradhānyavyāvahārikakārmāntikabalādhyakṣāḥ pakvānnasurāmāṃsapaṇyā rūpājīvāḥ tālāvacarā vaiśyāśca dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ adhivaseyuḥ
02.4.12 paścimadakṣiṇaṃ bhāgaṃ khara uṣṭraguptisthānaṃ karmagṛhaṃ ca, paścima uttaraṃ bhāgaṃ yānarathaśālāḥ
02.4.13 tataḥ paraṃ ūrṇāsūtraveṇucarmavarmaśastrāvaraṇakāravaḥ śūdrāśca paścimāṃ diśaṃ adhivaseyuḥ
02.4.14 uttarapaścimaṃ bhāgaṃ paṇyabhaiṣajyagṛhaṃ, uttarapūrvaṃ bhāgaṃ kośo gavāśvaṃ ca
02.4.15 tataḥ paraṃ nagararājadevatālohamaṇikāravo brāhmaṇāśca uttarāṃ diśaṃ adhivaseyuḥ
02.4.16 vāstucchidrānuśāleṣu śreṇīprapaṇinikāyā āvaseyuḥ
02.4.17 aparājitāpratihatajayantavaijayantakoṣṭhān śivavaiśravaṇāśviśrīmadirāgṛhāṇi ca puramadhye kārayet
02.4.18 yathā uddeśaṃ vāstudevatāḥ sthāpayet
02.4.19 brāhmāindrayāmyasaināpatyāni dvārāṇi
02.4.20 bahiḥ parikhāyā dhanuḥśatāpakṛṣṭāścaityapuṇyasthānavanasetubandhāḥ kāryāḥ, yathādiśaṃ ca digdevatāḥ
02.4.21 uttaraḥ pūrvo vā śmaśānabhāgo varṇa uttamānāṃ, dakṣiṇena śmaśānaṃ varṇāvarāṇām
02.4.22 tasyātikrame pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
02.4.23 pāṣaṇḍacaṇḍālānāṃ śmaśānānte vāsaḥ
02.4.24 karmāntakṣetravaśena kuṭumbināṃ sīmānaṃ sthāpayet
02.4.25 teṣu puṣpaphalavāṭān dhānyapaṇyanicayāṃścānujñātāḥ kuryuḥ
02.4.26 daśakulīvāṭaṃ kūpasthānam
02.4.27 sarvasnehadhānyakṣāralavaṇagandhabhaiṣajyaśuṣkaśākayavasavallūratṛṇakāṣṭhalohacarmāṅgārasnāyuviṣaviṣāṇaveṇuvalkalasāradārupraharaṇāvaraṇāśmanicayān anekavarṣa upabhogasahān kārayet
02.4.28 navenānavaṃ śodhayet
02.4.29 hasti'śvarathapādātaṃ anekamukhyaṃ avasthāpayet
02.4.30 anekamukhyaṃ hi parasparabhayāt para upajāpaṃ na upaiti
02.4.31 etenāntapāladurgasaṃskārā vyākhyātāḥ
02.4.32ab na ca bāhirikān kuryāt pure rāṣṭra upaghātakān ।
02.4.32chd kṣipej janapade ca etān sarvān vā dāpayet karān  (iti)

02.5.01 samnidhātā kośagṛhaṃ paṇyagṛhaṃ koṣṭhāgāraṃ kupyagṛhaṃ āyudhāgāraṃ bandhanāgāraṃ ca kārayet
02.5.02 catur'śrāṃ vāpīṃ an-udaka upasnehāṃ khānayitvā pṛthuśilābhirubhayataḥ pārśvaṃ mūlaṃ ca pracitya sāradārupañjaraṃ bhūmisamaṃ tritalaṃ anekavidhānaṃ kuṭṭimadeśasthānatalaṃ ekadvāraṃ yantrayuktasopānaṃ bhūmigṛhaṃ kārayet
02.5.03 tasya upari ubhayatoniṣedhaṃ sa-pragrīvaṃ aiṣṭakaṃ bhāṇḍavāhinīparikṣiptaṃ kośagṛhaṃ kārayet, prāsādaṃ vā
02.5.04 janapadānte dhruvanidhiṃ āpad'rthaṃ abhityaktaiḥ kārayet
02.5.05a pakva iṣṭakāstambhaṃ catuḥśālaṃ ekadvāraṃ anekasthānatalaṃ vivṛtastambhāpasāraṃ ubhayataḥ paṇyagṛhaṃ koṣṭhāgāraṃ ca
02.5.05b dīrghabahuśālaṃ kakṣyāvṛtakuḍyaṃ antaḥ kupyagṛhaṃ, tad eva bhūmigṛhayuktaṃ āyudhāgāraṃ
02.5.05ch pṛthagdharmasthīyaṃ mahāmātrīyaṃ vibhaktastrīpuruṣasthānaṃ apasārataḥ suguptakakṣyaṃ bandhanāgāraṃ kārayet
02.5.06 sarveṣāṃ śālāḥ khāta udapānavarcasnānagṛhāgniviṣatrāṇamārjāranakulārakṣāsvadaivatapūjanayuktāḥ kārayet
02.5.07 koṣṭhāgāre varṣamānaṃ aratnimukhaṃ kuṇḍaṃ sthāpayet
02.5.08 tatjātakaraṇādhiṣṭhitaḥ purāṇaṃ navaṃ ca ratnaṃ sāraṃ phalgu kupyaṃ vā pratigṛhṇīyāt
02.5.09 tatra ratna upadhāvuttamo daṇḍaḥ kartuḥ kārayituśca sāra upadhau madhyamaḥ, phalgukupya upadhau tat ca tāvat ca daṇḍaḥ
02.5.10 rūpadarśakaviśuddhaṃ hiraṇyaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt
02.5.11 aśuddhaṃ chedayet
02.5.12 āhartuḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
02.5.13 śuddhaṃ pūrṇaṃ abhinavaṃ ca dhānyaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt
02.5.14 viparyaye mūlyadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.5.15 tena paṇyaṃ kupyaṃ āyudhaṃ ca vyākhyātam
02.5.16 sarvādhikaraṇeṣu yukta upayuktatatpuruṣāṇāṃ paṇādicatuṣpaṇaparamāpahāreṣu pūrvamadhyama uttamavadhā daṇḍāḥ
02.5.17 kośādhiṣṭhitasya kośāvacchede ghātaḥ
02.5.18 tadvaiyāvṛtyakarāṇāṃ ardhadaṇḍāḥ
02.5.19 paribhāṣaṇaṃ avijñāte
02.5.20 corāṇāṃ abhipradharṣaṇe citro ghātaḥ

02.5.22a bāhyaṃ abhyantaraṃ cāyaṃ vidyād varṣaśatād api ।
02.5.22b yathā pṛṣṭo na sajjeta vyaye śeṣe ca sañcaye  (iti)

02.6.01 samāhartā durgaṃ rāṣṭraṃ khaniṃ setuṃ vanaṃ vrajaṃ vaṇikpathaṃ cāvekṣeta
02.6.02 śulkaṃ daṇḍaḥ pautavaṃ nāgariko lakṣaṇādhyakṣo mudrā'dhyakṣaḥ surā sūnā sūtraṃ tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣāraḥ sauvarṇikaḥ paṇyasaṃsthā veśyā dyūtaṃ vāstukaṃ kāruśilpigaṇo devatā'dhyakṣo dvārabahirikā''deyaṃ ca durgam
02.6.03 sītā bhāgo baliḥ karo vaṇik nadīpālaḥ taro nāvaḥ pattanaṃ vivicitaṃ vartanī rajjuścorarajjuśca rāṣṭram
02.6.04 suvarṇarajatavajramaṇimuktāpravālaśaṅkhalohalavaṇabhūmiprastararasadhātavaḥ khaniḥ
02.6.05 puṣpaphalavāṭaṣaṇḍakedāramūlavāpāḥ setuḥ
02.6.06 paśumṛgadravyahastivanaparigraho vanam
02.6.07 gomahiṣaṃ ajāvikaṃ khara uṣtraṃ aśvāśvataraṃ ca vrajaḥ
02.6.08 sthalapatho vāripathaśca vaṇikpathaḥ
02.6.09 ityāyaśarīram
02.6.10 mūlyaṃ bhāgo vyājī parighaḥ klptam(klṛptam) rūpikaṃ atyayaścāyamukham
02.6.11 devapitṛpūjādānārthaṃ, svastivācanaṃ, antaḥpuraṃ, mahānasaṃ, dūtaprāvartimaṃ, koṣṭhāgāraṃ, āyudhāgāraṃ, paṇyagṛhaṃ, kupyagṛhaṃ, karmānto, viṣṭiḥ, patti'śvarathadvipaparigraho, gomaṇḍalaṃ, paśumṛgapakṣivyālavāṭāḥ, kāṣṭhatṛṇavāṭāśca iti vyayaśarīram
02.6.12 rājavarṣaṃ māsaḥ pakṣo divasaśca vyuṣṭaṃ, varṣāhemantagrīṣmāṇāṃ tṛtīyasaptamā divasa ūnāḥ pakṣāḥ śeṣāḥ pūrṇāḥ, pṛthag'dhimāsakaḥ, iti kālaḥ
02.6.13 karaṇīyaṃ siddhaṃ śeṣaṃ āyavyayau nīvī ca
02.6.14 saṃsthānaṃ pracāraḥ śarīrāvasthāpanaṃ ādānaṃ sarvasamudayapiṇḍaḥ sañjātaṃ - etat karaṇīyam
02.6.15 kośārpitaṃ rājahāraḥ puravyayaśca praviṣṭaṃ paramasaṃvatsarānuvṛttaṃ śāsanamuktaṃ mukhājñaptaṃ cāpātanīyaṃ - etat siddham
02.6.16 siddhikarmayogaḥ daṇḍaśeṣaṃ āharaṇīyaṃ balātkṛtapratiṣṭabdhaṃ avamṛṣṭaṃ ca praśodhyaṃ - etatśeṣaṃ, asāraṃ alpasāraṃ ca
02.6.17 vartamānaḥ paryuṣito'nyajātaścāyaḥ
02.6.18 divasānuvṛtto vartamānaḥ
02.6.19 paramasāṃvatsarikaḥ parapracārasaṅkrānto vā paryuṣitaḥ
02.6.20 naṣṭaprasmṛtaṃ āyuktadaṇḍaḥ pārśvaṃ pārihīṇikaṃ aupāyanikaṃ ḍamaragatakasvaṃ aputrakaṃ nidhiścānyajātaḥ
02.6.21 vikṣepavyādhitāntarārambhaśeṣaṃ ca vyayapratyāyaḥ
02.6.22 vikriye paṇyānāṃ arghavṛddhirupajā, māna unmānaviśeṣo vyājī, krayasaṅgharṣe vārdhavṛddhiḥ - ityāyaḥ
02.6.23 nityo nitya utpādiko lābho lābha utpādika iti vyayaḥ
02.6.24 divasānuvṛtto nityaḥ
02.6.25 pakṣamāsasaṃvatsaralābho lābhaḥ
02.6.26 tayorutpanno nitya utpādiko lābha utpādika iti vyayaḥ
02.6.27 sañjātād āyavyayaviśuddhā nīvī, prāptā cānuvṛttā ca
02.6.28ab evaṃ kuryāt samudayaṃ vṛddhiṃ cāyasya darśayet ।
02.6.28chd hrāsaṃ vyayasya ca prājñaḥ sādhayecca viparyayam  (iti)

02.7.01 akṣapaṭalaṃ adhyakṣaḥ prānmukhaṃ udanmukhaṃ vā vibhakta upasthānaṃ nibandhapustakasthānaṃ kārayet
02.7.02 tatrādhikaraṇānāṃ saṅkhyāpracārasañjātāgraṃ, karmāntānāṃ dravyaprayogavṛddhikṣayavyayaprayāmavyājīyogasthānavetanaviṣṭipramāṇaṃ, ratnasāraphalgukupyānāṃ arghaprativarṇakamānapratimāna unmānāvamānabhāṇḍaṃ, deśagrāmajātikulasaṅghānāṃ dharmavyavahāracaritrasaṃsthānaṃ, rāja upajīvināṃ pragrahapradeśabhogaparihārabhaktavetanalābhaṃ, rājñaśca patnīputrāṇāṃ ratnabhūmilābhaṃ nirdeśa utpātikapratīkāralābhaṃ, mitrāmitrāṇāṃ ca sandhivigrahapradānādānaṃ nibandhapustakasthaṃ kārayet
02.7.03 tataḥ sarvādhikaraṇānāṃ karaṇīyaṃ siddhaṃ śeṣaṃ āyavyayau nīvīṃ upasthānaṃ pracāraṃ caritraṃ saṃsthānaṃ ca nibandhena prayacchet
02.7.04 uttamamadhyamāvareṣu ca karmasu tajjātikaṃ adhyakṣaṃ kuryāt, sāmudayikeṣvavaklṛptikam(avakḷptikam) yaṃ upahatya rājā nānutapyeta
02.7.05 sahagrāhiṇaḥ pratibhuvaḥ karma upajīvinaḥ putrā bhrātaro bhāryā duhitaro bhṛtyāścāsya karmacchedaṃ vaheyuḥ
02.7.06 triśataṃ catuḥpañcāśat cāhorātrāṇāṃ karmasaṃvatsaraḥ
02.7.07 taṃ āṣāḍhīparyavasānaṃ ūnaṃ pūrṇaṃ vā dadyāt
02.7.08 karaṇādhiṣṭhitaṃ adhimāsakaṃ kuryāt
02.7.09 apasarpādhiṣṭhitañca pracāram
02.7.10 pracāracaritrasaṃsthānānyanupalabhamāno hi prakṛtaḥ samudayaṃ ajñānena parihāpayati, utthānakleśāsahatvād ālasyena, śabdādiṣvindriyārtheṣu prasaktaḥ pramādena, saṅkrośādharmānarthabhīrubhāyena, kāryārthiṣvanugrahabuddhiḥ kāmena, hiṃsābuddhiḥ kopena, vidyādravyavallabhāpāśrayād darpeṇa, tulāmānatarkagaṇitāntara upadhānāt lobhena
02.7.11 teṣāṃ ānupūrvyā yāvān artha upaghātaḥ tāvān eka uttaro daṇḍaḥ iti mānavāḥ
02.7.12 sarvatrāṣṭaguṇaḥ iti pārāśarāḥ
02.7.13 daśaguṇaḥ iti bārhaspatyāḥ
02.7.14 viṃśatiguṇaḥ ityauśanasāḥ
02.7.15 yathā'parādhaṃ iti kauṭilyaḥ
02.7.16 gāṇanikyāni āṣāḍhīṃ āgaccheyuḥ
02.7.17 āgatānāṃ samudrapustakabhāṇḍanīvīkānāṃ ekatrāsambhāṣā'varodhaṃ kārayet
02.7.18 āyavyayanīvīnāṃ agrāṇi śrutvā nīvīṃ avahārayet
02.7.19 yaccāgrād āyasyāntaraparṇe nīvyāṃ vardheta vyayasya vā yat parihāpayet, tad aṣṭaguṇaṃ adhyakṣaṃ dāpayet
02.7.20 viparyaye taṃ eva prati syāt
02.7.21 yathākālaṃ anāgatānāṃ apustakabhāṇḍanīvīkānāṃ vā deyadaśabandho daṇḍaḥ
02.7.22 kārmike ca upasthite kāraṇikasyāpratibadhnataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
02.7.23 viparyaye kārmikasya dviguṇaḥ
02.7.24 pracārasamaṃ mahāmātrāḥ samagrāḥ śrāvayeyuraviṣamamantrāḥ
02.7.25 pṛthagbhūto mithyāvādī ca eṣāṃ uttamaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt
02.7.26 akṛtāhorūpaharaṃ māsaṃ ākāṅkṣeta
02.7.27 māsād ūrdhvaṃ māsadviśata uttaraṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt
02.7.28 alpaśesalekhyanīvīkaṃ pañcarātraṃ ākāṅkṣeta
02.7.29 tataḥ paraṃ kośapūrvaṃ ahorūpaharaṃ dharmavyavahāracaritrasaṃsthānasaṅkalananirvartanānumānacāraprayogairavekṣeta
02.7.30 divasapañcarātrapakṣamāsacāturmāsyasaṃvatsaraiśca pratisamānayet
02.7.31 vyuṣṭadeśakālamukha utpatti'nuvṛttipramāṇadāyakadāpakanibandhakapratigrāhakaiścāyaṃ samānayet
02.7.32 vyuṣṭadeśakālamukhalābhakāraṇadeyayogapramāṇājñāpaka uddhārakavidhātṛkapratigrāhakaiśca vyayaṃ samānayet
02.7.33 vyuṣṭadeśakālamukhānuvartanarūpalakṣaṇapramāṇanikṣepabhājanagopāyakaiśca nīvīṃ samānayet
02.7.34 rājārthe kāraṇikasyāpratibadhnataḥ pratiṣedhayato vā''jñāṃ nibandhād āyavyayaṃ anyathā nīvīṃ avalikhato dviguṇaḥ
02.7.35 kramāvahīnaṃ utkramaṃ avijñātaṃ punar।uktaṃ vā vastukaṃ avalikhato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.7.36 nīvīṃ avalikhato dviguṇaḥ
02.7.37 bhakṣayato'ṣṭaguṇaḥ
02.7.38 nāśayataḥ pañcabandhaḥ pratidānaṃ ca
02.7.39 mithyāvāde steyadaṇḍaḥ

02.8.01 kośapūrvāḥ sarvārambhāḥ
02.8.02 tasmāt pūrvaṃ kośaṃ avekṣeta
02.8.03 pracārasamṛddhiścaritrānugrahaścoranigraho yuktapratiṣedhaḥ sasyasampat paṇyabāhulyaṃ upasargapramokṣaḥ parihārakṣayo hiraṇya upāyanaṃ iti kośavṛddhiḥ
02.8.04 pratibandhaḥ prayogo vyavahāro'vastāraḥ parihāpaṇaṃ upabhogaḥ parivartanaṃ apahāraśca iti kośakṣayaḥ
02.8.05 siddhīnāṃ asādhanaṃ anavatāraṇaṃ apraveśanaṃ vā pratibandhaḥ

02.8.07 kośadravyāṇāṃ vṛddhiprayogāḥ prayogaḥ
02.8.08 paṇyavyavahāro vyavahāraḥ
02.8.09 tatra phaladviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.8.10 siddhaṃ kālaṃ aprāptaṃ karoti aprāptaṃ prāptaṃ vā ityavastāraḥ
02.8.11 tatra pañcabandho daṇḍaḥ
02.8.12 klṛptam(kḷptam) āyaṃ parihāpayati vyayaṃ vā vivardhayati iti parihāpaṇam
02.8.13 tatra hīnacaturguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.8.14 svayaṃ anyairvā rājadravyāṇāṃ upabhojanaṃ upabhogaḥ
02.8.15 tatra ratna upabhoge ghātaḥ, sāra upabhoge madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, phalgukupya upabhoge tacca tāvat ca daṇḍaḥ
02.8.16 rājadravyāṇāṃ anyadravyenādānaṃ parivartanam
02.8.17 tad upabhogena vyākhyātam
02.8.18 siddhaṃ āyaṃ na praveśayati, nibaddhaṃ vyayaṃ na prayacchati, prāptāṃ nīvīṃ vipratijānīta ityapahāraḥ
02.8.19 tatra dvādaśaguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.8.20 teṣāṃ haraṇa upāyāścatvāriṃśat
02.8.21a pūrvaṃ siddhaṃ paścād avatāritaṃ, paścāt siddhaṃ pūrvaṃ avatāritaṃ, sādhyaṃ na siddhaṃ, asādhyaṃ siddhaṃ, siddhaṃ asiddhaṃ kṛtaṃ, asiddhaṃ siddhaṃ kṛtaṃ, alpasiddhaṃ bahu kṛtaṃ, bahusiddhaṃ alpaṃ kṛtaṃ, anyat siddhaṃ anyat kṛtaṃ, anyataḥ siddhaṃ anyataḥ kṛtaṃ,
02.8.21b deyaṃ na dattaṃ, adeyaṃ dattaṃ, kāle na dattaṃ, akāle dattaṃ, alpaṃ dattaṃ bahu kṛtaṃ, bahu dattaṃ alpaṃ kṛtaṃ, anyad dattaṃ anyat kṛtaṃ, anyato dattaṃ anyataḥ kṛtaṃ,
02.8.21ch praviṣṭaṃ apraviṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ, apraviṣṭaṃ praviṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ, kupyaṃ adattamūlyaṃ praviṣṭaṃ, dattamūlyaṃ na praviṣṭaṃ
02.8.21d saṅkṣepo vikṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ, vikṣepaḥ saṅkṣepo vā, mahā'rghaṃ alpārgheṇa parivartitaṃ, alpārghaṃ mahā'rgheṇa vā
02.8.21e samāropito'rghaḥ, pratyavaropito vā, saṃvatsaro māsaviṣamaḥ kṛtaḥ, māso divasaviṣamo vā, samāgamaviṣamaḥ, mukhaviṣamaḥ, kārmikaviṣamaḥ
02.8.21f nirvartanaviṣamaḥ, piṇḍaviṣamaḥ, varṇaviṣamaḥ, arghaviṣamaḥ, mānaviṣamaḥ, māpanaviṣamaḥ, bhājanaviṣamaḥ - iti haraṇa upāyāḥ
02.8.22 tatra upayuktanidhāyakanibandhakapratigrāhakadāyakadāpakamantrivaiyāvṛtyakarān eka ekaśo'nuyuñjīta
02.8.23 mithyāvāde ca eṣāṃ yuktasamo daṇḍaḥ
02.8.24 pracāre cāvaghoṣayet amunā prakṛtena upahatāḥ prajñāpayantu iti
02.8.25 prajñāpayato yathā upaghātaṃ dāpayet
02.8.26 anekeṣu cābhiyogeṣvapavyayamānaḥ sakṛd eva para uktaḥ sarvaṃ bhajeta
02.8.27 vaiṣamye sarvatrānuyogaṃ dadyāt
02.8.28 mahatyarthāpahāre cālpenāpi siddhaḥ sarvaṃ bhajeta
02.8.29 kṛtapratighātāvasthaḥ sūcako niṣpannārthaḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ aṃśaṃ labheta, dvādaśaṃ aṃśaṃ bhṛtakaḥ
02.8.30 prabhūtābhiyogād alpaniṣpattau niṣpannasyāṃśaṃ labheta
02.8.31 aniṣpanne śārīraṃ hairaṇyaṃ vā daṇḍaṃ labheta, na cānugrāhyaḥ
02.8.32ab niṣpattau nikṣiped vādaṃ ātmānaṃ vā'pavāhayet ।

02.9.01 amātyasampadā upetāḥ sarvādhyakṣāḥ śaktitaḥ karmasu niyojyāḥ
02.9.02 karmasu ca eṣāṃ nityaṃ parīkṣāṃ kārayet, cittānityatvāt manuṣyānām
02.9.03 aśvasadharmāṇo hi manuṣyā niyuktāḥ karmasu vikurvate
02.9.04 tasmāt kartāraṃ karaṇaṃ deśaṃ kālaṃ kāryaṃ prakṣepaṃ udayaṃ ca eṣu vidyāt
02.9.05 te yathāsandeśaṃ asaṃhatā avigṛhītāḥ karmāṇi kuryuḥ
02.9.06 saṃhatā bhakṣayeyuḥ, vigṛhītā vināśayeyuḥ
02.9.07 na cānivedya bhartuḥ kañcid ārambhaṃ kuryuḥ, anyatrāpatpratīkārebhyaḥ
02.9.08 pramādasthāneṣu ca eṣāṃ atyayaṃ sthāpayed divasavetanavyayadviguṇam
02.9.09 yaśca eṣāṃ yathā''diṣṭaṃ arthaṃ saviśeṣaṃ vā karoti sa sthānamānau labheta
02.9.10 alpāyatiścet mahāvyayo bhakṣayati
02.9.11 viparyaye yathā''yativyayaśca na bhakṣayati ityācāryāḥ
02.9.12 apasarpeṇa eva upalabhyeta iti kauṭilyaḥ
02.9.13 yaḥ samudayaṃ parihāpayati sa rājārthaṃ bhakṣayati
02.9.14 sa ced ajñānādibhiḥ parihāpayati tad enaṃ yathāguṇaṃ dāpayet
02.9.15 yaḥ samudayaṃ dviguṇaṃ udbhāvayati sa janapadaṃ bhakṣayati
02.9.16 sa ced rājārthaṃ upanayatyalpāparādhe vārayitavyaḥ, mahati yathā'parādhaṃ daṇḍayitavyaḥ
02.9.17 yaḥ samudayaṃ vyayaṃ upanayati sa puruṣakarmāṇi bhakṣayati
02.9.18 sa karmadivasadravyamūlyapuruṣavetanāpahāreṣu yathā'parādhaṃ daṇḍayitavyaḥ
02.9.19 tasmād asya yo yasminn adhikaraṇe śāsanasthaḥ sa tasya karmaṇo yāthātathyaṃ āyavyayau ca vyāsasamāsābhyāṃ ācakṣīta
02.9.20 mūlaharatādātvikakadaryāṃśca pratiṣedhayet
02.9.21 yaḥ pitṛpaitāmahaṃ arthaṃ anyāyena bhakṣayati sa mūlaharaḥ
02.9.22 yo yad yad utpadyate tat tad bhakṣayati sa tādātvikaḥ
02.9.23 yo bhṛtyātmapīḍābhyāṃ upacinotyarthaṃ sa kadaryaḥ
02.9.24 sa pakṣavāṃśced anādeyaḥ, viparyaye paryādātavyaḥ
02.9.25 yo mahatyarthasamudaye sthitaḥ kadaryaḥ samnidhatte'vanidhatte'vasrāvayati vā - samnidhatte svaveśmani, avanidhatte paurajānapadeṣu, avasrāvayati paraviṣaye - tasya sattrī mantrimitrabhṛtyabandhupakṣaṃ āgatiṃ gatiṃ ca dravyāṇāṃ upalabheta
02.9.26 yaścāsya paraviṣaye sañcāraṃ kuryāt taṃ anupraviśya mantraṃ vidyāt
02.9.27 suvidite śatruśāsanāpadeśena enaṃ ghātayet
02.9.28 tasmād asyādhyakṣāḥ saṅkhyāyakalekhakarūpadarśakanīvīgrāhaka uttarādhyakṣasakhāḥ karmaṇi kuryuḥ
02.9.29 uttarādhyakṣā hasti'śvarathārohāḥ
02.9.30 teṣāṃ antevāsinaḥ śilpaśaucayuktāḥ saṅkhyāyakādīnāṃ apasarpāḥ
02.9.31 bahumukhyaṃ anityaṃ cādhikaraṇaṃ sthāpayet
02.9.32ab yathā hyanāsvādayituṃ na śakyaṃ  jihvātalasthaṃ madhu7 vā viṣaṃ vā ।
02.9.32chd arthaḥ tathā hyarthacareṇa rājñaḥ  svalpo'pyanāsvādayituṃ na śakyaḥ
02.9.33ab matsyā yathā'ntaḥ salile caranto  jñātuṃ na śakyāḥ salilaṃ pibantaḥ ।
02.9.33chd yuktāḥ tathā kāryavidhau niyuktā jñātuṃ na śakyā dhanaṃ ādadānāḥ
02.9.34ab api śakyā gatirjñātuṃ patatāṃ khe patatriṇām ।
02.9.34chd na tu pracchannabhāvānāṃ yuktānāṃ caratāṃ gatiḥ
02.9.35ab āsrāvayecca upacitān viparyasyecca karmasu ।

02.12.01 ākarādhyakṣaḥ śulbadhātuśāstrarasapākamaṇirāgajñaḥ tajjñasakho vā tajjātakarmakara upakaraṇasampannaḥ kiṭṭamūṣāṅgārabhasmaliṅgaṃ vā''karaṃ bhūtapūrvaṃ abhutapūrvaṃ vā bhūmiprastararasadhātuṃ atyarthavarṇagauravaṃ ugragandharasaṃ parīkṣeta
02.12.02 parvatānāṃ abhijñāta uddeśānāṃ bilaguha upatyakālayanagūḍhakhāteṣvantaḥ prasyandino jambūcūtatālaphalapakvaharidrābhedaguḍa(gūḍa?)haritālamanaḥśilākṣaudrahiṅgulukapuṇḍarīkaśukamayūrapattravarṇāḥ savarṇa udakoṣadhiparyantāścikkaṇā viśadā bhārikāśca rasāḥ kāñcanikāḥ

02.12.06 śaṅkhakarpūrasphaṭikanavanītakapotapārāvatavimalakamayūragrīvāvarṇāḥ sasyakagomedakaguḍamatsyaṇḍikāvarṇāḥ kovidārapadmapāṭalīkalāyakṣaumātasīpuṣpavarṇāḥ sa-sīsāḥ sāñjanā visrā bhinnāḥ śvetābhāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ kṛṣṇābhāḥ śvetāḥ sarve vā lekhābinducitrā mṛdavo dhmāyamānā na sphuṭanti bahuphenadhūmāśca rūpyadhātavaḥ

02.13.04 kiñjalkavarṇaṃ mṛdu snigdhaṃ anādi bhrājiṣṇu ca śreṣṭhaṃ, raktapītakaṃ madhyamaṃ, raktaṃ avaram
02.13.05 śreṣṭhānāṃ pāṇḍu śvetaṃ cāprāptakam
02.13.06 tad yenāprāptakaṃ taccaturguṇena sīsena śodhayet
02.13.07 sīsānvayena bhidyamānaṃ śuṣkapaṭalairdhmāpayet
02.13.08 rūkṣatvād bhidyamānaṃ tailagomaye niṣecayet
02.13.09 ākara udgataṃ sīsānvayena bhidyamānaṃ pākapattrāṇi kṛtvā gaṇḍikāsu kuṭṭayet, kadalīvajrakandakalke vā niṣecayet
02.13.10 tuttha udgataṃ gauḍikaṃ kāmbukaṃ cākravālikaṃ ca rūpyam
02.13.11 śvetaṃ snigdhaṃ mṛdu ca śreṣṭham
02.13.12 viparyaye sphoṭanaṃ ca duṣṭam
02.13.13 tatsīsacaturbhāgena śodhayet
02.13.14 udgatacūlikaṃ acchaṃ bhrājiṣṇu dadhivarṇaṃ ca śuddham
02.13.15 śuddhasya eko hāridrasya suvarṇo varṇakaḥ
02.13.16 tataḥ śulbakākaṇy।uttarāpasāritā ācatuḥsīmāntād iti ṣoḍaśa varṇakāḥ
02.13.17 suvarṇaṃ pūrvaṃ nikaṣya paścād varṇikāṃ nikaṣayet
02.13.18 samarāgalekhaṃ animna unnate deśe nikaṣitaṃ, parimṛditaṃ parilīḍhaṃ nakhāntarād vā gairikeṇāvacūrṇitaṃ upadhiṃ vidyāt
02.13.19 jātihiṅgulukena puṣpakāsīsena vā gomūtrabhāvitena digdhenāgrahastena saṃspṛṣṭaṃ suvarṇaṃ śvetībhavati
02.13.20 sa-kesaraḥ snigdho mṛdurbhājiṣṇuśca nikaṣarāgaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ
02.13.21 kāliṅgakaḥ tāpīpāṣāṇo vā mudgavarṇo nikaṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ
02.13.22 samarāgī vikrayakrayahitaḥ
02.13.23 hasticchavikaḥ saharitaḥ pratirāgī vikrayahitaḥ
02.13.24 sthiraḥ paruṣo viṣamavarṇaścāpratirāgī krayahitaḥ
02.13.25 chedaścikkaṇaḥ samavarṇaḥ ślakṣṇo mṛdurbhājiṣṇuśca śreṣṭhaḥ
02.13.26 tāpo bahir'ntaśca samaḥ kiñjalkavarṇaḥ kuraṇḍakapuṣpavarṇo vā śreṣṭhaḥ
02.13.27 śyāvo nīlaścāprāptakaḥ
02.13.28 tulāpratimānaṃ pautavādhyakṣe vakṣyāmaḥ
02.13.29 tena upadeśena rūpyasuvarṇaṃ dadyād ādadīta ca
02.13.30 akṣaśālāṃ anāyukto na upagacchet
02.13.31 abhigacchann ucchedyaḥ
02.13.32 āyukto vā sarūpyasuvarṇaḥ tena eva jīyeta
02.13.33 vicitavastrahastaguhyāḥ kāñcanapṛṣatatvaṣṭṛtapanīyakāravo dhmāyakacarakapāṃsudhāvakāḥ praviśeyurniṣkaseyuśca
02.13.34 sarvaṃ ca eṣāṃ upakaraṇaṃ aniṣṭhitāśca prayogāḥ tatra evāvatiṣṭheran
02.13.35 gṛhītaṃ suvarṇaṃ dhṛtaṃ ca prayogaṃ karaṇamadhye dadyāt
02.13.36 sāyaṃ prātaśca lakṣitaṃ kartṛkārayitṛmudrābhyāṃ nidadhyāt
02.13.37 kṣepaṇo guṇaḥ kṣudrakaṃ iti karmāṇi
02.13.38 kṣepaṇaḥ kācārpaṇādīni
02.13.39 guṇaḥ sūtravānādīni
02.13.40 ghanaṃ suṣiraṃ pṛṣatādiyuktaṃ kṣudrakaṃ iti
02.13.41 arpayet kācakarmaṇaḥ pañcabhāgaṃ kāñcanaṃ daśabhāgaṃ kaṭumānam
02.13.42 tāmrapādayuktaṃ rūpyaṃ rūpyapādayuktaṃ vā suvarṇaṃ saṃskṛtakaṃ, tasmād rakṣet
02.13.43 pṛṣatakācakarmaṇaḥ trayo hi bhāgāḥ paribhāṇḍaṃ dvau vāstukaṃ, catvāro vā vāstukaṃ trayaḥ paribhāṇḍam
02.13.44 tvaṣṭṛkarmaṇaḥ śulbabhāṇḍaṃ samasuvarṇena samyūhayet
02.13.45 rūpyabhāṇḍaṃ ghanaṃ suṣiraṃ vā suvarṇārdhenāvalepayet
02.13.46 caturbhāgasuvarṇaṃ vā vālukāhiṅgulukasya rasena cūrṇena vā vāsayet ।
02.13.47 tapanīyaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ suvarṇaṃ surāgaṃ samasīsātikrāntaṃ pākapattrapakvaṃ saindhavikayā ujjvālitaṃ nīlapītaśvetaharitaśukapattravarṇānāṃ prakṛtirbhavati
02.13.48 tīkṣṇaṃ cāsya mayūragrīvābhaṃ śvetabhaṅgaṃ cimicimāyitaṃ pītacūrṇitaṃ kākaṇikaḥ suvarṇarāgaḥ
02.13.49 tāraṃ upaśuddhaṃ vā - asthitutthe catuḥ samasīse catuḥ śuṣkatutthe catuḥ kapāle trirgomaye dvirevaṃ saptadaśatutthātikrāntaṃ saindhavikayā ujjvālitam
02.13.50 etasmāt kākaṇy।uttaramād vimāṣād iti suvarṇe deyaṃ, paścād rāgayogaḥ, śvetatāraṃ bhavati ।
02.13.51 trayo'ṃśāḥ tapanīyasya dvātriṃśadbhāgaśvetatāraṃ ūrcchitāḥ tat śvetalohitakaṃ bhavati
02.13.52 tāmraṃ pītakaṃ karoti
02.13.53 tapanīyaṃ ujjvālya rāgatribhāgaṃ dadyāt, pītarāgaṃ bhavati
02.13.54 śvetatārabhāgau dvāvekaḥ tapanīyasya mudgavarṇaṃ karoti
02.13.55 kālāyasasyārdhabhāgābhyaktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ bhavati
02.13.56 pratilepinā rasena dviguṇābhyaktaṃ tapanīyaṃ śukapattravarṇaṃ bhavati
02.13.57 tasyārambhe rāgaviśeṣeṣu prativarṇikāṃ gṛhṇīyāt
02.13.58 tīkṣṇatāmrasaṃskāraṃ ca budhyeta
02.13.59 tasmād vajramaṇimuktāpravālarūpāṇāṃ apaneyimānaṃ ca rūpyasuvarṇabhāṇḍabandhapramāṇāni ca
02.13.60ab samarāgaṃ samadvandvaṃ asaktapṛṣataṃ sthiram ।
02.13.60chd supramṛṣṭaṃ asampītaṃ vibhaktaṃ dhāraṇe sukham
02.13.61ab abhinītaṃ prabhāyuktaṃ saṃsthānaṃ adhuraṃ samam ।
02.13.61chd manonetrābhirāmaṃ ca tapanīyaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Activity of the goldsmitH in the market-highRay
02.14.01 sauvarṇikaḥ paurajānapadānāṃ rūpyasuvarṇaṃ āveśanibhiḥ kārayet
02.14.02 nirdiṣṭakālakāryaṃ ca karma kuryuḥ, anirdiṣṭakālaṃ kāryāpadeśam
02.14.03 kāryasyānyathākaraṇe vetananāśaḥ, taddviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ
02.14.04 kālātipātane pādahīnaṃ vetanaṃ taddviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ
02.14.05 yathāvarṇapramāṇaṃ nikṣepaṃ gṛhṇīyuḥ tathāvidhaṃ evārpayeyuḥ
02.14.06 kālāntarād api ca tathāvidhaṃ eva pratigṛhṇīyuḥ, anyatra kṣīṇapariśīrṇābhyām
02.14.07 āveśanibhiḥ suvarṇapudgalalakṣaṇaprayogeṣu tattaj jānīyāt
02.14.08 taptakaladhautakayoḥ kākaṇikaḥ suvarṇe kṣayo deyaḥ
02.14.09 tīkṣṇakākaṇī - rūpyadviguṇaḥ - rāgaprakṣepaḥ, tasya ṣaḍbhāgaḥ kṣayaḥ
02.14.10 varṇahīne māṣāvare pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, pramāṇahīne madhyamaḥ, tulāpratimāna upadhāvuttamaḥ, kṛtabhāṇḍa upadhau ca
02.14.11 sauvarṇikenādṛṣṭaṃ anyatra vā prayogaṃ kārayato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.14.12 karturdviguṇaḥ sa-apasāraścet
02.14.13 anapasāraḥ kaṇṭakaśodhanāya nīyeta
02.14.14 kartuśca dviśato daṇḍaḥ paṇacchedanaṃ vā
02.14.15 tulāpratimānabhāṇḍaṃ pautavahastāt krīṇīyuḥ
02.14.16 anyathā dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.14.17 ghanaṃ suṣiraṃ samyūhyaṃ avalepyaṃ saṅghātyaṃ vāsitakaṃ ca kārukarma
02.14.18 tulāviṣamaṃ apasāraṇaṃ visrāvaṇaṃ peṭakaḥ piṅkaśca iti haraṇa upāyāḥ
02.14.19 samnāminyutkīrṇikā bhinnamastaka upakaṇṭhī kuśikyā sakaṭukakṣyā parivelyā'yaskāntā ca duṣṭatulāḥ
02.14.20 rūpyasya dvau bhāgāvekaḥ śulbasya tripuṭakam
02.14.21 tenākarod gataṃ apasāryate tattripuṭakāpasāritam
02.14.22 śulbena śulbāpasāritaṃ, vellakena vellakāpasāritaṃ, śulbārdhasāreṇa hemnā hemāpasāritam
02.14.23 mūkamūṣā pūtikiṭṭaḥ karaṭukamukhaṃ nālī sandaṃśo joṅganī suvarcikālavaṇaṃ tad eva suvarṇaṃ ityapasāraṇamārgāḥ
02.14.24 pūrvapraṇihitā vā piṇḍavālukā mūṣābhedād agniṣṭhād uddhriyante
02.14.25 paścād bandhane ācitakapattraparīkṣāyāṃ vā rūpyarūpeṇa parivartanaṃ visrāvaṇaṃ, piṇḍavālukānāṃ lohapiṇḍavālukābhirvā
02.14.26 gāḍhaścābhyuddhāryaśca peṭakaḥ samyūhyāvalepyasaṅghātyeṣu kriyate
02.14.27 sīsarūpaṃ suvarṇapattreṇāvaliptaṃ abhyantaraṃ aṣṭakena baddhaṃ gāḍhapeṭakaḥ
02.14.28 sa eva paṭalasampuṭeṣvabhyuddhāryaḥ
02.14.29 pattraṃ āśliṣṭaṃ yamakapattraṃ vā'valepyeṣu kriyate
02.14.30 śulbaṃ tāraṃ vā garbhaḥ pattrāṇāṃ saṅghātyeṣu kriyate
02.14.31 śulbarūpaṃ suvarṇapattrasaṃhataṃ pramṛṣṭaṃ supārśvaṃ, tad eva yamakapattrasaṃhataṃ pramṛṣṭaṃ tāmratārarupaṃ ca uttaravarṇakaḥ
02.14.32 tad ubhayaṃ tāpanikaṣābhyāṃ nihśabda ullekhanābhyāṃ vā vidyāt
02.14.33 abhyuddhāryaṃ badarāmle lavaṇa udake vā sādayanti iti peṭakaḥ
02.14.34 ghane suṣire vā rūpe suvarṇamṛnmālukāhiṅgulukakalpo vā tapto'vatiṣṭhate
02.14.35 dṛḍhavāstuke vā rūpe vālukāmiśraṃ jatu gāndhārapaṅko vā tapto'vatiṣṭhate
02.14.36 tayoḥ tāpanaṃ avadhvaṃsanaṃ vā śuddhiḥ
02.14.37 sa-paribhāṇḍe vā rūpe lavaṇaṃ ulkayā kaṭuśarkarayā taptaṃ avatiṣṭhate
02.14.38 tasya kvāthanaṃ śuddhiḥ
02.14.39 abhrapaṭalaṃ aṣṭakena dviguṇavāstuke vā rūpe badhyate
02.14.40 tasyāpihitakācakasya udake nimajjata ekadeśaḥ sīdati, paṭalāntareṣu vā sūcyā bhidyate
02.14.41 maṇayo rūpyaṃ suvarṇaṃ vā ghanasuṣirāṇāṃ piṅkaḥ
02.14.42 tasya tāpanaṃ avadhvaṃsanaṃ vā śuddhiḥ । iti piṅkaḥ
02.14.43 tasmād vajramaṇimuktāpravālarūpāṇāṃ jātirūpavarṇapramāṇapudgalalakṣaṇānyupalabheta
02.14.44 kṛtabhāṇḍaparīkṣāyāṃ purāṇabhāṇḍapratisaṃskāre vā catvāro haraṇa upāyāḥ - parikuṭṭanaṃ avacchedanaṃ ullekhanaṃ parimardanaṃ vā
02.14.45 peṭakāpadeśena pṛṣataṃ guṇaṃ piṭakāṃ vā yat pariśātayanti tatparikuṭṭanam
02.14.46 yaddviguṇavāstukānāṃ vā rūpe sīsarūpaṃ prakṣipyābhyantaraṃ avacchindanti tad avacchedanam
02.14.47 yad ghanānāṃ tīkṣṇena ullikhanti tad ullekhanam
02.14.48 haritālamanaḥśilāhiṅgulukacūrṇānāṃ anyatamena kuruvindacūrṇena vā vastraṃ samyūhya yat parimṛdnanti tat parimardanam
02.14.49 tena sauvarṇarājatāni bhāṇḍāni kṣīyante, na ca eṣāṃ kiñcid avarugṇaṃ bhavati
02.14.50 bhagnakhaṇḍaghṛṣṭānāṃ samyūhyānāṃ sadṛśenānumānaṃ kuryāt
02.14.51 avalepyānāṃ yāvad utpāṭitaṃ tāvad utpāṭyānumānaṃ kuryāt
02.14.52 virūpāṇāṃ vā tāpanaṃ udakapeṣaṇaṃ ca bahuśaḥ kuryāt
02.14.53 avakṣepaḥ pratimānaṃ agnirgaṇḍikā bhaṇḍikādhikaraṇī piñchaḥ sūtraṃ cellaṃ bollanaṃ śira utsaṅgo makṣikā svakāya īkṣā dṛtirudakaśarāvaṃ agniṣṭhaṃ iti kācaṃ vidyāt
02.14.54 rājatānāṃ visraṃ malagrāhi paruṣaṃ prastīnaṃ vivarṇaṃ vā duṣṭaṃ iti vidyāt
02.14.55ab evaṃ navaṃ ca jīrṇaṃ ca virūpaṃ cāpi bhāṇḍakam ।
02.14.55chd parīkṣetātyayaṃ ca eṣāṃ yathā uddiṣṭaṃ prakalpayet  (iti)
   Chapt .   Superintendent of the magashin
02.15.01 koṣṭhāgārādhyakṣaḥ sītārāṣṭrakrayimaparivartakaprāmityakāpamityakasaṃhanikānyajātavyayapratyāya upasthānānyupalabhet
02.15.02 sītā'dhyakṣa upanītaḥ sasyavarṇakaḥ sītā
02.15.03 piṇḍakaraḥ ṣaḍbhāgaḥ senābhaktaṃ baliḥ kara utsaṅgaḥ pārśvaṃ pārihīṇikaṃ aupāyanikaṃ kauṣṭheyakaṃ ca rāṣṭram
02.15.04 dhānyamūlyaṃ kośanirhāraḥ prayogapratyādānaṃ ca krayimam
02.15.05 sasyavarṇānāṃ arghāntareṇa vinimayaḥ parivartakaḥ
02.15.06 sasyayācanaṃ anyataḥ prāmityakam
02.15.07 tad eva pratidānārthaṃ āpamityakam
02.15.08 kuṭṭakarocakasaktuśuktapiṣṭakarma tajjīvaneṣu tailapīḍanamaudracākrikeṣvikṣūṇāṃ ca kṣārakarma saṃhanikā
02.15.09 naṣṭaprasmṛtādiranyajātaḥ
02.15.10 vikṣepavyādhitāntarārambhaśeṣaṃ ca vyayapratyāyaḥ
02.15.11 tulāmānāntaraṃ hastapūraṇaṃ utkaro vyājī paryuṣitaṃ prārjitaṃ ca upasthānam । iti
02.15.12 dhānyasnehakṣāralavaṇānāṃ dhānyakalpaṃ sītā'dhyakṣe vakṣyāmaḥ
02.15.13 sarpistailavasāmajjānaḥ snehāḥ
02.15.14 phāṇitaguḍamatsyaṇḍikākhaṇḍaśarkarāḥ kṣāravargaḥ
02.15.15 saindhavasāmudrabiḍayavakṣārasauvarcala udbhedajā lavaṇavargaḥ
02.15.16 kṣaudraṃ mārdvīkaṃ ca madhu
02.15.17 ikṣurasaguḍamadhuphāṇitajāmbavapanasānāṃ anyatamo meṣaśṛṅgīpippalīkvāthābhiṣuto māsikaḥ ṣāṇmāsikaḥ sāṃvatsariko vā cidbhiṭorvāruka ikṣukāṇḍāmraphalāmalakāvasutaḥ śuddho vā śuktavargaḥ
02.15.18 vṛkṣāmlakaramardāmravidalāmalakamātuluṅgakolabadarasauvīrakaparūṣakādiḥ phalāmlavargaḥ
02.15.19 dadhidhānyāmlādirdravāmlavargaḥ
02.15.20 pippalīmaricaśṛṅgiberā'jājīkirātatiktagaurasarṣapakustumburucorakadamanakamaruvakaśigrukāṇḍādiḥ kaṭukavargaḥ
02.15.21 śuṣkamatsyamāṃsakandamūlaphalaśākādi ca śākavargaḥ
02.15.22 tato'rdhaṃ āpad'rthaṃ jānapadānāṃ sthāpayed, ardhaṃ upayuñjīta
02.15.23 navena cānavaṃ śodhayet
02.15.24 kṣuṇṇaghṛṣṭapiṣṭabhṛṣṭānāṃ ārdraśuṣkasiddhānāṃ ca dhānyānāṃ vṛddhikṣayapramāṇāni pratyakṣīkurvīta
02.15.25 kodravavrīhīṇāṃ ardhaṃ sāraḥ, śālīnāṃ ardhabhāga ūnaḥ, tribhāga ūno varakāṇām
02.15.26 priyaṅgūṇāṃ ardhaṃ sāro navabhāgavṛddhiśca
02.15.27 udārakaḥ tulyaḥ, yavā godhūmāśca kṣuṇṇāḥ, tilā yavā mudgamāṣāśca ghṛṣṭāḥ
02.15.28 pañcabhāgavṛddhirgodhūmaḥ, saktavaśca

02.15.30 mudgamāṣāṇāṃ ardhapāda ūnā
02.15.31 śaumbyānāṃ ardhaṃ sāraḥ, tribhāga ūno masūrāṇām
02.15.32 piṣṭaṃ āmaṃ kulmāṣāścādhyardhaguṇāḥ
02.15.33 dviguṇo yāvakaḥ, pulākaḥ, piṣṭaṃ ca siddham
02.15.34 kodravavaraka udārakapriyaṅgūṇāṃ triguṇaṃ annaṃ, caturguṇaṃ vrīhīṇāṃ, pañcaguṇaṃ śālīnām
02.15.35 timitaṃ aparānnaṃ dviguṇaṃ, ardhādhikaṃ virūḍhānām
02.15.36 pañcabhāgavṛddhirbhṛṣṭānām
02.15.37 kalāyo dviguṇaḥ, lājā bharujāśca
02.15.38 ṣaṭkaṃ tailaṃ atasīnām
02.15.39 nimbakuśāmrakapitthādīnāṃ pañcabhāgaḥ
02.15.40 caturbhāgikāḥ tilakusumbhamadhūka iṅgudīsnehāḥ
02.15.41 kārpāsakṣaumāṇāṃ pañcapale palaṃ sūtram
02.15.42 pañcadroṇe śālīnāṃ dvādaśāḍhakaṃ taṇḍulānāṃ kalabhabhojanaṃ, ekādaśakaṃ vyālānāṃ, daśakaṃ aupavāhyānāṃ navakaṃ sāmnāhyānāṃ, aṣṭakaṃ pattīnāṃ, saptakaṃ mukhyānāṃ, ṣaṭkaṃ devīkumārāṇāṃ, pañcakaṃ rājñāṃ, akhaṇḍapariśuddhānāṃ vā tuaṇḍulānāṃ prasthaḥ
02.15.43 taṇḍulānāṃ prasthaḥ caturbhāgaḥ sūpaḥ sūpaṣoḍaśo lavaṇasyāṃśaḥ caturbhāgaḥ sarpiṣaḥ tailasya vā ekaṃ āryabhaktaṃ puṃsaḥ
02.15.44 ṣaḍbhāgaḥ sūpaḥ ardhasnehaṃ avarāṇām
02.15.45 pāda ūnaṃ strīṇām
02.15.46 ardhaṃ bālānām
02.15.47 māṃsapalaviṃśatyā snehārdhakuḍubaḥ paliko lavaṇasyāṃśaḥ kṣārapalayogo dvidharaṇikaḥ kaṭukayogo dadhnuścārdhaprasthaḥ
02.15.48 tena uttaraṃ vyākhyātam
02.15.49 śākānāṃ adhyardhaguṇaḥ, śuṣkāṇāṃ dviguṇaḥ, sa caiva yogaḥ

02.21.01 śulkādhyakṣaḥ śulkaśālāṃ dhvajaṃ ca prānmukhaṃ udanmukhaṃ vā mahādvārābhyāśe niveśayet
02.21.02 śulkādāyinaścatvāraḥ pañca vā sārtha upayātān vaṇijo likheyuḥ - ke kutastyāḥ kiyatpaṇyāḥ kva cābhijñānaṃ mudrā vā kṛtā iti
02.21.03 amudrāṇāṃ atyayo deyadviguṇaḥ
02.21.04 kūṭamudrāṇāṃ śulkāṣṭaguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.21.05 bhinnamudrāṇāṃ atyayo ghaṭikāsthāne sthānam
02.21.06 rājamudrāparivartane nāmakṛte vā sa-pādapaṇikaṃ vahanaṃ dāpayet
02.21.07 dhvajamūla upasthitasya pramāṇaṃ arghaṃ ca vaidehikāḥ paṇyasya brūyuḥ etatpramāṇenārgheṇa paṇyaṃ idaṃ kaḥ kretā iti
02.21.08 triruddha uṣitaṃ arthibhyo dadyāt
02.21.09 kretṛsaṅgharṣe mūlyavṛddhiḥ sa-śulkā kośaṃ gacchet
02.21.10 śulkabhayāt paṇyapramāṇa mūlyaṃ vā hīnaṃ bruvataḥ tad atiriktaṃ rājā haret
02.21.11 śulkaṃ aṣṭaguṇaṃ vā dadyāt
02.21.12 tad eva niviṣṭapaṇyasya bhāṇḍasya hīnaprativarṇakenārghāpakarṣaṇe sārabhāṇḍasya phalgubhāṇḍena praticchādane ca kuryāt
02.21.13 pratikretṛbhayād vā paṇyamūlyād upari mūlyaṃ vardhayato mūlyavṛddhiṃ rājā haret, dviguṇaṃ vā śulkaṃ kuryāt
02.21.14 tad evāṣṭaguṇaṃ adhyakṣasyac । chādayataḥ
02.21.15 tasmād vikrayaḥ paṇyānāṃ dhṛto mito gaṇito vā kāryaḥ, tarkaḥ phalgubhāṇḍānāṃ ānugrāhikāṇāṃ ca
02.21.16 dhvajamūlaṃ atikrāntānāṃ cākṛtaśulkānāṃ śulkād aṣṭaguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.21.17 pathika utpathikāḥ tad vidyuḥ
02.21.18 vaivāhikaṃ anvāyanaṃ aupāyikaṃ yajñakṛtyaprasavanaimittikaṃ deva ijyācaula upanayanagodānavratadīkṣā''diṣu kriyāviśeṣeṣu bhāṇḍaṃ ucchulkaṃ gacchet
02.21.19 anyathāvādinaḥ steyadaṇḍaḥ
02.21.20 kṛtaśulkenākṛtaśulkaṃ nirvāhayato dvitīyaṃ ekamudrayā bhittvā paṇyapuṭaṃ apaharato vaidehakasya tacca tāvacca daṇḍaḥ
02.21.21 śulkasthānād gomayapalālaṃ pramāṇaṃ kṛtvā'paharata uttamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
02.21.22 śastravarmakavacaloharatharatnadhānyapaśūnāṃ anyatamaṃ anirvāhyaṃ nirvāhayato yathā'vaghuṣito daṇḍaḥ paṇyanāśaśca
02.21.23 teṣāṃ anyatamasyānayane bahireva ucchulko vikrayaḥ
02.21.24 antapālaḥ sa-pādapaṇikāṃ vartanīṃ gṛhṇīyāt paṇyavahanasya, paṇikāṃ ekakhurasya, paśūnāṃ ardhapaṇikāṃ kṣudrapaśūnāṃ pādikāṃ, aṃsabhārasya māṣikām
02.21.25 naṣṭāpahṛtaṃ ca pratividadhyāt
02.21.26 vaideśyaṃ sārthaṃ kṛtasāraphalgubhāṇḍavicayanaṃ abhijñānaṃ mudrāṃ ca dattvā preṣayed adhyakṣasya
02.21.27 vaidehakavyañjano vā sārthapramāṇaṃ rājñaḥ preṣayet
02.21.28 tena pradeśena rājā śulkādhyakṣasya sārthapramāṇaṃ upadiśet sarvajñakhyāpanārtham
02.21.29 tataḥ sārthaṃ adhyakṣo'bhigamya brūyāt idaṃ amuṣyāṃ uṣya ca sārabhāṇḍaṃ phalgubhāṇḍaṃ ca, na nihūhitavyaṃ, eṣa rājñaḥ prabhāvaḥ iti
02.21.30 nihūhataḥ phalgubhāṇḍaṃ śulkāṣṭaguṇo daṇḍaḥ, sārabhāṇḍaṃ sarvāpahāraḥ
02.21.31ab rāṣṭrapīḍākaraṃ bhāṇḍaṃ ucchindyād aphalaṃ ca yat ।

   Chapt .   Tariff of duties and tolls

02.23.01 sūtrādhyakṣaḥ sūtravarmavastrarajjuvyavahāraṃ tajjātapuruṣaiḥ kārayet

02.24.01 sītā'dhyakṣaḥ kṛṣitantraśulbavṛkṣāyurvedajñaḥ tajjñasakho vā sarvadhānyapuṣpaphalaśākakandamūlavāllikyakṣaumakārpāsabījāni yathākālaṃ gṛhṇīyāt

02.26.01 sūnā'dhyakṣaḥ pradiṣṭābhayānāṃ abhayavanavāsināṃ ca mṛgapaśupakṣimatsyānāṃ bandhavadhahiṃsāyāṃ uttamaṃ daṇḍaṃ kārayet, kuṭumbināṃ abhayavanaparigraheṣu madhyamam
02.26.02 apravṛttavadhānāṃ matsyapakṣiṇāṃ bandhavadhahiṃsāyāṃ pāda ūnasaptaviṃśatipaṇaṃ atyayaṃ kuryāt, mṛgapaśūnāṃ dviguṇam
02.26.03 pravṛttahiṃsānāṃ aparigṛhītānāṃ ṣaḍbhāgaṃ gṛhṇīyāt, matsyapakṣiṇāṃ daśabhāgaṃ vā'dhikaṃ, mṛgapaśūnāṃ śulkaṃ vā'dhikam

02.27.01 gaṇikā'dhyakṣo gaṇikā'nvayāṃ agaṇikā'nvayāṃ vā rūpayauvanaśilpasampannāṃ sahasreṇa gaṇikāṃ kārayet, kuṭumbārdhena pratigaṇikām
02.27.02 niṣpatitāpretayorduhitā bhaginī vā kuṭumbaṃ bhareta, mātā vā pratigaṇikāṃ sthāpayet
02.27.03 tāsāṃ abhāve rājā haret
02.27.04 saubhāgyālaṅkāravṛddhyā sahasreṇa vāraṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ madhyamaṃ uttamaṃ vā''ropayet chatrabhṛṅgāravyajanaśibikāpīṭhikāratheṣu ca viśeṣārtham

02.27.14 gaṇikāṃ akāmāṃ rundhato niṣpātayato vā vraṇavidāraṇena vā rūpaṃ।upaghnataḥ sahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ
02.27.15 sthānviśeṣeṇa vā daṇḍavṛddhiḥ āniṣkrayadviguṇāt

02.27.17 mātṛkāduhitṛkārūpadāsīnāṃ ghāte uttamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ

02.27.20 bhogaṃ gṛhītvā dviṣatyā bhogadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.27.21 vasatibhogāpahāre bhogaṃ aṣṭaguṇaṃ dadyād anyatra vyādhipuruṣadoṣebhyaḥ
02.27.22 puruṣaṃ ghnatyāścitāpratāpe'psu praveśanaṃ vā

02.27.24 gaṇikā bhogaṃ āyatiṃ puruṣaṃ ca nivedayet
02.27.25 etena naṭanartakagāyanavādakavāgjīvanakuśīlavaplavakasaubhikacāraṇānāṃ strīvyavahāriṇāṃ striyo gūḍhājīvāśca vyākhyātāḥ

02.28.20 parasya bhāryāṃ kanyāṃ vittaṃ vā'paharantaṃ śavittaṃ vā'paharantaṃ śaṅkitaṃ āvignaṃ udbhāṇḍīkṛtaṃ mahābhāṇḍena mūrdhni bhāreṇāvacchādayantaṃ sadyogṛhītaliṅginaṃ aliṅginaṃ vā pravrajitaṃ alakṣyavyādhitaṃ bhayavikāriṇaṃ gūḍhasārabhāṇḍaśāsanaśastrāgniyogaṃ viṣahastaṃ dīrghapathikaṃ amudraṃ ca upagrāhayet
02.28.21 kṣudrapaśurmanuṣyaśca sabhāro māṣakaṃ dadyāt, śirobhāraḥ kāyabhāro gavāśvaṃ ca dvau, uṣṭramahiṣaṃ caturaḥ, pañca labhuyānaṃ, ṣaḍ goliṅgaṃ, sapta śakaṭaṃ, panyabhāraḥ pādam

02.29.01 go'dhyakṣo vetana upagrāhikaṃ karapratikaraṃ bhagna utsṛṣṭakaṃ bhāgānupraviṣṭakaṃ vrajaparyagraṃ naṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ kṣīraghṛtasañjātaṃ ca upalabheta
02.29.02 gopālakapiṇḍārakadohakamanthakalubdhakāḥ śataṃ śataṃ dhenūnāṃ hiraṇyabhṛtāḥ pālayeyuḥ

02.30.01 aśvādhyakṣaḥ paṇyāgārikaṃ kraya upāgataṃ āhavalabdhaṃ ājātaṃ sāhāyyāgatakaṃ paṇasthitaṃ yāvatkālikaṃ vā'śvaparyagraṃ kulavayovarṇacihnavargāgamairlekhayet

02.30.04 aśvavibhavenāyatāṃ aśvāyāṃ adviguṇavistārāṃ caturdvāra upāvartanamadhyāṃ sa-pragrīvāṃ pradvārāsanaphalakayuktānāṃ vānaramayūrapṛṣatanakulacakoraśukasārikākīrṇāṃ śālāṃ niveśayet

02.30.07 vaḍavāvṛṣakiśorāṇāṃ ekānteṣu

02.30.09 ata ūrdhvaṃ saktuprasthaḥ snehabhaiṣajyapratipānaṃ daśarātram
02.30.10 tataḥ pulāko yavasaṃ ārtavaścāhāraḥ
02.30.11 daśarātrād ūrdhvaṃ kiśorasya ghṛtacaturbhāgaḥ saktukuḍubaḥ kṣīraprasthaścāhāra āṣaṇmāsāt
02.30.12 tataḥ paraṃ māsa uttaraṃ ardhavṛddhiryavaprastha ātrivarṣāt, droṇa ācaturvarṣāt
02.30.13 ata ūrdhvaṃ caturvarṣaḥ pañcavarṣo vā karmaṇyaḥ pūrṇapramāṇaḥ
02.30.14 dvātriṃśad'ṅgulaṃ mukhaṃ uttamāśvasya, pañcamukhānyāyāmo, viṃśaty'ṅgulā jaṅghā, caturjaṅgha utsedhaḥ
02.30.15 try'ṅgulāvaraṃ madhyamāvarayoḥ
02.30.16 śatāṅgulaḥ pariṇāhaḥ
02.30.17 pañcabhāgāvaro madhyamāvarayoḥ
02.30.18 uttamāśvasya dvidroṇaṃ śālivrīhiyavapriyaṅgūṇāṃ ardhaśuṣkaṃ ardhasiddhaṃ vā mudgamāṣāṇāṃ vā pulākaḥ snehaprasthaśca, pañcapalaṃ lavaṇasya, māṃsaṃ pañcāśatpalikaṃ rasasyāḍhakaṃ dviguṇaṃ vā dadhnaḥ piṇḍakledanārthaṃ, kṣārapañcapalikaḥ surāyāḥ prasthaḥ payaso vā dviguṇaḥ pratipānam
02.30.19 dīrghapathabhāraklāntānāṃ ca khādanārthaṃ snehaprastho'nuvāsanaṃ kuḍubo nasyakarmaṇaḥ, yavasasyārdhabhāraḥ tṛṇasya dviguṇaḥ ṣaḍ'ratniparikṣepaḥ puñjīlagraho vā
02.30.20 pādāvaraṃ etan madhyamāvarayoḥ
02.30.21 uttamasamo rathyo vṛṣaśca madhyamaḥ
02.30.22 madhyamasamaścāvaraḥ
02.30.23 pādahīnaṃ vaḍavānāṃ pāraśamānāṃ ca
02.30.24 ato'rdhaṃ kiśorāṇāṃ ca
02.30.25 iti vidhāyogaḥ
02.30.26 vidhāpācakasūtragrāhakacikitsakāḥ pratisvādabhājaḥ
02.30.27 yuddhavyādhijarākarmakṣīṇāḥ piṇḍagocarikāḥ syuḥ
02.30.28 asamaraprayogyāḥ paurajānapadānāṃ arthena vṛṣā vaḍavāsvāyojyāḥ
02.30.29 prayogyānāṃ uttamāḥ kāmbojasaindhavāraṭṭavanāyujāḥ, madhyamā bāhlīkapāpeyakasauvīrakataitalāḥ, śeṣāḥ pratyavarāḥ
02.30.30 teṣāṃ tīṣkṇabhadramandavaśena sāmnāhyaṃ aupavāhyakaṃ vā karma prayojayet
02.30.31 catur'śraṃ karmāśvasya sāmnāhyam
02.30.32 valgano nīcairgato laṅghano ghoraṇo nāroṣṭraścāupavāhyāḥ
02.30.33 tatrāupaveṇuko vardhamānako yamaka ālīḍhaplutaḥ pṛthug'strikacālī ca valganaḥ
02.30.34 sa eva śiraḥkarṇaviśuddho nīcairgataḥ, ṣoḍaśamārgo vā
02.30.35 prakīrṇakaḥ prakīrṇa uttaro niṣaṇṇaḥ pārśvānuvṛtta ūrmimārgaḥ śarabhakrīḍitaḥ śarabhaplutaḥ tritālo bāhyānuvṛttaḥ pañcapāṇiḥ siṃhāyataḥ svādhūtaḥ kliṣṭaḥ śliṅgito bṛṃhitaḥ puṣpābhikīrṇaśca iti nīcairgatamārgaḥ
02.30.36 kapipluto bhekapluteṇapluta ekapādaplutaḥ kokilasañcāry।urasyo bakacārī ca laṅghanaḥ
02.30.37 kāṅko vārikāṅko māyūro'rdhamāyūro nākulordhanākulo vārāho'rdhavārāhaśca iti dhoraṇaḥ
02.30.38 saṃjñāpratikāro nāra uṣṭra iti
02.30.39 ṣaṇṇava dvādaśa iti yojanānydhvā rathyānāṃ, pañca yojanānyardhāṣṭamāni daśa iti pṛṣṭhavāhināṃ aśvānāṃ adhvā
02.30.40 vikramo bhadrāśvāso bhāravāhya iti mārgāḥ
02.30.41 vikramo valgitaṃ upakaṇṭhaṃ upajavo javaśca dhārāḥ
02.30.42 teṣāṃ bandhana upakaraṇaṃ yogyācāryāḥ pratidiśeyuḥ, sāṅgrāmikaṃ rathāśvālaṅkāraṃ ca sūtāḥ
02.30.43 aśvānāṃ cikitsakāḥ śarīrahrāsavṛddhipratīkāraṃ ṛtuvibhaktaṃ cāhāram
02.30.44 sūtragrāhakāśvabandhakayāvasikavidhāpācakasthānapālakeśakārajāṅgulīvidaśca svakarmabhiraśvān ārādhayeyuḥ
02.30.45 karmātikrame ca eṣāṃ divasavetanacchedanaṃ kuryāt
02.30.46 nīrājana uparuddhaṃ vāhayataścikitsaka uparuddhaṃ vā dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.30.47 kriyābhaiṣajyasaṅgena vyādhivṛddhau pratīkāradviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.30.48 tad'parādhena vailomye pattramūlyaṃ daṇḍaḥ
02.30.49 tena gomaṇḍalaṃ khara uṣṭramahiṣaṃ ajāvikaṃ ca vyākhyātam
02.30.50ab dvirahnaḥ snānaṃ aśvānāṃ gandhamālyaṃ ca dāpayet ।
02.30.50chd kṛṣṇasandhiṣu bhūta ijyāḥ śukleṣu svastivācanam
02.30.51ab nīrājanāṃ āśvayuje kārayennavame'hani ।

02.31.01 hasty'dhyakṣo hastivanarakṣāṃ damyakarmakṣāntānāṃ hastihastinīkalabhānāṃ śālāsthānaśayyākarmavidhāyavasapramāṇaṃ karmasvāyogaṃ bandhana upakaraṇaṃ sāṅgrāmikaṃ alaṅkāraṃ cikitsakānīkasthāupasthāyikavargaṃ cānutiṣṭhet
02.31.02 hasty।āyāmadviguṇa utsedhaviṣkambhāyāmāṃ hastinīsthānādhikāṃ sapragrīvāṃ kumārīsaṅgrahāṃ prānmukhīṃ udanmukhīṃ vā śālāṃ niveśayet
02.31.03 hasty।āyāmacatur'śraślakṣṇālānastambhaphalakāstarakaṃ sa-mūtrapurīṣa utsargaṃ sthānaṃ niveśayet
02.31.04 sthānasamāṃ śayyāṃ ardhāpāśrayāṃ durge sāmnāhyāupavāhyānāṃ bahirdamyavyālānām
02.31.05 prathamasaptama aṣṭamabhāgāvahnaḥ snānakālau, tad'nantaraṃ vidhāyāḥ
02.31.06 pūrvāhne vyāyāmakālaḥ, paścāhnaḥ pratipānakālaḥ
02.31.07 rātribhāgau dvau svapnakālā, tribhāgaḥ saṃveśana utthānikaḥ
02.31.08 grīṣme grahaṇakālaḥ
02.31.09 viṃśativarṣo grāhyaḥ
02.31.10 vikko moḍho makkaṇo vyāthito garbhiṇī dhenukā hastinī cāgrāhyāḥ
02.31.11 saptāratni utsedho navāyāmo daśa pariṇāhaḥ pramāṇataścatvāriṃśadvarṣo bhavatyuttamaḥ, triṃśadvarṣo madhyamaḥ, pañcaviṃśativarṣo'varaḥ
02.31.12 tayoḥ pādāvaro vidhāvidhiḥ
02.31.13 aratnau taṇuladroṇaḥ, ardhāḍhakaṃ tailasya, sarpiṣaḥ trayaḥ prasthāḥ, daśapalaṃ lavaṇasya, māṃsaṃ pañcāśatpalikaṃ, rasasyāḍhakaṃ dviguṇaṃ vā dadhnaḥ piṇḍakledanārthaṃ, kṣāradaśapalikaṃ madyasyāḍhakaṃ dviguṇaṃ vā payasaḥ pratipānaṃ, gātrāvasekaḥ tailaprasthaḥ, śiraso'ṣṭabhāgaḥ prādīpikaśca, yavasasya dvau bhārau sa-pādau, śaṣpasya śuṣkasyārdhatṛtīyo bhāraḥ, kaḍaṅkarasyāniyamaḥ
02.31.14 saptāratninā tulyabhojano'ṣṭāratniratyarālaḥ
02.31.15 yathāhastaṃ avaśeṣaḥ ṣaḍ'ratniḥ pañcāratniśca

02.31.17 sañjātalohitā praticchannā samliptapakṣā samakakṣyā vyatikīrṇamāṃsā samatalpatalā jātadroṇikā iti śobhāḥ
02.31.18ab śobhāvaśena vyāyāmaṃ bhadrma mandaṃ ca kārayet ।

02.32.01 karmaskandhāścatvāro damyaḥ sāmnāhya aupavāhyo vyālaśca

02.32.03 tasya upavicāro vikkakarma
02.32.04 sāmnāhyaḥ saptakriyāpatha upasthānaṃ saṃvartanaṃ samyānaṃ vadhāvadho hastiyuddhaṃ nāgarāyaṇaṃ sāṅgrāmikaṃ ca

02.35.01 samāhartā caturdhā janāpdaṃ vibhajya jyeṣṭhamadhyamakaniṣṭhavibhāgena grāmāgraṃ parihārakaṃ āyudhīyaṃ dhānyapaśuhiraṇyakupyaviṣṭipratikaraṃ idaṃ etāvad iti nibandhayet
02.35.02 tatpradiṣṭaḥ pañcagrāmīṃ daśagrāmīṃ vā gopaścintayet
02.35.03 sīmāvarodhena grāmāgraṃ, kṛṣṭākṛṣṭasthalakedārārāmaṣaṇḍavāṭavanavāstucaityadevagṛhasetubandhaśmaśānasattraprapāpuṇyasthānavivītapathisaṅkhyānena kṣetrāgraṃ, tena sīmnāṃ kṣetrāṇāṃ ca karadākaradasaṅkhyānena

02.36.18 pādaḥ pañcaghaṭīnāṃ kumbhadroṇinihśreṇīparaśuśūrpāṅkuśakacagrahaṇīdṛtīnāṃ cākaraṇe
02.36.19 tṛṇakaṭacchannānyapanayet
02.36.20 agnijīvina ekasthān vāsayet
02.36.21 svagṛhapradvāreṣu gṛhasvāmino vaseyuḥ asampātino rātrau
02.36.22 rathyāsu kuṭavrajāḥ sahasraṃ tiṣṭheyuḥ, catuṣpathadvārarājaparigraheṣu ca
02.36.23 pradīptaṃ anabhidhāvato gṛhasvāmino dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, ṣaṭpaṇo'vakrayiṇaḥ
02.36.24 pramādād dīpteṣu catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.36.25 pradīpiko'gninā vadhyaḥ
02.36.26 pāṃsunyāse rathyāyāṃ aṣṭabhāgo daṇḍaḥ, paṅka udakasamnirodhe pādaḥ
02.36.27 rājamārge dviguṇaḥ
02.36.28 paṇyasthāna udakasthānadevagṛharājaparigraheṣu paṇa uttarā viṣṭādaṇḍāḥ, mūtreṣvardhadaṇḍāḥ
02.36.29 bhaiṣajyavyādhibhayanimittaṃ adaṇḍyāḥ
02.36.30 mārjāraśvanakulasarpapretānāṃ nagarasyāntar।utsarge tripaṇo daṇḍaḥ, khara uṣṭrāśvatarāśvapretānāṃ ṣaṭpaṇaḥ, manuṣyapretānāṃ pañcāśatpaṇaḥ
02.36.31 mārgaviparyāse śavadvārād anyataśca śavanirṇayane pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
02.36.32 dvāḥsthānāṃ dviśatam
02.36.33 śmaśānād anyatra nyāse dahane ca dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.36.34 viṣaṇṇālikaṃ ubhayatorātraṃ yāmatūryam
02.36.35 tūryaśabde rājño gṛhābhyāśe sapādapaṇaṃ'kṣaṇatāḍanaṃ prathamapaścimayāmikaṃ, madhyamayāmikaṃ dviguṇaṃ, antaścaturguṇam
02.36.36 śaṅkanīye deśe liṅge pūrvāpadāne ca gṛhītaṃ anuyuñjīta
02.36.37 rājaparigraha upagamane nagararakṣā''rohaṇe ca madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
02.36.38 sūtikācikitsakapretapradīpayānanāgarikatūryaprekṣā'gninimittaṃ mudrābhiścāgrāhyāḥ
02.36.39 cārarātriṣu pracchannaviparītaveṣāḥ pravrajitā daṇḍaśastrahastāśca manuṣyā doṣato daṇḍyāḥ
02.36.40 rakṣiṇāṃ avāryaṃ vārayatāṃ vāryaṃ cāvārayatāṃ kṣaṇadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
02.36.41 striyaṃ dāsīṃ adhimehayatāṃ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, adāsīṃ madhyamaḥ, kṛtāvarodhāṃ uttamaḥ, kulastriyaṃ vadhaḥ
02.36.42 cetanācetanikaṃ rātridoṣaṃ aśaṃsato nāgarikasya doṣānurūpo daṇḍaḥ, pramādasthāne ca
02.36.43 nityaṃ udakasthānamārgabhramacchannapathavapraprākārarakṣā'vekṣaṇaṃ naṣṭaprasmṛtāpasṛtānāṃ ca rakṣaṇam
02.36.44 bandhanāgāre ca bālavṛddhavyādhitānāthānāṃ jātanakṣatrapaurṇamāsīṣu visargaḥ
02.36.45 paṇyaśīlāḥ samayānubaddhā vā doṣaniṣkrayaṃ dadyuḥ
02.36.46ab divase pañcarātre vā bandhanasthān viśodhayet ।

03.1.01 dharmasthāḥ trayaḥ trayo'mātyā janapadasandhisaṅgrahaṇadroṇamukhasthānīyeṣu vyāvahārikān arthān kuryuḥ
03.1.02 tirohitāntar'gāranaktāraṇya upadhy।upahvarakṛtāṃśca vyavahārān pratiṣedhayeyuḥ
03.1.03 kartuḥ kārayituḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.1.04 śrotṝṇāṃ eka ekaṃ pratyardhadaṇḍāḥ
03.1.05 śraddheyānāṃ tu dravyavyapanayaḥ
03.1.06 parokṣeṇādhika।ṛṇagrahaṇaṃ avaktavyakarā vā tirohitāḥ sidhyeyuḥ
03.1.07 dāyanikṣepa upanidhivivāhayuktāḥ strīṇāṃ aniṣkāsinīnāṃ vyādhitānāṃ cāmūḍhasaṃjñānāṃ antar'gārakṛtāḥ sidhyeyuḥ
03.1.08 sāhasānupraveśakalahavivāharājaniyogayuktāḥ pūrvarātravyavahāriṇāṃ ca rātrikṛtāḥ sidhyeyuḥ
03.1.09 sārthavrajāśramavyādhacāraṇamadhyeṣvaraṇyacarāṇāṃ araṇyakṛtāḥ sidhyeyuḥ
03.1.10 gūḍhājīviṣu ca upadhikṛtāḥ sidhyeyuḥ
03.1.11 mithaḥsamavāye ca upahvarakṛtāḥ sidhyeyuḥ
03.1.12 ato'nyathā na sidhyeyuḥ, apāśrayavadbhiśca kṛtāḥ, pitṛmatā putreṇa, pitrā putravatā, niṣkulena bhrātrā, kaniṣṭhenāvibhaktāṃśena, patimatyā putravatyā ca striyā, dāsāhitakābhyāṃ, aprāptātītavyavahārābhyāṃ, abhiśastapravrajitanyaṅgavyasanibhiśca, anyatra niṣṛṣṭavyavahārebhyaḥ
03.1.13 tatrāpi kruddhenārtena mattena unmattenāvagṛhītena vā kṛtā vyavahārā na sidhyeyuḥ
03.1.14 kartṛkārayitṛśrotṝṇāṃ pṛthag yathā uktā daṇḍāḥ
03.1.15 sve sve tu varge deśe kāle ca svakaraṇakṛtāḥ sampūrṇācārāḥ śuddhadeśā dṛṣṭarūpalakṣaṇapramāṇaguṇāḥ sarvavyavahārāḥ sidhyeyuḥ
03.1.16 paścimaṃ ca eṣāṃ karaṇaṃ ādeśādhivarjaṃ śraddheyam iti vyavahārasthāpanā ।
03.1.17 saṃvatsaraṃ ṛtuṃ māsaṃ pakṣaṃ divasaṃ karaṇaṃ adhikaraṇaṃ ṛṇaṃ vedakāvedakayoḥ kṛtasamarthāvasthayordeśagrāmajātigotranāmakarmāṇi cābhilikhya vādiprativādipraśnān arthānupūrvyā niveśayet
03.1.18 niviṣṭāṃścāvekṣeta
03.1.19 nibaddhaṃ vādaṃ utsṛjyānyaṃ vādaṃ saṅkrāmati, pūrva uktaṃ paścimenārthena nābhisandhatte, paravākyaṃ anabhigrāhyaṃ abhigrāhyāvatiṣṭhate, pratijñāya deśaṃ nirdiśa ityukte na nirdiśati, hīnadeśaṃ adeśaṃ vā nirdiśati, nirdiṣṭād deśād anyaṃ deśaṃ upasthāpayati, upasthite deśe'rthavacanaṃ na evaṃ ityapavyayate, sākṣibhiravadhṛtaṃ na icchati, asambhāṣye deśe sākṣibhirmithaḥ sambhāṣate, iti parā uktahetavaḥ
03.1.20 parā uktadaṇḍaḥ pañcabandhaḥ
03.1.21 svayaṃvādidaṇḍo daśabandhaḥ
03.1.22 puruṣabhṛtiraṣṭāṃśaḥ
03.1.23 pathibhaktaṃ arghaviśeṣataḥ
03.1.24 tad ubhayaṃ niyamyo dadyāt
03.1.25 abhiyukto na pratyabhiyuñjīta, anyatra kalahasāhasasārthasamavāyebhyaḥ
03.1.26 na cābhiyukte'bhiyoge'sti
03.1.27 abhiyoktā cet pratyuktaḥ tad'hareva na pratibrūyāt parā uktaḥ syāt
03.1.28 kṛtakāryaviniścayo hyabhiyoktā nābhiyuktaḥ
03.1.29 tasyāpratibruvataḥ trirātraṃ saptarātraṃ iti
03.1.30 ata ūrdhvaṃ tripaṇāvarārdhyaṃ dvādaśapaṇaparaṃ daṇḍaṃ kuryāt
03.1.31 tripakṣād ūrdhvaṃ apratibruvataḥ parā uktadaṇḍaṃ kṛtvā yānyasya dravyāṇi syuḥ tato'bhiyoktāraṃ pratipādayed, anyatra vṛtty।upakaraṇebhyaḥ

03.1.36 ādhiṃ vā sa kāmaṃ praveśayet
03.1.37 rakṣoghnarakṣitaṃ vā karmaṇā pratipādayed, anyatra brāhmaṇāt
03.1.38ab caturvarṇāśramasyāyaṃ lokasyācārarakṣaṇāt ।
03.1.38chd naśyatāṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ rājā dharmapravartakaḥ
03.1.39ab dharmaśca vyavahāraśca caritraṃ rājaśāsanam ।
03.1.39chd vivādārthaścatuṣpādaḥ paścimaḥ pūrvabādhakaḥ
03.1.40ab tatra satye sthito dharmo vyavahāraḥ tu sākṣiṣu ।
03.1.40chd caritraṃ saṅgrahe puṃsāṃ rājñāṃ ājñā tu śāsanam
03.1.41ab rājñaḥ svadharmaḥ svargāya prajā dharmeṇa rakṣituḥ ।
03.1.41chd arakṣiturvā kṣepturvā mithyādaṇḍaṃ ato'nyathā
03.1.42ab daṇḍo hi kevalo lokaṃ paraṃ ca imaṃ ca rakṣati ।
03.1.42chd rājñā putre ca śatrau ca yathādoṣaṃ samaṃ dhṛtaḥ
03.1.43ab anuśāsadd hi dharmeṇa vyavahāreṇa saṃsthayā ।
03.1.43chd nyāyena ca caturthena catur'ntāṃ vā mahīṃ jayet
03.1.44ab saṃsthā yā dharmaśāstreṇa śāstraṃ vā vyāvahārikam ।
03.1.44chd yasminn arthe virudhyeta dharmeṇārthaṃ vinirṇayet

03.1.45chd nyāyaḥ tatra pramāṇaṃ syāt tatra pāṭho hi naśyati
03.1.46ab dṛṣṭadoṣaḥ svayaṃvādaḥ svapakṣaparapakṣayoḥ ।
03.1.46chd anuyogārjavaṃ hetuḥ śapathaścārthasādhakaḥ

03.2.20 labdhvā vā vindamānā sa-vṛddhikaṃ ubhayaṃ dāpyeta

03.2.22 niveśakālaṃ hi dīrghapravāse vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
03.2.23 śvaśuraprātilomyena vā niviṣṭā śvaśurapatidattaṃ jīyeta
03.2.24 jñātihastād'bhimṛṣṭāyā jñātayo yathāgṛhītaṃ dadyuḥ
03.2.25 nyāya upagatāyāḥ pratipattā strīdhanaṃ gopayet
03.2.26 patidāyaṃ vindamānā jīyeta
03.2.27 dharmakāmā bhuñjīta

03.2.30 putrabharaṇārthaṃ vā vindamānā putrārthaṃ sphātīkuryāt
03.2.31 bahupuruṣaprajānāṃ putrāṇāṃ yathāpitṛdattaṃ strīdhanaṃ avasthāpayet
03.2.32 kāmakaraṇīyaṃ api strīdhanaṃ vindamānā putrasaṃsthaṃ kuryāt

03.2.35 ūrdhvaṃ dāyādaṃ gacchet

03.2.37 śulkaṃ anvādheyaṃ anyad vā bandhubhirdattaṃ bāndhavā hareyuḥ iti strīdhanakalpaḥ ।
03.2.38 varṣāṇyaṣṭāvaprajāyamānāṃ aputrāṃ vandhyāṃ cākāṅkṣeta, daśa ninduṃ, dvādaśa kanyāprasavinīm
03.2.39 tataḥ putrārthī dvitīyāṃ vindeta

03.3.01 dvādaśavarṣā strī prāptavyavahārā bhavati, ṣoḍaśavarṣaḥ pumān
03.3.02 ata ūrdhvaṃ aśuśrūṣāyāṃ dvādaśapaṇaḥ striyā daṇḍaḥ, puṃso dviguṇaḥ iti śuśrūṣā ।
03.3.03 bharmaṇyāyāṃ anirdiṣṭakālāyāṃ grāsācchādanaṃ vā'dhikaṃ yathāpuruṣaparivāpaṃ saviśeṣaṃ dadyāt
03.3.04 nirdiṣṭakālāyāṃ tad eva saṅkhyāya bandhaṃ ca dadyāt
03.3.05 śulkastrīdhanādhivedanikānāṃ anādāne ca
03.3.06 śvaśurakulapraviṣṭāyāṃ vibhaktāyāṃ vā nābhiyojyaḥ patiḥ iti bharma ।
03.3.07 naṣṭe vinaṣṭe nyaṅge apitṛke amātṛke ityanirdeśena vinayagrāhaṇam
03.3.08 veṇudalarajjuhastānāṃ anyatamena vā pṛṣṭhe trirāghātaḥ
03.3.09 tasyātikrame vāgdaṇḍapāruṣyadaṇḍābhyāṃ ardhadaṇḍāḥ
03.3.10 tad eva striyā bhartari prasiddhadoṣāyāḥ
03.3.11 īrṣyayā bāhyavihāreṣu dvāreṣvatyayo yathānirdiṣṭaḥ iti pāruṣyam ।
03.3.12 bhartāraṃ dviṣatī strī saptārtavānyamaṇḍayamānā tadānīṃ eva sthāpyābharaṇaṃ nidhāya bhartāraṃ anyayā saha śayānaṃ anuśayīta
03.3.13 bhikṣuky'nvādhijñātikulānāṃ anyatame vā bhartā dviṣan striyaṃ ekāṃ anuśayīta
03.3.14 dṛṣṭaliṅge maithunāpahāre savarṇāpasarpa upagame vā mithyāvādī dvādaśapaṇaṃ dadyāt
03.3.15 amokṣyā bharturakāmasya dviṣatī bhāryā, bhāryāyāśca bhartā
03.3.16 parasparandveṣān mokṣaḥ
03.3.17 strīviprakārād vā puruṣaścen mokṣaṃ icched yathāgṛhītaṃ asyai dadyāt
03.3.18 puruṣaviprakārād vā strī cen mokṣaṃ icchennāsyai yathāgṛhītaṃ dadyāt
03.3.19 amokṣo dharmavivāhānām iti dveṣaḥ ।
03.3.20 pratiṣiddhā strī darpamadyakrīḍāyāṃ tripaṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt
03.3.21 divā strīprekṣāvihāragamane ṣaṭpaṇo daṇḍaḥ, puruṣaprekṣāvihāragamane dvādaśapaṇaḥ
03.3.22 rātrau dviguṇaḥ
03.3.23 suptamattapravrajane bharturadāne ca dvārasya dvādaśapaṇaḥ

03.3.25 strīpuṃsayormaithunārthenāṅgaviceṣṭāyāṃ raho'ślīlasambhāṣāyāṃ vā caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ striyā daṇḍaḥ, puṃso dviguṇaḥ
03.3.26 keśanīvidantanakhālambaneṣu pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, puṃso dviguṇaḥ
03.3.27 śaṅkitasthāne sambhāṣāyāṃ ca paṇasthāne śiphādaṇḍaḥ
03.3.28 strīṇāṃ grāmamadhye caṇḍālaḥ pakṣāntare pañcaśiphā dadyāt
03.3.29 paṇikaṃ vā prahāraṃ mokṣayet ityatīcāraḥ ।
03.3.30 pratiṣiddhayoḥ strīpuṃsayoranyonya upakāre kṣudrakadravyāṇāṃ dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, sthūlakadravyāṇāṃ caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ, hiraṇyasuvarṇayoścatuṣpañcāśatpaṇaḥ striyā daṇḍaḥ, puṃsordviguṇaḥ
03.3.31 ta evāgamyayorardhadaṇḍāḥ, tathā pratiṣiddhapuruṣavyavahāreṣu ca iti pratiṣedhaḥ ।
