   Chapt .   Leaving home, goi.g away(with a man), Short absence from home, Long absence from home
03.4.01 patikulānniṣpatitāyāḥ striyāḥ ṣaṭpaṇo daṇḍaḥ, anyatra viprakārāt
03.4.02 pratiṣiddhāyāṃ dvādaśapaṇaḥ
03.4.03 prativeśagṛhātigatāyāḥ ṣaṭpaṇaḥ
03.4.04 prātiveśikabhikṣukavaidehakānāṃ avakāśabhikṣāpaṇyadāne dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.4.05 pratiṣiddhānāṃ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.4.06 paragṛhātigatāyāścaturviṃśatipaṇaḥ

03.4.09 pativiprakārāt patijñātisukhāvasthagrāmikānvādhibhikṣukījñātikulānāṃ anyatamaṃ apuruṣaṃ gantuṃ adoṣaḥ iti ācāryāḥ
03.4.10 sa-puruṣaṃ vā jñātikulam
03.4.11 kuto hi sādhvījanasyacchalam
03.4.12 sukhaṃ etad avaboddhuṃ, iti kauṭilyaḥ
03.4.13 pretavyādhivyasanagarbhanimittaṃ apratiṣiddhaṃ eva jñātikulagamanam
03.4.14 tannimittaṃ vārayato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.4.15 tatrāpi gūhamānā strīdhanaṃ jīyeta, jñātayo vā chādayantaḥ śulkaśeṣam iti niṣpatanaṃ ।
03.4.16 patikulānniṣpatya grāmāntaragamane dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ sthāpyā''bharaṇalopaśca
03.4.17 gamyena vā puṃsā saha prasthāne caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ sarvadharmalopaśca, anyatra bharmadānatīrthagamanābhyām
03.4.18 puṃsaḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ tulyaśreyasoḥ, pāpīyaso madhyamaḥ
03.4.19 bandhur'daṇḍyaḥ
03.4.20 pratiṣedhe'rdhadaṇḍāḥ
03.4.21 pathi vyantare gūḍhadeśābhigamane maithunārthena śaṅkitapratiṣiddhāyāṃ vā pathy'nusaraṇe saṅgrahaṇaṃ vidyāt
03.4.22 tālāvacaracāraṇamatsyabandhakalubdhakagopālakaśauṇḍikānāṃ anyeṣāṃ ca prasṛṣṭastrīkāṇāṃ pathy'nusaraṇaṃ adoṣaḥ
03.4.23 pratiṣiddhe vā nayataḥ puṃsaḥ striyo vā gacchantyāḥ ta evārdhadaṇḍāḥ iti pathy'nusaraṇam ।
03.4.24 hrasvapravāsināṃ śūdravaiśyakṣatriyabrāhmaṇānāṃ bhāryāḥ saṃvatsara uttaraṃ kālaṃ ākāṅkṣeran aprajātāḥ, saṃvatsarādhikaṃ prajātāḥ
03.4.25 prativihitā dviguṇaṃ kālam
03.4.26 aprativihitāḥ sukhāvasthā bibhṛyuḥ, paraṃ catvāri varṣāṇyaṣṭau vā jñātayaḥ
03.4.27 tato yathādattaṃ ādāya pramuñceyuḥ
03.4.28 brāhmaṇaṃ adhīyānaṃ daśavarṣāṇyaprajātā, dvādaśa prajātā, rājapuruṣaṃ āyuḥkṣayād ākāṅkṣeta
03.4.29 savarṇataśca prajātā nāpavādaṃ labheta
03.4.30 kuṭumba।ṛddhilope vā sukhāvasthairvimuktā yathā iṣṭaṃ vindeta, jīvitārthaṃ āpadgatā vā
03.4.31 dharmavivāhāt kumārī parigrahītāraṃ anākhyāya proṣitaṃ aśrūyamāṇaṃ sapta tīrthānyākāṅkṣeta, saṃvatsaraṃ śrūyamāṇam
03.4.32 ākhyāya proṣitaṃ aśrūyamāṇaṃ pañca tīrthānyākāṅkṣeta, daśa śrūyamāṇam
03.4.33 ekadeśadattaśulkaṃ trīṇi tīrthānyaśrūyamāṇaṃ, śrūyamāṇaṃ sapta tīrthānyākāṅkṣeta
03.4.34 dattaśulkaṃ pañca tīrthānyaśrūyamāṇaṃ, daśa śrūyamāṇam
03.4.35 tataḥ paraṃ dharmasthairvisṛṣṭā yathā iṣṭaṃ vindeta
03.4.36 tīrtha uparodho hi dharmavadha iti kauṭilyaḥ iti hrasvapravāsaḥ ॥

03.9.11 karṣakagopālakavṛddhāḥ pūrvabhuktikā vā bāhyāḥ setūnāṃ abhijñā bahava eko vā nirdiśya sīmasetūn viparītaveṣāḥ sīmānaṃ nayeyuḥ
03.9.12 uddiṣṭānāṃ setūnāṃ adarśane sahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ ।
03.9.13 tad eva nīte sīmāpahāriṇāṃ setucchidāṃ ca kuryāt
03.9.14 pranaṣṭasetubhogaṃ vā sīmānaṃ rājā yathā upakāraṃ vibhajet iti sīmavivādaḥ ।
03.9.15 kṣetravivādaṃ sāmantagrāmavṛddhāḥ kuryuḥ
03.9.16 teṣāṃ dvaidhībhāve yato bahavaḥ śucayo'numatā vā tato niyaccheyuḥ madhyaṃ vā gṛhṇīyuḥ
03.9.17 tad।ubhayaparā uktaṃ vāstu rājā haret, pranaṣṭasvāmikaṃ ca
03.9.18 yathā upakāraṃ vā vibhajet
03.9.19 prasahyādāne vāstuni steyadaṇḍaḥ
03.9.20 kāraṇādāne prayāsaṃ ājīvaṃ ca parisaṅkhyāya bandhaṃ dadyāt iti kṣetravivādaḥ ।
03.9.21 maryādā'paharaṇe pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.9.22 maryādābhede caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ
03.9.23 tena tapovanavivītamahāpathaśmaśānadevakulayajanapuṇyasthānavivādā vyākhyātāḥ iti maryādāsthāpanam ।
03.9.24 sarva eva vivādāḥ sāmantapratyayāḥ
03.9.25 vivītasthalakedāraṣaṇḍakhalaveśmavāhanakoṣṭhānāṃ pūrvampūrvaṃ ābādhaṃ saheta
03.9.26 brahmasomāraṇyadevayajanapuṇyasthānavarjāḥ sthalapradeśāḥ
03.9.27 ādhāraparivāhakedāra upabhogaiḥ parakṣetrakṛṣṭabījahiṃsāyāṃ yathā upaghātaṃ mūlyaṃ dadyuḥ
03.9.28 kedārārāmasetubandhānāṃ parasparahiṃsāyāṃ hiṃsādviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.9.29 paścānniviṣṭaṃ adharataṭākaṃ na uparitaṭākasya kedāraṃ udakenāplāvayet
03.9.30 upariniviṣṭaṃ nādharataṭākasya pūrāsrāvaṃ vārayed, anyatra trivarṣa uparatakarmaṇaḥ
03.9.31 tasyātikrame pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, taṭākavāmanaṃ ca
03.9.32 pañcavarṣa uparatakarmaṇaḥ setubandhasya svāmyaṃ lupyeta, anyatrāpadbhyaḥ
03.9.33 taṭākasetubandhānāṃ navapravartane pāñcavarṣikaḥ parihāraḥ, bhagna utsṛṣṭānāṃ cāturvarṣikaḥ, samupārūḍhānāṃ traivarṣikaḥ, sthalasya dvaivarṣikaḥ
03.9.34 svātmādhāne vikraye ca
03.9.35 khātaprāvṛttiṃ anadīnibandhāyatanataṭākakedārārāmaṣaṇḍavāpānāṃ sasyavarṇabhāga uttarikaṃ anyebhyo vā yathā upakāraṃ dadyuḥ
03.9.36 prakrayāvakrayādhibhāgabhoganiṣṛṣṭa upabhoktāraśca eṣāṃ pratikuryuḥ
03.9.37 arpatīkāre hīnadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.9.38ab setubhyo muñcataḥ toyaṃ avāre ṣaṭpaṇo damaḥ ।
03.9.38chd vāre vā toyaṃ anyeṣāṃ pramādena uparundhataḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Damage to pastures, fields and roads
03.10.01 karma udakamārgaṃ ucitaṃ rundhataḥ kurvato'nucitaṃ vā pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, setukūpapuṇyasthānacaityadevāyatanāni ca parabhūmau niveśayataḥ
03.10.02 pūrvānuvṛttaṃ dharmasetuṃ ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ vā nayato nāyayato vā madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, śrotṝṇāṃ uttamaḥ, anyatra bhagna utsṛṣṭāt
03.10.03 svāmyabhāve grāmāḥ puṇyaśīlā vā pratikuryuḥ
03.10.04 pathipramāṇaṃ durganiveśe vyākhyātam
03.10.05 kṣudrapaśumanuṣyapathaṃ rundhato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, mahāpaśupathaṃ caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ, hastikṣetrapathaṃ catuṣpañcāśatpaṇaḥ, setuvanapathaṃ ṣaṭśataḥ, śmaśānagrāmapathaṃ dviśataḥ, droṇamukhapathaṃ pañcaśataḥ, sthānīyarāṣṭravivītapathaṃ sāhasraḥ
03.10.06 atikarṣaṇe ca eṣāṃ daṇḍacaturthā daṇḍāḥ
03.10.07 karṣaṇe pūrva uktāḥ
03.10.08 kṣetrikasyākṣipataḥ kṣetraṃ upavāsasya vā tyajato bījakāle dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, anyatra doṣa upanipātāviṣahyebhyaḥ
03.10.09 karadāḥ karadeṣvādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ vā kuryuḥ, brahmadeyikā brahmadeyikeṣu
03.10.10 anyathā pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.10.11 karadasya vā'karadagrāmaṃ praviśataḥ
03.10.12 karadaṃ tu praviśataḥ sarvadravyeṣu prākāmyaṃ syāt, anyatrāgārāt
03.10.13 tad apyasmai dadyāt
03.10.14 anādeyaṃ akṛṣato'nyaḥ pañcavarṣāṇyupabhujya prayāsaniṣkrayeṇa dadyāt
03.10.15 akaradāḥ paratra vasanto bhogaṃ upajīveyuḥ
03.10.16 grāmārthena grāmikaṃ vrajantaṃ upavāsāḥ paryāyeṇānugaccheyuḥ
03.10.17 ananugacchantaḥ paṇārdhapaṇikaṃ yojanaṃ dadyuḥ
03.10.18 grāmikasya grāmād astenapāradārikaṃ nirasyataścaturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ, grāmasya uttamaḥ
03.10.19 nirastasya praveśo hyabhigamena vyākhyātaḥ
03.10.20 stambhaiḥ samantato grāmād dhanuḥśatāpakṛṣṭaṃ upasālaṃ kārayet
03.10.21 paśupracārārthaṃ vivītaṃ ālavanena upajīveyuḥ
03.10.22 vivītaṃ bhakṣayitvā'pasṛtānāṃ uṣṭramahiṣāṇāṃ pādikaṃ rūpaṃ gṛhṇīyuḥ, gavāśvakharāṇāṃ cārdhapādikaṃ, kṣudrapaśūnāṃ ṣoḍaśabhāgikam
03.10.23 bhakṣayitvā niṣaṇṇānāṃ eta eva dviguṇā daṇḍāḥ, parivasatāṃ caturguṇāḥ
03.10.24 grāmadevavṛṣā vā'nirdaśāhā vā dhenurukṣāṇo govṛṣāścādaṇḍyāḥ
03.10.25 sasyabhakṣaṇe sasya upaghātaṃ niṣpattitaḥ parisaṅkhyāya dviguṇaṃ dāpayet
03.10.26 svāminaścānivedya cārayato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, pramuñcataścaturviṃśatipaṇaḥ
03.10.27 pālināṃ ardhadaṇḍāḥ
03.10.28 tad eva ṣaṇḍabhakṣaṇe kuryāt
03.10.29 vāṭabhede dviguṇaḥ veśmakhalavalayagatānāṃ ca dhānyānāṃ bhakṣaṇe
03.10.30 hiṃsāpratīkāraṃ kuryāt
03.10.31 abhayavanamṛgāḥ parigṛhītā vā bhakṣayantaḥ svāmino nivedya yathā'vadhyāḥ tathā pratiṣeddhavyāḥ
03.10.32 paśavo raśmipratodābhyāṃ vārayitavyāḥ
03.10.33 teṣāṃ anyathā hiṃsāyāṃ daṇḍapāruṣyadaṇḍāḥ
03.10.34 prārthayamānā dṛṣṭāparādhā vā sarva upāyairniyantavyāḥ iti kṣetrapathahiṃsā ।
03.10.35 karṣakasya grāmaṃ abhyupetyākurvato grāma evātyayaṃ haret
03.10.36 karmākaraṇe karmavetanadviguṇaṃ, hiraṇyādāne pratyaṃśadviguṇaṃ, bhakṣyapeyādāne ca prahavaṇeṣu dviguṇaṃ aṃśaṃ dadyāt
03.10.37 prekṣāyāṃ anaṃśadaḥ, sa-svajano na prekṣeta
03.10.38 pracchannaśravaṇa īkṣaṇe ca sarvahite ca karmaṇi nigraheṇa dviguṇaṃ aṃśaṃ dadyāt
03.10.39 sarvahitaṃ ekasya bruvataḥ kuryurājñām
03.10.40 akaraṇe dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.10.41 taṃ cet sambhūya vā hanyuḥ pṛthag eṣāṃ aparādhadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.10.42 upahantṛṣu viśiṣṭaḥ
03.10.43 brāhmaṇaśca eṣāṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ niyamyeta
03.10.44 prahavaṇeṣu ca eṣāṃ brāhmaṇā nākāmāḥ kuryuḥ, aṃśaṃ ca labheran
03.10.45 tena deśajātikulasaṅghānāṃ samayasyānapākarma vyākhyātam
03.10.46ab rājā deśahitān setūn kurvatāṃ pathi saṅkramān ।
03.10.46chd grāmaśobhāśca rakṣāśca teṣāṃ priyahitaṃ caret  (iti)
   Chapt .   Non-payment of debts
03.11.01 sapādapaṇā dharmyā māsavṛddhiḥ paṇaśatasya, pañcapaṇā vyāvahārikī, daśapaṇā kāntāragāṇāṃ, viṃśatipaṇā sāmudrāṇām
03.11.02 tataḥ paraṃ kartuḥ kārayituśca pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, śrotṝṇāṃ eka ekaṃ pratyardhadaṇḍaḥ
03.11.03 rājanyayogakṣemāvahe tu dhanikadhāraṇikayoścaritraṃ avekṣeta
03.11.04 dhānyavṛddhiḥ sasyaniṣpattāvupārdhā, paraṃ mūlyakṛtā vardheta
03.11.05 prakṣepavṛddhirudayād ardhaṃ samnidhānasannā vārṣikī deyā
03.11.06 cirapravāsaḥ stambhapraviṣṭo vā mūlyadviguṇaṃ dadyāt
03.11.07 akṛtvā vṛddhiṃ sādhayato vardhayato vā, mūlyaṃ vā vṛddhiṃ āropya śrāvayato bandhacaturguṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.11.08 tucchaśrāvaṇāyāṃ abhūtacaturguṇaḥ
03.11.09 tasya tribhāgaṃ ādātā dadyāt, śeṣaṃ pradātā
03.11.10 dīrghasattravyādhigurukula uparuddhaṃ bālaṃ asāraṃ vā naṛṇaṃ anuvardheta
03.11.11 mucyamānaṃ ṛṇaṃ apratigṛhṇato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.11.12 kāraṇāpadeśena nivṛttavṛddhikaṃ anyatra tiṣṭhet
03.11.13 daśavarṣa upekṣitaṃ ṛṇaṃ apratigrāhyaṃ, anyatra bālavṛddhavyādhitavyasaniproṣitadeśatyāgarājyavibhramebhyaḥ
03.11.14 pretasya putrāḥ kusīdaṃ dadyuḥ, dāyādā vā rikthaharāḥ, sahagrāhiṇaḥ, pratibhuvo vā
03.11.15 na prātibhāvyaṃ anyat
03.11.16 asāraṃ bālaprātibhāvyam
03.11.17 asaṅkhyātadeśakālaṃ tu putrāḥ pautrā dāyādā vā rikthaṃ haramāṇā dadyuḥ
03.11.18 jīvitavivāhabhūmiprātibhāvyaṃ asaṅkhyātadeśakālaṃ tu putrāḥ pautrā vā vaheyuḥ
03.11.19 nānāṛṇasamavāye tu na ekaṃ dvau yugapad abhivadeyātāṃ, anyatra pratiṣṭhamānāt
03.11.20 tatrāpi gṛhītānupūrvyā rājaśrotriyadravyaṃ vā pūrvaṃ pratipādayet
03.11.21 dampatyoḥ pitāputrayoḥ bhrātṝṇāṃ cāvibhaktānāṃ paraspara।kṛtaṃ ṛṇaṃ asādhyam
03.11.22 agrāhyāḥ karmakāleṣu karṣakā rājapuruṣāśca
03.11.23 strī cāpratiśrāviṇī patikṛtaṃ ṛṇaṃ, anyatra gopālakārdhasītikebhyaḥ
03.11.24 patiḥ tu grāhyaḥ strīkṛtaṃ ṛṇaṃ, apratividhāya proṣita iti
03.11.25 sampratipattāvuttamaḥ
03.11.26 asmapratipattau tu sākṣiṇaḥ pramāṇaṃ prātyayikāḥ śucayo'numatā vā trayo'varārdhyāḥ
03.11.27 pakṣānumatau vā dvau, ṛṇaṃ prati na tveva ekaḥ
03.11.28 pratiṣiddhāḥ syālasahāyānvarthidhanikadhāraṇikavairinyaṅgadhṛtadaṇḍāḥ, pūrve cāvyavahāryāḥ
03.11.29 rājaśrotriyagrāmabhṛtakakuṣṭhivraṇinaḥ patitacaṇḍālakutsitakarmāṇo'ndhabadhiramūkāhaṃvādinaḥ strīrājapuruṣāśca, anyatra svavargebhyaḥ
03.11.30 pāruṣyasteyasaṅgrahaṇeṣu tu vairisyālasahāyavarjāḥ
03.11.31 rahasyavyavahāreṣvekā strī puruṣa upaśrotā upadraṣṭā vā sākṣī syād rājatāpasavarjam
03.11.32 svāmino bhṛtyānāṃ ṛtvig।ācāryāḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ mātāpitarau putrāṇāṃ cānigraheṇa sākṣyaṃ kuryuḥ, tesāṃ itare vā
03.11.33 parasparābhiyoge ca eṣāṃ uttamāḥ parā uktā daśabandhaṃ dadyuḥ, avarāḥ pañcabandham iti sākṣy'dhikāraḥ ॥

03.11.34 brāhmaṇa udakumbhāgnisakāśe sākṣiṇaḥ parigṛhṇīyāt
03.11.35 tatra brāhmaṇaṃ brūyāt satyaṃ brūhi iti
03.11.36 rājanyaṃ vaiśyaṃ vā mā tava iṣṭāpūrtaphalaṃ, kapālahastaḥ śatrukulaṃ bhikṣā'rthī gaccheḥ iti
03.11.37 śūdraṃ janmamaraṇāntare yad vaḥ puṇyaphalaṃ tad rājānaṃ gacched, rājñaśca kilbiṣaṃ yuṣmān anyathāvāde, daṇḍaścānubaddhaḥ, paścād api jñāyeta yathādṛṣṭaśrutaṃ, ekamantrāḥ satyaṃ upaharata iti
03.11.38 anupaharatāṃ saptarātrād ūrdhvaṃ dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, tripakṣād ūrdhvaṃ abhiyogaṃ dadyuḥ
03.11.39 sākṣibhede yato bahavaḥ śucayo'numatā vā tato niyaccheyuḥ, madhyaṃ vā gṛhṇīyuḥ
03.11.40 tad vā dravyaṃ rājā haret
03.11.41 sākṣiṇaśced abhiyogād ūnaṃ brūyuratiriktasyābhiyoktā bandhaṃ dadyāt
03.11.42 atiriktaṃ vā brūyuḥ tad'tiriktaṃ rājā haret
03.11.43 bāliśyād abhiyokturvā duhśrutaṃ durlikhitaṃ pretābhiniveśaṃ vā samīkṣya sākṣipratyayaṃ eva syāt
03.11.44 sākṣibāliṣyeṣveva pṛthag'nuyoge deśakālakāryāṇāṃ pūrvamadhyama uttamā daṇḍāḥ ityauśanasāḥ
03.11.45 kūṭasākṣiṇo yaṃ arthaṃ abhūtaṃ kuryurbhūtaṃ vā nāśayeyuḥ tad daśaguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyuḥ iti mānavāḥ
03.11.46 bāliśyād vā visaṃvādayatāṃ citro ghātaḥ iti bārhaspatyāḥ
03.11.47 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
03.11.48 dhruvaṃ hi sākṣibhiḥ śrotavyam
03.11.49 aśṛṇvatāṃ caturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ, tato'rdhaṃ abruvāṇānām
03.11.50ab deśakālāvidūrasthān sākṣiṇaḥ pratipādayet ।
03.11.50chd dūrasthān aprasārān vā svāmivākyena sādhayet  (iti)
   Chapt .   Deposits
03.12.01 upanidhirṛṇena vyākhyātaḥ
03.12.02 paracakrāṭavikābhyāṃ durgarāṣṭravilope vā, pratirodhakairvā grāmasārthavrajavilope, cakrayuktanāśe vā, grāmamadhyāgny।udakābādhe jvālāvega uparuddhe vā, nāvi nimagnāyāṃ muṣitāyāṃ vā svayaṃ uparūḍho na upanidhiṃ abhyāvahet
03.12.03 upanidhibhoktā deśakālānurūpaṃ bhogavetanaṃ dadyāt, dvādaśapaṇaṃ ca daṇḍam
03.12.04 upabhoganimittaṃ naṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ vā'bhyāvahet, caturviṃśatipaṇaśca daṇḍaḥ, anyathā vā niṣpatane
03.12.05 pretaṃ vyasanagataṃ vā na upanidhiṃ abhyāvahet
03.12.06 ādhānavikrayāpavyayaneṣu cāsya caturguṇapañcabandho daṇḍaḥ
03.12.07 parivartane niṣpātane vā mūlyasamaḥ
03.12.08 tenādhipraṇāśa upabhogavikrayādhānāpahārā vyākhyātāḥ
03.12.09 nādhiḥ sa-upakāraḥ sīdet, na cāsya mūlyaṃ vardheta, anyatra nisargāt
03.12.10 nirupakāraḥ sīdet, mūlyaṃ cāsya vardheta
03.12.11 upasthitasyādhiṃ aprayacchato dvādaśaṇpaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.12.12 prayojakāsamnidhāne vā grāmavṛddheṣu sthāpayitvā niṣkrayaṃ ādhiṃ pratipadyeta
03.12.13 nivṛttavṛddhiko vā''dhiḥ tatkālakṛtamūlyaḥ tatra evāvatiṣṭheta, anāśavināśakaraṇādhiṣṭhito vā
03.12.14 dhāraṇikāsamnidhāne vā vināśabhayād udgatārghaṃ dharmasthānujñāto vikrīṇīta, ādhipālapratyayo vā
03.12.15 sthāvaraḥ tu prayāsabhogyaḥ phalabhogyo vā prakṣepavṛddhimūlyaśuddhaṃ ājīvaṃ amūlyakṣayeṇa upanayet
03.12.16 anisṛṣṭa upabhoktā mūlyaśuddhaṃ ājīvaṃ bandhaṃ ca dadyāt
03.12.17 śeṣaṃ upanidhinā vyākhyātam
03.12.18 etenādeśo'nvādhiśca vyākhyātau
03.12.19 sārthenānvādhihasto vā pradiṣṭāṃ bhūmiṃ aprāptaścorairbhagna utsṛṣṭo vā nānvādhiṃ abhyāvahet
03.12.20 antare vā mṛtasya dāyādo'pi nābhyāvahet
03.12.21 śeṣaṃ upanidhinā vyakahyātam
03.12.22 yācitakaṃ avakrītakaṃ vā yathāvidhaṃ gṛhṇīyuḥ tathāvidhaṃ evārpayeyuḥ
03.12.23 bhreṣa upanipātābhyāṃ deśakāla uparodhi dattaṃ naṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ vā nābhyāvaheyuḥ
03.12.24 śeṣaṃ upanidhinā vyākhyātam
03.12.25 vaiyāvṛtyavikrayaḥ tu - vaiyāvṛtyakarā yathādeśakālaṃ vikrīṇānāḥ paṇyaṃ yathājātaṃ mūlyaṃ udayaṃ ca dadyuḥ
03.12.26 deśakālātipātane vā parihīṇaṃ sampradānakālikenārgheṇa mūlyaṃ udayaṃ ca dadyuḥ
03.12.27 yathāsambhāṣitaṃ vā vikrīṇānā na udayaṃ adhigaccheyuḥ, mūlyaṃ eva dadyuḥ
03.12.28 arghapatane vā parihīṇaṃ yathāparihīṇaṃ mūlyaṃ ūnaṃ dadyuḥ
03.12.29 sāṃvyavahārikeṣu vā prātyayikeṣvarājavācyeṣu bhreṣa upanipātābhyāṃ naṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ vā mūlyaṃ api na dadyuḥ
03.12.30 deśakālāntaritānāṃ tu paṇyānāṃ kṣayavyayaviśuddhaṃ mūlyaṃ udayaṃ ca dadyuḥ, paṇyasamavāyānāṃ ca pratyaṃśam
03.12.31 śeṣaṃ upanidhinā vyākhyātam
03.12.32 etena vaiyāvṛtyavikrayo vyākhyātaḥ
03.12.33 nikṣepaśca upanidhinā
03.12.34 taṃ anyena nikṣpitaṃ anyasyārpayato hīyeta
03.12.35 nikṣepāpahāre pūrvāpadānaṃ nikṣeptāraśca pramāṇam
03.12.36 aśucayo hi kāravaḥ
03.12.37 na eṣāṃ karaṇapūrvo nikṣepadharmaḥ
03.12.38 karaṇahīnaṃ nikṣepaṃ apavyayamānaṃ gūḍhabhittinyastān sākṣiṇo nikṣeptā rahasi praṇipātena prajñāpayet, vanānte vā madyaprahavaṇaviśvāsena
03.12.39 rahasi vṛddho vyādhito vā vaidehakaḥ kaścit kṛtalakṣaṇaṃ dravyaṃ asya haste nikṣipyāpagacchet
03.12.40 tasya pratideśena putro bhrātā vā'bhigamya nikṣepaṃ yāceta
03.12.41 dāne śuciḥ, anyathā nikṣepaṃ steyadaṇḍaṃ ca dadyāt
03.12.42 pravrajyā'bhimukho vā śraddheyaḥ kaścit kṛtalakṣaṇaṃ dravyaṃ asya haste nikṣipya pratiṣṭheta
03.12.43 tataḥ kālāntarāgato yāceta
03.12.44 dāne śuciḥ, anyathā nikṣepaṃ steyadaṇḍaṃ ca dadyāt
03.12.45 kṛtalakṣaṇena vā dravyeṇa pratyānayed enam
03.12.46 bāliśajātīyo vā rātrau rājadāyikākṣaṇabhītaḥ sāraṃ asya haste nikṣipyāpagacchet
03.12.47 sa enaṃ bandhanāgāragato yāceta
03.12.48 dāne śuciḥ, anyathā nikṣepaṃ steyadaṇḍaṃ ca dadyāt
03.12.49 abhijñānena cāsya gṛhe janaṃ ubhayaṃ yāceta
03.12.50 anyatartādāne yathā uktaṃ purastāt
03.12.51 dravyabhogānāṃ āgamaṃ cāsyānuyuñjīta, tasya cārthasya vyavahāra upaliṅganaṃ, abhiyoktuścārthasāmarthyam
03.12.52 etena mithaḥsamavāyo vyākhyātaḥ
03.12.53ab tasmāt sākṣimad acchannaṃ kuryāt samyagvibhāṣitam ।
03.12.53chd sve pare vā jane kāryaṃ deśakālāgravarṇataḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Law concerning slaves and labourers
03.13.01 udaradāsavarjaṃ āryaprāṇaṃ aprāptavyavahāraṃ śūdraṃ vikrayādhānaṃ nayataḥ svajanasya dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, vaiśyaṃ dviguṇaḥ, kṣatriyaṃ triguṇaḥ, brāhmaṇaṃ caturguṇaḥ
03.13.02 parajanasya pūrvamadhyama uttamavadhā daṇḍāḥ, kretṛśrotṝṇāṃ ca
03.13.03 mlecchānāṃ adoṣaḥ prajāṃ vikretuṃ ādhātuṃ vā
03.13.04 na tvevāryasya dāsabhāvaḥ
03.13.05 athavā''ryaṃ ādhāya kulabandhana āryāṇāṃ āpadi, niṣkrayaṃ cādhigamya bālaṃ sāhāyyadātāraṃ vā pūrvaṃ niṣkrīṇīran
03.13.06 sakṛd।ātmādhātā niṣpatitaḥ sīdet, dviranyenāhitakaḥ, sakṛd ubhau paraviṣayābhimukhau
03.13.07 vittāpahāriṇo vā dāsasyāryabhāvaṃ apaharato'rdhadaṇḍaḥ
03.13.08 niṣpatitapretavyasanināṃ ādhātā mūlyaṃ bhajeta
03.13.09 pretaviṇmūtra ucchiṣṭagrāhaṇaṃ āhitasya nagnasnāpanaṃ daṇḍapreṣaṇaṃ atikramaṇaṃ ca strīṇāṃ mūlyanāśakaraṃ, dhātrīparicārikārdhasītika upacārikāṇāṃ ca mokṣakaram
03.13.10 siddhaṃ upacārakasyābhiprajātasyāpakramaṇam
03.13.11 dhātrīṃ āhitikāṃ vā'kāmāṃ svavaśāṃ gacchataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, paravaśāṃ madhyamaḥ
03.13.12 kanyāṃ āhitikāṃ vā svayaṃ anyena vā duṣayato mūlyanāśaḥ śulkaṃ taddvuguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ
03.13.13 ātmavikrayiṇaḥ prajāṃ āryāṃ vidyāt
03.13.14 ātmādhigataṃ svāmikarmāviruddhaṃ labheta, pitryaṃ ca dāyam
03.13.15 mūlyena cāryatvaṃ gacchet
03.13.16 tena udaradāsāhitakau vyākhyātau
03.13.17 prakṣepānurūpaścāsya niṣkrayaḥ
03.13.18 daṇḍapraṇītaḥ karmaṇā daṇḍaṃ upanayet
03.13.19 āryaprāṇo dhvajāhṛtaḥ karmakālānurūpeṇa mūlyārdhena vā vimucyeta
03.13.20 gṛhejātadāyāgatalabdhakrītānāṃ anyatamaṃ dāsaṃ ūnāṣṭavarṣaṃ vibandhuṃ akāmaṃ nīce karmaṇi videśe dāsīṃ vā sagarbhāṃ aprativihitagarbhabharmaṇyāṃ vikrayādhānaṃ nayataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, kretṛśrotṝṇāṃ ca
03.13.21 dāsaṃ anurūpeṇa niṣkrayeṇāryaṃ akurvato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, saṃrodhaścākaraṇāt
03.13.22 dāsadravyasya jñātayo dāyādāḥ, teṣāṃ abhāve svāmī
03.13.23 svāminaḥ svasyāṃ dāsyāṃ jātaṃ samātṛkaṃ adāsaṃ vidyāt
03.13.24 gṛhyā cet kuṭumbārthacintanī mātā bhrātā bhaginī cāsyā adāsāḥ syuḥ
03.13.25 dāsaṃ dāsīṃ vā niṣkrīya punarvikrayādhānaṃ nayato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, anyatra svayaṃvādibhyaḥ iti dāsakalpaḥ ।
03.13.26 karmakarasya karmasambandhaṃ āsannā vidyuḥ
03.13.27 yathāsambhāṣitaṃ vetanaṃ labheta, karmakālānurūpaṃ asambhāṣitavetanaḥ
03.13.28 karṣakaḥ sasyānāṃ gopālakaḥ sarpiṣāṃ vaidehakaḥ paṇyānāṃ ātmanā vyavahṛtānāṃ daśabhāgaṃ asambhāṣitavetano labheta
03.13.29 sambhāṣitavetanaḥ tu yathāsambhāṣitam
03.13.30 kāruśilpikuśīlavacikitsakavāgjīvanaparicārakādirāśākārikavargaḥ tu yathā'nyaḥ tadvidhaḥ kuryād yathā vā kuśalāḥ kalpayeyuḥ tathā vetanaṃ labheta
03.13.31 sākṣipratyayaṃ eva syāt
03.13.32 sākṣiṇāṃ abhāve yataḥ karma tato'nuyuñjīta
03.13.33 vetanādāne daśabandho daṇḍaḥ, ṣaṭpaṇo vā
03.13.34 apavyayamāne dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, pañcabandho vā
03.13.35 nadīvegajvālāstenavyāla uparuddhaḥ sarvasvaputradārātmadānenārtaḥ trātāraṃ āhūya niṣtīrṇaḥ kuśalapradiṣṭaṃ vetanaṃ dadyāt
03.13.36 tena sarvatrārtadānānuśayā vyākhyātāḥ
03.13.37ab labheta puṃścalī bhogaṃ saṅgamasya upaliṅganāt ।
03.13.37chd atiyācnā tu jīyeta daurmatyāvinayena vā  (iti)
   Chapt .   Duties of servants
  Undertaking in partnership
03.14.01 gṛhītvā vetanaṃ karmākurvato bhṛtakasya dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, saṃrodhaścākaraṇāt
03.14.02 aśaktaḥ kutsite karmaṇi vyādhau vyasane vā'nuśayaṃ labheta, pareṇa vā kārayitum
03.14.03 tasyavyayakarmaṇā labheta bhartā vā kārayitum
03.14.04 nānyaḥ tvayā kārayitavyo, mayā vā nānyasya kartavyam ityavarodhe bharturakārayato bhṛtakasyākurvato vā dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.14.05 karmaniṣṭhāpane bharturanyatra gṛhītavetano nāsakāmaḥ kuryāt
03.14.06 upasthitaṃ akārayataḥ kṛtaṃ eva vidyād ityācāryāḥ
03.14.07 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
03.14.08 kṛtasya vetanaṃ nākṛtasyāsti
03.14.09 sa ced alpaṃ api kārayitvā na kārayet kṛtaṃ evāsya vidyāt
03.14.10 deśakālātipātanena karmaṇāṃ anyathākaraṇe vā nāsakāmaḥ kṛtaṃ anumanyeta
03.14.11 sambhāṣitād adhikakriyāyāṃ prayāsaṃ na moghaṃ kuryāt
03.14.12 tena saṅghabhṛtā vyākhyātāḥ
03.14.13 teṣāṃ ādhiḥ saptarātraṃ āsīta
03.14.14 tato'nyaṃ upasthāpayet, karmaniṣpākaṃ ca
03.14.15 na cānivedya bhartuḥ saṅghaḥ kañcit parihared upanayed vā
03.14.16 tasyātikrame caturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.14.17 saṅghena parihṛtasyārdhadaṇḍaḥ iti bhṛtakādhikāraḥ ॥

03.14.18 saṅghabhṛtāḥ sambhūyasamutthātāro vā yathāsambhāṣitaṃ vetanaṃ samaṃ vā vibhajeran
03.14.19 karṣaṇavaidehakā vā sasyapaṇyārambhaparyavasānāntare sannasya yathākṛtasya karmaṇaḥ pratyaṃśaṃ dadyuḥ
03.14.20 puruṣa upasthāne samagraṃ aṃśaṃ dadyuḥ
03.14.21 saṃsiddhe tu uddhṛtapaṇye sannasya tadānīṃ eva pratyaṃśaṃ dadyuḥ
03.14.22 sāmānyā hi pathisiddhiścāsiddhiśca
03.14.23 prakrānte tu karmaṇi svasthasyāpakrāmato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.14.24 na ca prākāmyaṃ apakramaṇe
03.14.25 coraṃ tvabhayapūrvaṃ karmaṇaḥ pratyaṃśena grāhayed, dadyāt pratyaṃśaṃ abhayaṃ ca
03.14.26 punaḥsteye pravāsanaṃ, anyatragamane ca
03.14.27 mahā'parādhe tu dūṣyavad ācaret
03.14.28 yājakāḥ svāpracāradravyavarjaṃ yathāsambhāṣitaṃ vetanaṃ samaṃ vā vibhajeran
03.14.29 agniṣṭomādiṣu ca kratuṣu dīkṣaṇād ūrdhvaṃ tṛtīyaṃ aṃśaṃ, madhyama upasada ūrdhvaṃ ardhaṃ aṃśaṃ, sutye prātaḥsavanād ūrdhvaṃ pāda ūnaṃ aṃśam
03.14.30 mādhyandināt savanād ūrdhvaṃ samagraṃ aṃśaṃ labheta
03.14.31 nītā hi dakṣiṇā bhavanti
03.14.32 bṛhaspatisavavarjaṃ pratisavanaṃ hi dakṣiṇā dīyante
03.14.33 tenāhargaṇadakṣiṇā vyākhyātāḥ
03.14.34 sanānāṃ ādaśāhorātrātśeṣabhṛtāḥ karma kuryuḥ, anye vā svapratyayāḥ
03.14.35 karmaṇyasamāpte tu yajamānaḥ sīded, ṛtvijaḥ karma samāpayya dakṣiṇāṃ hareyuḥ
03.14.36 asamāpte tu karmaṇi yājyaṃ yājakaṃ vā tyajataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.14.37ab anāhitāgniḥ śataguruyajvā ca sahasraguḥ ।
03.14.37chd surāpo vṛṣalībhartā brahmahā gurutalpagaḥ
03.14.38ab asatpratigrahe yuktaḥ stenaḥ kutsitayājakaḥ ।
03.14.38chd adoṣaḥ tyaktuṃ anyonyaṃ karmasaṅkaraniścayāt  (iti)
   Chapt .   Rescission of sale and purchase
03.15.01 vikrīya paṇyaṃ aprayacchato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, anyatra doṣa upanipātāviṣahyebhyaḥ
03.15.02 paṇyadoṣo doṣaḥ
03.15.03 rājacorāgny।udakabādha upanipātaḥ
03.15.04 bahuguṇahīnaṃ ārtakṛtaṃ vā'viṣahyam
03.15.05 vaidehakānāṃ ekarātraṃ anuśayaḥ, karṣakāṇāṃ trirātraṃ, gorakṣakāṇāṃ pañcarātram
03.15.06 vyāmiśrāṇāṃ uttamānāṃ ca varṇānāṃ vṛttivikraye saptarātram
03.15.07 ātipātikānāṃ paṇyānāṃ anyatrāvikreyam ityavarodhenānuśayo deyaḥ
03.15.08 tasyātikrame caturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ, paṇyadaśabhāgo vā
03.15.09 krītvā paṇyaṃ apratigṛhṇato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, anyatra doṣa upanipātāviṣahyebhyaḥ
03.15.10 samānaścānuśayo vikreturanuśayena
03.15.11 vivāhānāṃ tu trayāṇāṃ pūrveṣāṃ varṇānāṃ pāṇigrahaṇāt siddhaṃ upāvartanaṃ, śūdrāṇāṃ ca prakarmaṇaḥ
03.15.12 vṛttapāṇigrahaṇayorapi doṣaṃ aupaśāyikaṃ dṛṣṭvā siddhaṃ upāvartanam
03.15.13 na tvevābhiprajātayoḥ
03.15.14 kanyādoṣaṃ aupaśāyikaṃ anākhyāya prayacchataḥ kanyāṃ ṣaṇ~avatirdaṇḍaḥ, śulkastrīdhanapratidānaṃ ca
03.15.15 varayiturvā varadoṣaṃ anākhyāya vindato dviguṇaḥ, śulkastrīdhananāśaśca
03.15.16 dvipadacatuṣpadānāṃ tu kuṇṭhavyādhitāśucīnāṃ utsāhasvāsthyaśucīnāṃ ākhyāne dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.15.17 ātripakṣād iti catuṣpadānāṃ upāvartanaṃ, āsaṃvatsarād iti manuṣyāṇām
03.15.18 tāvatā hi kālena śakyaṃ śaucāśauce jñātum
03.15.19ab dātā pratigrahītā ca syātāṃ na upahatau yathā ।
03.15.19chd dāne kraye vā'nuśayaṃ tathā kuryuḥ sabhāsadaḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Non-conveyance of gifts
  sale without ownership
  Relation of ownership
03.16.01 dattasyāpradānaṃ ṛṇādānena vyākhyātam
03.16.02 dattaṃ avyavahāryaṃ ekatrānuśaye varteta
03.16.03 sarvasvaṃ putradāraṃ ātmānaṃ vā pradāyānuśayinaḥ prayacchet
03.16.04 dharmadānaṃ asādhuṣu karmasu cāupaghātikeṣu vā, arthadānaṃ anupakāriṣvapakāriṣu vā, kāmadānaṃ anarheṣu ca
03.16.05 yathā ca dātā pratigrahītā ca na upahatau syātāṃ tathā'nuśayaṃ kuśalāḥ kalpayeyuḥ
03.16.06 daṇḍabhayād ākrośabhayād anarthabhayād vā bhayadānaṃ pratigṛhṇataḥ steyadaṇḍaḥ, prayacchataśca
03.16.07 roṣadānaṃ parahiṃsāyāṃ, rājñāṃ upari darpadānaṃ ca
03.16.08 tatra uttamo daṇḍaḥ
03.16.09 prātibhāvyaṃ daṇḍaśulkaśeṣaṃ ākṣikaṃ saurikaṃ ca nākāmaḥ putro dāyādo vā rikthaharo dadyāt iti dattasyānapākarma ।
03.16.10 asvāmivikrayaḥ tu - naṣṭāpahṛtaṃ āsādya svāmī dharmasthena grāhayet
03.16.11 deśakālātipattau vā svayaṃ gṛhītvā upaharet
03.16.12 dharmasthaśca svāminaṃ anuyuñjīta kutaḥ te labdham iti
03.16.13 sa ced ācārakramaṃ darśayeta, na vikretāraṃ, tasya dravyasyātisargeṇa mucyeta
03.16.14 vikretā ced dṛśyeta, mūlyaṃ steyadaṇḍaṃ ca dadyāt
03.16.15 sa ced apasāraṃ adhigacched apasared ā'pasārakṣayāt
03.16.16 kṣaye mūlyaṃ steyadaṇḍaṃ ca dadyāt
03.16.17 nāṣṭikaśca svakaraṇaṃ kṛtvā naṣṭapratyāhṛtaṃ labheta
03.16.18 svakaraṇābhāve pañcabandho daṇḍaḥ
03.16.19 tacca dravyaṃ rājadharmyaṃ syāt
03.16.20 naṣṭāpahṛtaṃ anivedya utkarṣataḥ svāminaḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.16.21 śulkasthāne naṣṭāpahṛta utpannaṃ tiṣṭhet
03.16.22 tripakṣād ūrdhvaṃ anabhisāraṃ rājā haret, svāmī vā svakaraṇena
03.16.23 pañcapaṇikaṃ dvipadarūpasya niṣkrayaṃ dadyāt, catuṣpaṇikaṃ ekakhurasya, dvipaṇikaṃ gomahiṣasya, pādikaṃ kṣudrapaśūnām
03.16.24 ratnasāraphalgukupyānāṃ pañcakaṃ śataṃ dadyāt
03.16.25 paracakrāṭavīhṛtaṃ tu pratyānīya rājā yathāsvaṃ prayacchet
03.16.26 corahṛtaṃ avidyamānaṃ svadravyebhyaḥ prayacchet, pratyānetuṃ aśakto vā
03.16.27 svayaṅgrāheṇāhṛtaṃ pratyānīya tanniṣkrayaṃ vā prayacchet
03.16.28 paraviṣayād vā vikrameṇānītaṃ yathāpradiṣṭaṃ rājñā bhuñjīta, anyatrāryaprāṇebhyo devabrāhmaṇatapasvidravyebhyaśca ityasvāmivikrayaḥ ।
03.16.29 svasvāmisambandhaḥ tu - bhogānuvṛttirucchinnadeśānāṃ yathāsvaṃ dravyāṇām
03.16.30 yat svaṃ dravyaṃ anyairbhujyamānaṃ daśa varṣāṇyupekṣeta, hīyetāsya, anyatra bālavṛddhavyādhitavyasaniproṣitadeśatyāgarājyavibhramebhyaḥ
03.16.31 viṃśativarṣa upekṣitaṃ anavasitaṃ vāstu nānuyuñjīta
03.16.32 jñātayaḥ śrotriyāḥ pāṣaṇḍā vā rājñāṃ asaṃnidhau paravāstuṣu vivasanto na bhogena hareyuḥ, upanidhiṃ ādhiṃ nidhiṃ nikṣepaṃ striyaṃ sīmānaṃ rājaśrotriyadravyāṇi ca
03.16.33 āśramiṇaḥ pāṣaṇḍā vā mahatyavakāśe parasparaṃ abādhamānā vaseyuḥ
03.16.34 alpāṃ bādhāṃ saheran
03.16.35 pūrvāgato vā vāsaparyāyaṃ dadyāt
03.16.36 apradātā nirasyeta
03.16.37 vānaprasthayatibrahmacāriṇāṃ ācāryaśiṣyadharmabhrātṛsamānatīrthyā rikthabhājaḥ krameṇa
03.16.38 vivādapadeṣu ca eṣāṃ yāvantaḥ paṇā daṇḍāḥ tāvatī rātrīḥ kṣapaṇābhiṣekāgnikāryamahākacchavardhanāni rājñaścareyuḥ
03.16.39 ahiraṇyasuvarṇāḥ pāṣaḍhāḥ sādhavaḥ
03.16.40 te yathāsvaṃ upavāsavratairārādhayeyuḥ, anyatra pāruṣyasteyasāhasasaṅgrahaṇebhyaḥ
03.16.41 teṣu yathā uktā daṇḍāḥ kāryāḥ
03.16.42ab pravrajyāsu vṛthā''cārān rājā daṇḍena vārayet ।
03.16.42chd dharmo hyadharma upahataḥ śāstāraṃ hantyupekṣitaḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Forcible seizure
03.17.01 sāhasaṃ anvayavat prasabhakarma
03.17.02 niranvaye steyaṃ, apavyayane ca
03.17.03 ratnasāraphalgukupyānāṃ sāhase mūlyasamo daṇḍaḥ iti mānavāḥ
03.17.04 mūlyadviguṇaḥ ityauśanasāḥ
03.17.05 yathā'parādha iti kauṭilyaḥ
03.17.06 puṣpaphalaśākamūlakandapakvānnacarmaveṇumṛdbhāṇḍādīnāṃ kṣudrakadravyāṇāṃ dvādśapaṇāvaraścaturviṃśatipaṇaparo daṇḍaḥ
03.17.07 kālāyasakāṣṭharajjudravyakṣudrapaśupaṭādīnāṃ sthūlakadravyāṇāṃ caturviṃśatipaṇāvaro'ṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇaparo daṇḍaḥ
03.17.08 tāmravṛttakaṃsakācadantabhāṇḍādīnāṃ sthūlakadravyāṇāṃ aṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇāvaraḥ ṣaṇ~avatiparaḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.17.09 mahāpaśumanuṣyakṣetragṛhahiraṇyasuvarṇasūkṣmavastrādīnāṃ sthūlakadravyāṇāṃ dviśatāvaraḥ pañcaśataparo madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.17.10 striyaṃ puruṣaṃ vā'bhiṣahya badhnato bandhayato bandhaṃ vā mokṣayataḥ pañcaśatāvaraḥ sahasrapara uttamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ ityācāryāḥ ॥

03.17.11 yaḥ sāhasaṃ pratipattā iti kārayati sa dviguṇaṃ dadyāt
03.17.12 yāvadd hiraṇyaṃ upayokṣyate tāvad dāsyāmi iti sa caturguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt
03.17.13 yaḥ etāvadd hiraṇyaṃ dāsyāmi iti pramāṇaṃ uddiśya kārayati sa yathā uktaṃ hiraṇyaṃ daṇḍaṃ ca dadyāt iti bārhaspatyāḥ
03.17.14 sa cet kopaṃ madaṃ mohaṃ vā'padiśed yathā uktavad daṇḍaṃ enaṃ kuryād iti kauṭilyaḥ
03.17.15ab daṇḍakarmasu sarveṣu rūpaṃ aṣṭapaṇaṃ śatam ।
03.17.15chd śatāt pareṣu vyājīṃ ca vidyāt pañcapaṇaṃ śatam
03.17.16ab prajānāṃ doṣabāhulyād rājñāṃ vā bhāvadoṣataḥ ।

03.18.03 śobhanākṣimantaḥ iti kāṇakhañjādīnāṃ stutinindāyāṃ dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.18.04 kuṣṭha unmādaklaibyādibhiḥ kutsāyāṃ ca satyamithyāstutinindāsu dvādaśapaṇa uttarā daṇḍāḥ tulyeṣu
03.18.05 viśiṣṭeṣu dviguṇāḥ, hīneṣvardhadaṇḍāḥ, parastrīṣu dviguṇāḥ, pramādamadamohādibhirardhadaṇḍāḥ

03.18.07 prakṛty।upavāde brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrāntāvasāyināṃ apareṇa pūrvasya tripaṇa uttarā daṇḍāḥ, pūrveṇāparasya dvipaṇādharāḥ, kubrāhmaṇādibhiśca kutsāyām
03.18.08 tena śruta upavādo vāgjīvanānāṃ, kārukuśīlavānāṃ vṛtty।upavādaḥ, prājjūṇakagāndhārādīnāṃ ca janapada upavādā vyākhyātāḥ

03.19.09 avagūrṇe niṣkrayaḥ, sparśe'rdhadaṇḍaḥ
03.19.10 tena caṇḍālāśucayo vyākhyātaḥ
03.19.11 hastenāvagūrṇe tripaṇāvaro dvādaśapaṇaparo daṇḍaḥ, pādena dviguṇaḥ, duḥkha utpādanena dravyeṇa pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, prāṇābādhikena madhyamaḥ
03.19.12 kāṣṭhaloṣṭapāṣāṇalohadaṇḍarajjudravyāṇāṃ anyatamena duḥkhaṃ aśoṇitaṃ utpādayataścaturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ, śoṇita utpādane dviguṇaḥ, anyatra duṣṭaśoṇitāt
03.19.13 mṛtakalpaṃ aśoṇitaṃ ghnato hastapādapārañcikaṃ vā kurvataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, pāṇipādadantabhaṅge karṇanāsācchedane vraṇavidāraṇe cca, anyatra duṣṭavraṇebhyaḥ
03.19.14 sakthigrīvābhañjane netrabhedane vā vākyaceṣṭābhojana uparodheṣu ca madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ samutthānavyayaśca
03.19.15 vipattau kaṇṭakaśodhanāya nīyeta
03.19.16 mahājanasya ekaṃ ghnataḥ pratyekaṃ dviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.19.17 paryuṣitaḥ kalaho'nupraveśo vā nābhiyojyaḥ ityācāryāḥ
03.19.18 nāstyapakāriṇo mokṣa iti kauṭilyaḥ
03.19.19 kalahe pūrvāgato jayati, akṣamamāṇo hi pradhāvati ityācāryāḥ
03.19.20 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
03.19.21 pūrvaṃ paścād vā'bhigatasya sākṣiṇaḥ pramāṇaṃ, asākṣike ghātaḥ kalaha upaliṅganaṃ vā
03.19.22 ghātābhiyogaṃ apratibruvataḥ tad ahareva paścātkāraḥ
03.19.23 kalahe dravyaṃ apaharato daśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, kṣudrakadravyahiṃsāyāṃ tacca tāvacca daṇḍaḥ, sthūlakadravyahiṃsāyāṃ tacca dviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ, vastrābharaṇahiraṇyasuvarṇabhāṇḍahiṃsāyāṃ tacca pūrvaśca sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.19.24 parakuḍyaṃ abhighātena kṣobhayataḥ tripaṇo daṇḍaḥ, chedanabhedane ṣaṭpaṇaḥ, pratīkāraśca
03.19.25 duḥkha utpādanaṃ dravyaṃ anyaveśmani prakṣipato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, prāṇābādhikaṃ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.19.26 kṣudrapaśūnāṃ kāṣṭhādibhirduḥkha utpādane paṇo dviguṇo vā daṇḍaḥ, śoṇita utpādane dviguṇaḥ
03.19.27 mahāpaśūnāṃ eteṣveva sthāneṣvdviguṇo daṇḍaḥ samutthānavyayaśca
03.19.28 pura upavanavanaspatīnāṃ puṣpaphalacchāyāvatāṃ prarohacchedane ṣaṭpaṇaḥ, kṣudraśākhācchedane dvādaśapaṇaḥ, pīnaśākhāccchedane caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ, skandhavadhe pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, samucchittau madhyamaḥ

03.20.01 dyūtādhyakṣo dyūtaṃ ekamukhaṃ kārayet
03.20.02 anyatra dīvyato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍo gūḍhājīvijñāpanārtham
03.20.03 dyūtābhiyoge jetuḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, parājitasya madhyamaḥ
03.20.04 bāliśajātīyo hyeṣa jetukāmaḥ parājayaṃ na kṣamate ityācāryāḥ
03.20.05 na itykauṭilyaḥ
03.20.06 parājitaśced dviguṇadaṇḍaḥ kriyeta na kaścana rājānaṃ abhisariṣyati
03.20.07 prāyaśo hi kitavāḥ kūṭadevinaḥ
03.20.08 teṣāṃ adhyakṣāḥ śuddhāḥ kākaṇīrakṣāṃśca sthāpayeyuḥ
03.20.09 kākaṇy'kṣāṇāṃ anya upadhāne dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, kūṭakarmaṇi pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍo jitapratyādānaṃ, upadhau steyadaṇḍaśca
03.20.10 jitadravyād adhyakṣaḥ pañcakaṃ śataṃ ādadīta, kākaṇy'kṣārālāśalākā'vakrayaṃ udakabhūmikarmakrayaṃ ca
03.20.11 dravyāṇāṃ ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ ca kuryāt
03.20.12 akṣabhūmihastadoṣāṇāṃ cāpratiṣedhane dviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.20.13 tena samāhvayo vyākhyātaḥ, anyatra vidyāśilpasamāhvayāt । iti
03.20.14 prakīrṇakaṃ tu - yācitakāvakrītakāhitakanikṣepakāṇāṃ yathādeśakālaṃ adāne, yāmacchāyāsamupaveśasaṃsthitīnāṃ vā deśakālātipātane, gulmataradeyaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ sādhayataḥ, prativeśānuveśayorupari nimantraṇe ca dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.20.15 sandiṣṭaṃ arthaṃ aprayacchato, bhrātṛbhāryāṃ hastena laṅghayato, rūpājīvāṃ anya uparuddhāṃ gacchataḥ, paravaktavyaṃ paṇyaṃ krīṇānasya, samudraṃ gṛhaṃ udbhindataḥ, sāmantacatvāriṃśatkulyābādhāṃ ācarataścāṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ
03.20.16 kulanīvīgrāhakasyāpavyayane, vidhavāṃ chandavāsinīṃ prasahyādhicarataḥ, caṇḍālasyāryāṃ spṛśataḥ, pratyāsannaṃ āpadyanabhidhāvato, niṣkāraṇaṃ abhidhāvanaṃ kurvataḥ, śākyājīvakādīn vṛṣalapravrajitān devapitṛkāryeṣu bhojayataḥ śatyo daṇḍaḥ
03.20.17 śapathavākyānuyogaṃ aniṣṛṣṭaṃ kurvataḥ, yuktakarma cāyuktasya, kṣudrapaśuvṛṣāṇāṃ puṃstva upaghātinaḥ, dāsyā garbhaṃ auṣadhena pātayataśca pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
03.20.18 pitāputrayordampatyorbhrātṛbhaginyormātulabhagineyayoḥ śiṣyācāryayorvā parasparaṃ apatitaṃ tyajataḥ, sārthābhiprayātaṃ grāmamadhye vā tyajataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, kāntāre madhyamaḥ, tannimittaṃ bhreṣayata uttamaḥ, sahaprasthāyiṣvanyeṣvardhadaṇḍāḥ
03.20.19 puruṣaṃ abandhanīyaṃ badhnato bandhayato bandhaṃ vā mokṣayato, bālaṃ aprāptavyavahāraṃ badhnato bandhayato vā sahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ
03.20.20 puruṣāparādhaviśeṣeṇa daṇḍaviśeṣaḥ kāryaḥ
03.20.21 tīrthakaraḥ tapasvī vyādhitaḥ kṣutpipāsā'dhvaklāntaḥ tirojanapado daṇḍakhedī niṣkiñcanaścānugrāhyāḥ
03.20.22 devabrāhmaṇatapasvistrībālavṛddhavyādhitānāṃ anāthānāṃ anabhisaratāṃ dharmasthāḥ kāryāṇi kuryuḥ, na ca deśakālabhogacchalenātihareyuḥ
03.20.23 pūjyā vidyābuddhipauruṣābhijanakarmātiśayataśca puruṣāḥ

04.1.02 arthyapratīkārāḥ kāruśāsitāraḥ saṃnikṣeptāraḥ svavittakāravaḥ śreṇīpramāṇā nikṣepaṃ gṛhṇīyuḥ

04.1.04 nirdiṣṭadeśakālakāryaṃ ca karma kuryuḥ, anirdiṣṭadeśakālaṃ kāryāpadeśam
04.1.05 kālātipātane pādahīnaṃ vetanaṃ taddviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ

04.1.09 vṛddhicchede chedadviguṇo daṇḍaḥ

04.1.11 mānahīne hīnāvahīnaṃ vetanaṃ taddviguṇaśca daṇḍaḥ, tulāhīne hīnacaturguṇo daṇḍaḥ, sūtraparivartane mūlyadviguṇaḥ

04.1.16 mudgarāṅkād anyad vāsaḥ paridadhānāḥ tripaṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyuḥ
04.1.17 paravastravikrayāvakrayādhāneṣu ca dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, parivartane mūlyadviguṇo vastradānaṃ ca
04.1.18 mukulāvadātaṃ śilāpaṭṭaśuddhaṃ dhautasūtravarṇaṃ pramṛṣṭaśvetaṃ ca ekarātra uttaraṃ dadyuḥ
04.1.19 pañcarātrikaṃ tanurāgaṃ, ṣaḍrātrikaṃ nīlaṃ, puṣpalākṣāmañjiṣṭhāraktaṃ guruparikarma yatna upacāryaṃ jātyaṃ vāsaḥ saptarātrikam
04.1.20 tataḥ paraṃ vetanahāniṃ prāpnuyuḥ
04.1.21 śraddheyā rāgavivādeṣu vetanaṃ kuśalāḥ kalpayeyuḥ
04.1.22 parārdhyānāṃ paṇo vetanaṃ, madhyamānāṃ ardhapaṇaḥ, pratyavarāṇāṃ pādaḥ, sthūlakānāṃ māṣakadvimāṣakaṃ, dviguṇaṃ raktakānām
04.1.23 prathamanejane caturbhāgaḥ kṣayaḥ, dvitīye pañcabhāgaḥ
04.1.24 tena uttaraṃ vyākhyātam
04.1.25 rajakaiḥ tunnavāyā vyākhyātāḥ
04.1.26 suvarṇakārāṇāṃ aśucihastād rūpyaṃ suvarṇaṃ anākhyāya sarūpaṃ krīṇatāṃ dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, virūpaṃ caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ, corahastād aṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇaḥ
04.1.27 pracchannavirūpamūlyahīnakrayeṣu steyadaṇḍaḥ, kṛtabhāṇḍa upadhau ca

04.1.29 tena uttaraṃ vyākhyātam

04.1.31 tayorapacaraṇe rāgasyāpahāraṃ vidyāt

04.2.01 saṃsthā'dhyakṣaḥ paṇyasaṃsthāyāṃ purāṇabhāṇḍānāṃ svakaraṇaviśuddhānāṃ ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ vā sthāpayet
04.2.02 tulāmānabhāṇḍāni cāvekṣeta pautavāpacārāt
04.2.03 parimāṇīdroṇayorardhapalahīnātiriktaṃ adoṣaḥ
04.2.04 palahīnātirikte dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
04.2.05 tena pala uttarā daṇḍavṛddhirvyākhyātā
04.2.06 tulāyāḥ karṣahīnātiriktaṃ adoṣaḥ
04.2.07 dvikarṣahīnātirikte ṣaṭpaṇo daṇḍaḥ
04.2.08 tena karṣa uttarā daṇḍavṛddhirvyākhyātā

04.2.11 tena karṣa uttarā daṇḍavṛddhirvyākhyātā

04.2.13 tulāmānābhyāṃ atiriktābhyāṃ krītvā hīnābhyāṃ vikrīṇānasya ta eva dviguṇā daṇḍāḥ
04.2.14 gaṇyapaṇyeṣvaṣṭabhāgaṃ paṇyamūlyeṣvapaharataḥ ṣaṇ~avatirdaṇḍaḥ
04.2.15 kāṣṭhalohamaṇimayaṃ rajjucarmamṛṇmayaṃ sūtravalkaromamayaṃ vā jātyaṃ ityajātyaṃ vikrayādhānaṃ nayato mūlyāṣṭaguṇo daṇḍaḥ
04.2.16 sārabhāṇḍaṃ ityasārabhāṇḍaṃ tajjātaṃ ityatajjātaṃ rādhāyuktaṃ ityupadhiyuktaṃ samudgaparivartimaṃ vā vikrayādhānaṃ nayato hīnamūlyaṃ catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ, paṇamūlyaṃ dviguṇo, dvipaṇamūlyaṃ dviśataḥ
04.2.17 tenārghavṛddhau daṇḍavṛddhirvyākhyātā
04.2.18 kāruśilpināṃ karmaguṇāpakarṣaṃ ājīvaṃ vikrayakraya upaghātaṃ vā sambhūya samutthāpayatāṃ sahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ
04.2.19 vaidehakānāṃ vā sambhūya paṇyaṃ avarundhatāṃ anargheṇa vikrīṇatāṃ vā sahasraṃ daṇḍaḥ
04.2.20 tulāmānāntaraṃ arghavarṇāntaraṃ vā - dharakasya māyakasya vā paṇamūlyād aṣṭabhāgaṃ hastadoṣeṇācarato dviśato daṇḍaḥ
04.2.21 tena dviśata uttarā daṇḍavṛddhirvyākhyātā
04.2.22 dhānyasnehakṣāralavaṇagandhabhaiṣajyadravyāṇāṃ samavarṇa upadhāne dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ
04.2.23 yanniṣṛṣṭaṃ upajīveyuḥ tad eṣāṃ divasasañjātaṃ saṅkhyāya vaṇik sthāpayet
04.2.24 kretṛvikretrorantarapatitaṃ ādāyād anyad bhavati
04.2.25 tena dhānyapaṇyanicayāṃścānujñātāḥ kuryuḥ
04.2.26 anyathānicitaṃ eṣāṃ paṇyādhyakṣo gṛhṇīyāt
04.2.27 tena dhānyapaṇyavikraye vyavaharetānugraheṇa prajānām
04.2.28 anujñātakrayād upari ca eṣāṃ svadeśīyānāṃ paṇyānāṃ pañcakaṃ śataṃ ājīvaṃ sthāpayet, paradeśīyānāṃ daśakam
04.2.29 tataḥ paraṃ arghaṃ vardhayatāṃ kraye vikraye vā bhāvayatāṃ paṇaśate pañcapaṇād dviśato daṇḍaḥ
04.2.30 tenārghavṛddhau daṇḍavṛddhirvyākhyātā
04.2.31 sambhūyakraye ca eṣāṃ avikrīte nānyaṃ sambhūyakrayaṃ dadyāt
04.2.32 paṇya upaghāte ca eṣāṃ anugrahaṃ kuryāt

04.2.34 teṣvavikrīteṣu nānye vikrīṇīran

04.3.23 snuhikṣīraliptāni dhānyāni visṛjed, upaniṣadyogayuktāni vā

04.4.01 samāhartṛpraṇidhau janapadarakṣaṇaṃ uktam

04.4.03 samāhartā janapade siddhatāpasapravrajitacakracaracāraṇakuhakapracchandakakārtāntikanaimittikamauhūrtikacikitsaka unmattamūkabadhirajaḍāndhavaidehakakāruśilpikuśīlavaveśaśauṇḍikāpūpikapākvamāṃsikāudanikavyañjanān praṇidadhyāt
04.4.04 te grāmāṇāṃ adhyakṣāṇāṃ ca śaucāśaucaṃ vidyuḥ
04.4.05 yaṃ cātra gūḍhājīvinaṃ śaṅketa taṃ sattriṇā'pasarpayet
04.4.06 dharmasthaṃ viśvāsa upagataṃ sattrī brūyāt - asau me bandhurabhiyuktaḥ, tasyāyaṃ anarthaḥ pratikriyatāṃ, ayaṃ cārthaḥ pratigṛhyatām iti
04.4.07 sa cet tathā kuryād upadāgrāhaka iti pravāsyeta
04.4.08 tena pradeṣṭāro vyākhyātāḥ
04.4.09 grāmakūṭaṃ adhyakṣaṃ vā sattrī brūyāt - asau jālmaḥ prabhūtadravyaḥ, tasyāyaṃ anarthaḥ, tena enaṃ āhārayasva iti
04.4.10 sa cet tathā kuryād utkocaka iti pravāsyeta
04.4.11 kṛtakābhiyukto vā kūṭasākṣiṇo'bhijñātānarthavaipulyenārabheta
04.4.12 te cet tathā kuryuḥ kūṭasākṣiṇa iti pravāsyeran
04.4.13 tena kūṭaśrāvaṇakārakā vyākhyātāḥ
04.4.14 yaṃ vā mantrayogamūlakarmabhiḥ śmāśānikairvā saṃvadanakarakaṃ manyeta taṃ sattrī brūyāt - amuṣya bhāryāṃ snuṣāṃ duhitaraṃ vā kāmaye, sā māṃ pratikāmayatāṃ, ayaṃ cārthaḥ pratigṛhyatām iti
04.4.15 sa cet tathā kuryāt saṃvadanakāraka iti pravāsyeta
04.4.16 tena kṛtyābhicāraśīlau vyākhyātau
04.4.17 yaṃ vā rasasya kartāraṃ kretāraṃ vikretāraṃ bhaiṣajyāhāravyavahāriṇaṃ vā rasadaṃ manyeta taṃ sattrī brūyāt - asau me śatruḥ, tasya upaghātaḥ kriyatāṃ, ayaṃ cārthaḥ pratigṛhyatām iti
04.4.18 sa cet tathā kuryād rasada iti pravāsyeta
04.4.19 tena madanayogavyavahārī vyākhyātaḥ
04.4.20 yaṃ vā nānālohakṣārāṇāṃ aṅgārabhasmāsandaṃśamuṣṭikādhikaraṇībimba।ṭaṅkamūṣāṇāṃ abhīkṣṇakretāraṃ maṣībhasmadhūmadigdhahastavastraliṅgaṃ karmāra upakaraṇasaṃsargaṃ kūṭarūpakārakaṃ manyeta taṃ sattrī śiṣyatvena saṃvyavahāreṇa cānupraviśya prajñāpayet
04.4.21 prajñātaḥ kūṭarūpakāraka iti pravāsyeta
04.4.22 tena rāgasyāpahartā kūṭasuvarṇavyavahārī ca vyākhyātaḥ

04.5.01 sattriprayogād ūrdhvaṃ siddhavyañjanā māṇavān māṇavavidyābhiḥ pralobhayeyuḥ, prasvāpanāntardhānadvārāpohamantreṇa pratirodhakān, saṃvadanamantreṇa pāratalpikān
04.5.02 teṣāṃ kṛta utsāhānāṃ mahāntaṃ saṅghaṃ ādāya rātrāvanyaṃ grāmaṃ uddiśyānyaṃ grāmaṃ kṛtakastrīpuruṣaṃ gatvā brūyuḥ - iha eva vidyāprabhāvo dṛśyatāṃ, kṛcchraḥ paragrāmo gantum iti
04.5.03 tato dvārāpohamantreṇa dvārāṇyapohya praviśyatām iti brūyuḥ

04.6.03 rūpābhigrahaḥ tu - naṣṭāpahṛtaṃ avidyamānaṃ tajjātavyavahāriṣu nivedayet
04.6.04 taccenniveditaṃ āsādya pracchādayeyuḥ sācivyakaradoṣaṃ āpnuyuḥ
04.6.05 ajānanto'sya dravyasyātisargeṇa mucyeran
04.6.06 na cānivedya saṃsthā'dhyakṣasya purāṇabhāṇḍānāṃ ādhānaṃ vikrayaṃ vā kuryuḥ
04.6.07 taccenniveditaṃ āsādyeta, rūpābhigṛhītaṃ āgamaṃ pṛcchet kutaḥ te labdham iti
04.6.08 sa cet brūyāt dāyādyād avāptaṃ, amuṣmāllabdhaṃ krītaṃ kāritaṃ ādhipracchannaṃ, ayaṃ asya deśaḥ kālaśca upasamprāpteḥ, ayaṃ asyārghaḥ pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ mūlyaṃ ca iti, tasyāgamasamādhau mucyeta
04.6.09 nāṣṭikaścet tad eva pratisandadhyāt, yasyā pūrvo dīrghaśca paribhogaḥ śucirvā deśaḥ tasya dravyaṃ iti vidyāt
04.6.10 catuṣpadadvipadānāṃ api hi rūpaliṅgasāmānyaṃ bhavati, kiṃ aṅga punarekayonidravyakartṛprasūtānāṃ kupyābharaṇabhāṇḍānāṃ iti
04.6.11 sa ced brūyāt yācitakaṃ avakrītakaṃ āhitakaṃ nikṣepaṃ upanidhiṃ vaiyāvṛtyakarma vā'muṣya iti, tasyāpasārapratisandhānena mucyeta
04.6.12 na evam ityapasāro vā brūyāt, rūpābhigṛhītaḥ parasya dānakāraṇaṃ ātmanaḥ pratigrahakāraṇaṃ upaliṅganaṃ vā dāyakadāpakanibandhakapratigrāhaka upadraṣṭṛbhirupaśrotṛbhirvā pratisamānayet
04.6.13 ujjhitapranaṣṭaniṣpatita upalabdhasya deśakālalābha upaliṅganena śuddhiḥ
04.6.14 aśuddhaḥ tacca tāvacca daṇḍaṃ dadyāt
04.6.15 anyathā steyadaṇḍaṃ bhajeta iti rūpābhigrahaḥ ।
04.6.16 karmābhigrahaḥ tu - muṣitaveśmanaḥ praveśaniṣkasanaṃ advāreṇa, dvārasya sandhinā bījena vā vedhaṃ, uttamāgārasya jālavātāyananīpravedhaṃ, ārohaṇāvataraṇe ca kuḍyasya vedhaṃ, upakhananaṃ vā gūḍhadravyanikṣepaṇagrahaṇa upāyaṃ, upadeśa upalabhyaṃ abhyantaraccheda utkaraparimarda upakaraṇaṃ abhyantarakṛtaṃ vidyāt
04.6.17 viparyaye bāhyakṛtaṃ, ubhayata ubhayakṛtam
04.6.18a abhyantarakṛte puruṣaṃ āsannaṃ vyasaninaṃ krūrasahāyaṃ taskara upakaraṇasaṃsargaṃ, striyaṃ vā daridrakulāṃ anyaprasaktāṃ vā,
04.6.18b paricārakajanaṃ vā tadvidhācāraṃ, atisvapnaṃ, nidrāklāntaṃ, āvignaṃ । śuṣkabhinnasvaramukhavarṇaṃ, anavasthitaṃ,
04.6.18ch atipralāpinaṃ, uccārohaṇasaṃrabdhagātraṃ, vilūnanighṛṣṭabhinnapāṭitaśarīravastraṃ, jātakiṇasaṃrabdhahastapādaṃ,
04.6.18d pāṃsupūrṇakeśanakhaṃ vilūnabhugnakeśanakhaṃ vā, samyaksnātānuliptaṃ tailapramṛṣṭagātraṃ sadyodautahastapādaṃ vā,
04.6.18e pāṃsupicchileṣu tulyapādapadanikṣepaṃ, praveśaniṣkasanayorvā tulyamālyamadyagandhavastracchedavilepanasvedaṃ parīkṣeta
04.6.19 coraṃ pāradārikaṃ vā vidyāt
04.6.20ab sagopasthāniko bāhyaṃ pradeṣṭā coramārgaṇam ।
04.6.20chd kuryānnāgarikaścāntardurge nirdiṣṭahetubhiḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   In quest of sudden deaths
04.7.01 tailābhyaktaṃ āśumṛtakaṃ parīkṣeta
04.7.02 niṣkīrṇamūtrapurīṣaṃ vātapūrṇakoṣṭhatvakkaṃ śūnapādapāṇimān mīlitākṣaṃ savyañjanakaṇṭhaṃ pīṭananiruddha ucchvāsahataṃ vidyāt
04.7.03 taṃ eva saṅkucitabāhusakthiṃ udbandhahataṃ vidyāt
04.7.04 śūnapāṇipāda udaraṃ apagatākṣaṃ udvṛttanābhiṃ avaropitaṃ vidyāt
04.7.05 nistabdhagudākṣaṃ sandaṣṭajihvaṃ ādhmāta udaraṃ udakahataṃ vidyāt
04.7.06 śoṇitānusiktaṃ bhagnabhinnagātraṃ kāṣṭhairaśmabhirvā hataṃ vidyāt
04.7.07 sambhagnasphuṭitagātraṃ avakṣiptaṃ vidyāt
04.7.08 śyāvapāṇipādadantanakhaṃ śithilamāṃsaromacarmāṇaṃ phena upadigdhamukhaṃ viṣahataṃ vidyāt
04.7.09 taṃ eva sa-śoṇitadaṃśaṃ sarpakīṭahataṃ vidyāt ।
04.7.10 vikṣiptavastragātraṃ ativantaviriktaṃ madanayogahataṃ vidyāt
04.7.11 ato'nyatamena kāraṇena hataṃ hatvā vā daṇḍabhayād udbaddhanikṛttakaṇṭhaṃ vidyāt
04.7.12 viṣahatasya bhojanaśeṣaṃ vayobhiḥ parīkṣeta
04.7.13 hṛdayād uddhṛtyāgnau prakṣiptaṃ ciṭiciṭāyad।indradhanurvarṇaṃ vā viṣayuktaṃ vidyāt, dagdhasya hṛdayaṃ adagdhaṃ dṛṣṭvā vā
04.7.14 tasya paricārakajanaṃ vāgdaṇḍapāruṣyātilabdhaṃ mārgeta, duḥkha upahataṃ anyaprasaktaṃ vā strījanaṃ, dāyavṛttistrījanābhimantāraṃ vā bandhum
04.7.15 tad eva hata udbaddhasya parīkṣeta
04.7.16 svayaṃ udbaddhasya vā viprakāraṃ ayuktaṃ mārgeta
04.7.17 sarveṣāṃ vā strīdāyādyadoṣaḥ karmaspardhā pratipakṣadveṣaḥ paṇyasaṃsthāsamavāyo vā vivādapadānāṃ anyatamad vā roṣasthānam
04.7.18 roṣanimitto ghātaḥ
04.7.19 svayaṃ।ādiṣṭapuruṣairvā, corairarthanimittaṃ, sādṛśyād anyavairibhirvā hatasya ghātaṃ āsannebhyaḥ parīkṣeta
04.7.20 yenāhūtaḥ saha sthitaḥ prasthito hatabhūmiṃ ānīto vā taṃ anuyuñjīta
04.7.21 ye cāsya hatabhūmāvāsannacarāḥ tān eka ekaśaḥ pṛcchet kenāyaṃ ihānīto hato vā, kaḥ saśastraḥ saṅgūhamāna udvigno vā yuṣmābhirdṛṣṭaḥ iti
04.7.22 te yathā brūyuḥ tathā'nuyuñjīta
04.7.23ab anāthasya śarīrasthaṃ upabhogaṃ paricchadam ।
04.7.23chd vastraṃ veṣaṃ vibhūṣāṃ vā dṛṣṭvā tadvyavahāriṇaḥ
04.7.24ab anuyuñjīta saṃyogaṃ nivāsaṃ vāsakāraṇam ।
04.7.24chd karma ca vyavahāraṃ ca tato mārgaṇaṃ ācaret
04.7.25ab rajjuśastraviṣairvā'pi kāmakrodhavaśena yaḥ ।
04.7.25chd ghātayet svayaṃ ātmānaṃ strī vā pāpena mohitā
04.7.26ab rajjunā rājamārge tāṃścaṇḍālenāpakarṣayet ।
04.7.26chd na śmaśānavidhiḥ teṣāṃ na sambandhikriyāḥ tathā
04.7.27ab bandhuḥ teṣāṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt pretakāryakriyāvidhim ।
04.7.27chd tadgatiṃ sa caret paścāt svajanād vā pramucyate
04.7.28ab saṃvatsareṇa patati patitena samācaran ।

   Chapt .   Investigation througH interrogation and througH torture
04.8.01 muṣitasaṃnidhau bāhyānāṃ abhyantarāṇāṃ ca sākṣiṇāṃ abhiśastasya deśajātigotranāmakarmasārasahāyanivāsān anuyuñjīta
04.8.02 tāṃścāpadeśaiḥ pratisamānayet
04.8.03 tataḥ pūrvasyāhnaḥ pracāraṃ rātrau nivāsaṃ ca grahaṇād ityanuyuñjīta
04.8.04 tasyāpasārapratisandhāne śuddhaḥ syāt, anyathā karmaprāptaḥ
04.8.05 trirātrād ūrdhvaṃ agrāhyaḥ śaṅkitakaḥ pṛcchā'bhāvād anyatra upakaraṇadarśanāt
04.8.06 acoraṃ cora ityabhivyāharataścorasamo daṇḍaḥ, coraṃ pracchādayataśca
04.8.07 coreṇābhiśasto vairadveṣābhyāṃ apadiṣṭakaḥ śuddhaḥ syāt
04.8.08 śuddhaṃ parivāsayataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
04.8.09 śaṅkāniṣpannaṃ upakaraṇamantrisahāyarūpavaiyāvṛtyakarānniṣpādayet
04.8.10 karmaṇaśca pradeśadravyādānāṃśavibhāgaiḥ pratisamānayet
04.8.11 eteṣāṃ kāraṇānāṃ anabhisandhāne vipralapantaṃ acoraṃ vidyāt
04.8.12 dṛśyate hyacoro'pi coramārge yadṛcchayā saṃnipāte coraveṣaśastrabhāṇḍasāmānyena gṛhyamāṇaścorabhāṇḍasya upavāsena vā, yathā'ṇimāṇḍavyaḥ karmakleśabhayād acoraḥ coro'smi iti bruvāṇaḥ
04.8.13 tasmāt samāptakaraṇaṃ niyamayet
04.8.14 mandāparādhaṃ bālaṃ vṛddhaṃ vyādhitaṃ mattaṃ unmattaṃ kṣutpipāsā'dhvaklāntaṃ atyāśitaṃ āmakāśitaṃ durbalaṃ vā na karma kārayet
04.8.15 tulya śīlapuṃścalīprāpāvikakathā'vakāśabhojanadātṛbhirapasarpayet
04.8.16 evaṃ atisandadhyāt, yathā vā nikṣepāpahāre vyākhyātam
04.8.17 āptadoṣaṃ karma kārayet, na tveva striyaṃ garbhiṇīṃ sūtikāṃ vā māsāvaraprajātām
04.8.18 striyāḥ tvardhakarma, vākyānuyogo vā
04.8.19 brāhmaṇasya sattriparigrahaḥ śrutavataḥ tapasvinaśca
04.8.20 tasyātikrama uttamo daṇḍaḥ kartuḥ kārayituśca, karmaṇā vyāpādanena ca
04.8.21 vyāvahārikaṃ karmacatuṣkaṃ - ṣaḍ daṇḍāḥ, sapta kaśāḥ, dvāvuparinibandhau, udakanālikā ca
04.8.22 paraṃ pāpakarmaṇāṃ nava vetralatāḥ, dvādaśa kaśāḥ, dvāvūruveṣṭau, viṃśatirnaktamālalatāḥ, dvātriṃśattalāḥ, dvau vṛścikabandhau, ullambane ca dve, sūcī hastasya, yavāgūpītasya ekaparvadahanaṃ aṅgulyāḥ, snehapītasya pratāpanaṃ ekaṃ ahaḥ, śiśirarātrau balbajāgraśayyā ca
04.8.23 ityaṣṭādaśakaṃ karma
04.8.24 tasya upakaraṇaṃ pramāṇaṃ praharaṇaṃ pradharaṇaṃ avadhāraṇaṃ ca kharapaṭṭād āgamayet
04.8.25 divasāntaraṃ eka ekaṃ ca karma kārayet
04.8.26 pūrvakṛtāpadānaṃ pratijñāyāpaharantaṃ ekadeśadṛṣṭadravyaṃ karmaṇā rūpeṇa vā gṛhītaṃ rājakośaṃ avastṛṇantaṃ karmavadhyaṃ vā rājavacanāt samastaṃ vyastaṃ abhyastaṃ vā karma kārayet
04.8.27 sarvāparādheṣvapīḍanīyo brāhmaṇaḥ
04.8.28 tasyābhiśastāṅko lalāṭe syād vyavahārapatanāya, steyo śvā, manuṣyavadhe kabandhaḥ, gurutalpe bhagaṃ, surāpāne madyadhvajaḥ
04.8.29ab brāhmaṇaṃ pāpakarmāṇaṃ udghuṣyāṅkakṛtavraṇam ।
04.8.29chd kuryānnirviṣayaṃ rājā vāsayed ākareṣu vā  (iti)
   Chapt .   keeping a watch over officers of all departments
04.9.01 samāhartṛpradeṣṭāraḥ pūrvaṃ adhyakṣāṇāṃ adhyakṣapuruṣāṇāṃ ca niyamanaṃ kuryuḥ
04.9.02 khanisārakarmāntebhyaḥ sāraṃ ratnaṃ vā'paharataḥ śuddhavadhaḥ
04.9.03 phalgudravyakarmāntebhyaḥ phalgu dravyaṃ upaskaraṃ vā pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
04.9.04 paṇyabhūmibhyo vā rājapaṇyaṃ māṣamūlyād ūrdhvaṃ āpādamūlyād ityapaharato dvādaśapaṇo daṇḍaḥ, ādvipādamūlyād iti caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ, ātripādamūlyād iti ṣaṭtriṃśatpaṇaḥ, āpaṇamūlyād ityaṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇaḥ, ādvipaṇamūlyād iti pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, ācatuṣpaṇamūlyād iti madhyamaḥ, ā'ṣṭapaṇamūlyād ityuttamaḥ, ādaśapaṇamūlyād iti vadhaḥ
04.9.05 koṣṭhapaṇyakupyāyudhāgārebhyaḥ kupyabhāṇḍa upaskarāpahāreṣvardhamūlyeṣu eta eva daṇḍāḥ
04.9.06 kośabhāṇḍāgārākṣaśālābhyaścaturbhāgamūlyeṣu eta eva dviguṇā daṇḍāḥ
04.9.07 corāṇāṃ abhipradharṣaṇe citro ghātaḥ
04.9.08 iti rājaparigraheṣu vyākhyātam
04.9.09 bāhyeṣu tu - pracchannaṃ ahani kṣetrakhalaveśmāpaṇebhyaḥ kupyabhāṇḍaṃ upaskaraṃ vā māṣamūlyād ūrdhvaṃ āpādamūlyād ityapaharataḥ tripaṇo daṇḍaḥ, gomayapradehena vā pralipyāvaghoṣaṇam ādvipādamūlyād iti ṣaṭpaṇaḥ, gomayabhasmanā vā pralipyāvaghoṣaṇaṃ, ātripādamūlyād iti navapaṇaḥ, gomayabhasmanā vā pralipyāvaghoṣaṇaṃ, śarāvamekhalayā vā।āpaṇamūlyād iti dvādaśapaṇaḥ, muṇḍanaṃ pravrājanaṃ vā।ādvipaṇamūlyād iti caturviṃśatipaṇaḥ, muṇḍasya iṣṭakāśakalena pravrājanaṃ vā।ācatuṣpaṇamūlyād iti ṣaṭtriṃśatpaṇaḥ āpañcapaṇamūlyād ityaṣṭacatvāriṃśatpaṇaḥ, ādaśapaṇamūlyād iti pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ āviṃśatipaṇamūlyād it dviśataḥ ātriṃśatpaṇamūlyād iti pañcaśataḥ ācatvāriṃśatpaṇamūlyād iti sāhasraḥ āpañcāśatpaṇamūlyād iti vadhaḥ
04.9.10 prasahya divā rātrau vā''ntaryāmikaṃ apaharato'rdhamūlyeṣu eta eva daṇḍāḥ
04.9.11 prasahya divā rātrau vā sa-śastrasyāpaharataścaturbhāgamūlyeṣu eta eva dviguṇā daṇḍāḥ
04.9.12 kuṭumbikādhyakṣamukhyasvāmināṃ kūṭaśāsanamudrākarmasu pūrvamadhya uttamavadhā daṇḍāḥ, yathā'parādhaṃ vā
04.9.13 dharmasthaśced vivadamānaṃ puruṣaṃ tarjayati bhartsayatyapasārayatyabhigrasate vā pūrvaṃ asmai sāhasadaṇḍaṃ kuryāt, vākpāruṣye dviguṇam
04.9.14 pṛcchyaṃ na pṛcchati, apṛcchyaṃ pṛcchati, pṛṣṭvā vā visṛjati, śikṣayati, smārayati, pūrvaṃ dadāti vā, iti madhyamaṃ asmai sāhasadaṇḍaṃ kuryāt
04.9.15 deyaṃ deśaṃ na pṛcchati, adeyaṃ deśaṃ pṛcchati, kāryaṃ adeśenātivāhayati, chalenātiharati, kālaharaṇena śrāntaṃ apavāhayati, mārgāpannaṃ vākyaṃ utkramayati, matisāhāyyaṃ sākṣibhyo dadāti, tāritānuśiṣṭaṃ kāryaṃ punarapi gṛhṇāti, uttamaṃ asmai sāhasadaṇḍaṃ kuryāt
04.9.16 punar'parādhe dviguṇaṃ sthānād vyavaropaṇaṃ ca
04.9.17 lekhakaśced uktaṃ na likhati, anuktaṃ likhati, duruktaṃ upalikhati, sūktaṃ ullikhati, artha utpattiṃ vā vikalpayati, iti pūrvaṃ asmai sāhasadaṇḍaṃ kuryād, yathā'parādhaṃ vā
04.9.18 dharmasthaḥ pradeṣṭā vā hairaṇyadaṇḍaṃ adaṇḍye kṣipati kṣepadviguṇaṃ asmai daṇḍaṃ kuryāt, hīnātiriktāṣṭaguṇaṃ vā
04.9.19 śarīradaṇḍaṃ kṣipati śārīraṃ eva daṇḍaṃ bhajeta, niṣkrayadviguṇaṃ vā
04.9.20 yaṃ vā bhūtaṃ arthaṃ nāśayati abhūtaṃ arthaṃ karoti tad'ṣṭaguṇaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt
04.9.21 dharmasthīye cārake bandhanāgāre vā śayyā''sanabhojana uccārasañcārarodhabandhaneṣu tripaṇa uttarā daṇḍāḥ kartuḥ kārayituśca
04.9.22 cārakād abhiyuktaṃ muñcato niṣpātayato vā madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, abhiyogadānaṃ ca, bandhanāgārāt sarvasvaṃ vadhaśca
04.9.23 bandhanāgārādhyakṣasya saṃruddhakaṃ anākhyāya cārayataścaturviṃśatipaṇo daṇḍaḥ, karma kārayato dviguṇaḥ, sthānānyatvaṃ gamayato'nnapānaṃ vā rundhataḥ ṣaṇ~avatirdaṇḍaḥ, parikleśayata utkoṭayato vā madhyamaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, ghnataḥ sāhasraḥ
04.9.24 parigṛhītāṃ dāsīṃ āhitikāṃ vā saṃruddhikāṃ adhicarataḥ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ, coraḍa़āmarikabhāryāṃ madhyamaḥ, saṃruddhikāṃ āryāṃ uttamaḥ
04.9.25 saṃruddhasya vā tatra eva ghātaḥ
04.9.26 tad evākṣaṇagṛhītāyāṃ āryāyāṃ vidyāt, dāsyāṃ pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
04.9.27 cārakaṃ abhittvā niṣpātayato madhyamaḥ, bhittvā vadhaḥ, bandhanāgārāt sarvasvaṃ vadhaśca
04.9.28ab evaṃ arthacarān pūrvaṃ rājā daṇḍena śodhayet ।
04.9.28chd śodhayeyuśca śuddhāḥ te paurajānapadān damaiḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Redemption from the cutting of individual limbs
04.10.01 tīrthaghātagranthibheda ūrdhvakarāṇāṃ prathame'parādhe sandeśacchedanaṃ catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo vā daṇḍaḥ, dvitīye chedanaṃ paṇasya śatyo vā daṇḍaḥ, tṛtīye dakṣiṇahastavadhaścatuḥśato vā daṇḍaḥ, caturthe yathākāmī vadhaḥ
04.10.02 pañcaviṃśatipaṇāvareṣu kukkuṭanakulamārjāraśvasūkarasteyeṣu hiṃsāyāṃ vā catuṣpañcāśatpaṇo daṇḍaḥ, nāsāgracchedanaṃ vācaṇḍālāraṇyacarāṇāṃ ardhadaṇḍāḥ
04.10.03 pāśajālakūṭāvapāteṣu baddhānāṃ mṛgapaśupakṣivyālamatsyānāṃ ādāne tacca tāvacca daṇḍaḥ
04.10.04 mṛgadravyavanān mṛgadravyāpahāre śātyo daṇḍaḥ
04.10.05 bimbavihāramṛgapakṣisteye hiṃsāyāṃ vā dviguṇo daṇḍaḥ
04.10.06 kāruśilpikuśīlavatapasvināṃ kṣudrakadravyāpahāre śatyo daṇḍaḥ, sthūlakadravyāpahāre dviśataḥ, kṛṣidravyāpahāre ca
04.10.07 durgaṃ akṛtapraveśasya praviśataḥ prākāracchidrād vā nikṣepaṃ gṛhītvā'pasarataḥ kāṇḍarāvadho, dviśāto vā daṇḍaḥ
04.10.08 cakrayuktaṃ nāvaṃ kṣudrapaśuṃ vā'paharata ekapādavadhaḥ, triśato vā daṇḍaḥ
04.10.09 kūṭakākaṇy'kṣārālāśalākāhastaviṣamakāriṇa ekahastavadhaḥ, catuḥśato vā daṇḍaḥ
04.10.10 stenapāradārikayoḥ sācivyakarmaṇi striyāḥ saṅgṛhītāyāśca karṇanāsācchedanaṃ, pañcaśato vā daṇḍaḥ, puṃṣo dviguṇaḥ
04.10.11 mahāpaśuṃ ekaṃ dāsaṃ dāsīṃ vā'paharataḥ pretabhāṇḍaṃ vā vikrīṇānasya dvipādavadhaḥ, ṣaṭchato vā daṇḍaḥ
04.10.12 varṇa uttamānāṃ gurūṇāṃ ca hastapādalaṅghane rājayānavāhanādy।ārohaṇe ca ekahastapādavadhaḥ, saptaśato vā daṇḍaḥ
04.10.13 śūdrasya brāhmaṇavādino devadravyaṃ avastṛṇato rājadviṣṭaṃ ādiśato dvinetrabhedinaśca yogāñjanenāndhatvaṃ, aṣṭaśato vā daṇḍaḥ
04.10.14 coraṃ pāradārikaṃ vā mokṣayato rājaśāsanaṃ ūnaṃ atiriktaṃ vā likhataḥ kanyāṃ dāsīṃ vā sa-hiraṇyaṃ aparahataḥ kūṭavyavahāriṇo vimāṃsavikrayiṇaśca vāmahastadvipādavadho, navaśato vā daṇḍaḥ
04.10.15 mānuṣamāṃsavikraye vadhaḥ

05.1.01 durgarāṣṭrayoḥ kaṇṭakaśodhanaṃ uktam

05.1.03 rājānaṃ avagṛhya upajīvinaḥ śatrusādhāraṇā vā ye mukhyāḥ teṣu gūḍhapuruṣapraṇidhiḥ kṛtyapakṣa upagraho vā siddhiḥ yathā uktaṃ purastād, upajāpo'pasarpo vā yathā pāragrāmike vakṣyāmaḥ
05.1.04 rājya upaghātinaḥ tu vallabhāḥ saṃhatā vā ye mukhyāḥ prakāśaṃ aśakyāḥ pratiṣeddhuṃ dūṣyāḥ teṣu dharmarucirupāṃśudaṇḍaṃ prayuñjīta
05.1.05 dūṣyamahāmātrabhrātaraṃ asatkṛtaṃ sattrī protsāhya rājānaṃ darśayet
05.1.06 taṃ rājā dūṣyadravya upabhogātisargeṇa dūṣye vikramayet
05.1.07 śastreṇa rasena vā vikrāntaṃ tatra eva ghātayed bhrātṛghātako'yam iti
05.1.08 tena pāraśavaḥ paricārikāputraśca vyākhyātau
05.1.09 dūṣyaṃmahāmātraṃ vā sattriprotsāhito bhrātā dāyaṃ yāceta
05.1.10 taṃ dūṣyagṛhapratidvāri rātrāvupaśayānaṃ anyatra vā vasantaṃ tīkṣṇo hantā brūyād hato'yaṃ dāyakāmukaḥ iti
05.1.11 tato hatapakṣaṃ upagṛhya itaraṃ nigṛhṇīyāt
05.1.12 dūṣyasamīpasthā vā sattriṇo bhrātaraṃ dāyaṃ yācamānaṃ ghātena paribhartsayeyuḥ
05.1.13 taṃ rātrau iti samānam
05.1.14 dūṣyamahāmātrayorvā yaḥ putraḥ pituḥ pitā vā putrasya dārān adhicarati, bhrātā vā bhrātuḥ, tayoḥ kāpaṭikamukhaḥ kalahaḥ pūrveṇa vyākhyātaḥ
05.1.15 dūṣyamahāmātraputraṃ ātmasambhāvitaṃ vā sattrī rājaputraḥ tvaṃ, śatrubhayād iha nyasto'si ityupajapet
05.1.16 pratipannaṃ rājā rahasi pūjayet prāptayauvarājyakālaṃ tvāṃ mahāmātrabhayānnābhiṣiñcāmi iti
05.1.17 taṃ sattrī mahāmātravadhe yojayet
05.1.18 vikrāntaṃ tatra eva ghātayet pitṛghātako'yam iti
05.1.19 bhikṣukī vā dūṣyabhāryāṃ sāṃvadanikībhirauṣadhībhiḥ saṃvāsya rasenātisandadhyāt
05.1.20 ityāpyaprayogaḥ
05.1.21 dūṣyamahāmātraṃ aṭavīṃ paragrāmaṃ vā hantuṃ kāntāravyavahite vā deśe rāṣṭrapālaṃ antapālaṃ vā sthāpayituṃ nāgarasthānaṃ vā kupitaṃ avagrāhituṃ sārthātivāhyaṃ pratyante vā sa-pratyādeyaṃ ādātuṃ phalgubalaṃ tīkṣṇayuktaṃ preṣayet
05.1.22 rātrau divā vā yuddhe pravṛtte tīkṣṇāḥ pratirodhakavyañjanā vā hanyuḥ abhiyoge hataḥ iti
05.1.23 yātrāvihāragato vā dūṣyamahāmātrān darśanāyāhvayet
05.1.24 te gūḍhaśastraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ saha praviṣṭā madhyamakakṣyāyāṃ ātmavicayaṃ antaḥpraveśanārthaṃ dadyuḥ
05.1.25 tato dauvārikābhigṛhītāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ dūṣyaprayuktāḥ sma iti brūyuḥ
05.1.26 te tad'bhivikhyāpya dūṣyān hanyuḥ
05.1.27 tīkṣṇasthāne cānye vadhyāḥ
05.1.28 bahirvihāragato vā dūṣyān āsannāvāsān pūjayet
05.1.29 teṣāṃ devīvyañjanā vā duḥstrī rātrāvāvāseṣu gṛhyeta iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
05.1.30 dūṣyamahāmātraṃ vā sūdo bhakṣakāro vā te śobhanaḥ iti stavena bhakṣyabhojyaṃ yāceta, bahirvā kvacid adhvagataḥ pānīyam
05.1.31 tad।ubhayaṃ rasena yojayitvā pratisvādane tāveva upayojayet
05.1.32 tad'bhivikhyāpya rasadau iti ghātayet
05.1.33 abhicāraśīlaṃ vā siddhavyañjano godhākūrmakarkaṭakakūṭānāṃ lakṣaṇyānāṃ anyatamaprāśanena manorathān avāpsyasi iti grāhayet

05.1.37 ityupaniṣatpratiṣedhaḥ
05.1.38 ubhayadūṣyapratiṣedhaḥ tu
05.1.39 yatra dūṣyaḥ pratiṣeddhavyaḥ tatra dūṣyaṃ eva phalgubalatīkṣṇayuktaṃ preṣayet, gaccha, amuṣmin durge rāṣṭre vā sainyaṃ utthāpaya hiraṇyaṃ vā, vallabhād vā hiraṇyaṃ āhāraya, vallabhakanyāṃ vā prasahyānaya, durgasetuvaṇikpathaśūnyaniveśakhanidravyahastivanakarmaṇāṃ anyatamad vā kāraya rāṣṭrapālyaṃ antapālyaṃ vāyaśca tvā pratiṣedhayenna vā te sāhāyyaṃ dadyāt sa bandhavyaḥ syāt iti
05.1.40 tathaiva itareṣāṃ preṣayed amuṣyāvinayaḥ pratiṣeddhavyaḥ iti
05.1.41 taṃ eteṣu kalahasthāneṣu karmapratighāteṣu vā vivadamānaṃ tīkṣṇāḥ śastraṃ pātayitvā pracchannaṃ hanyuḥ
05.1.42 tena doṣeṇa itare niyantavyāḥ
05.1.43 purāṇāṃ grāmāṇāṃ kulānāṃ vā dūṣyāṇāṃ sīmākṣetrakhalaveśmamaryādāsu dravya upakaraṇasasyavāhanahiṃsāsu prekṣākṛtya utsaveṣu vā samutpanne kalahe tīkṣṇairutpādite vā tīkṣṇāḥ śastraṃ pātayitvā brūyuḥ evaṃ kriyante ye'munā kalahāyante: iti
05.1.44 tena doṣeṇa itare niyantavyāḥ
05.1.45 yeṣāṃ vā dūṣyāṇāṃ jātamūlāḥ kalahāḥ teṣāṃ kṣetrakhalaveśmānyādīpayitvā bandhusambandhiṣu vāhaneṣu vā tīkṣṇāḥ śastraṃ pātayitvā tathaiva brūyuḥ amunā prayuktāḥ smaḥ iti
04.4.46 tena doṣeṇa itare niyantavyāḥ
05.1.47 durgarāṣṭradūṣyān vā sattriṇaḥ parasparasyāveśanikān kārayeyuḥ
05.1.48 tatra rasadā rasaṃ dadyuḥ
05.1.49 tena doṣeṇa itare niyantavyāḥ
05.1.50 bhikṣukī vā dūṣyarāṣṭramukhyaṃ dūṣyarāṣṭramukhyasya bhāryā snuṣā duhitā vā kāmayate ityupajapet
05.1.51 pratipannasyābharaṇaṃ ādāya svāmine darśayet asau te mukhyo yauvana utsikto bhāryāṃ snuṣāṃ duhitaraṃ vā'bhimanyate iti
05.1.52 tayoḥ kalaho rātrau iti samānam
05.1.53 dūṣyadaṇḍa upanateṣu tu - yuvarājaḥ senāpatirvā kiñcid apakṛtyāpakrānto vikrameta
05.1.54 tato rājā dūṣyadaṇḍa upanatān eva preṣayet phalgubalatīkṣṇayuktān iti samānāḥ sarva eva yogāḥ
05.1.55 teṣāṃ ca putreṣvanukṣiyatsu yo nirvikāraḥ sa pitṛdāyaṃ labheta
05.1.56 evaṃ asya putrapautrān anuvartate rājyaṃ apāstapuruṣadoṣam
05.1.57ab svapakṣe parapakṣe vā tūṣṇīṃ daṇḍaṃ prayojayet ।
05.1.57chd āyatyāṃ ca tadātve ca kṣamāvān aviśaṅkitaḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Replenishment of the treasury
05.2.01 kośaṃ akośaḥ pratyutpannārthakṛcchraḥ saṅgṛhṇīyāt
05.2.02 janapadaṃ mahāntaṃ alpapramāṇaṃ vā'devamātṛkaṃ prabhūtadhānyaṃ dhānyasyāṃśaṃ tṛtīyaṃ caturthaṃ vā yāceta, yathāsāraṃ madhyaṃ avaraṃ vā
05.2.03 durgasetukarmavaṇikpathaśūnyaniveśakhanidravyahastivanakarma upakāriṇaṃ pratyantaṃ alpapramāṇaṃ vā na yāceta
05.2.04 dhānyapaśuhiraṇyādi niviśamānāya dadyāt
05.2.05 caturthaṃ aṃśaṃ dhānyānāṃ bījabhaktaśuddhaṃ ca hiraṇyena krīṇīyāt
05.2.06 araṇyajātaṃ śrotriyasvaṃ ca pariharet
05.2.07 tad apyanugraheṇa krīṇīyāt
05.2.08 tasyākaraṇe vā samāhartṛpuruṣā grīṣme karṣakāṇāṃ udvāpaṃ kārayeyuḥ
05.2.09 pramādāvaskannasyātyayaṃ dviguṇaṃ udāharanto bījakāle bījalekhyaṃ kuryuḥ
05.2.10 niṣpanne haritapakvādānaṃ vārayeyuḥ, anyatra śākakaṭabhaṅgamuṣṭibhyāṃ devapitṛpūjādānārthaṃ gavārthaṃ vā
05.2.11 bhikṣukagrāmabhṛtakārthaṃ ca rāśimūlaṃ parihareyuḥ
05.2.12 svasasyāpahāriṇaḥ pratipāto'ṣṭaguṇaḥ
05.2.13 parasasyāpahāriṇaḥ pañcāśadguṇaḥ sītā'tyayaḥ, svavargasya, bāhyasya tu vadhaḥ
05.2.14 caturthaṃ aṃśaṃ dhānyānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ vanyānāṃ tūlalākṣākṣaumavalkakārpāsaraumakauśeyakauṣadhagandhapuṣpaphalaśākapaṇyānāṃ kāṣṭhaveṇumāṃsavallūrāṇāṃ ca gṛhṇīyuḥ, dantājinasyārdham
05.2.15 tad anisṛṣṭaṃ vikrīṇānasya pūrvaḥ sāhasadaṇḍaḥ
05.2.16 iti karṣakeṣu praṇayaḥ
05.2.17 suvarṇarajatavajramaṇimuktāpravālāśvahastipaṇyāḥ pañcāśatkarāḥ
05.2.18 sūtravastratāmravṛttakaṃsagandhabhaiṣajyaśīdhupaṇyāścatvāriṃśatkarāḥ
05.2.19 dhānyarasalohapaṇyāḥ śakaṭavyavahāriṇaśca triṃśatkarāḥ
05.2.20 kācavyavahāriṇo mahākāravaśca viṃśatikarāḥ
05.2.21 kṣudrakāravo bandhakīpoṣakāśca daśakarāḥ
05.2.22 kāṣṭhaveṇupāṣāṇamṛdbhāṇḍapakvānnaharitapaṇyāḥ pañcakarāḥ
05.2.23 kuśīlavā rūpājīvāśca vetanārdhaṃ dadyuḥ
05.2.24 hiraṇyakaraṃ karmaṇyān āhārayeyuḥ, na ca eṣāṃ kañcid aparādhaṃ parihareyuḥ
05.2.25 te hyaparigṛhītaṃ abhinīya vikrīṇīran
05.2.26 iti vyavahāriṣu praṇayaḥ
05.2.27 kukkuṭasūkaraṃ ardhaṃ dadyāt, kṣudrapaśavaḥ ṣaḍbhāgaṃ, gomahiṣāśvatarakhara uṣṭrāśca daśabhāgam
05.2.28 bandhakīpoṣakā rājapreṣyābhiḥ paramarūpayauvanābhiḥ kośaṃ saṃhareyuḥ
05.2.29 iti yonipoṣakeṣu praṇayaḥ
05.2.30 sakṛd eva na dviḥ prayojyaḥ
05.2.31 tasyākaraṇe vā samāhartā kāryaṃ apadiśya paurajānapadān bhikṣeta
05.2.32 yogapuruṣāścātra pūrvaṃ atimātraṃ dadyuḥ
05.2.33 etena pradeśena rājā paurajānapadān bhikṣeta
05.2.34 kāpaṭikāśca enān alpaṃ prayacchataḥ kutsayeyuḥ
05.2.35 sārato vā hiraṇyaṃ āḍhyān yāceta, yathā upakāraṃ vā, svavaśā vā yad upahareyuḥ
05.2.36 sthānacchatraveṣṭanavibhūṣāśca eṣāṃ hiraṇyena prayacchet
05.2.37 pāṣaṇḍasaṅghadravyaṃ aśrotriya upabhogyaṃ devadravyaṃ vā kṛtyakarāḥ pretasya dagdhagṛhasya vā haste nyastaṃ ityupahareyuḥ
05.2.38 devatā'dhyakṣo durgarāṣṭradevatānāṃ yathāsvaṃ ekasthaṃ kośaṃ kuryāt, tathaiva ca upaharet
05.2.39 daivatacaityaṃ siddhapuṇyasthānaṃ aupapādikaṃ vā rātrāvutthāpya yātrāsamājābhyāṃ ājīvet
05.2.40 caitya upavanavṛkṣeṇa vā devatā'bhigamanaṃ anārtavapuṣpaphalayuktena khyāpayet
05.2.41 manuṣyakaraṃ vā vṛkṣe rakṣobhayaṃ prarūpayitvā siddhavyañjanāḥ paurajānapadānāṃ hiraṇyena pratikuryuḥ
05.2.42 suruṅgāyukte vā kūpe nāgaṃ aniyataśiraskaṃ hiraṇya upahāreṇa darśayet
05.2.43 nāgapratimāyāṃ antaśchannāyāṃ caityacchidre valmīkacchidre vā sarpadarśanaṃ āhāreṇa pratibaddhasaṃjñaṃ kṛtvā śraddadhānānāṃ darśayet
05.2.44 aśraddadhānānāṃ ācamanaprokṣaṇeṣu rasaṃ upacārya devatā'bhiśāpaṃ brūyāt, abhityaktaṃ vā daṃśayitvā
05.2.45 yogadarśanapratīkāreṇa vā kośābhisaṃharaṇaṃ kuryāt
05.2.46 vaidehakavyañjano vā prabhūtapaṇyāntevāsī vyavahareta
05.2.47 sa yadā paṇyamūlye nikṣepaprayogairupacitaḥ syāt tadā enaṃ rātrau moṣayet
05.2.48 etena rūpadarśakaḥ suvarṇakāraśca vyākhyātau
05.2.49 vaidehakavyañjano vā prakhyātavyavahāraḥ prahavaṇanimittaṃ yācitakaṃ avakrītakaṃ vā rūpyasuvarṇabhāṇḍaṃ anekaṃ gṛhṇīyāt
05.2.50 samāje vā sarvapaṇyasandohena prabhūtaṃ hiraṇyasuvarṇaṃ ṛṇaṃ gṛhṇīyāt, pratibhāṇḍamūlyaṃ ca
05.2.51 tad ubhayaṃ rātrau moṣayet
05.2.52 sādhvīvyañjanābhiḥ strībhirdūṣyān unmādayitvā tāsāṃ eva veśmasvabhigṛhya sarvasvānyāhareyuḥ
05.2.53 dūṣyakulyānāṃ vā vivāde pratyutpanne rasadāḥ praṇihitā rasaṃ dadyuḥ
05.2.54 tena doṣeṇa itare paryādātavyāḥ
05.2.55 dūṣyaṃ abhityakto vā śraddheyāpadeśaṃ paṇyaṃ hiraṇyanikṣepaṃ ṛṇaprayogaṃ dāyaṃ vā yāceta
05.2.56 dāsaśabdena vā dūṣyaṃ ālambeta, bhāryāṃ asya snuṣāṃ duhitaraṃ vā dāsīśabdena bhāryāśabdena vā
05.2.57 taṃ dūṣyagṛhapratidvāri rātrāvupaśayānaṃ anyatra vā vasantaṃ tīkṣṇo hatvā brūyāt hato'yaṃ arthakāmukaḥ iti
05.2.58 tena doṣeṇa itare paryādātavyāḥ
05.2.59 siddhavyañjano vā dūṣyaṃ jambhakavidyābhiḥ pralobhayitvā brūyāt akṣayahiraṇyaṃ rājadvārikaṃ strīhṛdayaṃ arivyādhikaraṃ āyuṣyaṃ putrīyaṃ vā karma jānāmi iti
05.2.60 pratipannaṃ caityasthāne rātrau prabhūtasurāmāṃsagandhaṃ upahāraṃ kārayet
05.2.61 ekarūpaṃ cātra hiraṇyaṃ pūrvanikhātaṃ pretāṅgaṃ pretaśiśurvā yatra nihitaḥ syāt, tato hiraṇyaṃ asya darśayed atyalpam iti ca brūyāt
05.2.62 prabhūtahiraṇyahetoḥ punarupahāraḥ kartavya iti svayaṃ eva etena hiraṇyena śvobhūte prabhūtaṃ aupahārikaṃ krīṇīhi iti
05.2.63 sa tena hiraṇyenāupahārikakraye gṛhyeta
05.2.64 mātṛvyañjanayā vā putro me tvayā hataḥ ityavakupitā syāt
05.2.65 saṃsiddhaṃ evāsya rātriyāge vanayāge vanakrīḍāyāṃ vā pravṛttāyāṃ tīkṣṇā viśasyābhityaktaṃ atinayeyuḥ
05.2.66 dūṣyasya vā bhṛtakavyañjano vetanahiraṇye kūṭarūpaṃ prakṣipya prarūpayet
05.2.67 karmakaravyañjano vā gṛhe karma kurvāṇaḥ stenakūṭarūpakāraka upakaraṇaṃ upanidadhyāt, cikitsakavyañjano vā garaṃ agadāpadeśena
05.2.68 pratyāsanno vā dūṣyasya sattrī praṇihitaṃ abhiṣekabhāṇḍaṃ amitraśāsanaṃ ca kāpaṭikamukhenācakṣīta, kāraṇaṃ ca brūyāt
05.2.69 evaṃ dūṣyeṣvadhārmikeṣu ca varteta, na itareṣu
05.2.70ab pakvaṃ pakvaṃ ivārāmāt phalaṃ rājyād avāpnuyāt ।

05.3.03 ṛtvig।ācāryamantripurohitasenāpatiyuvarājarājamātṛrājamahiṣyo'ṣṭacatvāriṃśatsāhasrāḥ

05.3.17 catuṣpadadvipadaparicārakapārikarmikāupasthāyikapālakaviṣṭibandhakāḥ ṣaṣṭivetanāḥ, āryayuktārohakamāṇavakaśailakhanakāḥ sarva upasthāyinaśca
05.3.18 ācāryā vidyāvantaśca pūjāvetanāni yathā'rhaṃ labheran pañcaśatāvaraṃ sahasraparam
05.3.19 daśapaṇiko yojane dūto madhyamaḥ, daśa uttare dviguṇavetana āyojanaśatād iti
05.3.20 samānavidyebhyaḥ triguṇavetano rājā rājasūyādiṣu kratuṣu

05.3.22 kāpaṭika udāsthitagṛhapatikavaidehakatāpasavyañjanāḥ sāhasrāḥ
05.3.23 grāmabhṛtakasattritīkṣṇarasadabhikṣukyaḥ pañcaśatāḥ
05.3.24 cārasañcāriṇo'rdhatṛtīyaśatāḥ, prayāsavṛddhavetanā vā

05.3.27 nityamukhyāḥ syuranekamukhyāśca

05.3.30 pretavyādhitasūtikākṛtyeṣu ca eṣāṃ arthamānakarma kuryāt
05.3.31 alpakośaḥ kupyapaśukṣetrāṇi dadyāt, alpaṃ ca hiraṇyam
05.3.32 śūnyaṃ vā niveśayituṃ abhyutthito hiraṇyaṃ eva dadyāt, na grāmaṃ grāmasañjātavyavahārasthāpanārtham
05.3.33 etena bhṛtānāṃ abhṛtānāṃ ca vidyākarmabhyāṃ bhaktavetanaviśeṣaṃ ca kuryāt
05.3.34 ṣaṣṭivetanasyāḍhakaṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyānurūpaṃ bhaktaṃ kuryāt
05.3.35 patty'śvarathadvipāḥ sūrya udaye bahiḥ sandhidivasavarjaṃ śilpayogyāḥ kuryuḥ
05.3.36 teṣu rājā nityayuktaḥ syāt, abhīkṣṇaṃ ca eṣāṃ śilpadarśanaṃ kuryāt
05.3.37 kṛtanara indrāṅkaṃ śastrāvaraṇaṃ āyudhāgāraṃ praveśayet
05.3.38 aśastrāścareyuḥ, anyatra mudrā'nujñātāt
05.3.39 naṣṭaṃvinaṣṭaṃ vā dviguṇaṃ dadyāt
05.3.40 vidhvastagaṇanāṃ ca kuryāt

05.3.42 yātrāṃ abhyutthito vā senāṃ udyojayet
05.3.43 tato vaidehakavyañjanāḥ sarvapaṇyānyāyudhīyebhyo yātrākāle dviguṇapratyādeyāni dadyuḥ

05.3.45 evaṃ avekṣitāyavyayaḥ kośadaṇḍavyasanaṃ nāvāpnoti

05.3.47chd daṇḍavṛddhāśca jānīyuḥ śaucāśaucaṃ atandritāḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   Proper conduct fora dependant
05.4.01 lokayātrāvid rājānaṃ ātmadravyaprakṛtisampannaṃ priyahitadvāreṇāśrayeta
05.4.02 yaṃ vā manyeta yathā'haṃ āśraya īpsurevaṃ asau vinaya īpsurābhigāmikaguṇayuktaḥ iti, dravyaprakṛtihīnaṃ apyenaṃ āśrayeta, na tvevānātmasampannam
05.4.03 anātmavā hi nītiśāstradveṣād anarthyasaṃyogād vā prāpyāpi mahad aiśvaryaṃ na bhavati
05.4.04 ātmavati labdhāvakāśaḥ śāstrānuyogaṃ dadyāt
05.4.05 avisaṃvādādd hi sthānasthairyaṃ avāpnoti
05.4.06 matikarmasu pṛṣṭhaḥ tadātve cāyatyāṃ ca dharmārthasaṃyuktaṃ samarthaṃ pravīṇavad apariṣadbhīruḥ kathayet
05.4.07 īpsitaḥ paṇeta dharmārthānuyogaṃ aviśiṣṭeṣu balavatsaṃyukteṣu daṇḍadhāraṇaṃ matsaṃyoge tadātve ca daṇḍadhāraṇaṃ iti na kuryāḥ, pakṣaṃ vṛttiṃ guhyaṃ ca me na upahanyāḥ, saṃjñayā ca tvāṃ kāmakrodhadaṇḍaneṣu vārayeyam iti
05.4.08 ādiṣṭaḥ pradiṣṭāyāṃ bhūmāvanujñātaḥ praviśet, upaviśecca pārśvataḥ saṃnikṛṣṭaviprakṛṣṭaḥ parāsanam
05.4.09 vigṛhya kathanaṃ asabhyaṃ apratyakṣaṃ aśraddheyaṃ anṛtaṃ ca vākyaṃ uccairanarmaṇi hāsaṃ vātaṣṭhīvane ca śabdavatī na kuryāt
05.4.10 mithaḥ kathanaṃ anyena, janavāde dvandvakathanaṃ, rājño veṣaṃ uddhatakuhakānāṃ ca, ratnātiśayaprakāśābhyarthanaṃ, ekākṣy।oṣṭhanirbhogaṃ bhrukuṭīkarma vākyāvakṣepaṇaṃ ca bruvati, balavat saṃyuktavirodhaṃ, strībhiḥ strīdarśibhiḥ sāmantadūtairdveṣyapakṣāvakṣiptān arthyaiśca pratisaṃsargaṃ ekārthacaryāṃ saṅghātaṃ ca varjayet
05.4.11ab ahīnakālaṃ rājārthaṃ svārthaṃ priyahitaiḥ saha ।
05.4.11chd parārthaṃ deśakāle ca brūyād dharmārthasaṃhitam
05.4.12ab pṛṣṭaḥ priyahitaṃ brūyānna brūyād ahitaṃ priyam ।
05.4.12chd apriyaṃ vā hitaṃ brūyātśṛṇvato'numato mithaḥ
05.4.13ab tūṣṇīṃ vā prativākye syād veṣyādīṃśca na varṇayet ।
05.4.13chd apriyā api dakṣāḥ syuḥ tadbhāvād ye bahiṣkṛtāḥ
05.4.14ab anarthyāśca priyā dṛṣṭāścittajñānānuvartinaḥ ।
05.4.14chd abhihāsyeṣvabhihased ghorahāsāṃśca varjayet  (iti)
05.4.15ab parāt saṅkrāmayed ghoraṃ na ca ghoraṃ pare vadet ।
05.4.15chd titikṣetātmanaścaiva kṣamāvān pṛthivīsamaḥ
05.4.16ab ātmarakṣā hi satataṃ pūrvaṃ kāryā vijānatā ।
05.4.16chd agnāviva hi samproktā vṛttī rājā upajīvinām
05.4.17ab ekadeśaṃ dahed agniḥ śarīraṃ vā paraṃ gataḥ ।

   Chapt .   Proper behaviour for a courtier
05.5.01 niyuktaḥ karmasu vyayaviśuddhaṃ udayaṃ darśayet
05.5.02 ābhyantaraṃ bāhyaṃ guhyaṃ prakāśyaṃ ātyayikaṃ upekṣitavyaṃ vā kāryaṃ idaṃ evam iti viśeṣayecca
05.5.03 mṛgayādyūtamadyastrīṣu prasaktaṃ na enaṃ anuvarteta praśaṃsābhiḥ
05.5.04 āsannaścāsya vyasana upaghāte prayateta, para upajāpātisandhāna upadhibhyaśca rakṣet
05.5.05 iṅgitākārau cāsya lakṣayet
05.5.06 kāmadveṣaharṣadainyavyavasāyabhayadvandvaviparyāsaṃ iṅgitākārābhyāṃ hi mantrasaṃvaraṇārthaṃ ācarati prājñaḥ
05.5.07 darśane prasīdati, vākyaṃ pratigṛhṇāti, āsanaṃ dadāti, vivikto darśayate, śaṅkāsthāne nātiśaṅkate, kathāyāṃ ramate, parijñāpyeṣvavekṣate, pathyaṃ uktaṃ sahate, smayamāno niyuṅkte, hastena spṛśati, ślāghye na upahasati, parokṣaṃ guṇaṃ bravīti, bhakṣyeṣu smarati, saha vihāraṃ yāti, vyasane'bhyupapadyate, tadbhaktīn pūjayati, guhyaṃ ācaṣṭe, mānaṃ vardhayati, arthaṃ karoti, anarthaṃ pratihanti - iti tuṣṭajñānam
05.5.08 etad eva viparītaṃ atuṣṭasya, bhūyaśca vakṣyāmaḥ
05.5.09 sandarśane kopaḥ, vākyasyāśravaṇapratiṣedhau, āsanacakṣuṣoradānaṃ, varṇasvarabhedaḥ, ekākṣibhrukuṭy।oṣṭhanirbhogaḥ, svedaśvāsasmitānāṃ asthāna utpattiḥ, paramantraṇaṃ, akasmādvrajanaṃ, vardhanaṃ anyasya, bhūmigātravilekhanaṃ, anyasya upatodanaṃ, vidyāvarṇadeśakutsā, samadoṣanindā, pratidoṣanindā, pratilomastavaḥ, sukṛtānavekṣaṇaṃ, duṣkṛtānukīrtanaṃ, pṛṣṭhāvadhānaṃ, atityāgaḥ, mithyā'bhibhāṣaṇaṃ, rājadarśināṃ ca tadvṛttānyatvam
05.5.10 vṛttivikāraṃ cāvekṣetāpyamānuṣāṇām
05.5.11 ayaṃ uccaiḥ siñcati iti kātyāyanaḥ pravavrāja, krauñco'pasavyam iti kaṇiṅko bhāradvājaḥ, tṛṇam iti dīrghaścārāyaṇaḥ, śītā śāṭī iti ghoṭamukhaḥ, hastī pratyaukṣīt iti kiñjalkaḥ, rathāśvaṃ prāśaṃsīt iti piśunaḥ, pratiravaṇe śunaḥ piśunaputraḥ
05.5.12 arthamānāvakṣepe ca parityāgaḥ

05.6.01 rājavyasanaṃ evaṃ amātyaḥ pratikurvīta
05.6.02 prāg eva maraṇābādhabhayād rājñaḥ priyahita upagraheṇa māsadvimāsāntaraṃ darśanaṃ sthāpayed deśapīḍā'pahaṃ amitrāpahaṃ āyuṣyaṃ putrīyaṃ vā karma rājā sādhayati ityapadeśena
05.6.03 rājavyañjanaṃ arūpavelāyāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ darśayet, mitrāmitradūtānāṃ ca
05.6.04 taiśca yathā ucitāṃ sambhāṣāṃ amātyamukho gacchet
05.6.05 dauvārikāntarvaṃśikamukhaśca yathā uktaṃ rājapraṇidhiṃ anuvartayet
05.6.06 apakāriṣu ca heḍaṃ prasādaṃ vā prakṛtikāntaṃ darśayet, prasādaṃ eva upakāriṣu
05.6.07 āptapuruṣādhiṣṭhitau durgapratyantasthau vā kośadaṇḍāvekasthau kārayet, kulyakumāramukhyāṃścānyāpadeśena
05.6.08 yaśca mukhyaḥ pakṣavān durgāṭavīstho vā vaiguṇyaṃ bhajeta taṃ upagrāhayet
05.6.09 bahv।ābādhaṃ vā yātrāṃ preṣayet, mitrakulaṃ vā
05.6.10 yasmācca sāmantād ābādhaṃ paśyet taṃ utsavavivāhahastibandhanāśvapaṇyabhūmipradānāpadeśenāvagrāhayet, svamitreṇa vā
05.6.11 tataḥ sandhiṃ adūṣyaṃ kārayet
05.6.12 āṭavikāmitrairvā vairaṃ grāhayet
05.6.13 tatkulīnaṃ aparuddhaṃ vā bhūṃy।ekadeśena upagrāhayet
05.6.14 kulyakumāramukhya upagrahaṃ kṛtvā vā kumāraṃ abhiṣiktaṃ eva darśayet
05.6.15 dāṇḍakarmikavad vā rājyakaṇṭakān uddhṛtya rājyaṃ kārayet
05.6.16 yadi vā kaścin mukhyaḥ sāmantādīnāṃ anyatamaḥ kopaṃ bhajeta taṃ ehi, rājānaṃ tvā kariṣyāmi ityāvāhayitvā ghātayet
05.6.17 āpatpratīkāreṇa vā sādhayet
05.6.18 yuvarāje vā krameṇa rājyabhāraṃ āropya rājavyasanaṃ khyāpayet
05.6.19 parabhūmau rājavyasane mitreṇāmitravyañjanena śatroḥ sandhiṃ avasthāpyāpagacchet
05.6.20 sāmantādīnāṃ anyatamaṃ vā'sya durge sthāpayitvā'pagacchet
05.6.21 kumāraṃ abhiṣicya vā prativyūheta
05.6.22 pareṇābhiyukto vā yathā uktaṃ āpatpratīkāraṃ kuryāt
05.6.23 evaṃ ekāiśvaryaṃ amātyaḥ kārayed iti kauṭilyaḥ
05.6.24 na evam iti bhāradvājaḥ
05.6.25 pramriyamāṇe vā rājanyamātyaḥ kulyakumāramukhyān parasparaṃ mukhyeṣu vā vikramayet
05.6.26 vikrāntaṃ prakṛtikopena ghātayet
05.6.27 kulyakumāramukhyān upāṃśudaṇḍena vā sādhayitvā svayaṃ rājyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt
05.6.28 rājyakāraṇādd hi pitā putrān putrāśca pitaraṃ abhidruhyanti, kiṃ aṅga punaramātyaprakṛtirhyekapragraho rājyasya
05.6.29 tat svayaṃ upasthitaṃ nāvamanyeta
05.6.30 svayaṃ ārūḍhā hi strī tyajyamānā'bhiśapati iti lokapravādaḥ
05.6.31ab kālaśca sakṛd abhyeti yaṃ naraṃ kālakāṅkṣiṇam ।
05.6.31chd durlabhaḥ sa punaḥ tasya kālaḥ karma cikīrṣataḥ
05.6.32 prakṛtikopakaṃ adharmiṣṭhaṃ anaikāntikaṃ ca etad iti kauṭilyaḥ
05.6.33 rājaputraṃ ātmasampannaṃ rājye sthāpayet
05.6.34 sampannābhāve'vyasaninaṃ kumāraṃ rājakanyāṃ garbhiṇīṃ devīṃ vā puraskṛtya mahāmātrān saṃnipātya brūyāt ayaṃ vo nikṣepaḥ, pitaraṃ asyāvekṣadhvaṃ sattvābhijanaṃ ātmanaśca, dhvajamātro'yaṃ bhavanta eva svāminaḥ, kathaṃ vā kriyatām iti
05.6.35 tathā bruvāṇaṃ yogapuruṣā brūyuḥ ko'nyo bhavatpurogād asmād rājñaścāturvarṇyaṃ arhati pālayitum iti
05.6.36 tathā ityamātyaḥ kumāraṃ rājakanyāṃ garbhiṇīṃ devīṃ vā'dhikurvīta, bandhusambandhināṃ mitrāmitradūtānāṃ ca darśayet
05.6.37 bhaktavetanaviśeṣaṃ amātyānāṃ āyudhīyānāṃ ca kārayet, bhūyaścāyaṃ vṛddhaḥ kariṣyati iti brūyāt
05.6.38 evaṃ durgarāṣṭramukhyān ābhāṣeta, yathā'rhaṃ ca mitrāmitrapakṣam
05.6.39 vinayakarmaṇi ca kumārasya prayateta
05.6.40 kanyāyāṃ samānajātīyād apatyaṃ utpādya vā'bhiṣiñcet
05.6.41 mātuścittakṣobhabhayāt kulyaṃ alpasattvaṃ chātraṃ ca lakṣaṇyaṃ upanidadhyāt
05.6.42 ṛtau ca enāṃ rakṣet
05.6.43 na cātmārthaṃ kañcid utkṛṣṭaṃ upabhogaṃ kārayet
05.6.44 rājārthaṃ tu yānavāhanābharaṇavastrastrīveśmaparivāpān kārayet
05.6.45ab yauvanasthaṃ ca yāceta viśramaṃ cittakāraṇāt ।
05.6.45chd parityajed atuṣyantaṃ tuṣyantaṃ cānupālayet
05.6.46ab nivedya putrarakṣā'rthaṃ gūḍhasāraparigrahān ।
05.6.46chd araṇyaṃ dīrghasattraṃ vā sevetārucyatāṃ gataḥ
05.6.47ab mukhyairavagṛhītaṃ vā rājānaṃ tatpriyāśritaḥ ।
05.6.47chd itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ bodhayed arthaśāstravit

06.1.03 mahākulīno daivabuddhisattvasampanno vṛddhadarśī dhārmikaḥ satyavāg avisaṃvādakaḥ kṛtajñaḥ sthūlalakṣo mahā utsāho'dīrghasūtraḥ śakyasāmanto dṛḍhabuddhirakṣudrapariṣatko vinayakāma ityābhigāmikā guṇāḥ
06.1.04 śuśrūṣāśravaṇagrahaṇadhāraṇavijñāna ūhāpohatattvābhiniveśāḥ prajñāguṇāḥ

06.1.06 vāgmī pragalbhaḥ smṛtimatibalavān udagraḥ sv'vagrahaḥ kṛtaśilpo'vyasano daṇḍanāyyupakārāpakārayordṛṣṭapratīkārī hrīmān āpatprakṛtyorviniyoktā dīrghadūradarśī deśakālapuruṣakārakāryapradhānaḥ sandhivikramatyāgasamyamapaṇaparacchidravibhāgī saṃvṛto'dīnābhihāsyajihmabhrukuṭīkṣaṇaḥ kāmakrodhalobhastambhacāpala upatāpapaiśunyahīnaḥ śaklaḥ smita udagrābhibhāṣī vṛddha upadeśācāra ityātmasampat

06.1.08 madhye cānte ca sthānavān ātmadhāraṇaḥ paradhāraṇaścāpadi svārakṣaḥ svājīvaḥ śatrudveṣī śakyasāmantaḥ paṅkapāṣāṇa uṣaraviṣamakaṇṭakaśreṇīvyālamṛgāṭavīhīnaḥ kāntaḥ sītākhanidravyahastivanavān gavyaḥ pauruṣeyo guptagocaraḥ paśumān adevamātṛko vāristhalapathābhyāṃ upetaḥ sāracitrabahupaṇyo daṇḍakarasahaḥ karmaśīlakarṣako'bāliśasvāmy'varavarṇaprāyo bhaktaśucimanuṣya iti janapadasampat

06.1.11 pitṛpaitāmaho nityo vaśyaḥ tuṣṭabhṛtaputradāraḥ pravāseṣvavisaṃvāditaḥ sarvatrāpratihato duḥkhasaho bahuyuddhaḥ sarvayuddhapraharaṇavidyāviśāradaḥ sahavṛddhikṣayikatvād advaidhyaḥ kṣatraprāya iti daṇḍasampat

06.2.34 evaṃ siddhiḥ trividhā eva - mantraśaktisādhyā mantrasiddhiḥ, prabhuśaktisādhyā prabhusiddhiḥ, utsāhaśaktisādhyā utsāhasiddhiḥ
06.2.35 tābhirabhyuccito jyāyān bhavati, apacito hīnaḥ, tulyaśaktiḥ samaḥ
06.2.36 tasmātśaktiṃ siddhiṃ ca ghaṭetātmanyāveśayituṃ, sādhāraṇo vā dravyaprakṛtiṣvānantaryeṇa śaucavaśena vā
06.2.37 dūṣyāmitrābhyāṃ vā'pakraṣṭuṃ yateta
06.2.38 yadi vā paśyet amitro me śaktiyukto vāgdaṇḍapāruṣyārthadūṣaṇaiḥ prakṛtīrupahaniṣyati, siddhiyukto vā mṛgayādyūtamadyastrībhiḥ pramādaṃ gamiṣyati, sa viraktaprakṛtirupakṣīṇaḥ pramatto vā sādhyo me bhaviṣyati, vigrahābhiyukto vā sarvasandohena ekastho'durgastho vā sthāsyati, sa saṃhatasainyo mitradurgaviyuktaḥ sādhyo me bhaviṣyati, balavān vā rājā parataḥ śatruṃ ucchettukāmaḥ taṃ ucchidya māṃ ucchindyād iti balavatā prārthitasya me vipannakarmārambhasya vā sāhāyyaṃ dāsyati, madhyamalipsāyāṃ ca, ityevaṃ।ādiṣu kāraṇeṣvamitrasyāpi śaktiṃ siddhiṃ ca icchet
06.2.39ab nemiṃ ekāntarān rājñaḥ kṛtvā cānantarān arān ।
06.2.39chd nābhiṃ ātmānaṃ āyacchennetā prakṛtimaṇḍale

07.1.02 sandhivigrahāsanayānasaṃśrayadvaidhībhāvāḥ ṣāḍguṇyam ityācāryāḥ

07.1.22 āśutarā me vṛddhirbhūyastarā vṛddhy।udayatarā vā bhaviṣyati, viparītā parasya iti jñātvā paravṛddhiṃ upekṣeta
07.1.23 tulyakālaphala udayāyāṃ vā vṛddhau sandhiṃ upeyāt

07.1.25 eṣa kṣayaḥ
07.1.26 ciratareṇālpataraṃ vṛddhy।udayataraṃ vā kṣeṣye, viparītaṃ paraḥ iti jñātvā kṣayaṃ upekṣeta
07.1.27 tulyakālaphala udaye vā kṣaye sandhiṃ upeyāt

07.1.30 tulyakālaphala udaye vā sthāne sandhiṃ upeyād ityācāryāḥ
07.1.31 na etad vibhāṣitaṃ iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.1.32a yadi vā paśyet sandhau sthito mahāphalaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ parakarmāṇyupahaniṣyāmi, mahāphalāni vā svakarmāṇyupabhokṣye, parakarmāṇi vā, sandhiviśvāsena vā yoga upaniṣatpraṇidhibhiḥ parakarmāṇyupahaniṣyāmi, sukhaṃ vā sānugrahaparihārasaukaryaṃ phalalābhabhūyastvena svakarmaṇāṃ parakarmayogāvahaṃ janaṃ āsrāvayiṣyāmi -
07.1.32b balinā'timātreṇa vā saṃhitaḥ paraḥ svakarma upaghātaṃ prāpsyati, yena vā vigṛhīto mayāsandhatte tenāsya vigrahaṃ dīrghaṃ kariṣyāmi, mayā vā saṃhitasya maddveṣiṇo janapadaṃ pīḍayiṣyati -
07.1.32ch para upahato vā'sya janapado māṃ āgamiṣyati, tataḥ karmasu vṛddhiṃ prāpsyāmi, vipannakarmārambho vā viṣamasthaḥ paraḥ karmasu na me vikrameta -
07.1.32d parataḥ pravṛttakarmārambho vā tābhyāṃ saṃhitaḥ karmasu vṛddhiṃ prāpsyāmi, śatrupratibaddhaṃ vā śatruṇā sandhiṃ kṛtvā maṇḍalaṃ bhetsyāmi -
07.1.32e bhinnaṃ avāpsyāmi, daṇḍānugraheṇa vā śatruṃ upagṛhya maṇḍalalipsāyāṃ vidveṣaṃ grāhayiṣyāmi, vidviṣṭaṃ tena eva ghātayiṣyāmi iti sandhinā vṛddhiṃ ātiṣṭhet
07.1.33a yadi vā paśyet āyudhīyaprāyaḥ śreṇīprāyo vā me janapadaḥ śailavananadīdurga ekadvārārakṣo vā śakṣyati parābhiyogaṃ pratihantuṃ, viṣayānte durgaṃ aviṣahyaṃ apāśrito vā śakṣyāmi parakarmāṇyupahantuṃ -
07.1.33b vyasanapīḍa upahata utsāho vā paraḥ samprāptakarma upaghātakālaḥ, vigṛhītasyānyato vā śakṣyāmi janapadaṃ apavāhayitum iti vigrahe sthito vṛddhiṃ ātiṣṭhet
07.1.34 yadi vā manyeta na me śaktaḥ paraḥ karmāṇyupahantuṃ nāhaṃ tasya karma upaghātī vā, vyasanaṃ asya, śvavarāhayoriva kalahe vā, svakarmānuṣṭhānaparo vā vardhiṣye ityāsanena vṛddhiṃ ātiṣṭhet
07.1.35 yadi vā manyeta yānasādhyaḥ karma upaghātaḥ śatroḥ, prativihitasvakarmārakṣaścāsmi iti yānena vṛddhiṃ ātiṣṭhet
07.1.36 yadi vā manyeta nāsmi śaktaḥ parakarmāṇyupahantuṃ, svakarma upaghātaṃ vā trātum iti, balavantaṃ āśritaḥ svakarmānuṣṭhānena kṣayāt sthānaṃ sthānād vṛddhiṃ cākāṅkṣeta
07.1.37 yadi vā manyeta sandhinā ekataḥ svakarmāṇi pravartayiṣyāmi, vigraheṇa ekataḥ parakarmāṇyupahaniṣyāmi iti dvaidhībhāvena vṛddhiṃ ātiṣṭhet

07.4.01 sandhivigrahayorāsanaṃ yānaṃ ca vyākhyātam
07.4.02 sthānaṃ āsanaṃ upekṣaṇaṃ ca ityāsanaparyāyāḥ
07.4.03 viśeṣaḥ tu - guṇa ekadeśe sthānaṃ, svavṛddhiprāpty'rthaṃ āsanaṃ, upāyānāṃ aprayoga upekṣaṇam
07.4.04 atisandhānakāmayorarivijigīṣvorupahantuṃ aśaktayorvigṛhyāsanaṃ sandhāya vā
07.4.05 yadā vā paśyet svadaṇḍairmitrāṭavīdaṇḍairvā samaṃ jyāyāṃsaṃ vā karśayituṃ utsahe iti tadā kṛtabāhyābhyantarakṛtyo vigṛhyāsīta
07.4.06 yadā vā paśyet utsāhayuktā me prakṛtayaḥ saṃhatā vivṛddhāḥ svakarmāṇyavyāhatāścariṣyanti parasya vā karmāṇyupahaniṣyanti iti tadā vigṛhyāsīta
07.4.07a yadā vā paśyet parasyāpacaritāḥ kṣīṇā lubdhāḥ svacakrastenāṭavīvyathitā vā prakṛtayaḥ svayaṃ upajāpena vā māṃ eṣyanti, sampannā me vārttā, vipannā parasya, tasya prakṛtayo durbhikṣa upahatā māṃ eṣyanti; vipannā me vārttā, sampannā parasya, -
07.4.07b taṃ me prakṛtayo na gamiṣyanti, vigṛhya cāsya dhānyapaśuhiraṇyānyāhariṣyāmi, svapaṇya upaghātīni vā parapaṇyāni nivartayiṣyāmi, -
07.4.07ch paravaṇikpathād vā saravanti māṃ eṣyanti vigṛhīte, na itaraṃ, dūṣyāmitrāṭavīnigrahaṃ vā vigṛhīto na kariṣyati, taireva vā vigrahaṃ prāpsyati, -
07.4.07d mitraṃ me mitrabhāvyabhiprayāto bahv'lpakālaṃ tanukṣayavyayaṃ arthaṃ prāpsyati, guṇavatīṃ ādeyāṃ vā bhūmiṃ, -
07.4.07e sarvasandohena vā māṃ anādṛtya prayātukāmaḥ kathaṃ na yāyād iti paravṛddhipratighātārthaṃ pratāpārthaṃ ca vigṛhyāsīta
07.4.08 taṃ eva hi pratyāvṛtto grasate ityācāryāḥ
07.4.09 na iti kauṭilyaḥ

07.4.12 tasmāt sarvasandohaprakṛtaṃ vigṛhyāsīta
07.4.13 vigṛhyāsanahetuprātilomye sandhāyāsīta
07.4.14 vigṛhyāsanahetubhirabhyuccitaḥ sarvasandohavarjaṃ vigṛhya yāyāt
07.4.15 yadā vā paśyet vyasanī paraḥ, prakṛtivyasanaṃ vā'sya śīṣaprakṛtibhirapratikāryaṃ, svacakrapīḍitā viraktā vā'sya prakṛtayaḥ karśitā nirutsāhāḥ parasparād vā bhinnāḥ śakyā lobhayituṃ, agny।udakavyādhimarakadurbhikṣanimittaṃ kṣīṇayugyapuruṣanicayarakṣāvidhānaḥ paraḥ iti tadā vigṛhya yāyāt
07.4.16 yadā vā paśyet mitraṃ ākrandaśca me śūravṛddhānuraktaprakṛtiḥ, viparītaprakṛtiḥ paraḥ pārṣṇigrāhaścāsāraśca, śakṣyāmi mitreṇāsāraṃ ākrandena pārṣṇigrāhaṃ vā vigṛhya yātum iti tadā vigṛhya yāyāt
07.4.17 yadā vā phalaṃ ekahāryaṃ alpakālaṃ paśyet tadā pārṣṇigrāhāsārābhyāṃ vigṛhya yāyāt
07.4.18 viparyaye sandhāya yāyāt
07.4.19 yadā vā paśyet na śakyaṃ ekena yātuṃ avaśyaṃ ca yātavyam iti tadā samahīnajyāyobhiḥ sāmavāyikaiḥ sambhūya yāyād, ekatra nirdiṣṭenāṃśena, anekatrānirdiṣṭenāṃśena
07.4.20 teṣāṃ asamavāye daṇḍaṃ anyatamasmānniviṣṭāṃśena yāceta
