07.4.22ab aṃśo daṇḍasamaḥ pūrvaḥ prayāsasama uttamaḥ ।
07.4.22chd vilopo vā yathālābhaṃ prakṣepasama eva vā  (iti)
   Chapt .   yātavyāmitrayorabhigrahacintāḥ - kṣayalobhavirāgahetavaḥ prakṛtīnāṃ - sāmavāyikaviparimarśaḥ
07.5.01 tulyasāmantavyasane yātavyaṃ amitraṃ vā ityamitraṃ abhiyāyāt, tatsiddhau yātavyam
07.5.02 amitrasiddhau hi yātavyaḥ sāhāyyaṃ dadyānnāmitro yātavyasiddhau
07.5.03 guruvyasanaṃ yātavyaṃ laghuvyasanaṃ amitraṃ vā iti guruvyasanaṃ saukaryato yāyād ityācāryāḥ
07.5.04 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.5.05 laghuvyasanaṃ amitraṃ yāyāt
07.5.06 laghvapi hi vyasanaṃ abhiyuktasya kṛcchraṃ bhavati
07.5.07 satyaṃ gurvapi gurutaraṃ bhavati
07.5.08 anabhiyuktaḥ tu laghuvyasanaḥ sukhena vyasanaṃ pratikṛtyāmitro yātavyaṃ abhisaret, pārṣṇiṃ vā gṛhṇīyāt
07.5.09 yātavyayaugapadye guruvyasanaṃ nyāyavṛttiṃ laghuvyasanaṃ anyāyavṛttiṃ viraktaprakṛtiṃ vā iti viraktaprakṛtiṃ yāyāt
07.5.10 guruvyasanaṃ nyāyavṛttiṃ abhiyuktaṃ prakṛtayo'nugṛhṇanti, laghuvyasanaṃ anyāyavṛttiṃ upekṣante, viraktā balavantaṃ apyucchindanti
07.5.11 tasmād viraktaprakṛtiṃ eva yāyāt
07.5.12 kṣīṇalubdhaprakṛtiṃ apacaritaprakṛtiṃ vā iti kṣīṇalubdhaprakṛtiṃ yāyāt, kṣīṇalubdhā hi prakṛtayaḥ sukhena upajāpaṃ pīḍāṃ vā upagacchanti, nāpacaritāḥ pradhānāvagrahasādhyāḥ ityācāryāḥ
07.5.13 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.5.14 kṣīṇalubdhā hi prakṛtayo bhartari snigdhā bhartṛhite tiṣṭhanti, upajāpaṃ vā visaṃvādayanti, anurāge sārvaguṇyaṃ iti
07.5.15 tasmād apacaritaprakṛtiṃ eva yāyāt
07.5.16 balavantaṃ anyāyavṛttiṃ durbalaṃ vā nyāyavṛttiṃ iti balavantaṃ anyāyavṛttiṃ yāyāt
07.5.17 balavantaṃ anyāyavṛttiṃ abhiyuktaṃ prakṛtayo nānugṛhṇanti, niṣpātayanti, amitraṃ vā'sya bhajante
07.5.18 durbalaṃ tu nyāyavṛttiṃ abhiyuktaṃ prakṛtayaḥ parigṛhṇanti, anuniṣpatanti vā
07.5.19ab avakṣepeṇa hi satāṃ asatāṃ pragraheṇa ca ।
07.5.19chd abhūtānāṃ ca hiṃsānāṃ adharmyāṇāṃ pravartanaiḥ
07.5.20ab ucitānāṃ caritrāṇāṃ dharmiṣṭhānāṃ nivartanaiḥ ।
07.5.20chd adharmasya prasaṅgena dharmasyāvagraheṇa ca
07.5.21ab akāryāṇāṃ ca karaṇaiḥ kāryāṇāṃ ca praṇāśanaiḥ ।
07.5.21chd apradānaiśca deyānāṃ adeyānāṃ ca sādhanaiḥ
07.5.22ab adaṇḍanaiśca daṇḍyānāṃ adaṇḍyānāṃ ca daṇḍanaiḥ ।
07.5.22chd agrāhyāṇāṃ upagrāhairgrāhyāṇāṃ cānabhigrahaiḥ
07.5.23ab anarthyānāṃ ca karaṇairarthyānāṃ ca vighātanaiḥ ।
07.5.23chd arakṣaṇaiśca corebhyaḥ svayaṃ ca parimoṣaṇaiḥ
07.5.24ab pātaiḥ puruṣakārāṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ guṇadūṣaṇaiḥ ।
07.5.24chd upaghātaiḥ pradhānānāṃ mānyānāṃ cāvamānanaiḥ
07.5.25ab virodhanaiśca vṛddhānāṃ vaiṣamyeṇānṛtena ca ।
07.5.25chd kṛtasyāpratikāreṇa sthitasyākaraṇena ca
07.5.26ab rājñaḥ pramādālasyābhyāṃ yogakṣemavadhena vā ।
07.5.26chd prakṛtīnāṃ kṣayo lobho vairāgyaṃ ca upajāyate
07.5.27ab kṣīṇāḥ prakṛtayo lobhaṃ lubdhā yānti virāgatām ।
07.5.27chd viraktā yāntyamitraṃ vā bhartāraṃ ghnanti vā svayam
07.5.28 tasmāt prakṛtīnāṃ kṣayalobhavirāgakāraṇāni na utpādayet, utpannāni vā sadyaḥ pratikurvīta
07.5.29 kṣīṇā lubdhā viraktā vā prakṛtaya iti
07.5.30 kṣīṇāḥ pīḍana ucchedanabhayāt sadyaḥ sandhiṃ yuddhaṃ niṣpatanaṃ vā rocayante
07.5.31 lubdhā lobhenāsantuṣṭāḥ para upajāpaṃ lipsante
07.5.32 viraktāḥ parābhiyogaṃ abhyuttiṣṭhante
07.5.33 tāsāṃ hiraṇyadhānyakṣayaḥ sarva upaghātī kṛcchrapratīkāraśca, yugyapuruṣakṣayo hiraṇyadhānyasādhyaḥ
07.5.34 lobha aikadeśiko mukhyāyattaḥ parārtheṣu śakyaḥ pratihantuṃ ādātuṃ vā
07.5.35 virāgaḥ pradhānāvagrahasādhyaḥ
07.5.36 niṣpradhānā hi prakṛtayo bhogyā bhavantyanupajāpyāścānyeṣāṃ, anāpatsahāḥ tu
07.5.37 prakṛtimukhyapragrahaiḥ tu bahudhā bhinnā guptā bhavantyāpatsahāśca
07.5.38 sāmavāyikānāṃ api sandhivigrahakāraṇānyavekṣya śaktiśaucayuktaiḥ sambhūya yāyāt
07.5.39 śaktimān hi pārṣṇigrahaṇe yātrāsāhāyyadāne vā śaktaḥ, śuciḥ siddhau cāsiddhau ca yathāsthitakārī iti
07.5.40 teṣāṃ jyāyasā ekena dvābhyāṃ samābhyāṃ vā sambhūya yātavyaṃ iti dvābhyāṃ samābhyāṃ śreyaḥ
07.5.41 jyāyasā hyavagṛhītaścarati, samābhyāṃ atisandhānādhikye vā
07.5.42 tau hi sukhau bhedayituṃ, duṣṭaśca eko dvābhyāṃ niyantuṃ bheda upagrahaṃ ca upagantuṃ iti
07.5.43 samena ekena dvābhyāṃ hīnābhyāṃ vā iti dvābhyāṃ hīnābhyāṃ śreyaḥ
07.5.44 tau hi dvikāryasādhakau vaśyau ca bhavataḥ
07.5.45ab kāryasiddhau tu - kṛtārthāj jyāyaso gūḍhaḥ sāpadeśaṃ apasravet ।
07.5.45chd aśuceḥ śucivṛttāt tu pratīkṣetā visarjanāt
07.5.46ab sattrād apasared yattaḥ kalatraṃ apanīya vā ।
07.5.46chd samād api hi labdhārthād viśvaḥ tasya bhayaṃ bhavet
07.5.47ab jyāyastve cāpi labdhārthaḥ samo'pi parikalpate ।
07.5.47chd abhyuccitaścāviśvāsyo vṛddhiścittavikāriṇī
07.5.48ab viśiṣṭād alpaṃ apyaṃśaṃ labdhvā tuṣṭamukho vrajet ।
07.5.48chd anaṃśo vā tato'syāṅke prahṛtya dviguṇaṃ haret
07.5.49ab kṛtārthaḥ tu svayaṃ netā visṛjet sāmavāyikān ।
07.5.49chd api jīyeta na jayen maṇḍala iṣṭaḥ tathā bhavet  (iti)
   Chapt .   saṃhitaprayāṇikaṃ - paripaṇitāparipaṇitāpasṛtāḥ sandhayaḥ
07.6.01 vijigīṣurdvitīyāṃ prakṛtiṃ evaṃ atisandadhyāt
07.6.02 sāmantaṃ saṃhitaprayāṇe yojayet tvaṃ ito yāhi, ahaṃ ito yāsyāmi, samāno lābhaḥ iti
07.6.03 lābhasāmye sandhiḥ, vaiṣamye vikramaḥ
07.6.04 sandhiḥ paripaṇitaścāparipaṇitaśca
07.6.05 tvaṃ etaṃ deśaṃ yāhi, ahaṃ imaṃ deśaṃ yāsyāmi iti paripaṇitadeśaḥ
07.6.06 tvaṃ etāvantaṃ kālaṃ ceṣṭasva, ahaṃ etāvantaṃ kālaṃ ceṣṭiṣye iti paripaṇitakālaḥ
07.6.07 tvaṃ etāvatkāryaṃ sādhaya, ahaṃ idaṃ kāryaṃ sādhayiṣyāmi iti paripaṇitārthaḥ
07.6.08 yadi vā manyeta śailavananadīdurgaṃ aṭavīvyavahitaṃ chinnadhānyapuruṣavīvadhāsāraṃ ayavasa indhana udakaṃ avijñātaṃ prakṛṣṭaṃ anyabhāvadeśīyaṃ vā sainyavyāyāmānāṃ alabdhabhaumaṃ vā deśaṃ paro yāsyati, viparītaṃ aham ityetasmin viśeṣe paripaṇitadeśaṃ sandhiṃ upeyāt
07.6.09 yadi vā manyeta pravarṣa uṣṇaśītaṃ ativyādhiprāyaṃ upakṣīṇāhāra upabhogaṃ sainyavyāyāmānāṃ cāuparodhikaṃ kāryasādhanānāṃ ūnaṃ atiriktaṃ vā kālaṃ paraśceṣṭiṣyate, viparītaṃ aham ityetasmin viśeṣe paripaṇitakālaṃ sandhiṃ upeyāt
07.6.10 yadi vā manyeta pratyādeyaṃ prakṛtikopakaṃ dīrghakālaṃ mahākṣayavyayaṃ alpaṃ anarthānubandhaṃ akalyaṃ adharmyaṃ madhyama udāsīnaviruddhaṃ mitra upaghātakaṃ vā kāryaṃ paraḥ sādhayiṣyati, viparītaṃ aham ityetasmin viśeṣe paripaṇitārthaṃ sandhiṃ upeyāt
07.6.11 evaṃ deśakālayoḥ kālakāryayordeśakāryayordeśakālakāryāṇāṃ cāvasthāpanāt saptavidhaḥ paripaṇitaḥ
07.6.12 tasmin prāg evārabhya pratiṣṭhāpya ca svakarmāṇi parakarmasu vikrameta
07.6.13 vyasanatvarāvamānālasyayuktaṃ ajñaṃ vā śatruṃ atisandhātukāmo deśakālakāryāṇāṃ anavasthāpanāt saṃhitau svaḥ iti sandhiviśvāsena paracchidraṃ āsādya prahared ityaparipaṇitaḥ
07.6.14 tatra etad bhavati
07.6.15ab sāmantena eva sāmantaṃ vidvān āyojya vigrahe ।
07.6.15chd tato'nyasya hared bhūmiṃ chittvā pakṣaṃ samantataḥ
07.6.16 sandherakṛtacikīrṣā kṛtaśleṣaṇaṃ kṛtavidūṣaṇaṃ avaśīrṇakriyā ca
07.6.17 vikramasya prakāśayuddhaṃ kūṭayuddhaṃ tūṣṇīṃyuddham
07.6.18 iti sandhivikramau
07.6.19 apūrvasya sandheḥ sānubandhaiḥ sāmādibhiḥ paryeṣaṇaṃ samahīnajyāyasāṃ ca yathābalaṃ avasthāpanaṃ akṛtacikīrṣā
07.6.20 kṛtasya priyahitābhyāṃ ubhayataḥ paripālanaṃ yathāsambhāṣitasya ca nibandhanasyānuvartanaṃ rakṣaṇaṃ ca kathaṃ parasmānna bhidyeta iti kṛtaśleṣaṇam
07.6.21 parasyāpasandheyatāṃ dūṣyātisandhānena sthāpayitvā vyatikramaḥ kṛtavidūṣaṇam
07.6.22 bhṛtyena mitreṇa vā doṣāpasṛtena pratisandhānaṃ avaśīrṇakriyā
07.6.23 tasyāṃ gatāgataścaturvidhaḥ - kāraṇād gatāgato, viparītaḥ, kāraṇād gato'kāraṇād āgato, viparītaśca iti
07.6.24 svāmino doṣeṇa gato guṇenāgataḥ parasya guṇena gato doṣeṇāgata iti kāraṇād gatāgataḥ sandheyaḥ
07.6.25 svadoṣeṇa gatāgato guṇaṃ ubhayoḥ parityajya akāraṇād gatāgataḥ calabuddhirasandheyaḥ
07.6.26 svāmino doṣeṇa gataḥ parasmāt svadoṣeṇāgata iti kāraṇād gato'kāraṇād āgataḥ tarkayitavyaḥ paraprayuktaḥ svena vā doṣeṇāpakartukāmaḥ, parasya ucchettāraṃ amitraṃ me jñātvā pratighātabhayād āgataḥ, paraṃ vā māṃ ucchettukāmaṃ parityajyānṛśaṃsyād āgataḥ iti
07.6.27 jñātvā kalyāṇabuddhiṃ pūjayed, anyathābuddhiṃ apakṛṣṭaṃ vāsayet
07.6.28 svadoṣeṇa gataḥ paradoṣeṇāgata ityakāraṇād gataḥ kāraṇād āgataḥ tarkayitavyaḥ  chidraṃ me pūrayiṣyati, ucito'yaṃ asya vāsaḥ, paratrāsya jano na ramate, mitrairme saṃhitaḥ, śatrubhirvigṛhītaḥ, lubdhakrūrād āvignaḥ śatrusaṃhitād vā parasmāt iti
07.6.29 jñātvā yathābuddhyavasthāpayitavyaḥ
07.6.30 kṛtapraṇāśaḥ śaktihānirvidyāpaṇyatvaṃ āśānirvedo deśalaulyaṃ aviśvāso balavadvigraho vā parityāgasthānam ityācāryāḥ
07.6.31 bhayaṃ avṛttiramarṣa iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.6.32 ihāpakārī tyājyaḥ, parāpakārī sandheyaḥ, ubhayāpakārī tarkayitavya iti samānam
07.6.33 asandheyena tvavaśyaṃ sandhātavye yataḥ prabhāvaḥ tataḥ pratividadhyāt
07.6.34ab sa upakāraṃ vyavahitaṃ guptaṃ āyuḥkṣayād iti ।
07.6.34chd vāsayed aripakṣīyaṃ avaśīrṇakriyāvidhau
07.6.35ab vikramayed bhartari vā siddhaṃ vā daṇḍacāriṇam
07.6.35chd kuryād amitrāṭavīṣu pratyante vā'nyataḥ kṣipet
07.6.36ab paṇyaṃ kuryād asiddhaṃ vā siddhaṃ vā tena saṃvṛtam
07.6.36chd tasya eva doṣeṇādūṣya parasandheyakāraṇāt
07.6.37ab atha vā śamayed enaṃ āyaty'rthaṃ upāṃśunā
07.6.37chd āyatyāṃ ca vadhaprepsuṃ dṛṣṭvā hanyād gatāgatam
07.6.38ab arito'bhyāgato doṣaḥ śatrusaṃvāsakāritaḥ
07.6.38chd sarpasaṃvāsadharmitvānnitya udvegena dūṣitaḥ
07.6.39ab jāyate plakṣabījāśāt kapotād iva śālmaleḥ
07.6.39chd udvegajanano nityaṃ paścād api bhayāvahaḥ
07.6.40ab prakāśayuddhaṃ nirdiṣṭe deśe kāle ca vikramaḥ
07.6.40chd vibhīṣaṇaṃ avaskandaḥ pramādavyasanārdanam
07.6.41ab ekatra tyāgaghātau ca kūṭayuddhasya mātṛkā
07.6.41chd yogagūḍha upajāpārthaṃ tūṣṇīṃyuddhasya lakṣaṇam  (iti)
   Chapt .   dvaidhībhāvikāḥ sandhivikramāḥ
07.7.01 vijigīṣurdvitīyāṃ prakṛtiṃ evaṃ upagṛhṇīyāt
07.7.02 sāmantaṃ sāmantena sambhūya yāyāt, yadi vā manyeta pārṣṇiṃ me na grahīṣyati, pārṣṇigrāhaṃ vārayiṣyati, yātavyaṃ nābhisariṣyati, baladvaiguṇyaṃ me bhaviṣyati, vīvadhāsārau me pravartayiṣyati, parasya vārayiṣyati, bahv।ābādhe me pathi kaṇṭakān mardayiṣyati, durgāṭavy'pasāreṣu daṇḍena cariṣyati, yātavyaṃ aviṣahye doṣe sandhau vā
 sthāpayiṣyati, labdhalābhāṃśo vā śatrūn anyān me viśvāsayiṣyati iti
07.7.03 dvaidhībhūto vā kośena daṇḍaṃ daṇḍena kośaṃ sāmantānāṃ anyatamāllipseta
07.7.04 teṣāṃ jyāyaso'dhikenāṃśena samāt samena hīnādd hīnena iti samasandhiḥ
07.7.05 viparyaye viṣamasandhiḥ
07.7.06 tayorviśeṣalābhād atisandhiḥ
07.7.07 vyasaninaṃ apāyasthāne saktaṃ anarthinaṃ vā jyāyāṃsaṃ hīno balasamena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.08 paṇitaḥ tasyāpakārasamartho vikrameta, anyathā sandadhyāt
07.7.09 evambhūto vā hīnaśaktipratāpapūraṇārthaṃ sambhāvyārthābhisārī mūlapārṣṇitrāṇārthaṃ vā jyāyāṃsaṃ hīno balasamād viśiṣṭena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.10 paṇitaḥ kalyāṇabuddhiṃ anugṛhṇīyāt, anyathā vikrameta
07.7.11 jātavyasanaprakṛtirandhraṃ upasthitānarthaṃ vā jyāyāṃsaṃ hīno durgamitrapratiṣṭabdho vā hrasvaṃ adhvānaṃ yātukāmaḥ śatruṃ ayuddhaṃ ekāntasiddhiṃ vā lābhaṃ ādātukāmo balasamādd hīnena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.12 paṇitaḥ tasyāpakārasamartho vikrameta, anyathā sandadhyāt
07.7.13 arandhravyasano vā jyāyān dur।ārabdhakarmāṇaṃ bhūyaḥ kṣayavyayābhyāṃ yoktukāmo dūṣyadaṇḍaṃ pravāsayitukāmo dūṣyadaṇḍaṃ āvāhayitukāmo vā pīḍanīyaṃ ucchedanīyaṃ vā hīnena vyathayitukāmaḥ sandhipradhāno vā kalyāṇabuddhirhīnaṃ lābhaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt
07.7.14 kalyāṇabuddhinā sambhūyārthaṃ lipseta, anyathā vikrameta
07.7.15 evaṃ samaḥ samaṃ atisandadhyād anugṛhṇīyād vā
07.7.16 parānīkasya pratyanīkaṃ mitrāṭavīnāṃ vā, śatrorvibhūmīnāṃ deśikaṃ mūlapārṣṇitrāṇārthaṃ vā samo balasamena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.17 paṇitaḥ kalyāṇabuddhiṃ anugṛhṇīyāt, anyathā vikrameta
07.7.18 jātavyasanaprakṛtirandhraṃ anekaviruddhaṃ anyato labhamāno vā samo balasamādd hīnena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.19 paṇitaḥ tasyāpakārasamartho vikrameta, anyathā sandadhyāt
07.7.20 evambhūto vā samaḥ sāmantāyattakāryaḥ kartavyabalo vā balasamād viśiṣṭena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.21 paṇitaḥ kalyāṇabuddhiṃ anugṛhṇīyāt anyathā vikrameta
07.7.22 jātavyasanaprakṛtirandhraṃ abhihantukāmaḥ sv।ārabdhaṃ ekāntasiddhiṃ vā'sya karma upahantukāmo mūle yātrāyāṃ vā prahartukāmo yātavyādbhūyo labhamāno vā jyāyāṃsaṃ hīnaṃ samaṃ vā bhūyo yāceta
07.7.23 bhūyo vā yācitaḥ svabalarakṣā'rthaṃ durdharṣaṃ anyadurgaṃ āsāraṃ aṭavīṃ vā paradaṇḍena marditukāmaḥ prakṛṣṭe'dhvani kāle vā paradaṇḍaṃ kṣayavyayābhyāṃ yoktukāmaḥ paradaṇḍena vā vivṛddhaḥ taṃ eva ucchettukāmaḥ paradaṇḍaṃ ādātukāmo vā bhūyo dadyāt
07.7.24 jyāyān vā hīnaṃ yātavyāpadeśena haste kartukāmaḥ paraṃ ucchidya vā taṃ eva ucchettukāmaḥ, tyāgaṃ vā kṛtvā pratyādātukāmo balasamād viśiṣṭena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.25 paṇitaḥ tasyāpakārasamartho vikrameta, anyathā sandadhyāt
07.7.26 yātavyasaṃhito vā tiṣṭhet, dūṣyāmitrāṭavīdaṇḍaṃ vā'smai dadyāt
07.7.27 jātavyasanaprakṛtirandhro vā jyāyān hīnaṃ balasamena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.28 paṇitaḥ tasyāpakārasamartho vikrameta, anyathā sandadhyāt
07.7.29 evambhūtaṃ hīnaṃ jyāyān balasamādd hīnena lābhena paṇeta
07.7.30 paṇitaḥ tasyāpakārasamartho vikrameta, anyathā sandadhyāt
07.7.31ab ādau budhyeta paṇitaḥ paṇamānaśca kāraṇam
07.7.31chd tato vitarkya ubhayato yataḥ śreyaśtato vrajet  (iti)
   Chapt .   yātavyavṛttiḥ - anugrāhyamitraviśeṣāḥ
07.8.01 yātavyo'bhiyāsyamānaḥ sandhikāraṇaṃ ādātukāmo vihantukāmo vā sāmavāyikānāṃ anyatamaṃ lābhadvaiguṇyena paṇeta
07.8.02 paṇamānaḥ kṣayavyayapravāsapratyavāyapara upakāraśarīrābādhāṃścāsya varṇayet
07.8.03 pratipannaṃ arthena yojayet
07.8.04 vairaṃ vā parairgrāhayitvā visaṃvādayet
07.8.05 durārabdhakarmāṇaṃ bhūyaḥ kṣayavyayābhyāṃ yoktukāmaḥ sv।ārabdhāṃ vā yātrāsiddhiṃ vighātayitukāmo mūle yātrāyāṃ vā prahartukāmo yātavyasaṃhitaḥ punaryācitukāmaḥ pratyutpannārthakṛcchraḥ tasminn aviśvasto vā tadātve lābhaṃ alpaṃ icchet, āyatyāṃ prabhūtam
07.8.06 mitra upakāraṃ amitra upaghātaṃ arthānubandhaṃ avekṣamāṇaḥ pūrva upakārakaṃ kārayitukāmo bhūyaḥ tadātve mahāntaṃ lābhaṃ utsṛjyāyatyāṃ alpaṃ icchet
07.8.07 dūṣyāmitrābhyāṃ mūlahareṇa vā jyāyasā vigṛhītaṃ trātukāmaḥ tathāvidhaṃ upakāraṃ kārayitukāmaḥ sambandhāvekṣī vā tadātve cāyatyāṃ ca lābhaṃ na pratigṛhṇīyāt
07.8.08 kṛtasandhiratikramitukāmaḥ parasya prakṛtikarśanaṃ mitrāmitrasandhiviśleṣaṇaṃ vā kartukāmaḥ parābhiyogātśaṅkamāno lābhaṃ aprāptaṃ adhikaṃ vā yāceta

07.8.10 tena pūrve vyākhyātāḥ
07.8.11 arivijigīṣvoḥ tu svaṃ svaṃ mitraṃ anugṛhṇatoḥ śakyakalyabhavyārambhisthirakarmānuraktaprakṛtibhyo viśeṣaḥ

07.8.13 sthirakarmā nāsamāpya karma uparamate
07.8.14 anuraktaprakṛtiḥ susahāyatvād alpenāpyanugraheṇa kāryaṃ sādhayati
07.8.15 ta ete kṛtārthāḥ sukhena prabhūtaṃ ca upakurvanti
07.8.16 ataḥ pratilomā nānugrāhyāḥ
07.8.17 tayorekapuruṣānugrahe yo mitraṃ mitrataraṃ vā'nugṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.8.18 mitrād ātmavṛddhiṃ hi prāpnoti, kṣayavyayapravāsapara upakārān itaraḥ
07.8.19 kṛtārthaśca śatrurvaiguṇyaṃ eti
07.8.20 madhyamaṃ tvanugṛhṇatoryo madhyamaṃ mitraṃ mitrataraṃ vā'nugṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.8.21 mitrād ātmavṛddhiṃ hi prāpnoti, kṣayavyayapravāsapara upakārān itaraḥ
07.8.22 madhyamaśced anugṛhīto viguṇaḥ syād amitro'tisandhatte
07.8.23 kṛtaprayāsaṃ hi madhyamāmitraṃ apasṛtaṃ ekārtha upagataṃ prāpnoti
07.8.24 tena udāsīnānugraho vyākhyātaḥ
07.8.25 madhyama udāsīnayorbalāṃśadāne yaḥ śūraṃ kṛtāstraṃ duḥkhasahaṃ anuraktaṃ vā daṇḍaṃ dadāti so'tisandhīyate
07.8.26 viparīto'tisandhatte
07.8.27 yatra tu daṇḍaḥ prahitaḥ taṃ vā cārthaṃ anyāṃśca sādhayati tatra maulabhṛtaśreṇīmitrāṭavībalānāṃ anyatamaṃ upalabdhadeśakālaṃ daṇḍaṃ dadyāt, amitrāṭavībalaṃ vā vyavahitadeśakālam
07.8.28 yaṃ tu manyeta kṛtārtho me daṇḍaṃ gṛhṇīyād, amitrāṭavy'bhūmy'nṛtuṣu vā vāsayed, aphalaṃ vā kuryād iti, daṇḍavyāsaṅgāpadeśena na enaṃ anugṛhṇīyāt
07.8.29 evaṃ avaśyaṃ tvanugrahītavye tatkālasahaṃ asmai daṇḍaṃ dadyāt
07.8.30 āsamāpteśca enaṃ vāsayed yodhayecca balavyasanebhyaśca rakṣet
07.8.31 kṛtārthācca sāpadeśaṃ apasrāvayet

   Chapt .   mitrahiraṇyabhūmikarmasandhayaḥ, tatra mitrasandhiḥ hiraṇyasandhiśca
07.9.01 saṃhitaprayāṇe mitrahiraṇyabhūmilābhānāṃ uttara uttaro lābhaḥ śreyān
07.9.02 mitrahiraṇye hi bhūmilābhād bhavataḥ, mitraṃ hiraṇyalābhāt
07.9.03 yo vā lābhaḥ siddhaḥ śeṣayoranyataraṃ sādhayati
07.9.04 tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca mitraṃ labhāvahe ityevaṃ।ādidḥ samasandhiḥ
07.9.05 tvaṃ mitram ityevaṃ।ādirviṣamasandhiḥ
07.9.06 tayorviśeṣalābhād atisandhiḥ
07.9.07 samasandhau tu yaḥ sampannaṃ mitraṃ mitrakṛcchre vā mitraṃ avāpnoti so'tisandhatte
07.9.08 āpadd hi sauhṛdasthairyaṃ utpādayati
07.9.09 mitrakṛcchre'pi nityaṃ avaśyaṃ anityaṃ vaśyaṃ vā iti nityaṃ avaśyaṃ śreyaḥ, tadd hi anupakurvad api nāpakaroti ityācāryāḥ
07.9.10 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.9.11 vaśyaṃ anityaṃ śreyaḥ
07.9.12 yāvad upakaroti tāvan mitraṃ bhavati, upakāralakṣaṇaṃ mitraṃ iti
07.9.13 vaśyayorapi mahābhogaṃ anityaṃ alpabhogaṃ vā nityaṃ iti mahābhogaṃ anityaṃ śreyaḥ, mahābhogaṃ anityaṃ alpakālena mahad।upakurvan mahānti vyayasthānāni pratikaroti ityācāryāḥ ॥

07.9.14 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.9.15 nityaṃ alpabhogaṃ śreyaḥ
07.9.16 mahābhogaṃ anityaṃ upakārabhayād apakrāmati, upakṛtya vā pratyādātuṃ īhate
07.9.17 nityaṃ alpabhogaṃ sātatyād alpaṃ upakurvan mahatā kālena mahad upakaroti
07.9.18 gurusamutthaṃ mahan mitraṃ laghusamutthaṃ alpaṃ vā iti gurusamutthaṃ mahan mitraṃ pratāpakaraṃ bhavati, yadā ca uttiṣṭhate tadā kāryaṃ sādhayati ityācāryāḥ
07.9.19 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.9.20 laghusamutthaṃ alpaṃ śreyaḥ
07.9.21 lagusamutthaṃ alpaṃ mitraṃ kāryakālaṃ nātipātayati daurbalyācca yathā iṣṭabhogyaṃ bhavati, na itarat prakṛṣṭabhaumam
07.9.22 vikṣiptasainyaṃ avaśyasainyaṃ vā iti vikṣiptaṃ sainyaṃ śakyaṃ pratisaṃhartuṃ vaśyatvād ityācāryāḥ
07.9.23 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.9.24 avaśyasainyaṃ śreyaḥ
07.9.25 avaśyaṃ hi śakyaṃ sāmādibhirvaśyaṃ kartuṃ, na itarat kāryavyāsaktaṃ pratisaṃhartum
07.9.26 puruṣabhogaṃ hiraṇyabhogaṃ vā mitraṃ iti puruṣabhogaṃ mitraṃ śreyaḥ, pruṣabhogaṃ mitraṃ pratāpakaraṃ bhavati, yadā ca uttiṣṭhate tadā kāryaṃ sādhayati ityācāryāḥ
07.9.27 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.9.28 hiraṇyabhogaṃ mitraṃ śreyaḥ
07.9.29 nityo hi hiraṇyena yogaḥ kadācid daṇḍena
07.9.30 daṇḍaśca hiraṇyenānye ca kāmāḥ prāpyanta iti
07.9.31 hiraṇyabhogaṃ bhūmibhogaṃ vā mitraṃ iti hiraṇyabhogaṃ gatimattvāt sarvavyayapratīkārakaram ityācāryāḥ
07.9.32 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.9.33 mitrahiraṇye hi bhūmilābhād bhavata ityuktaṃ purastād
07.9.34 tasmād bhūmibhogaṃ mitraṃ śreya iti
07.9.35 tulye puruṣabhoge vikramaḥ kleśasahatvaṃ anurāgaḥ sarvabalalābho vā mitrakulād viśeṣaḥ
07.9.36 tulye hiraṇyabhoge prārthitārthatā prābhūtyaṃ alpaprayasatā sātatyaṃ ca viśeṣaḥ
07.9.37 tatra etad bhavati
07.9.38ab nityaṃ vaśyaṃ laghu।utthānaṃ pitṛpaitāmahaṃ mahat ।
07.9.38chd advaidhyaṃ ca iti sampannaṃ mitraṃ ṣaḍguṇaṃ ucyate
07.9.39ab ṛte yad arthaṃ praṇayād rakṣyate yacca rakṣati ।
07.9.39chd pūrva upacitasambandhaṃ tan mitraṃ nityaṃ ucyate
07.9.40ab sarvacitramahābhogaṃ trividhaṃ vaśyaṃ ucyate ।
07.9.40chd ekatobhogyubhayataḥ sarvatobhogi cāparam

07.9.41chd mitraṃ nityaṃ avaśyaṃ taddurgāṭavy'pasāri ca
07.9.42ab anyato vigṛhītaṃ yallaghuvyasanaṃ eva vā ।
07.9.42chd sandhatte ca upakārāya tan mitraṃ vaśyaṃ adhruvam
07.9.43ab ekārthenātha sambaddhaṃ upakāryavikāri ca ।
07.9.43chd mitrabhāvi bhavatyetan mitraṃ advaidhyaṃ āpadi

07.9.44chd na kasyacid udāsīnaṃ dvayorubhayabhāvi tat

07.9.45chd upakāre'niviṣṭaṃ vā'śaktaṃ vā'nupakāri tat
07.9.46ab priyaṃ parasya vā rakṣyaṃ pūjyaṃ sambaddhaṃ eva vā ।
07.9.46chd anugṛhṇāti yan mitraṃ śatrusādhāraṇaṃ hi tat
07.9.47ab prakṛṣṭabhaumaṃ santuṣṭaṃ balavaccālasaṃ ca yat ।

07.9.49chd yo mitraṃ samupekṣeta sa mṛtyuṃ upagūhati

07.10.01 tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca bhūmiṃ labhāvahe iti bhūmisandhiḥ

07.10.03 tulye sampannālābhe yo balavantaṃ ākramya bhūmiṃ avāpnoti so'tisandhatte
07.10.04 bhūmilābhaṃ śatrukarśanaṃ pratāpaṃ ca hi prāpnoti
07.10.05 durbalādbhūmilābhe satyaṃ saukaryaṃ bhavati
07.10.06 durbala eva ca bhūmilābhaḥ, tatsāmantaśca mitraṃ amitrabhāvaṃ gacchati

07.11.01 tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca śūnyaṃ niveśayāvahe ityanavasitasandhiḥ
07.11.02 tayoryaḥ pratyupasthitārtho yathā uktaguṇāṃ bhūmiṃ niveśayati so'tisandhatte
07.11.03 tatrāpi sthalaṃ audakaṃ vā iti mahataḥ sthalād alpaṃ audakaṃ śreyaḥ, sātatyād avasthitatvācca phalānām

07.11.05 audakayorapi dhānyavāpaṃ adhānyavāpātśreyaḥ

07.11.20 viparītā śreṇīmanuṣyā, kope mahādoṣā
07.11.21 tasyāṃ cāturvarṇyaniveśe sarvabhogasahatvād avaravarṇaprāyā śreyasī, bāhulyād dhruvatvācca kṛṣyāḥ karṣakavatī, kṛṣyāścānyeṣāṃ cārambhāṇāṃ prayojakatvāt gorakṣakavatī, paṇyanicaya।ṛṇānugrahād āḍhyavaṇigvatī
07.11.22 bhūmiguṇānāṃ apāśrayaḥ śreyān

07.11.24 puruṣavad dhi rājyam

07.11.26 mahākṣayavyayaniveśāṃ tu bhūmiṃ avāptukāmaḥ pūrvaṃ eva kretāraṃ paṇeta durbalaṃ arājabījinaṃ nirutsāhaṃ apakṣaṃ anyāyavṛttiṃ vyasaninaṃ daivapramāṇaṃ yatkiñcanakāriṇaṃ vā
07.11.27 mahākṣayavyayaniveśāyāṃ hi bhūmau durbalo rājabījī niviṣṭaḥ sagandhābhiḥ prakṛtibhiḥ saha kṣayavyayenāvasīdati

07.11.29 nirutsāhaḥ tu daṇḍavān api daṇḍasyāpraṇetā sadaṇḍaḥ kṣayavyayenāvabhajyate

07.11.33 tena vyasanī vyākhyātaḥ
07.11.34 daivapramāṇo mānuṣahīno nirārambho vipannakarmārambho vā'vasīdati
07.11.35 yatkiñcanakārī na kiñcid āsādayati
07.11.36 sa ca eṣāṃ pāpiṣṭhatamo bhavati
07.11.37 yatkiñcid।ārabhamāṇo hi vijigīṣoḥ kadācicchidraṃ āsādayed ityācāryāḥ
07.11.38 yathā chidraṃ tathā vināśaṃ apyāsādayed iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.11.39 teṣāṃ alābhe yathā pārṣṇigrāha upagrahe vakṣyāmaḥ tathā bhūmiṃ avasthāpayet
07.11.40 ityabhihitasandhiḥ
07.11.41 guṇavatīṃ ādeyāṃ vā bhūmiṃ balavatā krayeṇa yācitaḥ sandhiṃ avasthāpya dadyāt
07.11.42 ityanibhṛtasandhiḥ
07.11.43 samena vā yācitaḥ kāraṇaṃ avekṣya dadyāt pratyādeyā me bhūmirvaśyā vā, anayā pratibaddhaḥ paro me vaśyo bhaviṣyati bhūmivikrayād vā mitrahiraṇyalābhaḥ kāryasāmarthyakaro me bhaviṣyati iti
07.11.44 tena hīnaḥ kretā vyākhyātaḥ
07.11.45ab evaṃ mitraṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca sajanāṃ ajanāṃ ca gām ।
07.11.45chd labhamāno'tisandhatte śāstravit sāmavāyikān  (iti)
   Chapt .   mitrahiraṇyabhūmikarmasaṃdhayaḥ, tatra karmasaṃdhiḥ
07.12.01 tvaṃ cāhaṃ ca durgaṃ kārayāvahe iti karmasandhiḥ
07.12.02 tayoryo daivakṛtaṃ aviṣahyaṃ alpavyayārambhaṃ durgaṃ kārayati so'tisandhatte
07.12.03 tatrāpi sthalanadīparvatadurgāṇāṃ uttara uttaraṃ śreyaḥ
07.12.04 setubandhayorapyāhārya udakāt saha udakaḥ śreyān
07.12.05 saha udakayorapi prabhūtavāpasthānaḥ śreyān
07.12.06 dravyavanayorapi yo mahatsāravaddravyāṭavīkaṃ viṣayānte nadīmātṛkaṃ dravyavanaṃ chedayati so'tisandhatte
07.12.07 nadīmātṛkaṃ hi sv।ājīvaṃ apāśrayaścāpadi bhavati
07.12.08 hastivanayorapi yo bahuśūramṛgaṃ durbalaprativeśaṃ'nantāvakleśi viṣayānte hastivanaṃ badhnāti so'tisandhatte
07.12.09 tatrāpi bahukuṇṭhālpaśūrayoḥ alpaśūraṃ śreyaḥ, śūreṣu hi yuddhaṃ, alpāḥ śūrā bahūn aśūrān bhañjanti, te bhagnāḥ svasainyāvaghātino bhavanti ityācāryāḥ
07.12.10 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.12.11 kuṇṭhā bahavaḥ śreyāṃsaḥ, skandhaviniyogād anekaṃ karma kurvāṇāḥ sveṣāṃ apāśrayo yuddhe, pareṣāṃ durdharṣā vibhīṣaṇāśca
07.12.12 bahuṣu hi kuṇṭheṣu vinayakarmaṇā śakyaṃ śauryaṃ ādhātuṃ, na tvevālpeṣu śūreṣu bahutvaṃ iti
07.12.13 khanyorapi yaḥ prabhūtasārāṃ adurgamārgāṃ alpavyayārambhāṃ khaniṃ khānayati, so'tisandhatte
07.12.14 tatrāpi mahāsāraṃ alpaṃ alpasāraṃ vā prabhūtaṃ iti mahāsāraṃ alpaṃ śreyaḥ, vajramaṇimuktāpravālahemarūpyadhāturhi prabhūtaṃ alpasāraṃ atyargheṇa grasate ityācāryāḥ
07.12.15 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.12.16 cirād alpo mahāsārasya kretā vidyate, prabhūtaḥ sātatyād alpasārasya
07.12.17 etena vaṇikpatho vyākhyātaḥ
07.12.18 tatrāpi vāristhalapathayorvāripathaḥ śreyān, alpavyayavyāyāmaḥ prabhūtapaṇya udayaśca ityācāryāḥ
07.12.19 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.12.20 samruddhagatirasārvakālikaḥ prakṛṣṭabhayayonirniṣpratīkāraśca vāripathaḥ, viparītaḥ sthalapathaḥ
07.12.21 vāripathe tu kūlasamyānapathayoḥ kūlapathaḥ paṇyapattanabāhulyātśreyān, nadīpatho vā, sātatyād viṣahyābādhatvācca
07.12.22 sthalapathe'pi haimavato dakṣiṇāpathātśreyān, hasty'śvagandhadantājinarūpyasuvarṇapaṇyāḥ sāravattarāḥ ityācāryāḥ
07.12.23 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.12.24 kambalājināśvapaṇyavarjāḥ śaṅkhavajramaṇimuktāsuvarṇapaṇyāśca prabhūtatarā dakṣiṇāpathe
07.12.25 dakṣiṇāpathe'pi bahukhaniḥ sārapaṇyaḥ prasiddhagatiralpavyayavyāyāmo vā vaṇikpathaḥ śreyān, prabhūtaviṣayo vā phalgupuṇyaḥ
07.12.26 tena pūrvaḥ paścimaśca vaṇikpatho vyākhyātaḥ
07.12.27 tatrāpi cakrapādapathayoścakrapatho vipulārambhatvātśreyān, deśakālasambhāvano vā khara uṣṭrapathaḥ
07.12.28 ābhyāṃ aṃsapatho vyākhyātaḥ
07.12.29 parakarma udayo netuḥ kṣayo vṛddhirviparyaye
07.12.30 tulye karmapathe sthānaṃ jñeyaṃ svaṃ vijigīṣuṇā
07.12.31 alpāgamātivyayatā kṣayo vṛddhirviparyaye

07.13.01 saṃhatyārivijigīṣvoramitrayoḥ parābhiyoginoḥ pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇatoryaḥ śaktisampannasya pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.13.02 śaktisampanno hyamitraṃ ucchidya pārṣṇigrāhaṃ ucchindyāt, na hīnaśaktiralabdhalābhaḥ
07.13.03 śaktisāmye yo vipulārambhasya pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.13.04 vipulārambho hyamitraṃ ucchidya pārṣṇigrāhaṃ ucchindyāt, nālpārambhaḥ saktacakraḥ
07.13.05 ārambhasāmye yaḥ sarvasandohena prayātasya pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.13.06 śūnyamūlo hyasya sukaro bhavati, naikadeśabalaprayātaḥ kṛtapārṣṇipratividhānaḥ
07.13.07 bala upādānasāmye yaścalāmitraṃ prayātasya pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.13.08 calāmitraṃ prayāto hi sukhenāvāptasiddhiḥ pārṣṇigrāhaṃ ucchindyāt, na sthitāmitraṃ prayātaḥ
07.13.09 asau hi durgapratihataḥ pārṣṇigrāhe ca pratinivṛttaḥ sthitenāmitreṇāvagṛhyate
07.13.10 tena pūrve vyākhyātāḥ
07.13.11 śatrusāmye yo dhārmikābhiyoginaḥ pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.13.12 dhārmikābhiyogī hi sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ ca dveṣyo bhavati, adhārmikābhiyogī sampriyaḥ
07.13.13 tena mūlaharatādātvikakadaryābhiyogināṃ pārṣṇigrahaṇaṃ vyākhyātam
07.13.14 mitrābhiyoginoḥ pārṣṇigrahaṇe ta eva hetavaḥ
07.13.15 mitraṃ amitraṃ cābhiyuñjānayoryo mitrābhiyoginaḥ pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.13.16 mitrābhiyogī hi sukhenāvāptasiddhiḥ pārṣṇigrāhaṃ ucchindyāt
07.13.17 sukaro hi mitreṇa sandhirnāmitreṇa
07.13.18 mitraṃ amitraṃ ca uddharatoryo'mitra uddhāriṇaḥ pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇāti so'tisandhatte
07.13.19 vṛddhamitro hyamitra uddhārī pārṣṇigrāhaṃ ucchindyāt, na itaraḥ svapakṣa upaghātī
07.13.20 tayoralabdhalābhāpagamane yasyāmitro mahato lābhād viyuktaḥ kṣayavyayādhiko vā sa pārṣṇigrāho'tisandhatte
07.13.21 labdhalābhāpagamane yasyāmitro lābhena śaktyā hīnaḥ sa pārṣṇigrāho'tisandhatte, yasya vā yātavyaḥ śatrorvigrahāpakārasamarthaḥ syāt
07.13.22 pārṣṇigrāhayorapi yaḥ śakyārambhabala upādānādhikaḥ sthitaśatruḥ pārśvasthāyī vā so'tisandhatte
07.13.23 pārśvasthāyī hi yātavyābhisāro mūlābādhakaśca bhavati, mūlābādhaka eva paścātsthāyī
07.13.24ab pārṣṇigrāhāḥ trayo jñeyāḥ śatrośceṣṭānirodhakāḥ ।
07.13.24chd sāmantaḥ pṛṣṭhato vargaḥ prativeśau ca pārśvayoḥ
07.13.25ab arernetuśca madhyastho durbalo'ntardhirucyate ।
07.13.25chd pratighāto balavato durgāṭavy'pasāravān
07.13.26 madhyamaṃ tvarivijigīṣvorlipsamānayormadhyamasya pārṣṇiṃ gṛhṇatorlabdhalābhāpagamane yo madhyamaṃ mitrād viyojayatyamitraṃ ca mitraṃ āpnoti so'tisandhatte
07.13.27 sandheyaśca śatrurupakurvāṇo, na mitraṃ mitrabhāvād utkrāntam
07.13.28 tena udāsīnalipsā vyākhyātā
07.13.29 pārṣṇigrahaṇābhiyānayoḥ tu mantrayuddhād abhyuccayaḥ
07.13.30 vyāyāmayuddhe hi kṣayavyayābhyāṃ ubhayoravṛddhiḥ
07.13.31 jitvā'pi hi kṣiṇadaṇḍakośaḥ parājito bhavati ityācāryāḥ

07.13.33 sumahatā'pi kṣayavyayena śatruvināśo'bhyupagantavyaḥ
07.13.34 tulye kṣayavyaye yaḥ purastād dūṣyabalaṃ ghātayitvā nihśalyaḥ paścād vaśyabalo yudhyeta so'tisandhatte
07.13.35 dvayorapi purastād dūṣyabalaghātinoryo bahulataraṃ śaktimattaraṃ atyantadūṣyaṃ ca ghātayet so'tisandhatte
07.13.36 tenāmitrāṭavībalaghāto vyākhyātaḥ
07.13.37ab pārṣṇigrāho'bhiyoktā vā yātavyo vā yadā bhavet ।
07.13.37chd vijigīṣuḥ tadā tatra netraṃ etat samācaret

07.13.38chd vigrāhya pūrvaṃ ākrandaṃ pārṣṇigrāhābhisāriṇā

07.13.39chd tathā''krandābhisāreṇa pārṣṇigrāhābhisāriṇam
07.13.40ab arimitreṇa mitraṃ ca purastād avaghaṭṭayet ।
07.13.40chd mitramitraṃ areścāpi mitramitreṇa vārayet

07.14.01 sāmavāyikairevaṃ abhiyukto vijigīṣuryaḥ teṣāṃ pradhānaḥ taṃ brūyāt tvayā me sandhiḥ, idaṃ hiraṇyaṃ, ahaṃ ca mitraṃ, dviguṇā te vṛddhiḥ, nārhasyātmakṣayeṇa mitramukhān amitrān vardhayituṃ, ete hi vṛddhāḥ tvāṃ eva paribhaviṣyanti iti
07.14.02 bhedaṃ vā brūyāt anapakāro yathā'haṃ etaiḥ sambhūyābhiyuktaḥ tathā tvāṃ apyete saṃhitabalāḥ svasthā vyasane vā'bhiyokṣyante, balaṃ hi cittaṃ vikaroti, tad eṣāṃ vighātaya iti
07.14.03 bhinneṣu pradhānaṃ upagṛhya hīneṣu vikramayet, hīnān anugrāhya vā pradhāne, yathā vā śreyo'bhimanyeta tathā
07.14.04 vairaṃ vā parairgrāhayitvā visaṃvādayet
07.14.05 phalabhūyastvena vā pradhānaṃ upajāpya sandhiṃ kārayet
07.14.06 atha ubhayavetanāḥ phalabhūyastvaṃ darśayantaḥ sāmavāyikān atisaṃhitāḥ stha ityudddūṣayeyuḥ
07.14.07 duṣṭeṣu sandhiṃ dūṣayet
07.14.08 atha ubhayavetanā bhūyo bhedaṃ eṣāṃ kuryuḥ evaṃ tad yad asmābhirdarśitam iti
07.14.09 bhinneṣvanyatama upagraheṇa ceṣṭeta
07.14.10 pradhānābhāve sāmavāyikānāṃ utsāhayitāraṃ sthirakarmāṇaṃ anuraktaprakṛktiṃ lobhād bhayād vā saṅghātaṃ upāgataṃ vijigīṣorbhītaṃ rājyapratisambaddhaṃ mitraṃ calāmitraṃ vā pūrvān uttarābhāve sādhayet - utsāhayitāraṃ ātmanisargeṇa, sthirakarmāṇaṃ sāntvapraṇipātena, anuraktaprakṛtiṃ kanyādānayāpanābhyāṃ, lubdhaṃ aṃśadvaiguṇyena, bhītaṃ ebhyaḥ kośadaṇḍānugraheṇa, svato bhītaṃ viśvāsya pratibhūpradānena, rājyapratisambaddhaṃ ekībhāva upagamanena, mitraṃ ubhayataḥ priyahitābhyāṃ, upakāratyāgena vā, calāmitraṃ avadhṛtaṃ anapakāra upakārābhyām
07.14.11 yo vā yathā'yogaṃ bhajeta taṃ tathā sādhayet, sāmadānabhedadaṇḍairvā yathā''patsu vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
07.14.12 vyasana upaghātatvarito vā kośadaṇḍābhyāṃ deśe kāle kārye vā'vadhṛtaṃ sandhiṃ upeyāt
07.14.13 kṛtasandhirhīnaṃ ātmānaṃ pratikurvīta
07.14.14 pakṣe hīno bandhumitrapakṣaṃ kurvīta, durgaṃ aviṣahyaṃ vā
07.14.15 durgamitrapratiṣṭabdho hi sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ ca pūjyo bhavati
07.14.16 mantraśaktihīnaḥ prājñapuruṣa upacayaṃ vidyāvṛddhasamyogaṃ vā kurvīta
07.14.17 tathā hi sadyaḥ śreyaḥ prāpnoti
07.14.18 prabhāvahīnaḥ prakṛtiyogakṣemasiddhau yateta
07.14.19 janapadaḥ sarvakarmaṇāṃ yoniḥ, tataḥ prabhāvaḥ
07.14.20 tasya sthānaṃ ātmanaścāpadi durgam
07.14.21 setubandhaḥ sasyānāṃ yoniḥ
07.14.22 nityānuṣakto hi varṣaguṇalābhaḥ setuvāpeṣu
07.14.23 vaṇikpathaḥ parātisandhānasya yoniḥ
07.14.24 vaṇikpathena hi daṇḍagūḍhapuruṣātinayanaṃ śastrāvaraṇayānavāhanakrayaśca kriyate, praveśo nirṇayanaṃ ca
07.14.25 khaniḥ saṅgrāma upakaraṇānāṃ yoniḥ, dravyavanaṃ durgakarmaṇāṃ yānarathayośca, hastivanaṃ hastināṃ, gavāśvakhara uṣṭrāṇāṃ ca vrajaḥ
07.14.26 teṣāṃ alābhe bandhumitrakulebhyaḥ samārjanam
07.14.27 utsāhahīnaḥ śreṇīpravīrapuruṣāṇāṃ coragaṇāṭavikamlecchajātīnāṃ parāpakāriṇāṃ gūḍhapuruṣāṇāṃ ca yathālābbhaṃ upacayaṃ kurvīta
07.14.28 paramiśrāpratīkāraṃ ābalīyasaṃ vā pareṣu prayuñjīta

07.15.01 durbalo rājā balavatā'bhiyuktaḥ tadviśiṣṭabalaṃ āśrayeta yaṃ itaro mantraśaktyā nātisandadhyāt
07.15.02 tulyamantraśaktīnāṃ āyattasampado vṛddhasamyogād vā viśeṣaḥ
07.15.03 viśiṣṭabalābhāve samabalaiḥ tulyabalasaṅghairvā balavataḥ sambhūya tiṣṭhed yānna mantraprabhāvaśaktibhyāṃ atisandadhyāt
07.15.04 tulyamantraprabhāvaśaktīnāṃ vipulārambhato viśeṣaḥ
07.15.05 samabalābhāve hīnabalaiḥ śucibhirutsāhibhiḥ pratyanīkabhūtairbalavataḥ sambhūya tiṣṭhed yānna mantraprabhāva utsāhaśaktibhiratisandadhyāt
07.15.06 tulya utsāhaśaktīnāṃ svayuddhabhūmilābhād viśeṣaḥ
07.15.07 tulyabhūmīnāṃ svayuddhakālalābhād viśeṣaḥ
07.15.08 tulyadeśakālānāṃ yugyaśastrāvaraṇato viśeṣaḥ
07.15.09 sahāyābhāve durgaṃ āśrayeta yatrāmitraḥ prabhūtasainyo'pi bhaktayavasa indhana udaka uparodhaṃ na kuryāt svayaṃ ca kṣayavyayābhyāṃ yujyeta
07.15.10 tulyadurgāṇāṃ nicayāpasārato viśeṣaḥ
07.15.11 nicayāpasārasampannaṃ hi manuṣyadurgaṃ icched iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.15.12a tad ebhiḥ kārṇairāśrayeta - pārṣṇigrāhaṃ āsāraṃ madhyamaṃ udāsīnaṃ vā pratipādayiṣyāmi, sāmantāṭavikatatkulīnāparuddhānāṃ anyatamenāsya rājyaṃ hārayiṣyāmi ghātayiṣyāmi vā -
07.15.12b kṛtyapakṣa upagraheṇa vā'sya durge rāṣṭre skandhāvāre vā kopaṃ samutthāpayiṣyāmi, śastrāgnirasapraṇidhānairaupaniṣadikairvā yathā iṣṭaṃ āsannaṃ haniṣyāmi -
07.15.12ch svayaṃ'dhiṣṭhitena vā yogapraṇidhānena kṣayavyayaṃ enaṃ upaneṣyāmi, kṣayavyayapravāsa upatapte vā'sya mitravarge sainye vā krameṇa upajāpaṃ prāpsyāmi -
07.15.12d vīvadhāsāraprasāravadhena vā'sya skandhāvārāvagrahaṃ kariṣyāmi, daṇḍa upanayena vā'sya randhraṃ utthāpya sarvasandohena prahariṣyāmi, pratihata utsāhena vā yathā iṣṭaṃ sandhiṃ avāpsyāmi, mayi pratibaddhasya vā sarvataḥ kopāḥ samutthāsyanti -
07.15.12e nirāsāraṃ vā'sya mūlaṃ mitrāṭavīdaṇḍairuddhātayiṣyāmi, mahato vā deśasya yogakṣemaṃ ihasthaḥ pālayiṣyāmi, svavikṣiptaṃ mitravikṣiptaṃ vā me sainyaṃ ihasthasya ekasthaṃ aviṣahyaṃ bhaviṣyati, nimnakhātarātriyuddhaviśāradaṃ vā me sainyaṃ pathyābādhamuktaṃ āsanne karma kariṣyati -
07.15.12f viruddhadeśakālaṃ ihāgato vā svayaṃ eva kṣayavyayābhyāṃ na bhaviṣyati, mahākṣayavyayābhigamyo'yaṃ deśo durgāṭavy'pasārabāhulyāt -
07.15.12g pareṣāṃ vyādhiprāyaḥ sainyavyāyāmānāṃ alabdhabhaumaśca, taṃ āpadgataḥ pravekṣyati, praviṣṭo vā na nirgamiṣyati iti
07.15.13 kāraṇābhāve balasamucchraye vā parasya durgaṃ unmucyāpagacchet
07.15.14 agnipataṅgavad amitre vā praviśet
07.15.15 anyatarasiddhirhi tyaktātmano bhavati ityācāryāḥ
07.15.16 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.15.17 sandheyatāṃ ātmanaḥ parasya ca upalabhya sandadhīta
07.15.18 viparyaye vikrameṇa sandhiṃ apasāraṃ vā lipseta
07.15.19 sandheyasya vā dūtaṃ preṣayet
07.15.20 tena vā preṣitaṃ arthamānābhyāṃ satkṛtya brūyāt idaṃ rājñaḥ paṇyāgāraṃ, idaṃ devīkumārāṇāṃ, devīkumāravacanāt, idaṃ rājyaṃ ahaṃ ca tvad'rpaṇaḥ iti
07.15.21 labdhasaṃśrayaḥ samayācārikavad bhartari varteta
07.15.22 durgādīni ca karmāṇi āvāhavivāhaputrābhiṣekāśvapaṇyahastigrahaṇasattrayātrāvihāragamanāni cānujñātaḥ kurvīta
07.15.23 svabhūmy'vasthitaprakṛtisandhiṃ upaghātaṃ apasṛteṣu vā sarvaṃ anujñātaḥ kurvīta
07.15.24 duṣṭapaurajānapado vā nyāyavṛttiranyāṃ bhūmiṃ yāceta
07.15.25 duṣyavad upāṃśudaṇḍena vā pratikurvīta
07.15.26 ucitāṃ vā mitrād bhūmiṃ dīyamānāṃ na pratigṛhṇīyāt
07.15.27 mantripurohitasenāpatiyuvarājānāṃ anyatamaṃ adṛśyamāne bhartari paśyet, yathāśakti ca upakuryāt
07.15.28 daivatasvastivācaneṣu tatparā āśiṣo vācayet
07.15.29 sarvatrātmanisargaṃ guṇaṃ brūyāt
07.15.30ab samyuktabalavatsevī viruddhaḥ śaṅkitādibhiḥ ।

07.16.01 anujñātasandhipaṇa udvegakaraṃ balavān vijigīṣamāṇo yataḥ svabhūmiḥ sva।ṛtuvṛttiśca svasainyānāṃ, adurgāpasāraḥ śatrur'pārṣṇiranāsāraśca, tato yāyāt
07.16.02 viparyaye kṛtapratīkāro yāyāt

07.16.05 grāmāraṇya upajīvivrajavaṇikpathānupālanaṃ ujjhitāpasṛtāpakāriṇāṃ cārpaṇaṃ iti sāntvaṃ ācaret

07.16.10 teṣāṃ paṇyapattanagrāmakhanisañjātena ratnasāraphalgukupyena dravyahastivanavrajasamutthena yānavāhanena vā yad bahuśa upakaroti taccitrabhogam

07.16.16a pārṣṇigrāhaścāṭavikaḥ śatrumukhyaḥ śatrurvā bhūmidānasādhyaḥ kaścid āsādyeta, nirguṇayā bhūmyā enaṃ upagrāhayet, apratisambaddhayā durgasthaṃ, nirupajīvyayā''ṭavikaṃ -
07.16.16b pratyādeyayā tatkulīnaṃ śatroḥ, apacchinnayā śatroraparuddhaṃ nityāmitrayā śreṇībalaṃ, balavatsāmantayā saṃhatabalaṃ, ubhābhyāṃ yuddhe pratilomaṃ, -
07.16.16ch alabdhavyāyāmayā utsāhinaṃ, śūyayā'ripakṣīyaṃ, karśitayā'pavāhitaṃ, mahākṣayavyayaniveśayā gatapratyāgataṃ, anapāśrayayā pratyapasṛtaṃ, pareṇānadhivāsyayā svayaṃ eva bhartāraṃ upagrāhayet
07.16.17 teṣāṃ mahā upakāraṃ nirvikāraṃ cānuvartayet
07.16.18 pratilomaṃ upāṃśunā sādhayet
07.16.19 upakāriṇaṃ upakāraśaktyā toṣayet

07.16.22 paribhava upaghātakutsātivādāṃśca eṣu na prayuñjīta
07.16.23 dattvā cābhayaṃ pitā ivānugṛhṇīyāt

07.16.32 svayaṃ vā rājyaṃ prāṇān vā'syābhimanyante

07.17.01 śamaḥ sandhiḥ samādhirityeko'rthaḥ
07.17.02 rājñāṃ viśvāsa upagamaḥ śamaḥ sandhiḥ samādhiriti
07.17.03 satyaṃ śapatho vā calaḥ sandhiḥ, pratibhūḥ pratigraho vā sthāvaraḥ ityācāryāḥ
07.17.04 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
07.17.05 satyaṃ śapatho vā paratra iha ca sthāvaraḥ sandhiḥ, ihārtha eva pratibhūḥ pratigraho vā balāpekṣaḥ
07.17.06 saṃhitāḥ smaḥ iti satyasandhāḥ pūrve rājānaḥ satyena sandadhire
07.17.07 tasyātikrame śapathena agny।udakasītāprākāraloṣṭahastiskandhāśvapṛṣṭaratha upasthaśastraratnabījagandharasasuvarṇahiraṇyānyālebhire hanyuretāni tyajeyuśca enaṃ yaḥ śapathaṃ atikrāmet iti
07.17.08 śapathātikrame mahatāṃ tapasvināṃ mukhyānāṃ vā prātibhāvyabandhaḥ pratibhūḥ

07.17.10 viparīto'tisandhīyate
07.17.11 bandhumukhyapragrahaḥ pratigrahaḥ
07.17.12 tasmin yo dūṣyāmātyaṃ dūṣyāpatyaṃ vā dadāti, so'tisandhatte
07.17.13 viparīto'tisandhīyate
07.17.14 pratigrahagrahaṇaviśvastasya hi paraśchidreṣu nirapekṣaḥ praharati
07.17.15 apatyasamādhau tu kanyāputradāne dadat tu kanyāṃ atisandhatte
07.17.16 kanyā hyadāyādā pareṣāṃ evārthāyākleśyā(?) ca
07.17.17 viparītaḥ putraḥ
07.17.18 putrayorapi yo jātyaṃ prājñaṃ śūraṃ kṛtāstraṃ ekaputraṃ vā dadāti so'tisandhīyate
07.17.19 viparīto'tisandhatte
07.17.20 jātyād ajātyo hi luptadāyādasantānatvād ādhātuṃ śreyān, prājñād aprājño mantraśaktilopāt, śūrād aśūra utsāhaśaktilopāt, kṛtāstrād akṛtāstraḥ prahartavyasampallopāt, ekaputrād anekaputro nirapekṣatvāt
07.17.21 jātyaprājñayorjātyaṃ aprājñaṃ aiśvaryaprakṛtiranuvartate, prājñaṃ ajātyaṃ mantrādhikāraḥ
07.17.22 mantrādhikāre'pi vṛddhasamyogāj jātyaḥ prājñaṃ atisandhatte
07.17.23 prājñaśūrayoḥ prājñaṃ aśūraṃ matikarmaṇāṃ yogo'nuvartate, śūraṃ aprājñaṃ vikramādhikāraḥ
07.17.24 vikramādhikāre'pi hastinaṃ iva lubdhakaḥ prājñaḥ śūraṃ atisandhatteś
07.17.25 śūrakṛtāstrayoḥ śūraṃ akṛtāstraṃ vikramavyavasāyo'nuvartate, kṛtāstraṃ aśūraṃ lakṣyalambhādhikāraḥ
07.17.26 lakṣyalambhādhikāre'pi sthairyapratipatty'sammoṣaiḥ śūraḥ kṛtāstraṃ atisandhatte
07.17.27 bahv।ekaputrayorbahuputra ekaṃ dattvā śeṣapratiṣṭabdhaḥ sandhiṃ atikrāmati, na itaraḥ
07.17.28 putrasarvasvadāne sandhiścet putraphalato viśeṣaḥ
07.17.29 samaphalayoḥ śaktaprajananato viśeṣaḥ
07.17.30 śaktaprajananayorapyupasthitaprajananato viśeṣaḥ
07.17.31 śaktimatyekaputre tu luptaputra utpattirātmānaṃ ādadhyāt, na ca ekaputraṃ iti
07.17.32 abhyuccīyamānaḥ samādhimokṣaṃ kārayet
07.17.33 kumārāsannāḥ sattriṇaḥ kāruśilpivyañjanāḥ karmāṇi kurvāṇāḥ suruṅgayā rātrāvupakhānayitvā kumāraṃ apahareyuḥ

07.17.41 paricārakacchadmanā vā kiñcid arūpavelāyāṃ ādāya nirgacchet, suruṅgāmukhena vā niśā upahāreṇa
07.17.42 toyāśaye vā vāruṇaṃ yogaṃ ātiṣṭhet

   Chapt .   madhyamacaritaṃ - udāsīnacaritaṃ - maṇḍalacaritam
07.18.01 madhyamasyātmā tṛtīyā pañcamī ca prakṛtī prakṛtayaḥ
07.18.02 dvitīyā caturthī ṣaṣṭhī ca vikṛtayaḥ
07.18.03 tacced ubhayaṃ madhyamo'nugṛhṇīyāt, vijigīṣurmadhyamānulomaḥ syāt
07.18.04 na ced anugṛhṇīyāt, prakṛty'nulomaḥ syāt
07.18.05 madyamaśced vijigīṣormitraṃ mitrabhāvi lipseta, mitrasyātmanaśca mitrāṇyutthāpya madhyamācca mitrāṇi bhedayitvā mitraṃ trāyeta
07.18.06 maṇḍalaṃ vā protsāhayet atipravṛddho'yaṃ madhyamaḥ sarveṣāṃ no vināśāyābhyutthitaḥ, sambhūyāsya yātrāṃ vihanāma iti
07.18.07 taccen maṇḍalaṃ anugṛhṇīyāt, madhyamāvagraheṇātmānaṃ upabṛṃhayet
07.18.08 na ced anugṛhṇīyāt, kośadaṇḍābhyāṃ mitraṃ anugṛhya ye madhyamadveṣiṇo rājānaḥ parasparānugṛhītā vā bahavaḥ tiṣṭheyuḥ, ekasiddhau vā bahavaḥ sidhyeyuḥ, parasparād vā śaṅkitā na uttiṣṭheran, teṣāṃ pradhānaṃ ekaṃ āsannaṃ vā sāmadānābhyāṃ labheta
07.18.09 dviguṇo dvitīyaṃ trigunaḥ tṛtīyam
07.18.10 evaṃ abhyuccito madhyamaṃ avagṛhṇīyāt
07.18.11 deśakālātipattau vā sandhāya madhyamena mitrasya sācivyaṃ kuryāt, dūṣyeṣu vā karmasandhim
07.18.12 karśanīyaṃ vā'sya mitraṃ madhyamo lipseta, pratistambhayed enaṃ ahaṃ tvā trāyeya iti ā karśanāt
07.18.13 karśitaṃ enaṃ trāyeta
07.18.14 ucchedanīyaṃ vā'sya mitraṃ madhyamo lipseta, karśitaṃ enaṃ trāyeta madhyamavṛddhibhayāt
07.18.15 ucchinnaṃ vā bhūmy'nugraheṇa haste kuryād anyatrāpasārabhayāt
07.18.16 karśanīya ucchedanīyayoścen mitrāṇi madhyamasya sācivyakarāṇi syuḥ, puruṣāntareṇa sandhīyeta
07.18.17 vijigīṣorvā tayormitrāṇyavagrahasamarthāni syuḥ, sandhiṃ upeyāt
07.18.18 amitraṃ vā'sya madhyamo lipseta, sandhiṃ upeyāt
07.18.19 evaṃ svārthaśca kṛto bhavati madhyamasya priyaṃ ca
07.18.20 madhyamaścet svamitraṃ mitrabhāvi lipseta, puruṣāntareṇa sandadhyāt
07.18.21 sāpekṣaṃ vā nārhasi mitraṃ ucchettum iti vārayet
07.18.22 upekṣeta vā maṇḍalaṃ asya kupyatu svapakṣavadhāt iti
07.18.23 amitraṃ ātmano vā madhyamo lipseta, kośadaṇḍābhyāṃ enaṃ adṛśyamāno'nugṛhṇīyāt
07.18.24 udāsīnaṃ vā madhyamo lipseta, asmai sāhāyyaṃ dadyād udāsīnād bhidyatām iti
07.18.25 madhyama udāsīnayoryo maṇḍalasyābhipretaḥ taṃ āśrayeta
07.18.26 madhyamacaritena udāsīnacaritaṃ vyākhyātam
07.18.27 udāsīnaścen madhyamaṃ lipseta, yataḥ śatruṃ atisandadhyān mitrasya upakāraṃ kuryād udāsīnaṃ vā daṇḍa upakāriṇaṃ labheta tataḥ pariṇameta
07.18.28 evaṃ upabṛhyātmānaṃ ariprakṛtiṃ karśayen mitraprakṛtiṃ ca upagṛhṇīyāt
07.18.29a satyapyamitrabhāve tasyānātmavānnityāpakārī śatruḥ śatrusaṃhitaḥ pārṣṇigrāho vā vyasanī yātavyo vyasane vā neturabhiyoktā ityaribhāvinaḥ, ekārthābhiprayātaḥ pṛthag'rthābhiprayātaḥ sambhūyayātrikaḥ saṃhitaprayāṇikaḥ svārthābhiprayātaḥ sāmutthāyikaḥ kośadaṇḍayoranyatarasya kretā vikretā vā dvaidhībhāvika iti mitrabhāvinaḥ, -
07.18.29b sāmanto balavataḥ pratighāto'ntardhiḥ prativeśo vā balavataḥ pārṣṇigrāho vā svayaṃ upanataḥ pratāpa upanato vā daṇḍa upanata iti bhṛtyabhāvinaḥ sāmantāḥ
07.18.30 tairbhūmy।ekāntarā vyākhyātāḥ
07.18.31ab teṣāṃ śatruvirodhe yan mitraṃ ekārthatāṃ vrajet ।
07.18.31chd śaktyā tad'nugṛhṇīyād viṣaheta yayā param
07.18.32ab prasādhya śatruṃ yan mitraṃ vṛddhaṃ gacched avaśyatām ।
07.18.32chd sāmanta ekāntarābhyāṃ tatprakṛtibhyāṃ virodhayet
07.18.33ab tatkulīnāparuddhābhyāṃ bhūmiṃ vā tasya hārayet ।
07.18.33chd yathā vā'nugrahāpekṣaṃ vaśyaṃ tiṣṭhet tathā caret
07.18.34ab na upakuryād amitraṃ vā gacched yad atikarśitam ।
07.18.34chd tad ahīnaṃ avṛddhaṃ ca sthāpayen mitraṃ arthavit
07.18.35ab arthayuktyā calaṃ mitraṃ sandhiṃ yad upagacchati ।
07.18.35chd tasyāpagamane hetuṃ vihanyānna caled yathā
07.18.36ab arisādhāraṇaṃ yad vā tiṣṭhet tad aritaḥ śaṭham ।
07.18.36chd bhedayed bhinnaṃ ucchindyāt tataḥ śatruṃ anantaram
07.18.37ab udāsīnaṃ ca yat tiṣṭhet sāmantaiḥ tad virodhayet ।
07.18.37chd tato vigrahasantaptaṃ upakāre niveśayet
07.18.38ab amitraṃ vijigīṣuṃ ca yat sañcarati durbalam ।
07.18.38chd tad balenānugṛhṇīyād yathā syānna parānmukham
07.18.39ab apanīya tato'nyasyāṃ bhūmau vā samniveśayet ।
07.18.39chd niveśya pūrvaṃ tatrānyad daṇḍānugrahahetunā
07.18.40ab apakuryāt samarthaṃ vā na upakuryād yad āpadi ।
07.18.40chd ucchindyād eva tanmitraṃ viśvasyāṅkaṃ upasthitam
07.18.41ab mitravyasanato vā'riruttiṣṭhed yo'navagrahaḥ ।
07.18.41chd mitreṇa eva bhavet sādhyaśchāditavyasanena saḥ
07.18.41ab amitravyasanān mitraṃ utthitaṃ yad virajyati ।
07.18.41chd arivyasanasiddhyā tatśatruṇā eva prasidhyati
07.18.42ab vṛddhiṃ kṣayaṃ ca sthānaṃ ca karśana ucchedanaṃ tathā

08.2.05 dvairājyavairājyayordvairājyaṃ anyonyapakṣadveṣānurāgābhyāṃ parasparasaṅgharṣeṇa vā vinaśyati, vairājyaṃ tu prakṛticittagrahaṇāpekṣi yathāsthitaṃ anyairbhujyate ityācāryāḥ

08.2.14 na iti kauṭilyaḥ

08.4.01 daivapīḍanaṃ - agnirudakaṃ vyādhirdurbhikṣaṃ maraka iti
08.4.02 agny।udakayoragnipīḍanaṃ apratikāryaṃ sarvadāhi ca, śakyāpagamanaṃ tāryābādhaṃ udakapīḍanam ityācāryāḥ

08.4.05 vyādhidurbhikṣayorvyādhiḥ pretavyādhita upasṛṣṭaparicārakavyāyāma uparodhena karmāṇyupahanti, durbhikṣaṃ punarakarma upaghāti hiraṇyapaśukaradāyi ca ityācāryāḥ
08.4.06 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.07 ekadeśapīḍano vyādhiḥ śakyapratīkāraśca, sarvadeśapīḍanaṃ durbhikṣaṃ prāṇināṃ ajīvanāya iti
08.4.08 tena marako vyākhyātaḥ
08.4.09 kṣudrakamukhyakṣayayoḥ kṣudrakakṣayaḥ karmaṇāṃ ayogakṣemaṃ karoti, mukhyakṣayaḥ karmānuṣṭhāna uparodhadharmā ityācāryāḥ
08.4.10 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.11 śakyaḥ kṣudrakakṣayaḥ pratisandhātuṃ bāhulyāt kṣudrakāṇāṃ, na mukhyakṣayaḥ
08.4.12 sahasreṣu hi mukhyo bhavatyeko na vā sattvaprajñā''dhikyāt tad।āśrayatvāt kṣudrakāṇāṃ iti
08.4.13 svacakraparacakrayoḥ svacakraṃ atimātrābhyāṃ daṇḍakarābhyāṃ pīḍayatyaśakyaṃ ca vārayituṃ, paracakraṃ tu śakyaṃ praiyoddhuṃ upasāreṇa sandhinā vā mokṣayitum ityācāryāḥ
08.4.14 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.15 svacakrapīḍanaṃ prakṛtipuruṣamukhya upagrahavighātābhyāṃ śakyate vārayituṃ ekadeśaṃ vā pīḍayati, sarvadeśapīḍanaṃ tu paracakraṃ vilopaghātadāhavidhvaṃsanāpavāhanaiḥ pīḍayati iti
08.4.16 prakṛtirājavivādayoḥ prakṝtivivādaḥ prakṛtīnāṃ bhedakaḥ parābhiyogān āvahati, rājavivādaḥ tu prakṛtīnāṃ dviguṇabhaktavetanaparihārakaro bhavati ityācāryāḥ
08.4.17 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.18 śakyaḥ prakṛtivivādaḥ prakṛtimukhya upagraheṇa kalahasthānāpanayanena vā vārayitum
08.4.19 vivadamānāḥ tu prakṛtayaḥ parasparasaṅgharṣeṇa upakurvanti
08.4.20 rājavivādaḥ tu pīḍana ucchedanāya prakṛtīnāṃ dviguṇavyāyāmasādhya iti
08.4.21 deśarājavihārayordeśavihāraḥ traikālyena karmaphala upaghātaṃ karoti, rājavihāraḥ tu kāruśilpikuśīlavavāgjīvanarūpājīvāvaidehaka upakāraṃ karoti ityācāryāḥ
08.4.22 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.23 deśavihāraḥ karmaśramaṃ avadhā'rthaṃ alpaṃ bhakṣayati bhakṣayitvā ca bhūyaḥ karmasu yogaṃ gacchati, rājavihāraḥ tu svayaṃ vallabhaiśca svayaṅgrāhapraṇayapaṇyāgārakārya upagrahaiḥ pīḍayati iti
08.4.24 subhagākumārayoḥ kumāraḥ svayaṃ vallabhaiśca svayaṅgrāhapraṇayapaṇyāgārakārya upagrahaiḥ pīḍayati, subhagā vilāsa upabhogena ityācāryāḥ
08.4.25 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.26 śakyaḥ kumāro mantripurohitābhyāṃ vārayituṃ, na subhagā bāliśyād anarthyajanasamyogācca iti
08.4.27 śreṇīmukhyayoḥ śreṇī bāhulyād anavagrahā steyasāhasābhyāṃ pīḍayati, mukhyaḥ kāryānugrahavighātābhyām ityācāryāḥ
08.4.28 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.29 suvyāvartyā śreṇī samānaśīlavyasanatvāt, śreṇīmukhya ekadeśa upagraheṇa vā
08.4.30 stambhayukto mukhyaḥ paraprāṇadravya upaghātābhyāṃ pīḍayati iti
08.4.31 samnidhātṛsamāhartroḥ samnidhātā kṛtavidūṣaṇātyayābhyāṃ pīḍayati, samāhartā karaṇādhiṣṭhitaḥ pradiṣṭaphala upabhogī bhavati ityācāryāḥ
08.4.32 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.33 samnidhātā kṛtāvasthaṃ anyaiḥ kośapraveśyaṃ pratigṛhṇāti, samāhartā tu pūrvaṃ arthaṃ ātmanaḥ kṛtvā paścād rājārthaṃ karoti praṇāśayati vā, parasvādāne ca svapratyayaścarati iti
08.4.34 antapālavaidehakayorantapālaścoraprasargadeyātyādānābhyāṃ vaṇikpathaṃ pīḍayati, vaidehakāḥ tu paṇya।pratipaṇyānugrahaiḥ prasādhayanti ityācāryāḥ
08.4.35 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.36 antapālaḥ paṇyasampātānugraheṇa vartayati, vaidehakāḥ tu sambhūya paṇyānāṃ utkarṣāpakarṣaṃ kurvāṇāḥ paṇe paṇaśataṃ kumbhe kumbhaśataṃ ityājīvanti
08.4.37 abhijāta uparuddhā bhūmiḥ paśuvraja uparuddhā vā iti abhijāta uparuddhā bhūmiḥ mahāphalā'pyāyudhīya upakāriṇī na kṣamā mokṣayituṃ vyasanābādhabhayāt, paśuvraja uparuddhā tu kṛṣiyogyā kṣamā mokṣayitum
08.4.38 vivītaṃ hi kṣetreṇa bādhyate ityācāryāḥ
08.4.39 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.40 abhijāta uparuddhā bhūmiratyantamahā upakārā'pi kṣamā mokṣayituṃ vyasanābādhabhayāt, paśuvraja uparuddhā tu kośavāhana upakāriṇī na kṣamā mokṣayituṃ, anyatra sasyavāpa uparodhād iti
08.4.41 pratirodhakāṭavikayoḥ pratirodhakā rātrisattracarāḥ śarīrākramiṇo nityāḥ śatasahasrāhapāriṇaḥ pradhānakopakāśca vyavahitāḥ pratyantarāraṇyacarāścāṭavikāḥ prakāśā dṛsyāścaranti, ekadeśaghātakāśca ityācāryāḥ
08.4.42 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
08.4.43 pratirodhakāḥ pramattasyāparahanti, alpāḥ kuṇṭhāḥ sukhā jñātuṃ grahītuṃ ca, svadeśasthāḥ prabhūtā vikrāntāścāṭavikāḥ prakāśayodino'pahartāro hantāraśca deśānāṃ rājasadharmāṇa iti
08.4.44 mṛgahastivanayoḥ mṛgāḥ prabhūtāḥ prabhūtamāṃsacarma upakāriṇo mandagrāsāvakleśinaḥ suniyamyāśca
08.4.45 viparītā hastino gṛhyamāṇā duṣṭāśca deśavināśāya iti
08.4.46 svaparasthānīya upakārayoḥ svasthānīya upakāro dhānyapaśuhiraṇyakupya upakāro jānapadānāṃ āpadyātmadhāraṇaḥ
08.4.47 viparītaḥ parasthānīya upakāraḥ
08.4.48 iti pīḍanāni - ābhyantaro mukhyastambho bāhyo'mitrāṭavīstambhaḥ iti stambhavargah
08.4.49 tābhyāṃ pīḍanairyathā uktaiśca pīḍitaḥ, sakto mukhyeṣu, parihāra upahataḥ, prakīrṇo, mithyāsaṃhṛtaḥ, sāmantāṭavīhṛta iti kośasaṅgavargaḥ
08.4.50ab pīḍanānāṃ anutpattāvutpannānāṃ ca vāraṇe ।
08.4.50chd yateta deśavṛddhy'rthaṃ nāśe ca stambhasaṅgayoḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   balavyasanavargaḥ - mitravyasanavargaḥ
08.5.01 balavyasanāni - amānitaṃ, vimānitaṃ, abhṛtaṃ, vyādhitaṃ, navāgataṃ, dūrāyātaṃ, pariśrāntaṃ, parikṣīṇaṃ, pratihataṃ, hatāgravegaṃ, anṛtuprāptaṃ, abhūmiprāptaṃ, āśānirvedi, parisṛptaṃ, kalatragarbhi, antaḥśalyaṃ, kupitamūlaṃ, bhinnagarbhaṃ, apasṛtaṃ, atikṣiptaṃ, upaniviṣṭaṃ, samāptaṃ, uparuddhaṃ, parikṣiptaṃ, chinnadhānyapuruṣavīvadhaṃ, svavikṣiptaṃ, mitravikṣiptaṃ, dūṣyayuktaṃ, duṣṭapārṣṇigrāhaṃ, śūnyamūlaṃ, asvāmisaṃhataṃ, bhinnakūṭaṃ, andhaṃ iti
08.5.02 teṣāṃ amānitavimānitāniyatayoramānitaṃ kṛtārthamānaṃ yudhyeta, na vimānitaṃ antaḥkopam
08.5.03 abhṛtavyādhitayorabhṛtaṃ tadātvakṛtavetanaṃ yudhyeta, na vyādhitaṃ akarmaṇyam
08.5.04 navāgatadūrāyātayornavāgataṃ anyata upalabdhadeśaṃ anavamiśraṃ yudhyeta, na dūrāyataṃ āyatagataparikleśam
08.5.05 pariśrāntaparikṣīṇayoḥ pariśrāntaṃ snānabhojanasvapnalabdhaviśrāmaṃ yudhyeta, na parikṣīṇaṃ anyatrāhave kṣīṇayugyapuruṣam
08.5.06 pratihatahatāgravegayoḥ pratihataṃ agrapātabhagnaṃ pravīrapuruṣasaṃhataṃ yudhyeta, na hatāgravegaṃ agrapātahatavīram
08.5.07 anṛtv'bhūmiprāptayoranṛtuprāptaṃ yatha।ṛtuyugyaśastrāvaraṇaṃ yudhyeta, nābhūmiprāptaṃ avaruddhaprasāravyāyāmam
08.5.08 āśānirvediparisṛptayorāśānirvedi labdhābhiprāyaṃ yudhyeta, na parisṛptaṃ apasṛtamukhyam
08.5.09 kalatragarbhy'ntaḥśalyayoḥ kalatragarbhi unmucya kalatraṃ yudhyeta, nāntaḥśalyaṃ antaramitram
08.5.10 kupitamūlabhinnagarbhayoḥ kupitamūlaṃ praśamitakopaṃ sāmādibhiryudhyeta, na bhinnagarbhaṃ anyonyasmād bhinnam
08.5.11 apasṛtātikṣiptayorapasṛtaṃ ekarājyātikrāntaṃ mantravyāyāmābhyāṃ sattramitrāpāśrayaṃ yudhyeta, nātikṣiptaṃ anekarājyātikrāntaṃ bahv।ābādhatvāt
08.5.12 upaniviṣṭasamāptayorupaniviṣṭaṃ pṛthagyānasthānaṃ atisandhāyāriṃ yudhyeta, na samāptaṃ ariṇā ekasthānayānam
08.5.13 uparuddhaparikṣiptayoruparuddhaṃ anyato niṣkramya uparoddhāraṃ pratiyudhyeta, na parikṣiptaṃ sarvataḥ pratiruddham
08.5.14 chinnadhānyapuruṣavīvadhayoḥ chinnadhānyaṃ anyato dhānyaṃ ānīya jaṅgamasthāvarāhāraṃ vā yudhyeta, na chinnapuruṣavīvadhaṃ anabhisāram
08.5.15 svavikṣiptamitravikṣiptayoḥ svavikṣiptaṃ svabhūmau vikṣiptaṃ sainyaṃ āpadi śakyaṃ āvāhayituṃ, na mitravikṣiptaṃ viprakṛṣṭadeśakālatvāt
08.5.16 dūṣyayuktaduṣṭapārṣṇigrāhayordūṣyayuktaṃ āptapuruṣādhiṣṭhitaṃ asaṃhataṃ yudhyeta, na duṣṭapārṣṇigrāhaṃ pṛṣṭhābhighātatrastam
08.5.17 śūnyamūlāsvāmisaṃhatayoḥ śūnyamūlaṃ kṛtapaurajānapadārakṣaṃ sarvasandohena yudhyeta, nāsvāmisaṃhataṃ rājasenāpatihīnam
08.5.18 bhinnakūṭāndhayorbhinnakūṭaṃ anyādhiṣṭhitaṃ yudhyeta, nāndhaṃ adeśikaṃ - iti
08.5.19ab doṣaśuddhirbalāvāpaḥ sattrasthānātisaṃhitam ।
08.5.19chd sandhiśca uttarapakṣasya balavyasanasādhanam
08.5.20ab rakṣet svadaṇḍaṃ vyasane śatrubhyo nityaṃ utthitaḥ ।
08.5.20chd prahared daṇḍarandhreṣu śatrūṇāṃ nityaṃ utthitaḥ
08.5.21ab yato nimittaṃ vyasanaṃ prakṛtīnāṃ avāpnuyāt ।
08.5.21chd prāg eva pratikurvīta tannimittaṃ atandritaḥ ।
08.5.22ab abhiyātaṃ svayaṃ mitraṃ sambhūyānyavaśena vā
08.5.22chd parityaktaṃ aśaktyā vā lobhena praṇayena vā ।
08.5.23ab vikrītaṃ abhiyuñjāne saṅgrāme vā'pavartinā
08.5.23chd dvaidhībhāvena vā'mitraṃ yāsyatā vā'nyaṃ anyataḥ ।
08.5.24ab pṛthag vā sahayāne vā viśvāsenātisaṃhitam
08.5.24chd bhayāvamānālasyairvā vyasanānna pramokṣitam ।
08.5.25ab avaruddhaṃ svabhūmibhyaḥ samīpād vā bhayād gatam
08.5.25chd ācchedanād adānād vā dattvā vā'pyavamānitam ।
08.5.26ab atyāhāritaṃ arthaṃ vā svayaṃ paramukhena vā
08.5.26chd atibhāre niyuktaṃ vā bhaṅktvā paraṃ upasthitam ।
08.5.27ab upekṣitaṃ aśaktyā vā prārthayitvā virodhitam
08.5.27chd kṛcchreṇa sādhyate mitraṃ siddhaṃ cāśu virajyati ।
08.5.28ab kṛtaprayāsaṃ mānyaṃ vā mohān mitraṃ amānitam ।
08.5.28chd mānitaṃ vā na sadṛśaṃ śaktito vā nivāritam
08.5.29ab mitra upaghātatrastaṃ vā śaṅkitaṃ vā'risaṃhitāt ।
08.5.29chd dūṣyairvā bhedituṃ mitraṃ sādhyaṃ siddhaṃ ca tiṣṭhati
08.5.30ab tasmānna utpādayed enān doṣān mitra upaghātakān ।
08.5.30chd utpannān vā praśamayed guṇairdoṣa upaghātibhiḥ  (iti)

   Chapt .   śaktideśakālabalābalajñānaṃ - yātrākālāḥ
09.1.01 vijigīṣurātmanaḥ parasya ca balābalaṃ śaktideśakālayātrākālabalasamuddānakālapaścātkopakṣayavyayalābhāpadāṃ jñātvā viśiṣṭabalo yāyāt, anyathā''sīta
09.1.02 utsāhaprabhāvayorutsāhaḥ śreyān
09.1.03 svayaṃ hi rājā śūro balavān arogaḥ kṛtāstro daṇḍadvitīyo'pi śaktaḥ prabhāvavantaṃ rājānaṃ jetum
09.1.04 alpo'pi cāsya daṇḍaḥ tejasā kṛtyakaro bhavati
09.1.05 nirutsāhaḥ tu prabhāvavān rājā vikramābhipanno naśyati ityācāryāḥ
09.1.06 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
09.1.07 prabhāvavān utsāhavantaṃ rājānaṃ prabhāvenātisandhatte tadviśiṣṭaṃ anyaṃ rājānaṃ āvāhya bhṛtvā krītvā pravīrapuruṣān
09.1.08 prabhūtaprabhāvahayahastiratha upakaraṇasampannaścāsya daṇḍaḥ sarvatrāpratihataścarati
09.1.09 utsāhavataśca prabhāvavanto jitvā krītvā ca striyo bālāḥ paṅgavo'ndhāśca pṛthivīṃ jigyuriti
09.1.10 prabhāvamantrayoḥ prabhāvaḥ śreyān
09.1.11 mantraśaktisampanno hi vandhyabuddhiraprabhāvo bhavati
09.1.12 mantrakarma cāsya niścitaṃ aprabhāvo garbhadhānyaṃ avṛṣṭiriva upahanti ityācāryāḥ
09.1.13 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
09.1.14 mantraśaktiḥ śreyasī
09.1.15 prajñāśāstracakṣurhi rājā'lpenāpi prayatnena mantraṃ ādhātuṃ śaktaḥ parān utsāhaprabhāvavataśca sāmādibhiryoga upaniṣadbhyāṃ cātisandhātum
09.1.16 evaṃ utsāhaprabhāvamantraśaktīnāṃ uttara uttarādhiko'tisandhatte
09.1.17 deśaḥ pṛthivī
09.1.18 tasyāṃ himavatsamudrāntaraṃ udīcīnaṃ yojanasahasraparimāṇaṃ tiryak cakravartikṣetram
09.1.19 tatrāraṇyo grāmyaḥ parvata audako bhaumaḥ samo viṣama iti viśeṣāḥ
09.1.20 teṣu yathāsvabalavṛddhikaraṃ karma prayuñjīta
09.1.21 yatrātmanaḥ sainyavyāyāmānāṃ bhūmiḥ, abhūmiḥ parasya, sa uttamo deśaḥ, viparīto'dhamaḥ, sādhāraṇo madhyamaḥ
09.1.22 kālaḥ śīta uṣṇavarṣātmā
09.1.23 tasya rātrirahaḥ pakṣo māsa ṛturayanaṃ saṃvatsaro yugaṃ iti viśeṣāḥ
09.1.24 teṣu yathāsvabalavṛddhikaraṃ karmaprayuñjīta
09.1.25 yatrātmanaḥ sainyavyāyāmānāṃ ṛtuḥ anṛtuḥ parasya, sa uttamaḥ kālaḥ, viparīto'dhamaḥ, sādhāraṇo madhyamaḥ
09.1.26 śaktideśakālānāṃ tu śaktiḥ śreyasī ityācāryāḥ
09.1.27 śaktimān hi nimnasthalavato deśasya śīta uṣṇavarṣavataśca kālasya śaktaḥ pratīkāre bhavati
09.1.28 deśaḥ śreyān ityeke

09.1.30 kālaḥ śreyān ityeke

09.1.32 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
09.1.33 parasparasādhakā hi śaktideśakālāḥ
09.1.34 tairabhyuccitaḥ tṛtīyaṃ caturthaṃ vā daṇḍasyāṃśaṃ mūle pārṣṇyāṃ pratyantāṭavīṣu ca rakṣā vidhāya kāryasādhanasahaṃ kośadaṇḍaṃ cādāya kṣīṇapurāṇabhaktaṃ agṛhītanavabhaktaṃ asaṃskṛtadurgamamitraṃ vārṣikaṃ cāsya sasyaṃ haimanaṃ ca muṣṭiṃ upahantuṃ mārgaśīrṣīṃ yātrāṃ yāyāt
09.1.35 haimānaṃ cāsya sasyaṃ vāsantikaṃ ca muṣṭiṃ upahantuṃ caitrīṃ yātrāṃ yāyāt
09.1.36 kṣīṇakṛṇakāṣṭha udakaṃ asaṃskṛtadurgamamitraṃ vāsantikaṃ cāsya sasyaṃ vārṣikīṃ ca muṣṭiṃ upahantuṃ jyeṣṭhāmūlīyāṃ yātrāṃ yāyāt
09.1.37 atyuṣṇaṃ alpayavasa indhana udakaṃ vā deśaṃ hemante yāyāt

09.1.41 vyasanābhiyānaṃ vigṛhyayāne vyākhyātam

09.1.46 hastino hyantaḥsvedāḥ kuṣṭhino bhavanti

09.1.52chd dīrghāḥ kāryagurutvād vā varṣāvāsaḥ paratra ca  (iti)
   Chapt .   bala upādānakālāḥ -samnāhaguṇāḥ -pratibalakarma
09.2.01 maulabhṛtakaśreṇīmitrāmitrāṭavībalānāṃ samuddānakālāḥ
09.2.02 mūlarakṣaṇād atiriktaṃ maulabalaṃ, atyāvāpayuktā vā maulā mūle vikurvīran, bahulānuraktamaulabalaḥ sārabalo vā pratiyoddhā, vyāyāmena yoddhavyaṃ, prakṛṣṭe'dhvani kāle vā kṣayavyayasahatvān maulānāṃ, bahulānuraktasampāte ca yātavyasya upajāpabhayād anyasainyānāṃ bhṛtādīnāṃ aviśvāse, balakṣaye vā sarvasainyānāṃ - iti maulabalakālaḥ
09.2.03 prabhūtaṃ me bhṛtabalaṃ alpaṃ ca maulabalamṇ parasyālpaṃ viraktaṃ vā maulabalaṃ, phalguprāyaṃ asāraṃ vā bhṛtasainyamṇ mantreṇa yoddhavyaṃ alpavyāyāmenaṇ hrasvo deśaḥ kālo vā tanukṣayavyayahṇ alpāvāpaṃ śānta upajāpaṃ viśvastaṃ vā me sainyamṇ parasyālpaḥ prasāro hantavyahṇ - iti bhṛtabalakālaḥ
09.2.04 prabhūtaṃ me śreṇībalaṃ, śakyaṃ mūle yātrāyāṃ cādhātumṇ hrasvaḥ pravāsaḥ, śreṇībalaprāyaḥ pratiyoddhā mantravyāyāmābhyāṃ pratiyoddhukāmaḥ, daṇḍabalavyavahāraḥ - iti śreṇībalakālaḥ
09.2.05 prabhūtaṃ me mitrabalaṃ śakyaṃ mūle yātrāyāṃ cādhātumṇ alpaḥ pravāso mantrayuddhācca bhūyo vyāyāmayuddhamṇ mitrabalena vā pūrvaṃ aṭavīṃ nagarasthānaṃ āsāraṃ vā yodhayitvā paścāt svabalena yoddhayiṣyāmiṇ mitrasādhāraṇaṃ vā me kāryamṇ mitrāyattā vā me kāryasiddhihṇ āsannaṃ anugrāhyaṃ vā me mitramṇ atyāvāpaṃ vā'sya sādayiṣyāmi - iti mitrabalakālaḥ
09.2.06 prabhūtaṃ me śatrubalaṃ, śatrubalena yodhayiṣyāmi nagarasthānaṃ aṭavīṃ vā, tatra me śvavarāhayoḥ kalahe caṇḍālasya ivānyatarasiddhirbhaviṣyatiṇ āsārāṇāṃ aṭavīnāṃ vā kaṇṭakamardanaṃ etat kariṣyāmiṇ - atyupacitaṃ vā kopabhayānnityaṃ āsannaṃ aribalaṃ vāsayed, anyatrābhyantarakopaśaṅkāyāḥ - śatruyuddhāvarayuddhakālaśca - ityamitrabalakālaḥ
09.2.07 tenāṭavībalakālo vyākhyātaḥ
09.2.08 mārgādeśikaṃ, parabhūmiyogyaṃ, ariyuddhapratilomaṃ, aṭavībalaprāyaḥ śatrurvā, bilvaṃ bilvena hanyatāmṇ alpaḥ prasāro hantavyaḥ - ityaṭavībalakālaḥ
09.2.09 sainyaṃ anekaṃ anekasthaṃ uktaṃ anuktaṃ vā vilopārthaṃ yad uttiṣṭhati tad autsāhikaṃ - abhaktavetanaṃ vilopaviṣṭipratāpakaraṃ bhedyaṃ pareṣāṃ, abhedyaṃ tulyadeśajātiśilpaprāyaṃ saṃhataṃ mahat iti bala upādānakālāh
09.2.10 teṣāṃ kupyabhṛtaṃ amitrāṭavībalaṃ vilopabhṛtaṃ vā kuryāt
09.2.11 amitrasya vā balakāle pratyutpanne śatrubalaṃ avagṛhṇīyāt, anyatra vā preṣayet, aphalaṃ vā kuryāt, vikṣiptaṃ vā vāsayet, kāle vā'tikrānte visṛjet
09.2.12 parasya ca etad balasamuddānaṃ vighātayet, ātmanaḥ sampādayet
09.2.13 pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ ca eṣāṃ śreyaḥ samnāhayitum
09.2.14 tadbhāvabhāvitvānnityasatkārānugamācca maulabalaṃ bhṛtabalātśreyaḥ
09.2.15 nityānantaraṃ kṣipra utthāyi vaśyaṃ va bhṛtabalaṃ śreṇībalātśreyaḥ
09.2.16 jānapadaṃ ekārtha upagataṃ tulyasaṅgharṣāmarṣasiddhilābhaṃ ca śreṇībalaṃ mitrabalātśreyaḥ
09.2.17 aparimitadeśakālaṃ ekārtha upagamācca mitrabalaṃ amitrabalātśreyaḥ
09.2.18 āryādhiṣṭhitaṃ amitrabalaṃ aṭavībalātśreyaḥ
09.2.19 tad ubhayaṃ vilopārtham
09.2.20 avilope vyasane ca tābhyāṃ ahibhayaṃ syāt
09.2.21 brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrasainyānāṃ tejaḥprādhānyāt pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ śreyaḥ samnāhayitum ityācāryāḥ
09.2.22 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
09.2.23 praṇipātena brāhmaṇabalaṃ paro'bhihārayet
09.2.24 praharaṇavidyāvinītaṃ tu kṣatriyabalaṃ śreyaḥ, bahulasāraṃ vā vaiśyaśūdrabalaṃ iti
09.2.25 tasmād evambalaḥ paraḥ, tasya etat pratibalaṃ iti balasamuddānaṃ kuryāt
09.2.26 hastiyantraśakaṭagarbhakuntaprāsahāṭakaveṇuśalyavad hastibalasya pratibalam
09.2.27 tad eva pāṣāṇalaguḍāvaraṇāṅkuśakacagrahaṇīprāyaṃ rathabalasya pratibalam
09.2.28 tad evāśvānāṃ pratibalaṃ, varmiṇo vā hastino'śvā vā varmiṇaḥ
09.2.29 kavacino rathā āvaraṇinaḥ pattayaśca catur'ṅgabalasya pratibalam
09.2.30ab evaṃ balasamuddānaṃ parasainyanivāraṇam ।

   Chapt .   paścātkopacintā - bāhyābhyantaraprakṛtikopapratīkāraḥ
09.3.01 alpaḥ paścātkopo mahān purastāllābha iti alpaḥ paścātkopo garīyān
09.3.02 alpaṃ paścātkopaṃ prayātassya dūṣyāmitrāṭavikā hi sarvataḥ samedhayanti, prakṛtikopo vā
09.3.03 labdhaṃ api ca mahāntaṃ purastāllāhaṃ evambhūte bhṛtyamitrakṣayavyayā grasante
09.3.04 tasmāt sahasra ekīyaḥ purastāllābhasyāyogaḥ śata ekīyo vā paścātkopa iti na yāyāt
09.3.05 sūcīmukhā hyanarthā iti lokapravādaḥ
09.3.06 paścātkope sāmadānabhedadaṇḍān prayuñjīta
09.3.07 purastāllābhe senāpatiṃ kumāraṃ vā daṇḍacāriṇaṃ kurvīta
09.3.08 balavān vā rājā paścātkopāvagrahasamarthaḥ purastāllābhaṃ ādātuṃ yāyāt
09.3.09 abhyantarakopaśaṅkāyāṃ śaṅkitān ādāya yāyāt, bāhyakopaśaṅkāyāṃ vā putradāraṃ eṣām
09.3.10 abhyantarāvagrahaṃ kṛtvā śūnyapālaṃ anekabalavargaṃ anekamukhyaṃ ca sthāpayitvā yāyāt, na vā yāyāt
09.3.11 abhyantarakopo bāhyakopāt pāpīyān ityuktaṃ purastāt
09.3.12 mantrapurohitasenāpatiyuvarājānāṃ anyatamakopo'bhyantarakopaḥ
09.3.13 taṃ ātmadoṣatyāgena paraśakty'parādhavaśena vā sādhayet
09.3.14 mahā'parādhe'pi purohite samrodhanaṃ avasrāvaṇaṃ vā siddhiḥ, yuvarāje samrodhanaṃ nigraho vā guṇavatyanyasmin sati putre
09.3.15 putraṃ bhrātaraṃ anyaṃ vā kulyaṃ rājagrāhiṇaṃ utsāhena sādhayet, utsāhābbhāve gṛhītānuvartanasandhikarmabhyāṃ arisandhānabhayāt
09.3.16 anyebhyaḥ tadvidhebhyo vā bhūmidānairviśvāsayed enam
09.3.17 tadviśiṣṭaṃ svayaṅgrāhaṃ daṇḍaṃ vā preṣayet, sāmantāṭavikān vā, tairvigṛhītaṃ atisandadhyāt
09.3.18 aparuddhādānaṃ pāragrāmikaṃ vā yogaṃ ātiṣṭhet
09.3.19 etena mantrasenāpatī vyākhyātau
09.3.20 mantry।ādivarjānāṃ antar'mātyānāṃ anyatamakopo'ntar'mātyakopaḥ
09.3.21 tatrāpi yathā'rhaṃ upāyān prayuñjīta
09.3.22 rāṣṭramukhyāntapālāṭavikadaṇḍa upanatānāṃ anyatamakopo bāhyakopaḥ
09.3.23 taṃ anyonyenāvagrāhayet
09.3.24 atidurgapratiṣṭabdhaṃ vā sāmantāṭavikatatkulīnāparuddhānāṃ anyatamenāvagrāhayet
09.3.25 mitreṇa upagrāhayed vā yathā nāmitraṃ gacchet
09.3.26 amitrād vā sattrī bhedayed enaṃ - ayaṃ tvā yogapuruṣaṃ manyamāno bhartaryeva vikramayiṣyati, avāptārtho daṇḍacāriṇaṃ amitrāṭavikeṣu kṛcchre vā prayāse yokṣyati, viputradāraṃ ante vā vāsayiṣyati
09.3.27 pratihatavikramaṃ tvāṃ bhartarypaṇyaṃ kariṣyati, tvayā vā sandhiṃ kṛtvā bhartāraṃ eva prasādayiṣyati
09.3.28 mitraṃ upakṛṣṭaṃ vā'sya gaccha iti
09.3.29 pratipannaṃ iṣṭābhiprāyaiḥ pūjayet
09.3.30 apratipannasya saṃśrayaṃ bhedayed asau te yogapuruṣaḥ praṇihitaḥ iti
09.3.31 sattrī ca enaṃ abhityaktaśāsanairghātayet, gūḍhapuruṣairvā
09.3.32 sahaprasthāyino vā'sya pravīrapuruṣān yathā'bhiprāyakaraṇenāvāhayet
09.3.33 tena praṇihitān sattrī brūyāt
09.3.34 iti siddhiḥ
09.3.35 parasya ca enān kopān utthāpayet, ātmanaśca śamayet
09.3.36 yaḥ kopaṃ kartuṃ śamayituṃ vā śaktaḥ tatra upajāpaḥ kāryaḥ
09.3.37 yaḥ satyasandhaḥ śaktaḥ karmaṇi phalāvāptau cānugrahītuṃ vinipāte ca trātuṃ tatra pratijāpaḥ kāryaḥ, tarkayitavyaśca kalyāṇabuddhirutāho śaṭha iti
09.3.38 śaṭho hi bāhyo'bhyantaraṃ evaṃ upajapati - bhartāraṃ cedd hatvā māṃ pratipādayiṣyati śatruvadho bhūmilābhaśca me dvividho lābho bhaviṣyati, atha vā śatrurenaṃ āhaniṣyati iti hatabandhupakṣaḥ tulyadoṣadaṇḍena udvignaśca me bhūyān akṛtyapakṣo bhaviṣyati, tadvidhe vā'nyasminn api śaṅkito bhaviṣyati, anyaṃ anyaṃ cāsya mukhyaṃ abhityaktaśāsanena ghātayiṣyāmi iti
09.3.39 abhyantaro vā śaṭho bāhyaṃ evaṃ upajapati - kośaṃ asya hariṣyāmi, daṇḍaṃ vā'sya haniṣyāmi, duṣṭaṃ vā bhartāraṃ anena ghātayiṣyāmi, pratipannaṃ bāhyaṃ amitrāṭavikeṣu vikramayiṣyāmi cakraṃ asya sajyatāṃ, vairaṃ asya prasajyatāṃ, tataḥ svādhīno me bhaviṣyati, tato bhartāraṃ eva prasādayiṣyāmi, svayaṃ vā rājyaṃ grahīṣyāmiṇ baddhvā vā bāhyabhūmiṃ bhartṛbhūmiṃ ca ubhayaṃ avāpsyāmi, viruddhaṃ vā''vāhayitvā bāhyaṃ viśvastaṃ ghātayiṣyāmi, śūnyaṃ vā'sya mūlaṃ hariṣyāmi iti
09.3.40 kalyāṇabuddhiḥ tu sahajīvyarthaṃ upajapati
09.3.41 kalyāṇabuddhinā sandadhīta, śaṭhaṃ tathā iti pratigṛhyātisandadhyāt - iti

09.4.04 ādeyaḥ pratyādeyaḥ prasādakaḥ prakopako hrasvakālaḥ tanukṣayo'lpavyayo mahān vṛddhy।udayaḥ kalyo dharmyaḥ purogaśca iti lābhasampat
09.4.05 suprāpyānupālyaḥ pareṣāṃ apratyādeya ityādeyaḥ
09.4.06 viparyaye pratyādeyaḥ
09.4.07 taṃ ādadānaḥ tatrastho vā vināśaṃ prāpnoti
09.4.08 yadi vā paśyet pratyādeyaṃ ādāya kośadaṇḍanicayarakṣāvidhānānyavasrāvayiṣyāmi, khanidravyahastivanasetubandhavaṇikpathān uddhṛtasārān kariṣyāmi, prakṛtīrasya karśayiṣyāmi, apavāhayiṣyāmi, āyogenārādhayiṣyāmi vā, tāḥ paraṃ pratiyogena kopayiṣyati, pratipakṣe vā'sya paṇyaṃ enaṃ kariṣyāmi, mitraṃ aparuddhaṃ vā'sya pratipādayiṣyāmi, mitrasya svasya vā deśasya pīḍāṃ atrasthaḥ taskarebhyaḥ parebhyaśca pratikariṣyāmi, mitraṃ āśrayaṃ vā'sya vaiguṇyaṃ grāhayiṣyāmi, tad amitraviraktaṃ tatkulīnaṃ pratipatsyate, satkṛtya vā'smai bhūmiṃ dāsyāmi iti saṃhitasamutthitaṃ mitraṃ me cirāya bhaviṣyati iti pratyādeyaṃ api lābhaṃ ādadīta
09.4.09 ityādeyapratyādeyau vyākhyātau
09.4.10 adhārmikād dhārmikasya lābho labhyamānaḥ sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ ca prasādako bhavati
09.4.11 viparītaḥ prakopaka iti
09.4.12 mantriṇāṃ upadeśāllābho'labhyamānaḥ kopako bhavati ayaṃ asmābhiḥ kṣayavyayau grāhitaḥ iti
09.4.13 dūṣyamantriṇāṃ anādarāllābho labhyamānaḥ kopako bhavati siddhārtho'yaṃ asmān vināśayiṣyati iti

09.6.22 nivṛtta utsāhaṃ vigrahaśrāntaṃ pratihata upāyaṃ kṣayavyayābhyāṃ pravāsena ca upataptaṃ śaucenānyaṃ lipsamānaṃ anyasmād vā śaṅkamānaṃ maitrīpradhānaṃ vā kalyāṇabuddhiṃ sāmnā sādhayet
09.6.23 lubdhaṃ kṣīṇaṃ vā tapasvimukhyāvasthāpanāpūrvaṃ dānena sādhayet
09.6.24 tat pañcavidhaṃ - deyavisargo gṛhītānuvartanaṃ āttapratidānaṃ svadravyadānaṃ apūrvaṃ parasveṣu svayaṅgrāhadānaṃ ca
09.6.25 iti dānakarma
09.6.26 parasparadveṣavairabhūmiharaṇaśaṅkitaṃ ato'nyatamena bhedayet
09.6.27 bhīruṃ vā pratighātena kṛtasandhireṣa tvayi karmakariṣyati, mitraṃ asya nisṛṣṭaṃ, sandhau vā nābhyantaraḥ iti
09.6.28 yasya vā svadeśād anyadeśād vā paṇyāni paṇyāgāratayā''gaccheyuḥ tāni asya yātavyāllabdhāni iti sattriṇaścārayeyuḥ
09.6.29 bahulībhūte śāsanaṃ abhityaktena preṣayet etat te paṇyaṃ paṇyāgāraṃ vā mayā te preṣitaṃ, sāmavāyikeṣu vikramasva, apagaccha vā, tataḥ paṇaśeṣaṃ avāpsyasi iti
09.6.30 tataḥ sattriṇaḥ pareṣu grāhayeyuḥ etad aripradattam iti
09.6.31 śatruprakhyātaṃ vā paṇyaṃ avijñātaṃ vijigīṣuṃ gacchet
09.6.32 tad asya vaidehakavyañjanāḥ śatrumukhyeṣu vikrīṇīran
09.6.33 tataḥ sattriṇaḥ pareṣu grāhayeyuḥ etat paṇyaṃ aripradattam iti
09.6.34 mahā'parādhān arthamānābhyāṃ upagṛhya vā śastrarasāgnibhiramitre praṇidadhyāt
09.6.35 atha ekaṃ amātyaṃ niṣpātayet
09.6.36 tasya putradāraṃ upagṛhya rātrau hataṃ iti khyāpayet
09.6.37 athāmātyaḥ śatroḥ tān eka ekaśaḥ prarūpayet
09.6.38 te ced yathā uktaṃ kuryurna ca enān grāhayet
09.6.39 aśaktimato vā grāhayet
09.6.40 āptabhāva upagato mukhyād asyātmānaṃ rakṣaṇīyaṃ kathayet
09.6.41 athāmitraśāsanaṃ mukhya upaghātāya preṣitaṃ ubhayavetano grāhayet
09.6.42 utsāhaśaktimato vā preṣayet amuṣya rājyaṃ gṛhāṇa, yathā'sthito naḥ sandhiḥ iti
09.6.43 tataḥ sattriṇaḥ pareṣu grāhayeyuḥ
09.6.44 ekasya skandhāvāraṃ vīvadhaṃ āsāraṃ vā ghātayeyuḥ
09.6.45 itareṣu maitrīṃ bruvāṇāḥ tvaṃ eteṣāṃ ghātayitavyaḥ ityupajapeyuḥ
09.6.46 yasya vā pravīrapuruṣo hastī hayo vā mriyeta gūḍhapuruṣairhanyeta hriyeta vā sattriṇaḥ paraspara upahataṃ brūyuḥ
09.6.47 tataḥ śāsanaṃ abhiśastasya preṣayet bhūyaḥ kuru tataḥ paṇaśīṣaṃ avāpsyasi iti
09.6.48 tad ubhayavetanā grāhayeyuḥ
09.6.49 bhinneṣvanyatamaṃ labheta
09.6.50 tena senāpatikumāradaṇḍacāriṇo vyākhyātāḥ
09.6.51 sāndhikaṃ ca bhedaṃ prayuñjīta
09.6.52 iti bhedakarma
09.6.53 tīkṣṇaṃ utsāhinaṃ vyasaninaṃ sthitaśatruṃ vā gūḍhapuruṣāḥ śastrāgnirasādibhiḥ sādhayeyuḥ, saukaryato vā teṣāṃ anyatamaḥ
09.6.54 tīkṣṇo hyekaḥ śastrarasāgnibhiḥ sādhayet
09.6.55 ayaṃ sarvasandohakarma viśiṣṭaṃ vā karoti
09.6.56 ityupāyacaturvargaḥ
09.6.57 pūrvaḥ pūrvaścāsya laghiṣṭhaḥ
09.6.58 sāntvaṃ ekaguṇam
09.6.59 dānaṃ dviguṇaṃ sāntvapūrvam
09.6.60 bhedaḥ triguṇaḥ sāntvadānapūrvaḥ
09.6.61 daṇḍaścaturguṇaḥ sāntvadānabhedapūrvaḥ
09.6.62 ityabhiyuñjāneṣu uktam
09.6.63 svabhūmiṣṭheṣu tu ta eva upāyāḥ
09.6.64 viśeṣaḥ tu
09.6.65 svabhūmiṣṭhānāṃ anyatamasya paṇyāgārairabhijñātān dūtamukhyān abhīkṣṇaṃ preṣayet
09.6.66 ta enaṃ sandhau parahiṃsāyāṃ vā yojayeyuḥ
09.6.67 apratipadyamānaṃ kṛto naḥ sandhiḥ ityāvedayeyuḥ
09.6.68 taṃ itareṣāṃ ubhayavetanāḥ saṅkrāmayeyuḥ ayaṃ vo rājā duṣṭaḥ iti
09.6.69 yasya vā yasmād bhayaṃ vairaṃ dveṣo vā taṃ tasmād bhedayeyuḥ ayaṃ te śatruṇā sandhatte, purā tvāṃ atisandhatte, kṣiprataraṃ sandhīyasva, nigrahe cāsya prayatasva iti
09.6.70 āvāhavivāhābhyāṃ vā kṛtvā samyogaṃ asamyuktān bhedayet
09.6.71 sāmantāṭavikatatkulīnāparuddhaiśca eṣāṃ rājyāni ghātayet, sārthavrajāṭavīrvā, daṇḍaṃ vā'bhisṛtam
09.6.72 parasparāpāśrayāśca eṣāṃ jātisaṅghāśchidreṣu prahareyuḥ, gūḍhāścāgnirasaśastreṇa
09.6.73ab vītaṃsagilavaccārīn yogairācaritaiḥ śaṭhaḥ ।

09.7.01 kāmādirutsekaḥ svāḥ prakṛtīḥ kopayati, apanayo bāhyāḥ
09.7.02 tad ubhayaṃ āsurī vṛttiḥ
09.7.03 svajanavikāraḥ kopaḥ
09.7.04 paravṛddhihetuṣu āpad'rtho'narthaḥ saṃśaya iti
09.7.05 yo'rthaḥ śatruvṛddhiṃ aprāptaḥ karoti, prāptaḥ pratyādeyaḥ pareṣāṃ bhavati, prāpyamāṇo vā kṣayavyaya udayo bhavati, sa bhavatyāpad'rthaḥ
09.7.06 yathā sāmantānāṃ āmiṣabhūtaḥ sāmantavyasanajo lābhaḥ, śatruprārthito vā svabhāvādhigamyo lābhaḥ, paścāt kopena pārṣṇigrāheṇa vā vigṛhītaḥ purastāllābhaḥ, mitra ucchedena sandhivyatikrameṇa vā maṇḍalaviruddho lābhaḥ ityāpad'rthaḥ
09.7.07 svataḥ parato vā bhaya utpattirityanarthaḥ
09.7.08 tayoḥ artho na vā iti, anartho na vā iti, artho'nartha iti, anartho'rtha iti saṃśayaḥ
09.7.09 śatrumitraṃ utsāhayituṃ artho na vā iti saṃśayaḥ
09.7.10 śatrubalaṃ arthamānābhyāṃ āvāhayituṃ anartho na vā iti saṃśayaḥ
09.7.11 balavatsāmantāṃ bhūmiṃ ādātuṃ artho'nartha iti saṃśayaḥ
09.7.12 jāyasā sambhūyayānaṃ anartho'rtha iti saṃśayaḥ
09.7.13 teṣāṃ arthasaṃśayaṃ upagacchet
09.7.14 artho'rthānubandhaḥ, artho niranubandhaḥ, artho'narthānubandhaḥ, anartho'rthānubandhaḥ, anartho niranubandhaḥ, anartho'narthānubandhaḥ ityanubandhaṣaḍvargaḥ
09.7.15 śatruṃ utpāṭya pārṣṇigrāhādānaṃ artho'narthānubandhaḥ
09.7.16 udāsīnasya daṇḍānugrahaḥ phalena artho niranubandhaḥ
09.7.17 parasyāntar।ucchedanaṃ artho'narthānubandhaḥ

09.7.20 jyāyāṃsaṃ utthāpya nivṛttiranartho'narthānubandhaḥ
09.7.21 teṣāṃ pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ śreyān upasamprāptum
09.7.22 iti kāryāvasthāpanam
09.7.23 samantato yugapad'rtha utpattiḥ samantato'rthāpad bhavati
09.7.24 sā eva pārṣṇigrāhavigṛhītā samantato'rthasaṃśayāpad bhavati
09.7.25 tayormitrākranda upagrahāt siddhiḥ
09.7.26 samantataḥ śatrubhyo bhaya utpattiḥ samantto'narthāpad bhavati
09.7.27 sā eva mitravigṛhītā samantato'narthasaṃśayāpad bhavati
09.7.28 tayoścalāmitrākranda upagrahāt siddhiḥ, paramiśrāpratīkāro vā
09.7.29 ito lābha itarato lābha ityubhayato'rthāpad bhavati
09.7.30 tasyāṃ samantato'rthāyāṃ ca lābhaguṇayuktaṃ arthaṃ ādātuṃ yāyāt
09.7.31 tulye lābhaguṇe pradhānaṃ āsannaṃ anatipātinaṃ ūno vā yena bhavet taṃ ādātuṃ yāyāt
09.7.32 ito'nartha itarato'nartha ityubhayato'narthāpat
09.7.33 tasyāṃ samantato'narthāyāṃ ca mitrebhyaḥ siddhiṃ lipseta
09.7.34 mitrābhāve prakṛtīnāṃ laghīyasya ekato'narthāṃ sādhayet, ubhayato'narthāṃ jyāyasyā, samantato'narthāṃ mūlena pratikuryāt
09.7.35 aśakye sarvaṃ utsṛjyāpagacchet
09.7.36 dṛṣṭā hi jīvataḥ punar।āvṛttiryathā suyātrā udayanābhyām
09.7.37 ito lābha itarato rājyābhimarśa ityubhayato'rthānarthāpad bhavati
09.7.38 tasyāṃ anarthasādhako yo'rthaḥ taṃ ādātuṃ yāyāt
09.7.39 anyathā hi rājyābhimarśaṃ vārayet
09.7.40 etayā samantato'rthānarthāpad vyākhyātā
09.7.41 ito'nartha itarato'rthasaṃśaya ityubhayato'narthārthasaṃśayā
09.7.42 tasyāṃ pūrvaṃ anarthaṃ sādhayet, tatsiddhāvarthasaṃśayam
09.7.43 etayā samantato'narthārthasaṃśayā vyākhyātā
09.7.44 ito'rtha itarato'narthasaṃśaya ityubhayato'rthānarthasaṃśayāpad
09.7.45 etayā samantato'rthānarthasaṃśayā vyākhyātā
09.7.46 tasyāṃ pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ anarthasaṃśayān mokṣayituṃ yateta
09.7.47 śreyo hi mitraṃ anarthasaṃśaye tiṣṭhanna daṇḍaḥ, daṇḍo vā na kośa iti
09.7.48 samagramokṣaṇābhāve prakṛtīnāṃ avayavān mokṣayituṃ yateta
09.7.49 tatra puruṣaprakṛtīnāṃ bahulaṃ anuraktaṃ vā tīkṣṇalubdhavarjaṃ, dravyaprakṛtīnāṃ sāraṃ mahā upakāraṃ vā
09.7.50 sandhinā''sanena dvaidhībhāvena vā laghūni, viparyayairgurūṇi
09.7.51 kṣayasthānavṛddhīnāṃ ca uttara uttaraṃ lipseta
09.7.52 prātilomyena vā kṣayādīnāṃ āyatyāṃ viśeṣaṃ paśyet
09.7.53 iti deśāvasthāpanam

09.7.55 nirantarayogitvāccārthānarthasaṃśayānāṃ yātrā''dāvarthaḥ śreyān upasamprāptuṃ pārṣṇigrāhāsārapratighāte kṣayavyayapravāsapratyādeye mūlarakṣaṇeṣu ca bhavati
09.7.56 tathā'narthaḥ saṃśayo vā svabhūmiṣṭhasya viṣahyo bhavati
09.7.57 etena yātrāmadhye'rthānarthasaṃśayānāṃ upasamprāptirvyākhyātā

09.7.59 sāmavāyikānāṃ apurogasya tu yātrāmadhyāntago'narthaḥ saṃśayo vā śreyān upasamprāptuṃ anirbandhagāmitvāt
09.7.60 artho dharmaḥ kāma ityarthatrivargaḥ
09.7.61 tasya pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ śreyān upasamprāptum
09.7.62 anartho'dharmaḥ śoka ityanarthatrivargaḥ
09.7.63 tasya pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ śreyān pratikartum
09.7.64 artho'nartha iti, dharmo'dharma iti, kāmaḥ śoka iti saṃśayatrivargaḥ
09.7.65 tasya uttarapakṣasiddhau pūrvapakṣaḥ śreyān upasamprāptum
09.7.66 iti kālāvasthāpanam

09.7.68 putrabhrātṛbandhuṣu sāmadānābhyāṃ siddhiranurūpā, paurajānapadadaṇḍamukhyeṣu dānabhedābhyāṃ, sāmantāṭavikeṣu bhedadaṇḍābhyām

10.1.01 vāstukapraśaste vāstuni nāyakavardhaki mauhūrtikāḥ skandhāvāraṃ, vṛttaṃ dīrghaṃ catur'śraṃ vā bhūmivaśena vā, caturdvāraṃ ṣaṭpathaṃ navasaṃsthānaṃ māpayeyuḥ khātavaprasāladvārāṭṭālakasampannaṃ bhaye sthāne ca
10.1.02 madhyamasya uttare navabhāge rājavāstukaṃ dhanuḥśatāyāmaṃ ardhavistāraṃ, paścimārdhe tasyāntaḥpuram
10.1.03 antarvaṃśikasainyaṃ cānte niviśeta
10.1.04 purastād upasthānaṃ, dakṣiṇataḥ kośaśāsanakāryakaraṇāni, vāmato rājāupavāhyānāṃ hasty'śvarathānāṃ sthānam
10.1.05 ato dhanuḥśatāntarāścatvāraḥ śakaṭamethīpratatistambhasālaparikṣepāḥ
10.1.06 prathame purastān mantripurohitau, daṇṣiṇataḥ koṣṭhāgāraṃ mahānasaṃ ca, vāmataḥ kupyāyudhāgāram
10.1.07 dvitīye maulabhṛtānāṃ sthānaṃ aśvarathānāṃ senāpateśca
10.1.08 tṛtīye hastinaḥ śreṇyaḥ praśāstā ca
10.1.09 caturthe viṣṭirnāyako mitrāmitrāṭavībalaṃ svapuruṣādhiṣṭhitam
10.1.10 vaṇijo rūpājīvāścānumahāpatham
10.1.11 bāhyato lubdhakaśvagaṇinaḥ satūryāgnayaḥ, gūḍhāścārakṣāḥ
10.1.12 śatrūṇāṃ āpāte kūpakūṭāvapātakaṇṭakinīśca sthāpayet
10.1.13 aṣṭādaśavargāṇāṃ ārakṣaviparyāsaṃ kārayet
10.1.14 divāyāmaṃ ca kārayed apasarpajñānārtham

10.2.01 grāmāraṇyānāṃ adhvani niveśān yavasa indhana udakavaśena parisaṅkhyāya sthānāsanagamanakālaṃ ca yātrāṃ yāyāt
10.2.02 tatpratīkāradviguṇaṃ bhakta upakaraṇaṃ vāhayet
10.2.03 aśakto vā sainyeṣvāyojayet, antareṣu vā nicinuyāt
10.2.04 purastānnāyakaḥ, madhye kalatraṃ svāmī ca, pārśvayoraśvā bāhu।utsāraḥ, cakrānteṣu hastinaḥ prasāravṛddhirvā, paścāt senāpatiryāyāt niviśeta
10.2.05 sarvato vanājīvaḥ prasāraḥ
10.2.06 svadeśād anvāyatirvīvadhaḥ

10.2.10 pathidvaidhībhāve svabhūmito yāyāt

10.2.12 yojanaṃ adhamā, adhyardhaṃ madhyamā, dviyojanaṃ uttamā, sambhāvyā vā gatiḥ
10.2.13 āśrayakārī sampannaghātī pārṣṇirāsāro madhyama udāsīno vā pratikartavyaḥ, saṅkaṭo mārgaḥ śodhayitavyaḥ, kośo daṇḍo mitrāmitrāṭavībalaṃ viṣṭi।ṛturvā pratīkṣyāḥ, kṛtadurgakarmanicayarakṣākṣayaḥ krītabalanirvedo mitrabalanirvedaścāgamiṣyati, upajapitāro vā nātitvarayanti, śatrurabhiprāyaṃ vā pūrayiṣyati, iti śanairyāyāt, viparyaye śīghram
10.2.14 hastistambhasaṅkramasetubandhanaukāṣṭhaveṇusaṅghātairalābucarmakaraṇḍadṛtiplavagaṇḍikāveṇikābhiśca udakāni tārayet

10.2.17 dīrghakāntāraṃ anudakaṃ yavasa indhana udakahīnaṃ vā kṛcchrādhvānaṃ abhiyogapraskannaṃ kṣutpipāsā'dhvaklāntaṃ paṅkatoyagambhīrāṇāṃ vā nadīdarīśailānāṃ udyānāpayāne vyāsaktaṃ ekāyanamārge śailaviṣame saṅkaṭe vā bahulībhūtaṃ niveśe prasthite visamnāhaṃ bhojanavyāsaktaṃ āyatagatapariśrāntaṃ avasuptaṃ vyādhimarakadurbhikṣapīḍitaṃ vyādhitapatty'śvadvipaṃ abhūmiṣṭhaṃ vā balavyasaneṣu vā svasainyaṃ rakṣet, parasainyaṃ cābhihanyāt

   Chapt .   kūṭayuddhavikalpāḥ - svasainya utsāhanaṃ - svabalānyabalavyāyogaḥ

   Chapt .   yuddhabhūmayaḥ - patty'śvarathahastikarmāṇi
10.4.01 svabhūmiḥ patty'śvarathadvipānāṃ iṣṭā yuddhe niveśe ca
10.4.02 dhānvanavananimnasthalayodhināṃ khanakākāśadivārātriyodhināṃ ca puruṣāṇāṃ nādeyapārvatānūpasārasānāṃ ca hastināṃ aśvānāṃ ca yathāsvaṃ iṣṭā yuddhabhūmayaḥ kālāśca
10.4.03 samā sthirā'bhikāśā nirutkhātinyacakrakhurā'nakṣagrāhiṇyavṛkṣagulmavratatīstambhakedāraśvabhravalmīkasikatāpaṅkabhaṅgurā daraṇahīnā ca rathabhūmiḥ, hasty'śvayormanuṣyāṇāṃ ca same viṣame hitā yuddhe niveśe ca

10.4.12 etayā sarvabalaniveśā yuddhāni ca vyākhyātāni bhavanti
10.4.13 bhūmivāsavanavicayo'viṣamatoyatīrthavātaraśmigrahaṇaṃ vīvadhāsārayorghāto rakṣā vā viśuddhiḥ sthāpanā ca balasya prasāravṛddhirbāhu।utsāraḥ pūrvaprahāro vyāveśanaṃ vyāvedhanaṃ āśvāso grahaṇaṃ mokṣaṇaṃ mārgānusāravinimayaḥ kośakumārābhiharaṇaṃ jaghanakoṭy'bhighāto hīnānusāraṇaṃ anuyānaṃ samājakarma ityaśvakarmāṇi
10.4.14 puroyānaṃ akṛtamārgavāsatīrthakarma bāhu।utsāraḥ toyataraṇāvataraṇe sthānagamanāvataraṇaṃ viṣamasambādhapraveśo'gnidānaśamanaṃ ekāṅgavijayo bhinnasandhānaṃ abhinnabhedanaṃ vyasane trāṇaṃ abhighāto vibhīṣikā trāsanaṃ'udāryaṃ grahaṇaṃ mokṣaṇaṃ sāladvārāṭṭālakabhañjanaṃ kośavāhanāpavāhanaṃ iti hastikarmāṇi
10.4.15 svabalarakṣā catur'ṅgabalapratiṣedhaḥ saṅgrāme grahaṇaṃ mokṣaṇaṃ bhinnasandhānaṃ abhinnabhedanaṃ trāsanaṃ audāryaṃ bhīmaghoṣaśca iti rathakarmāṇi
10.4.16 sarvadeśakālaśastravahanaṃ vyāyāmaśca iti padātikarmāṇi

10.5.13 pañcacatvāriṃśad evaṃ rathā rathavyūhe bhavanti, dve śate pañcaviṃśatiścāśvāḥ, ṣaṭśatāni pañcasaptatiśca puruṣāḥ pratiyodhāraḥ, tāvantaḥ pādagopāḥ

10.5.19 evaṃ ojā daśa viṣamavyūhaprakṛtayo bhavanti
10.5.20 ataḥ sainyānāṃ vyūhaśeṣaṃ āvāpaḥ kāryaḥ

10.5.54 prakīrṇikāvarjānyetānyeva caturṇāṃ aṅgānāṃ vyastasamastānāṃ vā ghātaḥ, pakṣakakṣa urasyānāṃ ca prabhañjanaṃ avaskandaḥ sauptikaṃ ca iti hasityuddhāni

10.6.12 pakṣāvavasthāpya urasyātikrāntaḥ śyenaḥ
10.6.13 viparyaye cāpaṃ cāpakukuṣiḥ pratiṣṭhaḥ supratiṣṭhaśca
10.6.14 cāpapakṣaḥ sañjayaḥ
10.6.15 sa eva urasyātikrānto vijayaḥ
10.6.16 sthūlakarṇapakṣaḥ sthūṇākarṇaḥ
10.6.17 dviguṇapakṣasthūṇo viśālavijayaḥ
10.6.18 try'bhikrāntapakṣaścamūmukhaḥ
10.6.19 viparyaye jhaṣāsyaḥ
10.6.20 ūrdhvarājirdaṇḍaḥ sūcī
10.6.21 dvau daṇḍau valayaḥ
10.6.22 catvāro durjayaḥ
10.6.23 iti daṇḍavyūhāḥ
10.6.24 pakṣakakṣa urasyairviṣamaṃ vartamāno bhogaḥ
10.6.25 sa sarpasārī gomūtrikā vā
10.6.26 sa yugma urasyo daṇḍapakṣaḥ śakaṭaḥ
10.6.27 viparyaye makaraḥ
10.6.28 hasty'śvarathairvyatikīrṇaḥ śakaṭaḥ pāripatantakaḥ
10.6.29 iti bhogavyūhāḥ
10.6.30 pakṣakakṣa urasyānāṃ ekībhāve maṇḍalaḥ
10.6.31 sa sarvatomukhaḥ sarvatobhadraḥ
10.6.32 aṣṭānīko durjayaḥ
10.6.33 iti maṇḍalavyūhāḥ
10.6.34 pakṣakakṣa urasyānāṃ asaṃhatād asaṃhataḥ
10.6.35 sa pañcānīkānāṃ ākṛtisthāpanād vajro godhā vā
10.6.36 caturṇāṃ uddhānakaḥ kākapadī vā
10.6.37 trayāṇāṃ ardhacandrakaḥ karkaṭakaśṛṅgī vā
10.6.38 ityasaṃhatavyūhāḥ
10.6.39 ratha urasyo hastikakṣo'śvapṛṣṭho'riṣṭaḥ
10.6.40 pattayo'śvā rathā hastinaścānupṛṣṭhaṃ acalaḥ
10.6.41 hastino'śvā rathāḥ pattayaścānupṛṣṭhaṃ apratihataḥ
10.6.42 teṣāṃ pradaraṃ dṛḍhakena ghātayet, dṛḍhakaṃ asahyena, śyenaṃ cāpena, pratiṣṭhaṃ supratiṣṭhena, sañjayaṃ vijayena, sthūṇākarṇaṃ viśālavijayena, pāripatantakaṃ sarvatobhadreṇa
10.6.43 durjayena sarvān prativyūheta
10.6.44 patty'śvarathadvipānāṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ uttareṇa ghātayet, hīnāṅgaṃ adhikāṅgena ca iti
10.6.45 aṅgadaśakasya ekaḥ patiḥ patikaḥ, patikadaśakasya ekaḥ senāpatiḥ, taddaśakasya eko nāyaka iti
10.6.46 sa tūryaghoṣadhvajapatākābhirvyūhāṅgānāṃ saṃjñāḥ sthāpayed aṅgavibhāge saṅghāte sthāne gamane vyāvartane praharaṇe ca
10.6.47 same vyūhe deśakālasārayogāt siddhiḥ
10.6.48ab yantrairupaniṣadyogaiḥ tīkṣṇairvyāsaktaghātibhiḥ ।
10.6.48chd māyābhirdevasamyogaiḥ śakaṭairhastibhīṣaṇaiḥ
10.6.49ab dūṣyaprakopairgoyūthaiḥ skandhāvārapradīpanaiḥ ।
10.6.49chd koṭījaghanaghātairvā dūtavyañjanabhedanaiḥ
10.6.50ab durgaṃ dagdhaṃ hṛtaṃ vā te kopaḥ kulyaḥ samutthitaḥ ।
10.6.50chd śatrurāṭaviko vā iti parasya udvegaṃ ācaret
10.6.51ab ekaṃ hanyānna vā hanyād iṣuḥ kṣipto dhanuṣmatā ।
10.6.51chd prajñānena tu matiḥ kṣiptā hanyād garbhagatān api  (iti)
