   Chapt .   bheda upādānāni - upāṃśudaṇḍāḥ
11.1.01 saṅghalābho daṇḍamitralābhānāṃ uttamaḥ
11.1.02 saṅghā hi saṃhatatvād adhṛṣyāḥ pareṣām
11.1.03 tān anuguṇān bhuñjīta sāmadānābhyāṃ, viguṇān bhedadaṇḍābhyām
11.1.04 kāmbojasurāṣṭrakṣatriyaśreṇy।ādayo vārttaśastra upajīvinaḥ
11.1.05 licchivikavṛjikamallakamadrakakukurakurupāñcālādayo rājaśabda upajīvinaḥ
11.1.06 sarveṣāṃ āsannāḥ sattriṇaḥ saṅghānāṃ parasparanyaṅgadveṣavairakalahasthānānyupalabhya kramābhinītaṃ bhedaṃ upacārayeyuḥ asau tvā vijalpati iti
11.1.07 evaṃ ubhayatobaddharoṣāṇāṃ vidyāśilpadyūtavaihārikeṣvācāryavyañjanā bālakalahān utpādayeyuḥ
11.1.08 veśaśauṇḍikeṣu vā pratilomapraśaṃsābhiḥ saṅghamukhyamanuṣyāṇāṃ tīkṣṇāḥ kalahān utpādayeyuḥ, kṛtyapakṣa upagraheṇa vā
11.1.09 kumārakān viśiṣṭacchindikayā hīnacchindikān utsāhayeyuḥ
11.1.10 viśiṣṭānāṃ ca ekapātraṃ vivāhaṃ vā hīnebhyo vārayeyuḥ
11.1.11 hīnān vā viśiṣṭairekapātre vivāhe vā yojayeyuḥ
11.1.12 avahīnān vā tulyabhāva upagamane kulataḥ pauruṣataḥ sthānaviparyāsato vā
11.1.13 vyavahāraṃ avasthitaṃ vā pratilomasthāpanena niśāmayeyuḥ
11.1.14 vivādapadeṣu vā dravyapaśumanuṣyābhighātena rātrau tīkṣṇāḥ kalahān utpādayeyuḥ
11.1.15 sarveṣu ca kalahasthāneṣu hīnapakṣaṃ rājā kośadaṇḍābhyāṃ upagṛhya pratipakṣavadhe yojayet
11.1.16 bhinnān apavāhayed vā
11.1.17 bhūmau ca eṣāṃ pañcakulīṃ daśakulīṃ vā kṛṣyāyāṃ niveśayet
11.1.18 ekasthā hi śastragrahaṇasamarthāḥ syuḥ
11.1.19 samavāye ca eṣāṃ atyayaṃ sthāpayet
11.1.20 rājaśabdibhiravaruddhaṃ avakṣiptaṃ vā kulyaṃ abhijātaṃ rājaputratve sthāpayet
11.1.21 kārtāntikādiścāsya vargo rājalakṣaṇyatāṃ saṅgheṣu prakāśayet
11.1.22 saṅghamukhyāṃśca dharmiṣṭhān upajapet svadharmaṃ amuṣya rājñaḥ putre bhrātari vā pratipadyadhvam iti
11.1.23 pratipanneṣu kṛtyapakṣa upagrahārthaṃ arthaṃ daṇḍaṃ ca preṣayet
11.1.24 vikramakāle śauṇḍikavyañjanāḥ putradārapretāpadeśena naiṣecanikam iti madanarasayuktān madyakumbhānśataśaḥ prayaccheyuḥ
11.1.25 caityadaivatadvārarakṣāsthāneṣu ca sattriṇaḥ samayakarmanikṣepaṃ sahiraṇyābhijñānamudrāṇi hiraṇyabhājanāni ca prarūpayeyuḥ
11.1.26 dṛśyamāneṣu ca saṅgheṣu rājakīyāḥ ityāvedayeyuḥ
11.1.27 athāvaskandaṃ dadyāt
11.1.28 saṅghānāṃ vā vāhanahiraṇye kālike gṛhītvā saṅghamukhyāya prakhyātaṃ dravyaṃ prayacchet
11.1.29 tad eṣāṃ yācite dattaṃ amuṣmai mukhyāya iti brūyāt
11.1.30 etena skandhāvārāṭavībhedo vyākhyātaḥ
11.1.31 saṅghamukhyaputraṃ ātmasambhāvitaṃ vā sattrī grāhayet amuṣya rājñaḥ putraḥ tvaṃ, śatrubhayād iha nyasto'si iti
11.1.32 pratipannaṃ rājā kośadaṇḍābhyāṃ upagṛhya saṅgheṣu vikramayet
11.1.33 avāptārthaḥ taṃ api pravāsayet
11.1.34 bandhakīpoṣakāḥ plavakanaṭanartakasaubhikā vā praṇihitāḥ strībhiḥ paramarūpayauvanābhiḥ saṅghamukhyān unmādayeyuḥ
11.1.35 jātakāmānāṃ anyatamasya pratyayaṃ kṛtvā'nyatra gamanena prasabhaharaṇena vā kalahān utpādayeyuḥ
11.1.36 kalahe tīkṣṇāḥ karma kuryuḥ hato'yaṃ itthaṃ kāmukaḥ iti
11.1.37 visaṃvāditaṃ vā marṣayamāṇaṃ abhisṛtya strī brūyāt asau māṃ mukhyaḥ tvayi jātakāmāṃ bādhate, tasmiñjīvati na iha sthāsyāmi iti ghātaṃ asya prayojayet
11.1.38 prasahyāpahṛtā vā vanānte kriḍāgṛhe vā'pahartāraṃ rātrau tīkṣṇena ghātayet, svayaṃ vā rasena
11.1.39 tataḥ prakāśayet amunā me priyo hataḥ iti
11.1.40 jātakāmaṃ vā siddhavyañjanaḥ sāṃvadanikībhirauṣadhībhiḥ saṃvāsya rasenātisandhāyāpagacchet
11.1.41 tasminn apakrānte sattriṇaḥ paraprayogaṃ abhiśaṃseyuḥ
11.1.42 āḍhyavidhavā gūḍhājīvā yogastriyo vā dāyanikṣepārthaṃ vivadamānāḥ saṅghamukhyān unmādayeyuḥ, aditikauśikastriyo nartakīgāyanā vā
11.1.43 pratipannān gūḍhaveśmasu rātrisamāgamapraviṣṭāṃḥ tīkṣṇā hanyurbaddhvā hareyurvā
11.1.44 sattrī vā strīlolupaṃ saṅghamukhyaṃ prarūpayet amuṣmin grāme daridrakullaṃ apasṛtaṃ, tasya strī rājārhā, gṛhāṇa enām iti
11.1.45 gṛhītāyāṃ ardhamāsānantaraṃ siddhavyañjano dūṣyasaṅghamukhyamadhye prakrośet asau me mukhyo bhāryāṃ snuṣāṃ bhaginīṃ duhitaraṃ vā'dhicarati iti
11.1.46 taṃ cet saṅgho nigṛhṇīyāt, rājā enaṃ upagṛhya viguṇeṣu vikramayet
11.1.47 anigṛhīte siddhavyañjanaṃ rātrau tīkṣṇāḥ pravāsayeyuḥ
11.1.48 tataḥ tadvyañjanāḥ prakrośeyuḥ asau brahmahā brāhmaṇījāraśca iti
11.1.49 kārtāntikavyañjano vā kanyāṃ anyena vṛtāṃ anyasya prarūpayet amuṣya kanyā rājapatnī rājaprasavinī ca bhaviṣyati, sarvasvena prasahya vā enāṃ labhasva iti
11.1.50 alabhyamānāyāṃ parapakṣaṃ uddharṣayet
11.1.51 labdhāyāṃ siddhaḥ kalahaḥ
11.1.52 bhikṣukī vā priyabhāryaṃ mukhyaṃ brūyāt asau te mukhyo yauvana utsikto bhāryāyāṃ māṃ prāhiṇot, tasyāhaṃ bhayāllekhyaṃ ābharaṇaṃ gṛhītvā''gatā'smi, nirdoṣā te bhāryā, gūḍhaṃ asmin pratikartavyaṃ, ahaṃ api tāvat pratipatsyāmi iti
11.1.53 evaṃ।ādiṣu kalahasthāneṣu svayaṃ utpanne vā kalahe tīkṣṇairutpādite vā hīnapakṣaṃ rājā kośadaṇḍābhyāṃ upagṛhya viguṇeṣu vikramayed apavāhayed vā
11.1.54 saṅgheṣvevaṃ ekarājo varteta
11.1.55 saṅghāścāpyevaṃ ekarājād etebhyo'tisaṅghān ebhyo rakṣayeyuḥ
11.1.56ab saṅghamukhyaśca saṅgheṣu nyāyavṛttirhitaḥ priyaḥ ।
11.1.56chd dānto yuktajanaḥ tiṣṭhet sarvacittānuvartakaḥ  (iti)

   Chapt .   dūtakarma
12.1.01 balīyasā'bhiyukto durbalaḥ sarvatrānupraṇato vetasadharmā tiṣṭhet
12.1.02 indrasya hi sa praṇamati yo balīyaso namati iti bhāradvājaḥ
12.1.03 sarvasandohena balānāṃ yudhyeta
12.1.04 parākramo hi vyasanaṃ apahanti
12.1.05 svadharmaśca eṣa kṣatriyasya, yuddhe jayaḥ parājayo vā iti viśālākṣaḥ
12.1.06 na iti kauṭilyaḥ
12.1.07 sarvatrānupraṇataḥ kulaiḍaka iva nirāśo jīvite vasati
12.1.08 yudhyamānaścālpasainyaḥ samudraṃ ivāplavo'vagāhamānaḥ sīdati
12.1.09 tadviśiṣṭaṃ tu rājānaṃ āśrito durgaṃ aviṣahyaṃ vā ceṣṭeta
12.1.10 trayo'bhiyoktāro dharmalobhāsuravijayina iti
12.1.11 teṣāṃ abhyavapattyā dharmavijayī tuṣyati
12.1.12 taṃ abhyavapadyeta, pareṣāṃ api bhayāt
12.1.13 bhūmidravyaharaṇena lobhavijayī tuṣyati
12.1.14 taṃ arthenābhyavapadyeta
12.1.15 bhūmidravyaputradāraprāṇaharaṇenāsuravijayī
12.1.16 taṃ bhūmidravyābhyāṃ upagṛhyāgrāhyaḥ pratikurvīta
12.1.17 teṣāṃ anyatamaṃ uttiṣṭhamānaṃ sandhinā mantrayuddhena kūṭayuddhena vā prativyūheta
12.1.18 śatrupakṣaṃ asya sāmadānābhyāṃ, svapakṣaṃ bhedadaṇḍābhyām
12.1.19 durgaṃ rāṣṭraṃ skandhāvāraṃ vā'sya gūḍhāḥ śastrarasāgnibhiḥ sādhayeyuḥ
12.1.20 sarvataḥ pārṣṇiṃ asya grāhayet
12.1.21 aṭavībhirvā rājyaṃ ghātayet, tatkulīnāparuddhābhyāṃ vā hārayet
12.1.22 apakārānteṣu cāsya dūṭaṃ preṣayet
12.1.23 anapakṛtya vā sandhānam
12.1.24 tathā'pyabhiprayāntaṃ kośadaṇḍayoḥ pāda uttaraṃ ahorātra uttaraṃ vā sandhiṃ yāceta
12.1.25 sa ced daṇḍasandhiṃ yāceta, kuṇṭhaṃ asmai hasty'śvaṃ dadyād, utsāhitaṃ vā garayuktam
12.1.26 puruṣasandhiṃ yāceta, dūṣyāmitrāṭavībalaṃ asmai dadyād yogapuruṣādhiṣṭhitam
12.1.27 tathā kuryād yathā ubhayavināśaḥ syāt
12.1.28 tīkṣṇabalaṃ vā'smai dadyād yad avamānitaṃ vikurvīta, maulaṃ anuraktaṃ vā yad asya vyasane'pakuryāt
12.1.29 kośasandhiṃ yāceta, sāraṃ asmai dadyād yasya kretāraṃ nādhigacchet, kupyaṃ ayuddhayogyaṃ vā
12.1.30 bhūmisandhiṃ yāceta, pratyādeyāṃ nityāmitrāṃ anapāśrayāṃ mahākṣayavyayaniveśāṃ vā'smai bhūmiṃ dadyāt
12.1.31 sarvasvena vā rājadhānīvarjena sandhiṃ yāceta balīyasaḥ
12.1.32ab yat prasahya hared anyaḥ tat prayacced upāyataḥ ।
12.1.32chd rakṣet svadehaṃ na dhanaṃ kā hyanitye dhane dayā  (iti)
   Chapt .   mantrayuddha
12.2.01 sa cet sandhau nāvatiṣṭheta, brūyād enaṃ - ime śatruṣaḍvargavaśagā rājāno vinaṣṭāḥ, teṣāṃ anātmavatāṃ nārhasi mārgaṃ anugantum
12.2.02 dharmaṃ arthaṃ cāvekṣasva
12.2.03 mitramukhā hyamitrāḥ te ye tvā sāhasaṃ adharmaṃ arthātikramaṃ ca grāhayanti
12.2.04 śūraiḥ tyaktātmabhiḥ saha yoddhuṃ sāhasaṃ, janakṣayaṃ ubhayataḥ kartuṃ adharmaḥ, dṛṣṭaṃ arthaṃ mitraṃ aduṣṭaṃ ca tyaktuṃ arthātikramaḥ
12.2.05 mitravāṃśca sa rājā, bhūyaśca etenārthena mitrāṇyudyojayiṣyati yāni tvā sarvato'bhiyāsyanti
12.2.06 na ca madhyama udāsīnayormaṇḍalasya vā parityaktaḥ, bhavāṃḥ tu parityaktaḥ yattvā samudyuktaṃ upaprekṣante bhūyaḥ kṣayavyayābhyāṃ yujyatāṃ, mitrācca bhidyatāṃ, atha enaṃ parityaktamūlaṃ sukhena ucchetsyāmaḥ iti
12.2.07 sa bhavānnārhati mitramukhānāṃ amitrāṇāṃ śrotuṃ, mitrāṇyudvejayituṃ amitrāṃśca śreyasā yoktuṃ, prāṇasaṃśayaṃ anarthaṃ ca upagantum iti yacchet
12.2.08 tathā'pi pratiṣṭhamānasya prakṛtikopaṃ asya kārayed yathā saṅghavṛtte vyākhyātaṃ yogavāmane ca
12.2.09 tīkṣṇarasadaprayogaṃ ca
12.2.10 yad uktaṃ ātmarakṣitake rakṣyaṃ tatra tīkṣṇān rasadāṃśca prayuñjīta
12.2.11 bandhakīpoṣakāḥ paramarūpayauvanābhiḥ strībhiḥ senāmukhyān unmādayeyuḥ
12.2.12 bahūnāṃ ekasyāṃ dvayorvā mukhyayoḥ kāme jāte tīkṣṇāḥ kalahān utpādayeyuḥ
12.2.13 kalahe parājitapakṣaṃ paratrāpagamane yātrāsāhāyyadāne vā bharturyojayeyuḥ
12.2.14 kāmavaśān vā siddhavyañjanāḥ sāṃvadanikībhiroṣadhībhiratisandhānāya mukhyeṣu rasaṃ dāpayeyuḥ
12.2.15 vaidehakavyañjane vā rājamahiṣyāḥ subhagāyāḥ preṣyāṃ āsannāṃ kāmanimittaṃ arthenābhivṛṣya parityajet
12.2.16 tasya eva paricārakavyañjana upadiṣṭaḥ siddhavyañjanaḥ sāṃvadanikīṃ oṣadhīṃ dadyāt vaidehakaśarīre'vaghātavyā iti
12.2.17 siddhe subhagāyā apyenaṃ yogaṃ upadiśet rājaśarīre'vadhātavyā iti
12.2.18 tato rasenātisandadhyāt
12.2.19 kārtāntikavyañjano vā mahāmātraṃ rājalakṣaṇasampannam kramābhinītaṃ brūyāt
12.2.20 bhāryāṃ asya bhikṣukī rājapatnī rājaprasavinī vā bhaviṣyasi iti
12.2.21 bhāryāvyañjanā vā mahāmātraṃ brūyāt rājā kila māṃ avarodhayiṣyati, tavāntikāya pattralekhyaṃ ābharaṇaṃ ca idaṃ parivrājikayā''hṛtam iti
12.2.22 sūdārālikavyañjano vā rasaprayogārthaṃ rājavacanaṃ arthaṃ cāsya lobhanīyaṃ abhinayet
12.2.23 tad asya vaidehakavyañjanaḥ pratisandadhyāt, kāryasiddhiṃ ca brūyāt
12.2.24 evaṃ ekena dvābhyāṃ tribhirityupāyaireka ekaṃ asya mahāmātraṃ vikramāyāpagamanāya vā yojayet - iti
12.2.25 durgeṣu cāsya śūnyapālāsannāḥ sattriṇaḥ paurajānapadeṣu maitrīnimittaṃ āvedayeyuḥ - śūnyapālena uktā yodhāścādhikaraṇasthāśca kṛcchragato rājā jīvann āgamiṣyati, na vā, prasahya vittaṃ ārjayadhvaṃ, amitrāṃśca hata iti
12.2.26 bahulībhūte tīkṣṇāḥ paurānniśāsvāhārayeyuḥ, mukhyāṃścābhihanyuḥ evaṃ kriyante ye śūnyapālasya na śuśrūṣante iti
12.2.27 śūnyapālasthāneṣu ca saśoṇitāni śastravittabandhanānyutsṛjeyuḥ
12.2.28 tataḥ sattriṇaḥ śūnyapālo ghātayati vilopayati ca ityāvedayeyuḥ
12.2.29 evaṃ jānapadān samāharturbhedayeyuḥ
12.2.30 samāhartṛpuruṣāṃḥ tu grāmamadhyeṣu rātrau tīkṣṇā hatvā brūyuḥ evaṃ kriyante ye janapadaṃ adharmeṇa bādhante iti
12.2.31 samutpanne doṣe śūnyapālaṃ samāhartāraṃ vā prakṛtikopena ghātayeyuḥ
12.2.32 tatkulīnaṃ aparuddhaṃ vā pratipādayeyuḥ
12.2.33ab antaḥpurapuradvāraṃ dravyadhānyaparigrahān ।
12.2.33chd daheyuḥ tāṃśca hanyurvā brūyurasyārtavādinaḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   senāmukhyavadhah - maṇḍalaprotsāhanam
12.3.01 rājño rājavallabhānāṃ cāsannāḥ sattriṇaḥ patty'śvarathadvipamukhyānāṃ rājā kruddhaḥ iti suhṛdviśvāsena mitrasthānīyeṣu kathayeyuḥ
12.3.02 bahulībhūte tīkṣṇāḥ kṛtarātricārapratīkārā gṛheṣu svāmivacanenāgamyatām iti brūyuḥ
12.3.03 tānnirgacchata evābhihanyuḥ, svāmisandeśaḥ iti cāsannān brūyuḥ
12.3.04 ye cāpravāsitāḥ tān sattriṇo brūyuḥ etat tad yad asmābhiḥ kathitaṃ, jīvitukāmenāpakrāntavyam iti
12.3.05 yebhyaśca rājā yācito na dadāti tān sattriṇo brūyuḥ - uktaḥ śūnyapālo rājñā ayācyaṃ arthaṃ asau cāsau ca mā yācate, mayā pratyākhyātāḥ śatrusaṃhitāḥ, teṣāṃ uddharaṇe prayatasva iti
12.3.06 tataḥ pūrvavad ācaret
12.3.07 yebhyaśca rājā yācito dadāti tān sattriṇo brūyuḥ - uktaḥ śūnyapālo rājñā ayācyaṃ arthaṃ asau cāsau ca mā yācate, tebhyo mayā so'rtho viśvāsārthaṃ dattaḥ, śatrusaṃhitāḥ, teṣāṃ uddharaṇe prayatasva iti
12.3.08 tataḥ pūrvavad ācaret
12.3.09 ye ca enaṃ yācyaṃ arthaṃ na yācante tān sattriṇo brūyuḥ - uktaḥ śūnyapālo rājñā yācyaṃ arthaṃ asau cāsau ca mā na yācate, kiṃ anyat svadoṣaśaṅkitatvāt, teṣāṃ uddharaṇe prayatasva iti
12.3.10 tataḥ pūrvavad ācaret
12.3.11 etena sarvaḥ kṛtyapakṣo vyākhyātaḥ
12.3.12 pratyāsanno vā rājānaṃ sattrī grāhayet asau cāsau ca te mahāmātraḥ śatrupuruṣaiḥ sambhāṣate iti
12.3.13 pratipanne dūṣyān asya śāsanaharān darśayet etat tat iti
12.3.14 senāmukhyaprakṛtipuruṣān vā bhūmyā hiraṇyena vā lobhayitvā sveṣu vikramayed apavāhayed vā
12.3.15 yo'sya putraḥ samīpe durge vā prativasati taṃ sattriṇā upajāpayet ātmasampannataraḥ tvaṃ putraḥ, tathā'pyantarhitaḥ, tatkiṃ upekṣase vikramya gṛhāṇa, purā tvā yuvarājo vināśayati iti
12.3.16 tatkulīnaṃ aparuddhaṃ vā hiraṇyena pratilobhya brūyāt antarbalaṃ pratyantaskandhaṃ antaṃ vā'sya pramṛdnīhi iti
12.3.17 āṭavikān arthamānābhyāṃ upagṛhya rājyaṃ asya ghātayet
12.3.18 pārṣṇigrāhaṃ vā'sya brūyāt eṣa khalu rājā māṃ ucchidya tvāṃ ucchetsyati, pārṣṇiṃ asya gṛhāṇa, tvayi nivṛttasyāhaṃ pārṣṇiṃ grahīṣyāmi iti
12.3.19 mitrāṇi vā'sya brūyāt ahaṃ vaḥ setuḥ, mayi vibhinne sarvān eṣa vo rājā plāvayiṣyati, sambhūya vā'sya yātrāṃ vihanāma iti
12.3.20 tatsaṃhatānāṃ asaṃhatānāṃ ca preṣayet eṣa khalu rājā māṃ utpāṭya bhavatsu karma kariṣyati, budhyadhvaṃ, ahaṃ vaḥ śreyān abhyupapattum iti
12.3.21ab madhyamasya prahiṇuyād udāsīnasya vā punaḥ ।
12.3.21chd yathā''sannasya mokṣārthaṃ sarvasvena tad'rpaṇam  (iti)
   Chapt .   śastrāgnirasapraṇidhayaḥ - vīvadhāsāraprrasāravadhaḥ
12.4.01 ye cāsya durgeṣu vaidehakavyañjanāḥ, grāmesu gṛhapatikavyañjanāḥ, janapadasandhiṣu gorakṣakatāpasavyañjanāḥ, te sāmantāṭavikatatkulīnāparuddhānāṃ paṇyāgārapūrvaṃ preṣayeyuḥ ayaṃ deśo hāryaḥ iti
12.4.02 āgatāṃśca eṣāṃ durge gūḍhapuruṣān arthamānābhyāṃ abhisatkṛtya prakṛticchidrāṇi pradarśayeyuḥ
12.4.03 teṣu taiḥ saha prahareyuḥ
12.4.04 skandhāvāre vā'sya śauṇḍikavyañjanaḥ putraṃ abhityaktaṃ sthāpayitvā'vaskandakāle rasena pravāsayitvā naiṣecanikam iti madanarasayuktān madyakumbhānśataśaḥ prayacchet
12.4.05 śuddhaṃ vā madyaṃ pādyaṃ vā madyaṃ dadyād ekaṃ ahaḥ, uttaraṃ rassiddhaṃ prayacchet
12.4.06 śuddhaṃ vā madyaṃ daṇḍamukhyebhyaḥ pradāya madakāle rasasiddhaṃ prayacchet
12.4.07 daṇḍamukhyavyañjano vā putraṃ abhityaktaṃ iti samānam
12.4.08 pākvamāṃsikāudanikāuṇḍikāpūpikavyañjanā vā paṇyaviśeṣaṃ avaghoṣayitvā parasparasaṅgharṣeṇa kālikaṃ samarghataraṃ iti vā parān āhūya rasena svapaṇyānyapacārayeyuḥ
12.4.09 surākṣīradadhisarpistailāni vā tadvyavahartṛhasteṣu gṛhītā striyo bālāśca rasayukteṣu svabhājaneṣu parikireyuḥ
12.4.10 anenārgheṇa, viśiṣṭaṃ vā bhūyo dīyatām iti tatra evāvākireyuḥ
12.4.11 etānyeva vaidehakavyañjanāḥ, paṇyavireyeṇāhartāro vā
12.4.12 hasty'śvānāṃ vidhāyavaseṣu rasaṃ āsannā dadyuḥ
12.4.13 karmakaravyañjanā vā rasāktaṃ yavasaṃ udakaṃ vā vikrīṇīran
12.4.14 cirasaṃsṛṣṭā vā govāṇijakā gavāṃ ajāvīnāṃ vā yūthānyavaskandakāleṣu pareṣāṃ mohasthāneṣu pramuñceyuḥ, aśvakhara uṣṭramahiṣādīnāṃ duṣṭāṃśca
12.4.15 tadvyañjanā vā cucchundarīśoṇitāktākṣān
12.4.16 lubdhakavyañjanā vā vyālamṛgān pañjarebhyaḥ pramuñceyuḥ, sarpagrāhā vā sarpān ugraviṣān, hastijīvino vā hastinaḥ
12.4.17 agnijīvino vā'gniṃ avasṛjeyuḥ
12.4.18 gūḍhapuruṣā vā vimukhān patty'śvarathadvipamukhyān abhihanyuḥ, ādīpayeyurvā mukhyāvāsān
12.4.19 dūṣyāmitrāṭavikavyañjanāḥ praṇihitāḥ pṛṣṭhābhighātaṃ avaskandapratigrahaṃ vā kuryuḥ
12.4.20 vanagūḍhā vā pratyantaskandhaṃ upaniṣkṛṣyābhihanyuḥ, ekāyane vīvadhāsāraprasārān vā
12.4.21 sasaṅketaṃ vā rātriyuddhe bhūritūryaṃ āhatya brūyuḥ anupraviṣṭāḥ smo, labdhaṃ rājyam iti
12.4.22 rājāvāsaṃ anupraviṣṭā vā saṅkuleṣu rājānaṃ hanyuḥ
12.4.23 sarvato vā prayātaṃ ena(?eva?) mlecchāṭavikadaṇṭacāriṇaḥ sattrāpāśrayāḥ stambhavāṭāpāśrayā vā hanyuḥ
12.4.24 lubdhakavyañjanā vā'vaskandasaṅkuleṣu gūḍhayuddhahetubhirabhihanyuḥ
12.4.25 ekāyane vā śailastambhavāṭakhañjanāntar।udake vā svabhūmibalenābhihanyuḥ
12.4.26 nadīsarastaṭākasetubandhabhedavegena vā plāvayeyuḥ
12.4.27 dhānvanavanadurganimnadurgasthaṃ vā yogāgnidhūmābhyāṃ nāśayeyuḥ
12.4.28 saṅkaṭagataṃ agninā, dhānvanagataṃ dhūmena, nidhānagataṃ rasena, toyāvagāḍhaṃ duṣṭagrāhairudakacaraṇairvā tīkṣṇāḥ sādhayeyuḥ, ādīptāvāsānniṣpatantaṃ vā
12.4.29ab yogavāmanayogābhyāṃ yogenānyatamena vā ।
12.4.29chd amitraṃ atisandadhyāt saktaṃ uktāsu bhūmiṣu  (iti)
   Chapt .   yogātisaṃdhānaṃ - daṇḍātisaṃdhānaṃ - ekavijayaḥ
12.5.01 daivatejyāyām(devatā ijyāyām?) yātrāyāṃ amitrasya bahūni pūjā''gamasthānāni bhaktitaḥ
12.5.02 tatrāsya yogaṃ ubjayet
12.5.03 devatāgṛhapraviṣṭasya upari yantramokṣaṇena gūḍhabhittiṃ śilāṃ vā pātayet
12.5.04 śilāśastravarṣaṃ uttamāgārāt, kapāṭaṃ avapātitaṃ vā, bhittipraṇihitaṃ ekadeśabaddhaṃ vā parighaṃ mokṣayet
12.5.05 devatādehadhvajapraharaṇāni vā'sya upariṣṭāt pātayet
12.5.06 sthānāsanagamanabhūmiṣu vā'sya gomayapradehena gandha udakaprasekena vā rasaṃ aticārayet, puṣpacūrṇa upahāreṇa vā
12.5.07 gandhapraticchannaṃ vā'sya tīkṣṇaṃ dhūmaṃ atinayet
12.5.08 śūlakūpaṃ avapātanaṃ vā śayanāsanasyādhastād yantrabaddhatalaṃ enaṃ kīlamokṣaṇena praveśayet
12.5.09 pratyāsanne vā'mitre janapadāj janaṃ avarodhakṣamaṃ atinayet
12.5.10 durgāccānavarodhakṣamaṃ apanayet, pratyādeyaṃ ariviṣayaṃ vā preṣayet
12.5.11 janapadaṃ ca ekasthaṃ śailavananadīdurgeṣvaṭavīvyavahiteṣu vā putrabhrātṛparigṛhītaṃ sthāpayet
12.5.12 uparodhahetavo daṇḍa upanatavṛtte vyākhyātāḥ
12.5.13 tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ āyojanād dāhayet
12.5.14 udakāni ca dūṣayet, avasrāvayecca
12.5.15 kūpakūṭāvapātakaṇṭakinīśca bahirubjayet
12.5.16 suruṅgāṃ amitrasthāne bahumukhīṃ kṛtvā nicayamukhyān abhihārayet, amitraṃ vā
12.5.17 paraprayuktāyāṃ vā suruṅgāyāṃ parikhāṃ udakāntikīṃ khānayet, kūpaśālāṃ anusālaṃ vā
12.5.18 toyakumbhān kāṃsyabhāṇḍāni vā śaṅkāsthāneṣu sthāpayet khātābhijñānārtham
12.5.19 jñāte suruṅgāpathe pratisuruṅgāṃ kārayet
12.5.20 madhye bhittvā dhūmaṃ udakaṃ vā prayacchet
12.5.21 prativihitadurgo vā mūle dāyād kṛtvā pratilomāṃ asya diśaṃ gacchet, yato vā mitrairbandhubhirāṭavikairvā saṃsṛjyeta parasyāmitrairdūṣyairvā mahadbhiḥ, yato vā gato'sya mitrairviyogaṃ kuryāt pārṣṇiṃ vā gṛhṇīyāt rājyaṃ vā'sya hārayet vīvadhāsāraprasārān vā vārayet, yato vā śaknuyād ākṣikavad apakṣepeṇāsya prahartuṃ, yato vā svaṃ rājyaṃ trāyeta mūlasya upacayaṃ vā kuryāt
12.5.22 yataḥ sandhiṃ abhipretaṃ labheta tato vā gacchet
12.5.23 sahaprasthāyino vā'sya preṣayeyuḥ ayaṃ te śatrurasmākaṃ hastagataḥ, paṇyaṃ viprakāraṃ vā'padiśya hiraṇyaṃ antaḥsārabalaṃ ca preṣaya yasya enaṃ arpayema baddhaṃ pravāsitaṃ vā iti
12.5.24 pratipanne hiraṇyaṃ sārabalaṃ cādadīta
12.5.25 antapālo vā durgasampradāne bala ekadeśaṃ atinīya viśvastaṃ ghātayet
12.5.26 janapadaṃ ekasthaṃ vā ghātayituṃ amitrānīkaṃ āvāhayet
12.5.27 tad avaruddhadeśaṃ atinīya viśvastaṃ ghātayet
12.5.28 mitravyañjano vā bāhyasya preṣayet kṣīṇaṃ asmin durge dhānyaṃ snehāḥ kṣāro lavaṇaṃ vā, tad amuṣmin deśe kāle ca pravekṣyati, tad upagṛhāṇa iti
12.5.29 tato rasaviddhaṃ dhānyaṃ snehaṃ kṣāraṃ lavaṇaṃ vā dūṣyāmitrāṭavikāḥ praveśayeyuḥ, anye vā'bhityaktāḥ
12.5.30 tena sarvabhāṇḍavīvadhagrahaṇaṃ vyākhyātam
12.5.31 sandhiṃ vā kṛtvā hiraṇya ekadeśaṃ asmai dadyāt, vilambamānaḥ śeṣam
12.5.32 tato rakṣāvidhānānyavasrāvayet
12.5.33 agnirasaśastrairvā praharet
12.5.34 hiraṇyapratigrāhiṇo vā'sya vallabhān anugṛhṇīyāt
12.5.35 parikṣīṇo vā'smai durgaṃ dattvā nirgacchet
12.5.36 suruṅgayā kukṣipradareṇa vā prākārabhedena nirgacchet
12.5.37 rātrāvavaskandaṃ dattvā siddhaḥ tiṣṭhet, asiddhaḥ pārśvenāpagacchet
12.5.38 pāṣaṇḍacchadmanā mandaparivāro nirgacchet
12.5.39 pretavyañjano vā gūḍhairnihriyeta
12.5.40 strīveṣadhārī vā pretaṃ anugacchet
12.5.41 daivata upahāraśrāddhaprahavaṇeṣu vā rasaviddhaṃ annapānaṃ avasṛjya
12.5.42 kṛta upajāpo dūṣyavyañjanairniṣpatya gūḍhasainyo'bhihanyāt
12.5.43 evaṃ gṛhītadurgo vā prāśyaprāśaṃ caityaṃ upasthāpya daivatapratimācchidraṃ praviśyāsīta, gūḍhabhittiṃ vā, daivatapratimāyuktaṃ vā bhūmigṛham
12.5.44 vismṛte suruṅgayā rātrau rājāvāsaṃ anupraviśya suptaṃ amitraṃ hanyāt
12.5.45 yantraviśleṣaṇaṃ vā viśleṣyādhastād avapātayet
12.5.46 rasāgniyogenāvaliptaṃ gṛhaṃ jatugṛhaṃ vā'dhiśayānaṃ amitraṃ ādīpayet
12.5.47 pramadavanavihārāṇāṃ anyatame vā vihārasthāne pramattaṃ bhūmigṛhasuruṅgāgūḍhabhittipraviṣṭāḥ tīkṣṇā hanyuḥ, gūḍhapraṇihitā vā rasena
12.5.48 svapato vā niruddhe deśe gūḍhāḥ striyaḥ sarparasāgnidhūmān upari muñceyuḥ
12.5.49 pratyutpanne vā kāraṇe yad yad upapadyeta tat tad amitre'ntaḥpuragate gūḍhasañcāraḥ prayuñjīta
12.5.50 tato gūḍhaṃ evāpagacchet, svajanasaṃjñāṃ ca prarūpayet
12.5.51ab dvāhsthān varṣadharāṃścānyānnigūḍha upahitān pare ।

13.1.01 vijigīṣuḥ paragrāmaṃ avāptukāmaḥ sarvajñadaivatasamyogakhyāpanābhyāṃ svapakṣaṃ uddharṣayet, parapakṣaṃ ca udvejayet
13.1.02 sarvajñakhyāpanaṃ tu - gṛhaguhyapravṛttijñānena pratyādeśo mukhyānāṃ, kaṇṭakaśodhanāpasarpāvagamena prakāśanaṃ rājadviṣṭakāriṇāṃ, vijñāpya upāyanakhyāpanaṃ adṛṣṭasaṃsargavidyāsaṃjñā''dibhiḥ, videśapravṛttijñānaṃ tad ahareva gṛhakapotena mudrāsamyuktena
13.1.03 daivatasamyogakhyāpanaṃ tu - suruṅgāmukhenāgnicaityadaivatapratimācchidrān anupraviṣṭairagnicaityadaivatavyañjanaiḥ sambhāṣaṇaṃ pūjanaṃ ca, udakād utthitairvā nāgavaruṇavyañjanaiḥ sambhāṣaṇaṃ pūjanaṃ ca, rātrāvantar।udake samudravālukākośaṃ praṇidhāyāgnimālādarśanaṃ, śilāśikyāvagṛhīte plavake sthānaṃ, udakabastinā jarāyuṇā vā śiro'vagūḍhanāsaḥ pṛṣatāntrakulīranakraśiṃśumāra udravasābhirvā śatapākyaṃ tailaṃ nastaḥ prayogaḥ
13.1.04 tena rātrigaṇaścarati
13.1.05 ityudakacaraṇāni
13.1.06 tairvaruṇanāgakanyāvākyakriyā sambhāṣaṇaṃ ca, kopasthāneṣu mukhād agnidhūma utsargaḥ
13.1.07 tad asya svaviṣaye kārtāntikanaimittikamauhūrtikapaurāṇika ikṣaṇikagūḍhapuruṣāḥ sācivyakarāḥ taddarśinaśca prakāśayeyuḥ
13.1.08 parasya viṣaye daivatadarśanaṃ divyakośadaṇḍa utpattiṃ cāsya brūyuḥ
13.1.09 daivatapraśnanimittavāyasāṅgavidyāsvapnamṛgapakṣivyāhāreṣu cāsya vijayaṃ brūyuḥ, viparītaṃ amitrasya
13.1.10 sadundubhiṃ ulkāṃ ca parasya nakṣatre darśayeyuḥ
13.1.11 parasya mukhyān mitratvena upadiśanto dūtavyañjanāḥ svāmisatkāraṃ brūyuḥ, svapakṣabalādhānaṃ parapakṣapratighātaṃ ca
13.1.12 tulyayogakṣemaṃ amātyānāṃ āyudhīyānāṃ ca kathayeyuḥ
13.1.13 teṣu vyasanābhyudayāvekṣaṇaṃ apatyapūjanaṃ ca prayuñjīta
13.1.14 tena parapakṣaṃ utsāhayed yathā uktaṃ purastāt
13.1.15 bhūyaśca vakṣyāmaḥ
13.1.16 sādhāraṇagardabhena dakṣān, lakuṭaśākhāhananābhyāṃ daṇḍacāriṇaḥ, kula eḍakena ca udvignān, aśanivarṣeṇa vimānitān, vidulenāvakeśinā vāyasapiṇḍena kaitavajameghena iti vihatāśān durbhagālaṅkāreṇa dveṣiṇā iti pūjāphalān, vyāghracarmaṇā mṛtyukūṭena ca upahitān, pīluvikhādanena karakayoṣṭrayā gardabhīkṣīrā'bhimanthanena iti dhruva upakāriṇa iti
13.1.17 pratipannān arthamānābhyāṃ yojayet
13.1.18 dravyabhaktacchidreṣu ca enān dravyabhaktadānairanugṛhṇīyāt
13.1.19 apratigṛhṇatāṃ strīkumārālaṅkārān abhihareyuḥ
13.1.20 durbhikṣastenāṭavy।upaghāteṣu ca paurajānapadān utsāhayantaḥ sattriṇo brūyuḥ rājānaṃ anugrahaṃ yācāmahe niranugrahāḥ paratra gacchāmaḥ iti
13.1.21ab tathā iti pratipanneṣu dravyadhānyānyaparigrahaiḥ ।
13.1.21chd sācivyaṃ kāryaṃ ityetad upajāpād bhūtaṃ mahat  (iti)
   Chapt .   yogavāmanam
13.2.01 muṇḍo jaṭilo vā parvataguhāvāsī caturvarṣaśatāyurbruvāṇaḥ prabhūtajaṭilāntevāsī nagarābhyāśe tiṣṭhet
13.2.02 śiṣyāścāsya mūlaphala upagamanairamātyān rājānaṃ ca bhagavaddarśanāya yojayeyuḥ
13.2.03 samāgatāśca rājñā pūrvarājadeśābhijñānāni kathayet, śate śate ca varṣāṇāṃ pūrṇe'haṃ agniṃ praviśya punarbālo bhavāmi, tad iha bhavat samīpe caturthaṃ agniṃ pravekṣyāmi, avaśyaṃ me bhavān mānayitavyaḥ, trīn varān vṛṇīṣṇa(vṛṣīṣva) iti
13.2.04 pratipannaṃ brūyāt saptarātraṃ iha saputradāreṇa prekṣāprahavaṇapūrvaṃ vastavyam iti
13.2.05 vasantaṃ avaskandeta
13.2.06 muṇḍo vā jaṭilo vā sthānikavyañjanaḥ prabhūtajaṭilāntevāsī vastaśoṇitadigdhāṃ veṇuśalākāṃ suvarṇacūrṇenāvalipya valmīke nidadhyād upajihvikānusaraṇārthaṃ, svarṇanālikāṃ vā
13.2.07 tataḥ sattrī rājñaḥ kathayet asau siddhaḥ puṣpitaṃ nidhiṃ jānāti iti
13.2.08 sa rājñā pṛṣṭhaḥ tathā iti brūyāt, taccābhijñānaṃ darśayet, bhūyo vā hiraṇyaṃ antar।ādhāya
13.2.09 brūyācca enaṃ nāgarakṣito'yaṃ nidhiḥ praṇipātasādhyaḥ iti
13.2.10 pratipannaṃ brūyāt saptarātram iti samānam
13.2.11 sthānikavyañjanaṃ vā rātrau tejanāgniyuktaṃ ekānte tiṣṭhantaṃ sattriṇaḥ kramābhīnītaṃ rājñaḥ kathayeyuḥ asau siddhaḥ sāmedhikaḥ iti
13.2.12 taṃ rājā yaṃ arthaṃ yāceta taṃ asya kariṣyamāṇaḥ saptarātram iti samānam
13.2.13 siddhavyañjano vā rājānaṃ jambhakavidyābhiḥ pralobhayet
13.2.14 taṃ rājā iti samānam
13.2.15 siddhavyañjano vā deśadevatāṃ abhyarhitāṃ āśritya prahavaṇairabhīkṣṇaṃ prakṛtimukhyān abhisaṃvāsya krameṇa rājānaṃ atisandadhyāt
13.2.16 jaṭilavyañjanaṃ antar।udakavāsinaṃ vā sarvaśvetaṃ taṭasuruṅgābhūmigṛhāpasaraṇaṃ varuṇaṃ nāgarājaṃ vā sattriṇaḥ kramābhinītaṃ rājñaḥ kathayeyuḥ
13.2.17 taṃ rājā iti samānam
13.2.18 janapadāntevāsī siddhavyañjano vā rājānaṃ śatrudarśanāya yojayet
13.2.19 pratipannaṃ bimbaṃ kṛtvā śatruṃ āvāhayitvā niruddhe deśe ghātayet
13.2.20 aśvapaṇya upayātā vaidehakavyañjanāḥ paṇya upāyananimittaṃ āhūya rājānaṃ paṇyaparīkṣāyāṃ āsaktaṃ aśvavyatikīrṇaṃ vā hanyuḥ, aśvaiśca prahareyuḥ
13.2.21 nagarābhyāśe vā caityaṃ āruhya rātrau tīkṣṇāḥ kumbheṣu nālīn vā vidulāni dhamantaḥ svāmino mukhyānāṃ vā māṃsāni bhakṣayiṣyāmaḥ, pūjā no vartatām ityavyaktaṃ brūyuḥ
13.2.22 tad eṣāṃ naimittikamauhūrtikavyañjanāḥ khyāpayeyuḥ
13.2.23 maṅgalye vā hrade taṭākamadhye vā rātrau tejanatailābhyaktā nāgarūpiṇaḥ śaktimusalānyayomayāni niṣpeṣayantaḥ tathaiva brūyuḥ
13.2.24 ṛkṣacarmakañcukino vā'gnidhūma utsargayuktā rakṣorūpaṃ vahantaḥ trirapasavyaṃ nagaraṃ kurvāṇāḥ śvasṛgālavāśitāntareṣu tathaiva brūyuḥ
13.2.25 caityadaivatapratimāṃ vā tejanatailenābhrapaṭalacchannenāgninā vā rātrau prajvālya tathaiva brūyuḥ
13.2.26 tad anye khyāpayeyuḥ
13.2.27 daivatapratimānāṃ abhyarhitānāṃ vā śoṇitena prasrāvaṃ atimātraṃ kuryuḥ
13.2.28 tad anye devarudhirasaṃsrāve saṅgrāme parājayaṃ brūyuḥ
13.2.29 sandhirātriṣu śmaśānapramukhe vā caityaṃ ūrdhvabhakṣitairmanuṣyaiḥ prarūpayeyuḥ
13.2.30 tato rakṣorūpī manuṣyakaṃ yāceta
13.2.31 yaścātra śūravādiko'nyatamo vā draṣṭuṃ āgacchet taṃ anye lohamusalairhanyuḥ, yathā rakṣobhirhata iti jñāyeta
13.2.32 tad adbhutaṃ rājñaḥ taddarśinaḥ sattriṇaśca kathayeyuḥ
13.2.33 tato naimititkamauhūrtikavyañjanāḥ śāntiṃ prāyaścittaṃ brūyuḥ anyathā mahad akuśalaṃ rājño deśasya ca iti
13.2.34 pratipannaṃ eteṣu saptarātraṃ eka ekamantrabalihomaṃ svayaṃ rājñā kartavyam iti brūyuḥ
13.2.35 tataḥ samānam
13.2.36 etān vā yogān ātmani darśayitvā pratikurvīta pareṣāṃ upadeśārtham
13.2.37 tataḥ prayojayed yogān
13.2.38 yogadarśanapratīkāreṇa vā kośābhisaṃharaṇaṃ kuryāt
13.2.39 hastikāmaṃ vā nāgavanapālā hastinā lakṣaṇyena pralobhayeyuḥ
13.2.40 pratipannaṃ gahanaṃ ekāyanaṃ vā'tinīya ghātayeyuḥ, baddhvā vā'pahareyuḥ
13.2.41 tena mṛgayākāmo vyākhyātaḥ
13.2.42 dravyastrīlolupaṃ āḍhyavidhavābhirvā paramarūpayauvanābhiḥ strībhirdāyanikṣepārthaṃ upanītābhiḥ sattriṇaḥ pralobhayeyuḥ
13.2.43 pratipannaṃ rātrau sattracchannāḥ samāgame śastrarasābhyāṃ ghātayeyuḥ
13.2.44 siddhapravrajitacaityastūpadaivatapratimānāṃ abhīkṣṇābhigamaneṣu vā bhūmigṛhasuruṅgārūḍhabhittipraviṣṭāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ paraṃ abhihanyuḥ
13.2.45ab yeṣu deśeṣu yāḥ prekṣāḥ prekṣate pārthivaḥ svayam ।
13.2.45chd yātrāvihāre ramate yatra krīḍati vā'mbhasi
13.2.46ab dhig।ukty।ādiṣu sarveṣu yajñaprahavaṇeṣu vā ।
13.2.46chd sūtikāpretarogeṣu prītiśokabhayeṣu vā ।
13.2.47ab pramādaṃ yāti yasmin vā viśvāsāt svajana utsave
13.2.47chd yatrāsyārakṣisañcāro durdine saṅkuleṣu vā ।
13.2.48ab viprasthāne pradīpte vā praviṣṭe nirjane'pi vā ।
13.2.48chd vastrābharaṇamālyānāṃ phelābhiḥ śayanāsanaiḥ
13.2.49ab madyabhojanaphelābhiḥ tūryairvā'bhigatāḥ saha ।
13.2.49chd prahareyurariṃ tīkṣṇāḥ pūrvapraṇihitaiḥ saha  (iti)
13.2.50ab yathaiva praviśeyuśca dviṣataḥ sattrahetubhiḥ ।
13.2.50chd tathaiva cāpagaccheyurityuktaṃ yogavāmanam
   Chapt .   apasarpapraṇidhiḥ
13.3.01 śreṇīmukhyaṃ āptaṃ niṣpātayet
13.3.02 sa paraṃ āśrtya pakṣāpadeśena svaviṣayāt sācivyakarasahāya upādānaṃ kurvīta
13.3.03 kṛtāpasarpa upacayo vā paraṃ anumānya svāmino dūṣyagrāmaṃ vītahasty'śvaṃ dūṣyāmātyaṃ daṇḍaṃ ākrandaṃ vā hatvā parasya preṣayet
13.3.04 janapada ekadeśaṃ śreṇīṃ aṭavīṃ vā sahāya upādānārthaṃ saṃśrayeta
13.3.05 viśvāsaṃ upagataḥ svāminaḥ preṣayet
13.3.06 tataḥ svāmī hastibandhanaṃ aṭavīghātaṃ vā'padiśya gūḍhaṃ eva praharet
13.3.07 etenāmātyāṭavikā vyākhyātāḥ
13.3.08 śatruṇā maitrīṃ kṛtvā'mātyān avakṣipet
13.3.09 te tatśatroḥ preṣayeyuḥ bhartāraṃ naḥ prasādaya iti
13.3.10 sa yaṃ dūtaṃ preṣayet, taṃ upālabheta bhartā te māṃ amātyairbhedayati, na ca punarihāgantavyam iti
13.3.11 atha ekaṃ amātyaṃ niṣpātayet
13.3.12 sa paraṃ āśritya yogāpasarpāparaktadūṣyān aśaktimataḥ stenāṭavikān ubhaya upaghātakān vā parasya upaharet
13.3.13 āptabhāva upagataḥ pravīrapuruṣa upaghātaṃ asya upahared antapālaṃ āṭavikaṃ daṇḍacāriṇaṃ vā dṛḍhaṃ asau cāsau ca te śatruṇā sandhatte iti
13.3.14 atha paścād abhityaktaśāsanairenān ghātayet
13.3.15  daṇḍabalavyavahāreṇa vā śatruṃ udyojya ghātayet
13.3.16 kṛtyapakṣa upagraheṇa vā parasyāmitraṃ rājānaṃ ātmanyapakārayitvā'bhiyuñjīta
13.3.17 tataḥ parasya preṣayet asau te vairī mamāpakaroti, taṃ ehi sambhūya haniṣyāvaḥ, bhūmau hiraṇye vā te parigrahaḥ iti
13.3.18 pratipannaṃ abhisatkṛtyāgataṃ avaskandena prakāśayuddhena vā śatruṇā ghātayet
13.3.19 abhiviśvāsanārthaṃ bhūmidānaputrābhiṣekarakṣā'padeśena vā grāhayet
13.3.20 aviṣahyaṃ upāṃśudaṇḍena vā ghātayet
13.3.21 sa ced daṇḍaṃ dadyānna svayaṃ āgacchet taṃ asya vairiṇā ghātayet
13.3.22 daṇḍena vā prayātuṃ icchenna vijigīṣuṇā tathā'pyenaṃ ubhayataḥsampīḍanena ghātayet
13.3.23 aviśvasto vā pratyekaśo yātuṃ icched rājya ekadeśaṃ vā yātavyasyādātukāmaḥ, tathā'pyenaṃ vairiṇā sarvasandohena vā ghātayet
13.3.24 vairiṇā vā saktasya daṇḍa upanayena mūlaṃ anyato hārayet
13.3.25 śatrubhūmyā vā mitraṃ paṇeta, mitrabhūmyā vā śatrum
13.3.26 tataḥ śatrubhūmilipsāyāṃ mitreṇātmanyapakārayitvā'bhiyuñjīta - iti samānāḥ pūrveṇa sarva eva yogāḥ
13.3.27 śatruṃ vā mitrabhūmilipsāyāṃ pratipannaṃ daṇḍenānugṛhṇīyāt
13.3.28 tato mitragataṃ atisandadhyāt
13.3.29 kṛtapratividhāno vā vyasanaṃ ātmano darśayitvā mitreṇāmitraṃ utsāhayitvā''tmānaṃ abhiyojayet
13.3.30 tataḥ sampīḍanena ghātayet, jīvagrāheṇa vā rājyavinimayaṃ kārayet
13.3.31 mitreṇāśritaścetśatruragrāhye sthātuṃ icchet sāmantādibhirmūlaṃ asya hārayet
13.3.32 daṇḍena vā trātuṃ ichet taṃ asya ghātayet
13.3.33 tau cenna bhidyeyātāṃ prakāśaṃ evānyonyabhūmyā paṇeta
13.3.34 tataḥ parasparaṃ mitravyañjanā vā ubhayavetanā vā dūtān preṣayeyuḥ ayaṃ te rājā bhūmiṃ lipsate śatrusaṃhitaḥ iti
13.3.35 tayoranyataro jātāśaṅkāroṣaḥ, pūrvavacceṣteta
13.3.36 durgarāṣṭradaṇḍamukhyān vā kṛtyapakṣahetubhirabhivikhyāpya pravrājayet
13.3.37 te yuddhāvaskandāvarodhavyasaneṣu śatruṃ atisandadhyuḥ
13.3.38 bhedaṃ vā'sya svavargebhyaḥ kuryuḥ
13.3.39 abhityaktaśāsanaiḥ pratisamānayeyuḥ
13.3.40 lubdhakavyañjanā vā māṃsavikrayeṇa dvāhsthā dauvārikāpāśrayāścorābhyāgamaṃ parasya dviḥ tririti nivedya labdhapratyayā bharturanīkaṃ dvidhā niveśya grāmavadhe'vaskande ca dviṣato brūyuḥ āsannaścoragaṇaḥ, mahāṃścākrandaḥ, prabhūtaṃ sainyaṃ āgacchatu iti
13.3.41 tad arpayitvā grāmaghātadaṇḍasya sainyaṃ itarad ādāya rātrau durgadvāreṣu brūyuḥ hataścoragaṇaḥ, siddhayātraṃ idaṃ sainyaṃ āgataṃ, dvāraṃ apāvriyatām iti
13.3.42 pūrvapraṇihitā vā dvārāṇi dadyuḥ
13.3.43 taiḥ saha prahareyuḥ
13.3.44 kāruśilpipāṣaṇḍakuśīlavavaidehakavyañjanān āyudhīyān vvā paradurge praṇidadhyāt
13.3.45 teṣāṃ gṛhapatikavyañjanāḥ kāṣṭhatṛṇadhānyapaṇyaśakaṭaiḥ praharaṇāvaraṇānyabhihareyuḥ, devadhvajapratimābhirvā
13.3.46 tataḥ tadvyañjanāḥ pramattavadhaṃ avaskandapratigrahaṃ abhipraharaṇaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ śaṅkhadundubhiśabdena vā praviṣṭam ityāvedayeyuḥ
13.3.47 prākāradvārāṭṭālakadānaṃ anīkabhedaṃ ghātaṃ vā kuryuḥ
13.3.48 sārthagaṇavāsibhirātivāhikaiḥ kanyāvāhikairaśvapaṇyavyavahāribhirupakaraṇahārakairdhānyakretṛvikretṛbhirvā pravrajitaliṅgibhirdūtaiśca daṇaḍ'tinayanaṃ, sandhikarmaviśvāsanārtham
13.3.49 iti rājāpasarpāḥ
13.3.50 eta evāṭavīnāṃ apasarpāḥ kaṇṭakaśodhana uktāśca
13.3.51 vrajaṃ aṭavy।āsannaṃ apasarpāḥ sārthaṃ vā corairghātayeyuḥ
13.3.52 kṛtasaṅketaṃ annapānaṃ cātra madanarasaviddhaṃ vā kṛtvā'pagaccheyuḥ
13.3.53 gopālakavaidehakāśca tataścorān gṛhītaloptrabhārān madanarasavikārakāle'vaskandayeyuḥ
13.3.54 saṅkarṣaṇadaivatīyo vā muṇḍajaṭilavyañjanaḥ prahavaṇakarmaṇā madanarasayogenātisandadhyāt
13.3.55 athāvaskandaṃ dadyāt
13.3.56 śauṇḍikavyañjano vā daivatapretakārya utsavasamājeṣvāṭavikān surāvikraya upāyananimittaṃ madanarasayogenātisandadhyāt
13.3.57 athāvaskandaṃ dadyāt
13.3.58ab grāmaghātapraviṣṭāṃ vā vikṣipya bahudhā'ṭavīm ।
13.3.58chd ghātayed iti corāṇāṃ apasarpāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   paryupāsanakarma - avamardaḥ
13.4.01 karśanapūrvaṃ paryupāsanakarma
13.4.02 janapadaṃ yathāniviṣṭaṃ abhaye sthāpayet
13.4.03 utthitaṃ anugrahaparihārābhyāṃ niveṣayet, anyatrāpasarataḥ
13.4.04 saṅgrāmād anyasyāṃ bhūmau niveśayet, ekasyāṃ vā vāsayet
13.4.05 na hyajano janapado rājyaṃ ajanapadaṃ vā bhavati iti kauṭilyaḥ
13.4.06 viṣamasthasya muṣṭiṃ sasyaṃ vā hanyād, vīvadhaprasārau ca
13.4.07ab prasāravīvadhacchedān muṣṭisasyavadhād api ।
13.4.07chd vamanād gūḍhaghātācca jāyate prakṛtikṣayaḥ
13.4.08 prabhūtaguṇabaddha(vaddha) anyakupyayantraśastrāvaraṇaviṣṭiraśmisamagraṃ me sainyaṃ, ṛtuśca purastāt, apartuḥ parasya, vyādhidurbhikṣanicayarakṣākṣayaḥ krītabalanirvedo mitrabalanirvedaśca iti paryupāsīta
13.4.09 kṛtvā skandhāvārasya rakṣāṃ vīvadhāsārayoḥ pathaśca, parikṣipya durgaṃ khātasālābhyāṃ, dūṣayitvā udakaṃ, avasrāvya parikhāḥ sampūrayitvā vā, suruṅgābalakuṭikābhyāṃ vapraprākārau hārayet, dāraṃ ca guḍena
13.4.10 nimnaṃ vā pāṃsumālayā''cchādayet
13.4.11 bahulārakṣaṃ yantrairghātayet
13.4.12 niṣkirād upaniṣkṛṣyāśvaiśca prahareyuḥ
13.4.13 vikramāntareṣu ca niyogavikalpasamuccayaiśca upāyānāṃ siddhiṃ lipseta
13.4.14 durgavāsinaḥ śyenakākanaptṛbhāsaśukasārika ulūkakapotān grāhayitvā puccheṣvagniyogayuktān paradurge visṛjet
13.4.15 apakṛṣṭaskandhāvārād ucchritadhvajadhanvārakṣo vā mānuṣeṇāgninā paradurgaṃ ādīpayet
13.4.16 gūḍhapurṣāścāntardurgapālakā nakulavānarabiḍālaśunāṃ puccheṣvagniyogaṃ ādhāya kāṇḍanicayarakṣāvidhānaveśmasu visṛjeyuḥ
13.4.17 śuṣkamatsyānāṃ udareṣvagniṃ ādhāya vallūre vā vāyasa upahāreṇa vayobhirhārayeyuḥ
13.4.18 saraladevadārupūtitṛṇagugguluśrīveṣṭakasarjarasalākṣāgulikāḥ khara uṣṭrājāvīnāṃ leṇḍaṃ cāgnidhāraṇam
13.4.19 priyālacūrṇaṃ avalgujamaṣīmadhu।ucchiṣṭaṃ aśvakhara uṣṭragoleṇḍaṃ ityeṣa kṣepyo'gniyogaḥ
13.4.20 sarvalohacūrṇaṃ agnivarṇaṃ vā kumbhīsīsatrapucūrṇaṃ vā pāribhadrakapalāśapuṣpakeśamaṣītailamadhu।ucchiṣṭakaśrīveṣṭakayukto'gniyogo viśvāsaghātī vā
13.4.21 tenāvaliptaḥ śaṇatrapusavalkaveṣṭito bāṇa ityagniyogaḥ
13.4.22 na tveva vidyamāne parākrame'gniṃ avasṛjet
13.4.23 aviśvāsyo hyagnirdaivapīḍanaṃ ca, apratisaṅkhyātaprāṇidhānyapaśuhiraṇyakupyadravyakṣayakaraḥ
13.4.24 kṣīṇanicayaṃ cāvāptaṃ api rājyaṃ kṣayāya eva bhavati iti paryupāsanakarma
13.4.25 sarvārambha upakaraṇaviṣṭisampanno'smi, vyādhitaḥ para upadhāviruddhaprakṛtirakṛtadurgakarmanicayo vā, nirāsāraḥ sāsāro vā purā mitraiḥ sandhatte ityavamardakālaḥ
13.4.26  svayaṃ agnau jāte samutthāpite vā prahavaṇe prekṣā'nīkadarśanasaṅgasaurikakalaheṣu nityayuddhaśrāntabale bahulayuddhapratividdhapretapuruṣe jāgaraṇaklāntasuptajane durdine nadīvege vā nīhārasamplave vā'vamṛdnīyāt
13.4.27 skandhāvāraṃ utsṛjya vā vanagūḍhaḥ śatruṃ niṣkrāntaṃ ghātayet
13.4.28 mitrāsāramukhyavyañjano vā samruddhena maitrīṃ kṛtvā dūtaṃ abhityaktaṃ preṣayet - idaṃ te chidraṃ, ime dūṣyāḥ samroddhurvā chidraṃ, ayaṃ te kṛtyapakṣaḥ iti
13.4.29 taṃ pratidūtaṃ ādāya nirgacchantaṃ vijigīṣurgṛhītvā doṣaṃ abhivikhyāpya pravāsya apagacchet
13.4.30 tato mitrāsāravyañjano vā samruddhaṃ brūyāt māṃ trātuṃ upanirgaccha, mayā vā saha samroddhāraṃ jahi iti
13.4.31 pratipannaṃ ubhayataḥsampīḍanena ghātayet, jīvagrāheṇa vā rājyavinimayaṃ kārayet
13.4.32 nagaraṃ vā'sya pramṛdnīyāt
13.4.33 sārabalaṃ vā'sya vamayitvā'bhihanyāt
13.4.34 tena daṇḍa upanatāṭavikā vyākhyātāḥ
13.4.35 daṇḍa upanatāṭavikayoranyataro vā samruddhasya preṣayet - ayaṃ samroddhā vyādhitaḥ, pārṣṇigrāheṇābhiyuktaḥ, chidraṃ anyad utthitaṃ, anyasyāṃ bhūmāvapayātukāmaḥ iti
13.4.36 pratipanne samroddhā skandhāvāraṃ ādīpyāpayāyāt
13.4.37 tataḥ pūrvavad ācaret
13.4.38 paṇyasampātaṃ vā kṛtvā paṇyena enaṃ rasaviddhenātisandadhyāt
13.4.39 āsāravyañjano vā samruddhasya dūtaṃ preṣayet - mayā bāhyaṃ abhihataṃ upanirgacchābhihantum iti
13.4.40 pratipannaṃ pūrvavad ācaret
13.4.41 mitraṃ bandhuṃ vā'padiśya yogapuruṣāḥ śāsanamudrāhastāḥ praviśya durgaṃ grāhayeyuḥ
13.4.42 āsāravyañjñano vā samruddhasya preṣayet - amuṣmin deśe kāle ca skandhāvāraṃ abhihaniṣyāmi, yuṣmābhirapi yoddhavyam iti
13.4.43 pratipannaṃ yathā uktaṃ abhyāghātasaṅkulaṃ darśayitvā rātrau durgānniṣkrāntaṃ ghātayet
13.4.44 yad vā mitraṃ āvāhayed āṭavvikaṃ vā, taṃ utsāhayet vikramya samruddhe bhūmiṃ asya pratipadyasva iti
13.4.45 vikrāntaṃ prakṛtibhirdūṣyamukhya upagraheṇa vā ghātayet, svayaṃ vā rasena mitraghātako'yam ityavāptārthaḥ
13.4.46 vikramitukāmaṃ vā mitravyañjanaḥ parasyābhiśaṃset
13.4.47 āptabhāva upagataḥ pravīrapuruṣānasya upaghātayet
13.4.48 sandhiṃ vā kṛtvā janapadaṃ enaṃ niveśayet
13.4.49 niviṣṭaṃ asya janapadaṃ avijñāto hanyāt
13.4.50 apakārayitvā dūṣyāṭavikeṣu vā bala ekadeśaṃ atinīya durgaṃ avaskandena hārayet
13.4.51 dūṣyāmitrāṭavikadveṣyapratyapasṛtāśca kṛtārthamānasaṃjñācihnāḥ paradurgaṃ avaskandeyuḥ
13.4.52 paradurgaṃ avaskandya skandhāvāraṃ vā patitaparānmukhābhipannaṃ uktakeśaśastrabhayavirūpebhyaścābhayaṃ ayudhyamānebhyaśca dadyuḥ
13.4.53 paradurgaṃ avāpya viśuddhaśatrupakṣaṃ kṛta upāṃśudaṇḍapratīkāraṃ antarbahiśca praviśet
13.4.54 evaṃ vijigīṣuramitrabhūmiṃ labdhvā madhyamaṃ lipseta, tatsiddhāvudāsīnam
13.4.55 eṣa prathamo mārgaḥ pṛthivīṃ jetum
13.4.56 madhyama udāsīnayorabhāve guṇātiśayenāriprakṛtīḥ sādhayet, tata uttarāḥ prakṛtīḥ
13.4.57 eṣa dvitīyo mārgaḥ
13.4.58 maṇḍalasyābhāve śatruṇā mitraṃ mitreṇa vā śatruṃ ubhayataḥsampīḍanena sādhayet
13.4.59 eṣatṛtīyo mārgaḥ
13.4.60 śakyaṃ ekaṃ vā sāmantaṃ sādhayet, tena dviguṇo dvitīyaṃ, triguṇaḥ tṛtīyam
13.4.61 eṣa caturtho mārgaḥ pṛthivīṃ jetum
13.4.62 jitvā ca pṛthivīṃ vibhaktavarṇāśramāṃ svadharmeṇa bhuñjīta
13.4.63ab upajāpo'pasarpaśca vāmanaṃ paryupāsanam ।
13.4.63chd avamardaśca pañca ete durgalambhasya hetavaḥ  (iti)
   Chapt .   labdhapraśamanam
13.5.01 dvividhaṃ vijigīṣoḥ samutthānaṃ - aṭavy।ādikaṃ ekagrāmādikaṃ ca
13.5.02 trividhaścāsya lambhaḥ - navo, bhūtapūrvaḥ, pitrya iti
13.5.03 navaṃ avāpya lābhaṃ paradoṣān svaguṇaiśchādayet, guṇān guṇadvaiguṇyena
13.5.04 svadharmakarmānugrahaparihāradānamānakarmabhiśca prakṛtipriyahitānyanuvarteta
13.5.05 yathāsambhāṣitaṃ ca kṛtyapakṣaṃ upagrāhayet, bhūyaśca kṛtaprayāsam
13.5.06 aviśvāso hi visaṃvādakaḥ sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ ca bhavati, prakṛtiviruddhācāraśca
13.5.07 tasmāt samānaśīlaveṣabhāṣā''cāratāṃ upagachet
13.5.08 deśadaivatasmāja utsavavihāreṣu ca bhaktiṃ anuvarteta
13.5.09 deśagrāmajātisaṅghamukhyeṣu cābhīkṣṇaṃ sattriṇaḥ parasyāpacāraṃ darśayeyuḥ, māhābhāgyaṃ bhaktiṃ ca teṣu svāminaḥ, svāmisatkāraṃ ca vidyamānam
13.5.10 ucitaiśca enān bhogaparihārarakṣā'vekṣaṇairbhuñjīta
13.5.11 sarvadevatā''śramapūjanaṃ ca vidyāvākyadharmaśūrapuruṣāṇāṃ ca bhūmidravyadānaparihārān kārayet, sarvabandhanamokṣaṇaṃ anugrahaṃ dīnānāthavyādhitānāṃ ca
13.5.12 cāturmāsyeṣvardhamāsikaṃ aghātaṃ, paurṇamāsīṣu ca cātūrātrikaṃ rājadeśanakṣatreṣvaikarātrikam
13.5.13 yonibālavadhaṃ puṃstva upaghātaṃ ca pratiṣedhayet
13.5.14 yacca kośadaṇḍa upaghātakaṃ adharmiṣṭhaṃ vā caritraṃ manyeta tad apanīya dharmyavyavahāraṃ sthāpayet
13.5.15 coraprakṛtīnāṃ mlecchajātīnāṃ ca sthānaviparyāsaṃ anekasthaṃ kārayet, durgarāṣṭradaṇḍamukhyānāṃ ca
13.5.16 parā upagṛhītānāṃ ca mantripurohitānāṃ parasya pratyanteṣvanekasthaṃ vāsaṃ kārayet
13.5.17 apakārasamarthān anukṣiyato vā bhartṛvināśaṃ upāṃśudaṇḍena praśamayet
13.5.18 svadeśīyān vā pareṇa vā'paruddhān apavāhitasthāneṣu sthāpayet
13.5.19 yaśca tatkulīnaḥ pratyādeyaṃ ādātuṃ śaktaḥ, pratyantāṭavīstho vā prabādhituṃ abhijātaḥ, tasmai viguṇāṃ bhūmiṃ prayacchet, guṇavatyāścaturbhāgaṃ vā kośadaṇḍadānaṃ avasthāpya, yad upakurvāṇaḥ paurajānapadān kopayet
13.5.20 kupitaiḥ tairenaṃ ghātayet
13.5.21 prakṛtibhirupakruṣṭaṃ apanayet, aupaghātike vā deśe niveśayet - iti
13.5.22 bhūtapūrve yena doṣeṇāpavṛttaḥ taṃ prakṛtidoṣaṃ chādayet, yena ca guṇena upāvṛttaḥ taṃ tīvrīkuryāt - iti
13.5.23 pitrye piturdoṣāṃśchādayet, guṇāṃśca prakāśayet - iti
13.5.24ab caritraṃ akṛtaṃ dharmyaṃ kṛtaṃ cānyaiḥ pravartayet ।
13.5.24chd pravartayenna cādharmyaṃ kṛtaṃ cānyairnivartayet  (iti)

   Chapt .   parabalaghātaprayogaḥ
14.1.01 cāturvarṇyarakṣā'rthaṃ aupaniṣadikaṃ adharmiṣṭheṣu prayuñjīta
14.1.02 kālakūṭādirviṣavargaḥ śraddheyadeśaveṣaśilpabhāṣā'bhijanāpadeśaiḥ kubjavāmanakirātamūkabadhirajaḍāndhacchadmabhirmlecchajātīyairabhipretaiḥ strībhiḥ pumbhiśca paraśarīra upabhogeṣvavadhātavyaḥ
14.1.03 rājakrīḍābhāṇḍanidhānadravya upabbhogeṣu gūḍhāḥ śastranidhānaṃ kuryuḥ, sattrājīvinaśca rātricāriṇo'gnijīvinaścāgninidhānam
14.1.04 citrabhekakauṇḍinyakakṛkaṇapañcakuṣṭhaśatapadīcūrṇaṃ uccidiṇgakambalīśatakanda(kardama?) idhmakṛkalāsacūrṇaṃ gṛhagolikāndhāhikakrakaṇṭakapūtikīṭagomārikācūrṇaṃ bhallātakāvalgujarasamyuktaṃ sadyaḥprāṇaharaṃ, eteṣāṃ vā dhūmaḥ
14.1.05ab kīṭo vā'nyatamaḥ taptaḥ kṛṣṇasarpapriyaṅgubhiḥ ।
14.1.05chd śoṣayed eṣa samyogaḥ sadyaḥprāṇaharo mataḥ
14.1.06 dhāmārgavayātudhānamūlaṃ bhallātakapuṣpacūrṇayuktaṃ ārdhamāsikaḥ
14.1.07 vyāghātakamūlaṃ bhallātakapuṣpacūrṇayuktaṃ kīṭayogo māsikaḥ
14.1.08 kalāmātraṃ puruṣāṇāṃ, dviguṇaṃ kharāśvānāṃ, caturguṇaṃ hasty।uṣṭrāṇām
14.1.09 śatakardama uccidiṅgakaravīrakaṭutumbīmatsyadhūmo madanakodravapalālena hastikarṇapalāśapalālena vā pravātānuvāte praṇīto yāvaccarati tāvan mārayati
14.1.10 pūkikīṭamastyakaṭutumbīśatakardama idhma indragopacūrṇaṃ pūtikīṭakṣudrārālāhemavidārīcūrṇaṃ vā bastaśṛṅgakhuracūrṇayuktaṃ andhīkaro dhūmaḥ
14.1.11 pūtikarañjapattraharitālamanaḥśilāguñjāraktakārpāsapalālānyāsphoṭakācagośakṛdrasapiṣṭaṃ andhīkaro dhūmaḥ
14.1.12 sarpanirmokaṃ go'śvapurīṣaṃ andhāhikaśiraścāndhīkaro dhūmaḥ
14.1.13 pārāvataplavakakravyādānāṃ hastinaravarāhāṇāṃ ca mūtrapurīṣaṃ kāsīsahiṅguyavatuṣakaṇataṇḍulāḥ kārpāsakuṭajakośātakīnāṃ ca bījāni gomūtrikābhāṇḍīmūlaṃ nimbaśigruphaṇirjakākṣīvapīlukabhaṅgaḥ sarpaśapharīcarma hastinakhaśṛṅgacūrṇaṃ ityeṣa dhūmo madanakodravapalālena hastikarṇapalāśapalālena vā praṇītaḥ pratyekaśo yāvaccarati tāvan mārayati
14.1.14 kālīkuṣṭhanaḍaśatāvalīmūlaṃ sarpapracalākakṛkaṇapañcakuṣṭhacūrṇaṃ vā dhūmaḥ pūrvakalpenārdraśuṣkapalālena vā praṇītaḥ saṅgrāmāvataraṇāvaskandanasaṅkuleṣu kṛtanejana udakākṣipratīkāraiḥ praṇītaḥ sarvaprāṇināṃ netraghnaḥ
14.1.15 śārikākapotabakabalākāleṇḍaṃ arkākṣipīlukasnuhikṣīrapiṣṭaṃ andhīkaraṇaṃ añjanaṃ udakadūṣaṇaṃ ca
14.1.16 yavakaśālimūlamadanaphalajātīpattranaramūtrayogaḥ plakṣavidārīmūlayukto mūka udumbaramadanakodravakvāthayukto hastikarṇapalāśakvāthayukto vā madanayogaḥ
14.1.17 śṛṅgigautamavṛkakaṇṭakāramayūrapadīyogo guñjālāṅgalīviṣamūlika iṅgudīyogaḥ karavīrākṣipīlukārkamṛgamāraṇīyogo madnakodravakvāthayukto hastikarṇapalāśakvāthayukto vā madanayogaḥ
14.1.18 samastā vā yavasa indhana udakadūṣaṇāḥ
14.1.19 kṛtakaṇḍalakṛkalāsagṛhagolikāndhāhikadhūmo netravadhaṃ unmādaṃ ca karoti
14.1.20 kṛkalāsagṛhagolikāyogaḥ kuṣṭhakaraḥ
14.1.21 sa eva citraṃ ekāntramadhuyuktaḥ pramehaṃ āpādayati, manuṣyalohitayuktaḥ śoṣam
14.1.22 dūṣīviṣaṃ madanakodravacūrṇaṃ apajihvikāyogaḥ
14.1.23 mātṛvāhakāñjalikārapracalākabhekākṣipīlukayogo viṣūcikākaraḥ
14.1.24 pañcakuṣṭhakakauṇḍinyakarājavṛkṣapuṣpamadhuyogo jvarakaraḥ
14.1.25 bhāsanakulajihvāgranthikāyogaḥ kharīkṣīrapiṣṭo mūkabadhira।karo māsārdhamāsikaḥ
14.1.26 kalāmātraṃ puruṣāṇāṃ it samānaṃ pūrveṇa
14.1.27 bhaṅgakvātha upanayanaṃ auṣadhānāṃ, cūrṇaṃ prāṇabhṛtāṃ, sarveṣāṃ vā kvātha upanayanaṃ, evaṃ vīryavattaraṃ bhavti
14.1.28 iti yogasampat
14.1.29 śālmalī vidārīdhānyasiddho mūlavatsanābhasamyuktaścucchundarīśoṇitapralepena digdho bāṇo yaṃ vidhyati sa viddho'nyān daśapuruṣān daśati, te daṣṭā daśānyān daśanti puruṣān
14.1.30 ballātakayātudhānāvānudhāmārgavabāṇānāṃ puṣpairelakākṣigugguluhālāhalānāṃ ca kaṣāyaṃ bastanaraśoṇitayuktaṃ daṃśayogaḥ
14.1.31 tato'rdhadharaṇiko yogaḥ saktupiṇyākābhyāṃ udake praṇīto dhanuḥśatāyāmaṃ udakāśayaṃ dūṣayati
14.1.32 matsyaparamparā hyetena daṣṭā'bhimṛṣṭā vā viṣībhavati, yaśca etad udakaṃ pibati spṛśati vā
14.1.33 raktaśvetasarṣapairgodhā tripakṣaṃ uṣṭrikāyāṃ bhūmau nikhātāyāṃ nihitā vadhyena uddhṛtā yāvat paśyati tāvan mārayati, kṛṣṇasarpo vā
14.1.34 vidyutpradagdho'ṅgāro jvālo vā vidyutpradagdhaiḥ kāṣṭhairgṛhītaścānuvāsitaḥ kṛttikāsu bharaṇīṣu vā raudreṇa karmaṇā'bhihuto'gniḥ praṇītaśca nispratīkāro dahati
14.1.35ab karmārād agniṃ āhṛtya kṣaudreṇa juhuyāt pṛthak ।
14.1.35chd surayā śauṇḍikād agniṃ mārgato'gniṃ ghṛtena ca
14.1.36ab mālyena ca ekapatny'gniṃ puṃścaly'gniṃ ca sarṣapaiḥ ।
14.1.36chd dadhnā ca sūtikāsvagniṃ āhitāgniṃ ca taṇḍulaiḥ
14.1.37ab caṇḍālāgniṃ ca māṃsena citāgniṃ mānuṣeṇa ca
14.1.37chd samastān bastavasayā mānuṣeṇa dhruveṇa ca
14.1.38ab juhuyād agnimantreṇa rājavṛkṣasya dārubhiḥ ।
14.1.38chd eṣa niṣpratikāro'gnirdviṣatāṃ netramohanaḥ

14.2.01 śirīṣa udumbaraśamīcūrṇaṃ sarpiṣā saṃhṛtyārdhamāsikaḥ kṣudyogaḥ
14.2.02 kaśeruka utpalakandekṣumūlabisadūrvākṣīraghṛtamaṇḍasiddho māsikaḥ
14.2.03 māṣayavakulatthadarbhamūlacūrṇaṃ vā kṣīraghṛtābhyāṃ, vallīkṣīraghṛtaṃ vā samasiddhaṃ, sālapṛśniparṇīmūlakalkaṃ payasā pītvā, payo vā tatsiddhaṃ madhughṛtābhyāṃ aśitvā māsaṃ upavasati
14.2.04 śvetabastamūtre saptarātra uṣitaiḥ siddhārthakaiḥ siddhaṃ tailaṃ kaṭukālābau māsārdhamāsasthitaṃ catuṣpadadvipadānāṃ virūpakaraṇam
14.2.05 takrayavabhakṣasya saptarātrād ūrdhvaṃ śvetagardabhasya leṇḍayavaiḥ siddhaṃ gaurasarṣapatailaṃ virūpakaraṇam
14.2.06 etayoranyatarasya mūtraleṇḍarasasiddhaṃ siddhārthakatailaṃ arkatūlapataṅgacūrṇapratīvāpaṃ śvetīkaraṇam
14.2.07 śvetakukkuṭājagaraleṇḍayogaḥ śvetīkaraṇam

14.2.09 kaṭukālābau valīgate gataṃ'rdhamāsasthitaṃ gaurasarṣapapiṣṭaṃ romṇāṃ śvetīkaraṇam
14.2.10ab alojuneti yaḥ kīṭaḥ śvetā ca gṛhagolikā ।

14.2.13 śukapittāṇḍarasābhyaṅgaḥ kuṣṭhayogaḥ

14.2.17 śakunakaṇgutailayuktā haritālamanaḥśilāḥ śyāmīkaraṇam

14.2.19 khadyotagaṇḍūpadacūrṇaṃ samudrajantūnāṃ bhṛṅgakapālānāṃ khadirakarṇikārāṇāṃ puṣpacūrṇaṃ vā śakunakaṅgutailayuktaṃ tejanacūrṇam
14.2.20 pāribhadrakatvanmaṣī maṇḍūkavasayā yuktā gātraprajvālanaṃ agninā

14.2.25 maṇḍūkakulīrādīnāṃ vasayā samabhāgaṃ tailaṃ siddhaṃ abhyaṅgaṃ gātrāṇāṃ agniprajvālanam
14.2.26 veṇumūlaśaivalaliptaṃ aṅgaṃ maṇḍūkavasādigdhaṃ agninā jvalati
14.2.27 pāribhadrakappatibalāvañjulavajrakadalīmūlakalkena maṇḍūkavasāsiddhena tailenābhyaktapādo'ṅgāreṣu gacchati
14.2.28ab upa udakā pratibalā vañjulaḥ pāribhadrakaḥ ।
14.2.28chd eteṣāṃ mūlakalkena maṇḍūkavasayā saha

14.2.29chd aṅgārarāśau vicared yathā kusumasañcaye
14.2.30 haṃsakrauñcamayūrāṇāṃ anyeṣāṃ vā mahāśakunīnāṃ udakaplavānāṃ puccheṣu baddhā naladīpikā rātrāvulkādarśanam

14.2.32 strīpuṣpapāyitā māṣā vrajakulīmūlaṃ maṇḍūkavasāmiśraṃ culluyāṃ dīptāyāṃ apācanam
14.2.33 cullīśodhanaṃ pratīkāraḥ
14.2.34 pīlumayo maṇiragnigarbhaḥ suvarcalāmūlagranthiḥ sūtragranthirvā picupariveṣṭito mukhyād agnidhūma utsargaḥ
14.2.35 kuśāmraphalatailasikto'gnirvarṣapravāteṣu jvalati
14.2.36 samudraphenakaḥ tailayukto'mbhasi plavamāno jvalati
14.2.37 plavamānānāṃ asthiṣu kalmāṣaveṇunā nirmathito'gnirna udakena śāmyati, udakena jvalati
14.2.38 śastrahatasya śūlaprotasya vā puruṣasya vāmapārśvaparśukāsthiṣu kalmāṣaveṇunā nirmathito'gniḥ striyāḥ puruṣasya vā'sthiṣu manuṣyaparśukayā nirmathito'gniryatra trirapasavyaṃ gacchati na cātrānyo'gnirjvalati
14.2.39ab cuccundarī khañjarīṭaḥ khārakīṭaśca piṣyate ।
14.2.39chd aśvamūtreṇa saṃsṛṣṭā nigalānāṃ tu bhañjanam
14.2.40 ayaskānto vā pāṣāṇaḥ kulīradardurakhārakīṭavasāpradehena dviguṇaḥ
14.2.41 nārakagarbhaḥ kaṅkabhāsapārśva utpala udakapiṣṭaścatuṣpadadvipadānāṃ pādalepaḥ
14.2.42 ulūkagṛdhravasābhyāṃ uṣṭracarma upānahāvabhyajya vaṭapattraiḥ praticchādya pañcāśadyojanānyaśrānto gacchati
14.2.43 śyenakaṅkakākagṛdhrahaṃsakrauñcavīcīrallānāṃ majjāno retāṃsi vā yojanaśatāya, siṃhavyāghradvīpakāka ulūkānāṃ majjāno retāṃsi vā
14.2.44 sārvavarṇikāni garbhapatanānyuṣṭrikāyāṃ abhiṣūya śmaśāne pretaśiśūn vā tatsamutthitaṃ medo yojanaśatāya
14.2.45a aniṣṭairadbhuta utpātaiḥ parasya udvegaṃ ācaret ।
14.2.45b ārājyāya iti nirvādaḥ samānaḥ kopa ucyate  (iti)
   Chapt .   pralambhanaṃ, tatra bhaiṣajyamantrayogaḥ
14.3.01 mārjāra uṣṭravṛkavarāhaśvāvidvāgulīnaptṛkāka ulūkānāṃ anyeṣāṃ vā niśācarāṇāṃ sattvānāṃ ekasya dvayorbahūnāṃ vā dakṣiṇāni vāmāni cākṣīṇi gṛhītvā dvidhā cūrṇaṃ kārayet
14.3.02 tato dakṣiṇaṃ vāmena vāmaṃ dakṣiṇena samabhyajya rātrau tamasi ca paśyati
14.3.03ab ekāmlakaṃ varāhākṣi khadyotaḥ kālaśārivā ।
14.3.03chd etenābhyaktanayano rātrau rūpāṇi paśyati
14.3.04 trirātra upoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa śastrahatasya śūlaprotasya vā puṃsaḥ śiraḥkapāle mṛttikāyāṃ yavān āvāsyāvikṣīreṇa secayet
14.3.05 tato yavavirūḍhamālāṃ ābadhya naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati
14.3.06 triratra upoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa śvamārjāra ulūkavāgulīnāṃ dakṣiṇāni vāmāni cākṣīṇi dvidhā cūrṇaṃ kārayet
14.3.07 tato yathāsvaṃ abhyaktākṣo naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati
14.3.08 trirātra upoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa puruṣaghātinaḥ kāṇḍakasya śalākāṃ añjanīṃ ca kārayet
14.3.09 tato anyatamenākṣicūrṇenābhyaktākṣo naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati
14.3.10 trirātra upoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa kālāyasīṃ añjanīṃ śalākāṃ ca kārayet
14.3.11 tato niśācarāṇāṃ sattvānāṃ anyatamasya śiraḥkapālaṃ añjanena pūrayitvā mṛtāyāḥ striyā yonau praveśya dāhayet
14.3.12 tad añjanaṃ puṣyeṇa uddhṛtya tasyāṃ añjanyāṃ nidadhyāt
14.3.13 tenābhyaktākṣo naṣṭachāyārūpaścarati
14.3.14 yatra brāhmaṇaṃ āhitāgniṃ dagdhaṃ dahyamānaṃ vā paśyet tatra trirātra upoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa svayaṃmṛtasya vāsasā prasevaṃ kṛtvā citābhasmanā pūrayitvā taṃ ābadhya naṣṭacchāyārūpaścarati
14.3.15 brāhmaṇasya pretakārye yo gaurmāryate tasyāsthimajjacūrṇapūrṇā'hibhastrā paśūnāṃ antardhānam
14.3.16 sarpadaṣṭasya bhasmanā pūrṇā pracalākabhastrā mṛgāṇāṃ antardhānam
14.3.17 ulūkavāgulīpucchapurīṣajānv'sthicūrṇapūrṇā'hibhastrā pakṣiṇāṃ antardhānam
14.3.18 ityaṣṭāvantardhānayogaḥ
14.3.19ab baliṃ vairocanaṃ vande śatamāyaṃ ca śambaram ।
14.3.19chd bhaṇḍīrapākaṃ narakaṃ nikumbhaṃ kumbhaṃ eva ca
14.3.20ab devalaṃ nāradaṃ vande vande sāvarṇigālavam ।
14.3.20chd eteṣāṃ anuyogena kṛtaṃ te svāpanaṃ mahat
14.3.21ab yathā svapantyajagarāḥ svapantyapi camūkhalāḥ ।
14.3.21chd tathā svapantu puruṣā ye ca grāme kutūhalāḥ
14.3.22ab bhaṇḍakānāṃ sahasreṇa rathanemiśatena ca ।
14.3.22chd imaṃ gṛhaṃ pravekṣyāmi tūṣṇīṃ āsantu bhāṇḍakāḥ
14.3.23ab namaskṛtvā ca manave baddhvā śunakaphelakāḥ ।
14.3.23chd ye devā devalokeṣu mānuṣeṣu ca brāhmaṇāḥ
14.3.24ab adhyayanapāragāḥ siddhā ye ca kaulāsa tāpasāḥ ।
14.3.24chd etebhyaḥ sarvasiddhebhyaḥ kṛtaṃ te svāpanaṃ mahat
14.3.25 atigacchanti ca mayyapagacchantu saṃhatāḥ
14.3.26 alite, valite, manave svāhā
14.3.27 etasya prayogaḥ
14.3.28 trirātra upoṣitaḥ kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ puṣyayoginyāṃ śvapākīhastād vilakhāvalekhanaṃ krīṇīyāt
14.3.29 tanmāṣaiḥ saha kaṇḍolikāyāṃ kṛtvā'saṅkīrṇa ādahane nikhānayet
14.3.30 dvitīyasyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ uddhṛtya kumāryā peṣayitvā gulikāḥ kārayet
14.3.31 tata ekāṃ gulikāṃ abhimantrayitvā yatra etana mantreṇa kṣipati tat sarvaṃ prasvāpayati
14.3.32 etena eva kalpena śvāvidhaḥ śalyakaṃ trikālaṃ triśvetaṃ asaṅkīrṇa ādahane nikhānayet
14.3.33 dvitīyasyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ uddhṛtyādahanabhasmanā saha yatra etena mantreṇa kṣipati tat sarvaṃ prasvāpayati
14.3.34ab suvarṇapuṣpīṃ brahmāṇīṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca kuśadhvajam ।
14.3.34chd sarvāśca devatā vande vande sarvāṃśca tāpasān
14.3.35ab vaśaṃ me brāhmaṇā yāntu bhūmipālāśca kṣatriyāḥ ।
14.3.35chd vaśaṃ vaiśyāśca śūdrāśca vaśatāṃ yāntu me sadā
14.3.36 svāhā - amile kimile vayucāre prayoge phakke vayuhve vihāle dantakaṭake svāhā
14.3.37ab sukhaṃ svapantu śunakā ye ca grāme kutūhalāḥ ।
14.3.37chd śvāvidhaḥ śalyakaṃ ca etat triśvetaṃ brahmanirmitam
14.3.38ab prasuptāḥ sarvasiddhā hi etat te svāpanaṃ kṛtam ।
14.3.38chd yāvad grāmasya sīmāntaḥ sūryasya udgamanād iti
14.3.39 svāhā
14.3.40 etasya prayogaḥ
14.3.41 śvāvidhaḥ śalyakāni triśvetāni, saptarātra upoṣitaḥ kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ khādirābhiḥ samidhāmir(?) agniṃ etena mantreṇāṣṭaśatasampātaṃ kṛtvā madhughṛtābhyāṃ abhijuhuyāt
14.3.42 tata ekaṃ etena mantreṇa grāmadvāri gṛhadvāri vā yatra nikhanyate tat sarvaṃ prasvāpayati
14.3.43ab baliṃ vairocanaṃ vande śatamāyaṃ ca śambaram ।
14.3.43chd nikumbhaṃ narakaṃ kumbhaṃ tantukacchaṃ mahā'suram
14.3.44ab armālavaṃ pramīlaṃ ca maṇḍa ulūkaṃ ghaṭa ubalam ।
14.3.44chd kṛṣṇakaṃsa upacāraṃ ca paulomīṃ ca yaśasvinīm
14.3.45ab abhimantrayitvā gṛhṇāmi siddhy'rthaṃ śavaśārikām ।
14.3.45chd jayatu jayati ca namaḥ śalakabhūtebhyaḥ svāhā
14.3.46ab sukhaṃ svapantu śunakā ye ca grāme kutūhalāḥ ।
14.3.46chd sukhaṃ svapantu siddhārthā yaṃ arthaṃ mārgayāmahe ।
14.3.46ech yāvad astaṃ ayād udayo yāvad arthaṃ phalaṃ mama
14.3.47 iti svāhā
14.3.48 etasya prayogaḥ
14.3.49 caturbhakta upavāsī kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ asaṅkīrṇa ādahane baliṃ kṛtvā etena mantreṇa śavaśārikāṃ gṛhītvā pautrīpoṭṭalikaṃ badhnīyāt
14.3.50 tanmadhye śvāvidhaḥ śalyakena viddhvā yatra etena mantreṇa nikhanyate tat sarvaṃ prasvāpayati
14.3.51ab upaimi śaraṇaṃ cāgniṃ daivatāni diśo daśa ।
14.3.51chd apayāntu ca sarvāṇi vaśatāṃ yāntu me sadā
14.3.52 svāhā
14.3.53 etasya prayogaḥ
14.3.54 trirātra uposṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa śarkarā ekaviṃśatisampātaṃ kṛtvā madhughṛtābhyāṃ abhijuhuyāt
14.3.55 tato gandhamālyena pūjayitvā nikhānayet
14.3.56 dvitīyena puṣyeṇa uddhṛtya ekāṃ śarkarāṃ abhimantrayitvā kapāṭaṃ āhanyāt
14.3.57 abhyantarṃ catasṛṇāṃ śarkarāṇāṃ dvāraṃ apāvriyate
14.3.58 caturbhakta upavāsī kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ bhagnasya puruṣasyāsthnā ṛṣabhaṃ kārayet, abhimantrayecca etena
14.3.59 dvigoyuktaṃ goyānaṃ āhṛtaṃ bhavati
14.3.60 tataḥ paramākāśe virāmati
14.3.61 ravisagandhaḥ parighamati sarvaṃ pṛṇāti
14.3.62 caṇḍālīkumbhītumbakaṭukasāroghaḥ sanārībhago'si - svāhā
14.3.63 tāla udghāṭanaṃ prasvāpanaṃ ca
14.3.64 trirātra upoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa śastrahatasya śūlaprotasya vā puṃsaḥ śiraḥkapāle mṛttikāyāṃ tuvarīrāvāsya udakena secayet
14.3.65 jātānāṃ puṣyeṇa eva gṛhītvā rajjukāṃ vartayet
14.3.66 tataḥ sajyānāṃ dhanuṣāṃ yantrāṇāṃ ca purastācchedanaṃ jyācchedanaṃ karoti
14.3.67 udakāhibhastrāṃ ucchvāsamṛttikayā striyāḥ puruṣasya vā pūrayet, nāsikābandhanaṃ mukhagrahaśca
14.3.68 varāhabhastrāṃ ucchvāsamṛttikayā pūrayitvā markaṭasnāyunā'vabadhnīyāt, ānāhakāraṇam
14.3.69 kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ śastrahatāyā goḥ kapilāyāḥ pittena rājavṛkṣamayīṃ amitrapratimāṃ añjyāt, andhīkaraṇam
14.3.70 caturbhakta upavāsī kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ baliṃ kṛtvā śūlaprotasya puruṣasyāsthnā kīlakān kārayet
14.3.71 eteṣāṃ ekaḥ purīṣe mūtre vā nikhāta ānāhaṃ karoti, pade'syāsane vā nikhātaḥ śoṣeṇa mārayati, āpaṇe kṣetre gṛhe vā vṛtticchedaṃ karoti
14.3.72 etena eva kalpena vidyuddagdhasya vṛkṣasya kīlakā vyākhyātāḥ
14.3.73ab punarnavaṃ avācīnaṃ nimbaḥ kāmamadhuśca yaḥ ।
14.3.73chd kapiroma manuṣyāsthi baddhvā mṛtakavāsasā
14.3.74ab nikhanyate gṛhe yasya dṛṣṭvā vā yat padaṃ nayet ।
14.3.74chd saputradāraḥ sadhanastrīn pakṣānnātivartate
14.3.75ab punarnavaṃ avācīnaṃ nimbaḥ kāmamadhuśca yaḥ ।
14.3.75chd svayaṅguptā manuṣyāsthi pade yasya nikhanyate
14.3.76ab dvāre gṛhasya senāyā grāmasya nagarasya vā ।
14.3.76chd saputradāraḥ sadhanastrīn pakṣānnātivartate
14.3.77ab ajamarkaṭaromāṇi mārjāranakulasya ca ।
14.3.77chd brāhmaṇānāṃ śvapākānāṃ kāka ulūkasya cāharet ।
14.3.77chd etena viṣṭhā'vakṣuṇṇā sadya utsādakārikā
14.3.78ab pretanirmālikā kiṇvaṃ romāṇi nakulasya ca ।
14.3.78chd vṛścikāly(?) ahikṛttiśca pade yasya nikhanyate ।
14.3.78ef bhavatyapuruṣaḥ sadyo yāvat tannāpanīyate
14.3.79 trirātra upoṣitaḥ puṣyeṇa śastrahatasya śūlaprotasya vā puṃsaḥ śiraḥkapāle mṛttikāyāṃ guñjā āvāsya udakena secayet
14.3.80 jātānāṃ amāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā puṣyayoginyāṃ guñjavallīrgrāhayitvā maṇḍalikāni kārayet
14.3.81 teṣvannapānabhājanāni nyastāni na kṣīyante
14.3.82 rātriprekṣāyāṃ pravṛttāyāṃ pradīpāgniṣu mṛtadhenoḥ stanān utkṛtya dāhayet
14.3.83 dagdhān vṛṣamūtreṇa peṣayitvā navakumbhaṃ antarlepayet
14.3.84 taṃ grāmaṃ apasavyaṃ pariṇīya yat tatra nyastaṃ navanītaṃ eṣāṃ tat sarvaṃ āgacchati
14.3.85 kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ puṣyayoginyāṃ śuno lagnakasya yonau kālāyasīṃ mudrikāṃ preṣayet
14.3.85 tāṃ svayaṃ patitāṃ gṛhṇīyāt
14.3.87 tayā vṛkṣaphalānyākāritānyāgacchanti
14.3.88ab mantrabhaiṣajyasamyuktā yogā māyākṛtāśca ye ।
14.3.88chd upahanyād amitrāṃḥ taiḥ svajanaṃ cābhipālayet  (iti)
   Chapt .   svabala upaghātapratīkāraḥ
14.4.01 svapakṣe paraprayuktānāṃ dūṣīviṣagarāṇāṃ pratīkāraḥ
14.4.02 śleṣmātakakapitthadantidantaśaṭhagojiśirīṣapāṭalībalāsyonāgapunarnavāśvetavāraṇakvāthayuktam(?) candanasālāvṛkīlohitayuktaṃ nejana udakaṃ rāja upabhogyānāṃ guhyaprakṣālanaṃ strīṇāṃ, senāyāśca viṣapratīkāraḥ
14.4.03 pṛṣatanakulanīlakaṇṭhagodhāpittayuktaṃ mahīrājīcūrṇaṃ sinduvāritavaraṇavāruṇītaṇḍulīyakaśataparvāgrapiṇḍītakayogo madanadoṣaharaḥ
14.4.04 sṛgālavinnāmadanasinduvāritavaraṇavāraṇavalīmūlakaṣāyāṇāṃ anyatamasya samastānāṃ vā kṣīrayuktaṃ pānaṃ madanadoṣaharam
14.4.05 kaiḍaryapūtitilatailaṃ unmādaharaṃ nastaḥkarma
14.4.06 priyaṅgunaktamālayogaḥ kuṣṭhaharaḥ
14.4.07 kuṣṭhalodhrayogaḥ pākaśoṣaghnaḥ
14.4.08 kaṭaphaladravantīvilaṅgacūrṇaṃ nastaḥkarma śirorogaharam

14.4.10 manuṣyāṇāṃ akṣamātraṃ, gavāśvānāṃ dviguṇaṃ, caturguṇaṃ hasty।uṣṭrāṇām
14.4.11 rukmagarbhaśca eṣāṃ maṇiḥ sarvaviṣaharaḥ
14.4.12 jīvantīśvetāmuṣkakapuṣpavandākānāṃ akṣīve jātasyāśvatthasya maṇiḥ sarvaviṣaharaḥ
14.4.13ab tūryāṇāṃ taiḥ praliptānāṃ śabdo viṣavināśanaḥ ।
14.4.13chd liptadhvajaṃ patākāṃ vā dṛṣṭvā bhavati nirviṣaḥ
14.4.14ab etaiḥ kṛtvā pratīkāraṃ svasainyānāṃ athātmanaḥ ।
14.4.14chd amitreṣu prayuñjīta viṣadhūmāmbudūṣaṇān  (iti)

15.1.01 manuṣyāṇāṃ vṛttirarthaḥ, manuṣyavatī bhūmirityarthaḥ
15.1.02 tasyāḥ pṛthivyā lābhapālana upāyaḥ śāstraṃ arthaśāstraṃ iti
15.1.03 taddvātriṃśad yuktiyuktaṃ - adhikaraṇaṃ, vidhānaṃ, yogaḥ, padārthaḥ, hetv'rthaḥ, uddeśaḥ, nirdeśaḥ, upadeśaḥ, apadeśaḥ, atideśaḥ, pradeśaḥ, upamānaṃ, arthāpattiḥ, saṃśayaḥ, prasaṅgaḥ, viparyayaḥ, vākyaśeṣaḥ, anumataṃ, vyākhyānaṃ, nirvacanaṃ, nidarśanaṃ, apavargaḥ, svasaṃjñā, pūrvapakṣaḥ, uttarapakṣaḥ, ekāntaḥ, anāgatāvekṣaṇaṃ, atikrāntāvekṣaṇaṃ, niyogaḥ, vikalpaḥ, samuccayaḥ ūhyaṃ iti
15.1.04 yaṃ arthaṃ adhikṛtya ucyate tad adhikaraṇam
15.1.05 pṛthivyā lābhe pālane ca yāvantyarthaśāstrāṇi pūrvācāryaiḥ prasthāpitāni prāyaśaḥ tāni saṃhṛtya ekaṃ idaṃ arthaśāstraṃ kṛtam iti
15.1.06 śāstrasya prakaraṇānupūrvī vidhānam
15.1.07 vidyāsamuddeśaḥ, vṛddhasamyogaḥ, indriyajayaḥ, amātya utpattiḥ ityevaṃ।ādikaṃ iti
15.1.08 vākyayojanā yogaḥ
15.1.09 caturvarṇāśramo lokaḥ iti
15.1.10 padāvadhikaḥ padārthaḥ
15.1.11 mūlahara iti padam
15.1.12 yaḥ pitṛpaitāmahaṃ arthaṃ anyāyena bhakṣayati sa mūlaharaḥ ityarthaḥ
15.1.13 heturarthasādhako hetv'rthaḥ
15.1.14 arthamūlau hi dharmakāmau iti
15.1.15 samāsavākyaṃ uddeśaḥ
15.1.16 vidyāvinayaheturindriyajayaḥ iti
15.1.17 vyāsavākyaṃ nirdeśaḥ
15.1.18 karṇatvag'kṣijihvāghrāṇa indriyāṇāṃ śabdasparśarūparasagandheṣvavipratipattirindriyajayaḥiti
15.1.19 evaṃ vartitavyaṃ ityupadeśaḥ
15.1.20 dharmārthavirodhena kāmaṃ seveta, na nihsukhaḥ syāt iti
15.1.21 evaṃ asāvāha ityapadeśaḥ
15.1.22 mantripariṣadaṃ dvādaśāmātyān kurvīta iti mānavāḥ - ṣoḍaśa iti bārhaspatyāḥ - viṃśatiṃ ityauśanasāḥ - yathāsāmarthyaṃ iti kauṭilyaḥ iti
15.1.23 uktena sādhanaṃ atideśaḥ
15.1.24 dattasyāpradānaṃ ṛṇādānena vyākhyātam iti
15.1.25 vaktavyena sādhanaṃ pradeśaḥ
15.1.26 sāmadānabhedadaṇḍairvā, yathā''patsu vyākhyāsyāmaḥ iti
15.1.27 dṛṣṭenādṛṣṭasya sādhanaṃ upamānam
15.1.28 nivṛttaparihārān pitā ivānugṛhṇīyāt iti
15.1.29 yad anuktaṃ arthād āpadyate sā'rthāpattiḥ
15.1.30 lokayātrāvid rājānaṃ ātmadravyaprakṛtisampannaṃ priyahitadvāreṇāśrayeta
15.1.31 nāpriyahitadvāreṇāśrayeta ityarthād āpannaṃ bhavati iti
15.1.32 ubhayatohetumān arthaḥ saṃśayaḥ
15.1.33 kṣīṇalubdhaprakṛtiṃ apacaritaprakṛtiṃ vā iti
15.1.34 prakaraṇāntareṇa samāno'rthaḥ prasaṅgaḥ
15.1.35 kṛṣikarmapradiṣṭāyāṃ bhūmau - iti samānaṃ pūrveṇa iti
15.1.36 pratilomena sādhanaṃ viparyayaḥ
15.1.37 viparītaṃ atuṣṭasya iti
15.1.38 yena vākyaṃ samāpyate sa vākyaśeṣaḥ
15.1.39 chinnapakṣasya iva rājñaśceṣṭānāśaśca iti
15.1.40 tatra śakuneḥ iti vākyaśeṣaḥ
15.1.41 paravākyaṃ apratiṣiddhaṃ anumatam
15.1.42 pakṣāvurasyaṃ pratigraha ityauśanaso vyūhavibhāgaḥ iti
15.1.43 atiśayavarṇanā vyākhyānam
15.1.44 viśeṣataśca saṅghānāṃ saṅghadharmiṇāṃ ca rājakulānāṃ dyūtanimitto bhedaḥ tannimitto vināśa ityasatpragrahaḥ pāpiṣṭhatamo vyasanānāṃ tantradaurbalyāt iti
15.1.45 guṇataḥ śabdaniṣpattirnirvacanam
15.1.46 vyasyatyenaṃ śreyasa iti vyasanam iti
15.1.47 dṛṣṭānto dṛṣṭāntayukto nidarśanam
15.1.48 vigṛhīto hi jyāyasā hastinā pādayuddhaṃ ivābhyupaiti iti
15.1.49 abhiplutavyapakarṣaṇaṃ apavargaḥ
15.1.50 nityaṃ āsannaṃ aribalaṃ vāsayed anyatrābhyantarakopaśaṅkāyāḥ iti
15.1.51 parairasamitaḥ śabdaḥ svasaṃjñā
15.1.52 prathamā prakṛtiḥ, tasya bhūmy'nantarā dvitīyā, bhūmy।ekāntarā tṛtīyā iti
15.1.53 pratiṣeddhavyaṃ vākyaṃ pūrvapakṣaḥ
15.1.54 svāmy'mātyavyasanayoramātyavyasanaṃ garīyaḥ iti
15.1.55 tasya nirṇayanavākyaṃ uttarapakṣaḥ
15.1.56 tad।āyattatvāt, tatkūṭasthānīyo hi svāmī iti
15.1.57 sarvatrāyattaṃ ekāntaḥ
15.1.58 tasmād utthānaṃ ātmanaḥ kurvīta iti
15.1.59 paścād evaṃ vihitaṃ ityanāgatāvekṣaṇam
15.1.60 tulāpratimānaṃ pautavādhyakṣe vakṣyāmaḥ iti
15.1.61 purastād evaṃ vihitaṃ ityatikrāntāveṣkaṇam
15.1.62 amātyasampad uktā purastāt iti
15.1.63 evaṃ nānyathā iti niyogaḥ
15.1.64 tasmād dharmyaṃ arthyaṃ cāsya upadiśet, nādharmyaṃ anarthayṃ ca iti
15.1.65 anena vā'nena vā iti vikalpaḥ
15.1.66 duhitaro vā dharmiṣṭheṣu vivāheṣu jātāḥ iti
15.1.67 anena cānena ca iti samuccayaḥ
15.1.68 svayañjātaḥ piturbandhūnāṃ ca dāyādaḥ iti
15.1.69 anuktakaraṇaṃ ūhyam
15.1.70 yathā ca dātā pratigrahītā ca na upahatau syātāṃ tathā'nuśayaṃ kuśalāḥ kalpayeyuḥ iti
15.1.71ab evaṃ śāstraṃ idaṃ yuktaṃ etābhiḥ tantrayuktibhiḥ ।
15.1.71chd avāptau pālane ca uktaṃ lokasyāsya parasya ca
15.1.72ab dharmaṃ arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca pravartayati pāti ca ।
15.1.72chd adharmānarthavidveṣān idaṃ śāstraṃ nihanti ca
15.1.73ab yena śāstraṃ ca śastraṃ ca nandarājagatā ca bhūḥ ।
15.1.73chd amarṣeṇa uddhṛtānyāśu tena śāstraṃ idaṃ kṛtam  (iti)
 End of the ArthashAstra
